 ON &d;&ae;re tide &d;e Gotan of Sci&d;&d;iu m&ae;g&d;e wi&d; Romana rice gewin up ahofon  &amp; mid heora cyningum  R&ae;dgota &amp; Eallerica w&ae;ron hatne  Romane burig abr&ae;con  &amp; eall Italia rice &t;&ae;t is betwux &t;am muntum &amp; Sicilia &t;am ealonde in anwald gerehton  &amp; &t;a &ae;fter &t;am foresprecenan cyningum &T;eodric feng to &t;am ilcan rice. 
 Se &d;eodric w&ae;s Amulinga; he w&ae;s cristen  &t;eah he on &t;am arrianiscan gedwolan &t;urhwunode. 
 He gehet Romanum his freondscipe  swa &t;&ae;t hi mostan heora ealdrihta wyr&d;e beon. 
 Ac he &t;a gehat swi&d;e yfele gel&ae;ste  &amp; swi&d;e wra&d;e geendode mia manegum mane. 
 &t;&ae;t w&ae;s toeacan o&d;rum unarimedum yflum &t;&ae;t he Iohannes &t;one papan het ofslean. 
 &t;a w&ae;s sum consul  &t;&ae;t we heretoha hata&d;  Boetius w&ae;s gehaten; se w&ae;s in boccr&ae;ftum &amp; on woruld&t;eawum se rihtwisesta. 
 Se &t;a ongeat &t;a manigfealdan yfel &t;e se cyning &D;eodric wi&d; &t;am cristenandome &amp; wi&d; &t;am romaniscum witum dyde. 
 He &t;a gemunde &t;ara e&d;nessa &amp; &t;ara ealdrihta &t;e hi under &t;am caserum h&ae;fdon heora ealdhlafordum. 
 &t;a ongan he smeagan &amp; leornigan on him selfum hu he &t;&ae;t rice &t;am unrihtwisan cyninge aferran mihte  &amp; on ryhtgeleaffulra &amp; on rihtwisra anwealde gebringan. 
 Sende &t;a digellice arendgewritu to &t;am kasere to Constentinopolim  &t;&ae;r is Creca heahburg &amp; heora cynestol  for&t;am se kasere w&ae;s heora ealdhlafordcynnes. 
 b&ae;don hine &t;&ae;t he him to heora cristendome &amp; to heora ealdrihtum gefultumede. 
 &t;a &t;&ae;t ongeat se w&ae;lhreowa cyning &d;eodric  &t;a het he hine gebringan on carcerne &amp; &t;&ae;rinne belucan. 
 &t;a hit &d;a gelomp &t;&ae;t se arwyr&d;a w&ae;s on swa micelre nearanesse becom  &t;a w&ae;s he swa micle swi&d;or on his mode gedrefed swa his mod &ae;r swi&d;or to &t;am worulds&ae;l&t;um gewunod w&ae;s. 
 &amp; he &t;a nanre frofre beinnan &t;am carcerne ne gemunde; ac he gefeoll niwol ofdune on &t;a flor  &amp; hine astrehte swi&d;e unrot  &amp; ormod hine selfne ongan wepan &amp; &t;us singend cw&ae;&d;: &d;a lio&d; &t;e ic wrecca geo lustb&ae;rlice song ic sceal nu heofiende singan  &amp; mid swi&t;e ungeradum wordum gesettan  &t;eah ic geo hwilum gecoplice funde; ac ic nu wepende &amp; gisciende ofgeradra worda misfo. 
 Me ablendan &t;as ungetreowan worulds&ae;l&t;a  &amp; me &t;a forletan swa blindne on &t;is dimme hol &amp; me &t;a bereafodon &ae;lcere lustb&ae;rnesse &t;a &d;a ic him &ae;fre betst truwode; &t;a wendon hi me heora b&ae;c to  &amp; me mid ealle from gewitan. 
 To hwon sceoldan la mine friend seggan &t;&ae;t ic ges&ae;lig mon w&ae;re? 
 Hu m&ae;g se beon ges&ae;lig se &t;e on &t;am ges&ae;l&t;um &t;urhwunian ne mot? 
 &T;a ic &t;a &t;is leo&d;  cw&ae;&d; Boetius  geomriende asungen h&ae;fde  &t;a com &t;&ae;r gan in to me heofencund Wisdom  &amp; &t;&ae;t min murnende mod mid his wordum gegrette  &amp; &t;us cw&ae;&d;: Hu ne eart &d;u se mon &t;e on minre scole w&ae;re afed &amp; gel&ae;red? 
 Ac hwonon wurde &t;u mid &t;issum woruldsorgum &t;us swi&d;e geswenced? 
 buton ic wat &t;&ae;t &t;u h&ae;fst &t;ara w&ae;pna to hra&d;e forgiten &t;e ic &t;e &ae;r sealde. 
 &d;a clipode se Wisdom &amp; cw&ae;&d;: Gewita&t; nu awirgede woruldsorga of mines &t;egenes mode  for&t;am ge sind &t;a m&ae;stan scea&t;an. 
 L&ae;ta&t; hine eft hweorfan to minum larum. 
 &d;a eode se Wisdom near  cw&ae;&d; Boetius  minum hreowsiendum ge&t;ohte  &amp; hit swa niowul &t;a hw&ae;thwega up ar&ae;rde; adrigde &t;a mines modes eagan  &amp; hit fran bli&t;um wordum hw&ae;&d;er hit oncneowe his fostermodor. 
 Mid &t;am &t;e &d;a &t;&ae;t Mod wi&d; his bewende  &t;a gecneow hit swi&d;e sweotele his agne modor; &t;&ae;t w&ae;s se Wisdom &d;e hit lange &ae;r tyde &amp; l&ae;rde. 
 Ac hit ongeat his lare swi&d;e toterenne &amp; swi&d;e tobrocene mid dysigra hondum  &amp; hine &t;a fran hu &t;&ae;t gewurde. 
 &d;a andwyrde se Wisdom him &amp; s&ae;de &t;&ae;t his gingran h&ae;fdon hine swa toterenne  &t;&ae;r &t;&ae;r hi teohhodon &t;&ae;t hi hine eallne habban sceoldon. ac hi gegaderia&d; monifeald dysig on &d;&ae;re fortruwunga &amp; on &t;am gilpe  butan heora hwelc eft to hyre bote gecirre. 
 &d;a ongan se Wisdom hreowsian for &t;&ae;s Modes tydernesse  &amp; ongan &t;a giddian &amp; &t;us cw&ae;&d;: Eala on hu grundleasum sea&d;e &t;&ae;t mod drig&d;  &t;onne hit bestyrma&d; &t;isse worulde unge&t;w&ae;rnessa. 
 Gif hit &t;onne forget his ahgen leoht  &t;&ae;t is ece gefea  &amp; &d;ring&d; on &t;a fremdan &t;istro  &t;&ae;t sind woruldsorga  swa swa &d;is Mod nu de&d;  nu hit nauht elles nat butan gnornunga. 
 &t;a se Wisdom &t;a &amp; seo Gesceadwisnes &t;is leo&d; asungen h&ae;fdon  &t;a ongan he eft sprecan &amp; cw&ae;&d; to &t;an Mode: Ic geseo &t;&ae;t &t;e is nu frofres mare &t;earf &t;onne unrotnesse. 
 For&t;an gif &t;u &t;e ofsceamian wilt &t;ines gedwolan  &t;onne onginne ic &t;e sona beran &amp; bringe mid me to heofonum. 
 &t;a andsworode him &t;&ae;t unrote Mod &amp; cw&ae;&d;: Hw&ae;t la hw&ae;t  sint &t;is nu &t;a god &amp; &t;a edlean &t;e &t;u ealne weg gehete &t;am monnum &t;e &t;e heorsumian woldan? 
 Is &t;is nu se cwide &t;e &t;u me geo s&ae;dest &t;&ae;t se wisa Plato cw&ae;de  &t;&ae;t was &t;&ae;t nan anweald n&ae;re riht butan rihtum &t;eawum? 
 Gesihst &t;u nu &t;&ae;t &t;a rihtwisan sint la&d;e &amp; for&t;rycte  for&t;am hi &t;inum willan woldan fulgan  &amp; &t;a unryhtwisan seondan up ahafene &t;urh heora won d&ae;da &amp; &t;urh heora selflice? 
 &t;&ae;t hi &d;y e&d; m&ae;gen heora unriht gewill for&d;bringan hi sind mid gifum &amp; mid gestreonum gefyr&d;rode. 
 For&t;am ic nu wille geornlice to Gode cleopian. 
 Ongan &d;a giddien  &amp; &t;us singende cw&ae;&d;: EALA &t;u scippend heofones &amp; eor&t;an  &t;u &t;e on &t;am ecan setle ricsast  &t;u &t;e on hr&ae;dum f&ae;relde &t;one heofon ymbhweorfest  &amp; &t;a tunglu &t;u gedest &t;e gehyrsume  &amp; &t;a sunnan &t;u gedest &t;&ae;t heo mid heore beorhtan sciman &t;a &t;eostro adw&ae;sc&d; &t;&ae;re sweartan nihte. 
 Swa de&d; eac se mona mid his blacan leohte &t;&ae;t &t;a beorhtan steorran dunnia&d; on &t;am heofone  ge eac hwilum &t;a sunnan heore leohtes bereafa&t;  &t;onne he betwux us &amp; hire wyr&d;. 
 ge eac hwilum &t;one beorhtan steorran &t;e we hata&d; morgensteorra  &t;one ilcan we hata&d; o&d;re naman &ae;fensteorra. 
 &t;u &t;e &d;am winterdagum selest scorte tida &amp; &t;&ae;s sumeres dahum langran; &t;u &t;e &t;a treowu &t;urh &t;one stearcan wind nor&t;an &amp; eastan on h&ae;rfesttid heora leafa bereafast  &amp; eft on lencten o&t;ru leaf sellest &t;urh &t;one smyltan su&d;anwesternan wind. 
 Hw&ae;t  &t;e ealle gesceafta heorsumia&d;  &amp; &t;a gesetnessa &t;inra beboda healda&d;  butan men anum; se &t;e oferheor&d;. 
 Eala &t;u almihtiga scippend &amp; rihtend eallra gesceafta  help nu &t;inum earmum moncynne. 
 Hwy &t;u la Drihten &ae;fre woldest &t;&ae;t seo wyrd swa hwyrfan sceolde? 
 heo &t;reat &t;a unscildigan &amp; nauht ne &d;rea&t; &t;am scildigum. 
 Sitta&d; manfulle on heahsetlum  &amp; halige under heora fotum &t;ryca&d;; sticia&d; gehydde beorhte cr&ae;ftas  &amp; &t;a unrihtwisan t&ae;la&d; &t;a rihtwisan. 
 Nauht ne derega&d; monnum mane a&t;as  ne &t;&ae;t lease lot &t;e beo&d; mid &t;am wrencum bewrigen. 
 For&t;am went nu fulneah eall moncyn on tweonunga  gif seo wyrd swa hweorfan mot on yfelra manna gewill  &amp; &t;u heore nelt stiran. 
 Eala min Drihten  &t;u &t;e ealle gesceafta ofersihst  hawa nu mildelice on &t;as earman eor&t;an  &amp; eac on eall moncyn  for&t;am hit nu eall win&d; on &t;am y&d;um &t;isse worulde. 
 &t;a &t;&ae;t Mod &t;a &t;illic sar cwe&d;ende w&ae;s  &amp; &t;is leo&d; singende w&ae;s  se Wisdom &t;a &amp; seo Gesceadwisnes him bli&d;um eahum on locodon. 
 &amp; he for &t;&ae;s Modes geomerunge n&ae;s nauht gedrefed  ac cw&ae;&d; to &t;am Mode: Sona swa ic &t;e &ae;rest on &t;isse unrotnesse geseah &t;us murciende ic ongeat &t;&ae;t &t;u w&ae;re ut afaren of &t;ines f&ae;der e&d;ele  &t;&ae;t is for minum larum. 
 &t;&ae;r &d;u him fore of &t;a &t;u &t;ine f&ae;str&ae;dnesse forlete  &amp; wendest &t;&ae;t seo weord &t;as woruld wende heore agenes &d;onces buton Godes ge&t;eahte &amp; his &t;afunge &amp; monna gewyrhtum. 
 Ic wiste &t;&ae;t &t;u ut afaren w&ae;re  ac ic nysste hu feor  &ae;r &d;u &t;e self hit me gerehtest mid &t;inum sarcwidum. 
 Ac &t;eah &t;u nu fyr seo &d;onne &t;u w&ae;re  ne eart &t;u &t;eah ealles of &t;am earde adrifen  &d;eah &t;u &t;&ae;ron gedwolode. 
 Ne gebrohte &t;e eac nan o&d;er man on &t;am gedwolan butan &t;e sylfum &t;urh &t;ine agene gemeleste. 
 Ne sceolde &t;e eac nan man swelces to gelefan &t;&ae;r &t;u gemunan woldest hwylcra gebyrda &t;u w&ae;re &amp; hwylcra burgwara for worulde. 
 o&d;&d;e eft gastlice hwilces geferscipes &t;u w&ae;re on &t;inum mode  &amp; on &d;inre gesceadwisnesse; &t;&ae;t is &t;&ae;t &t;u eart on &t;ara rihtwisena &amp; &t;ara ryhtwillendra; &t;a beo&d; &t;&ae;re heofencundan Ierusalem burgware. 
 Of &d;&ae;re n&ae;fre nan  buta he self wolde  ne wear&d; adrifen  &t;&ae;t is of his godan willan; w&ae;re &t;er he w&ae;re  simle he h&ae;fde &t;one mid him. 
 &t;on he &d;one mid him h&ae;fde  w&ae;re &t;&ae;r he w&ae;re  &t;onne w&ae;re he mid his agnum cynne &amp; mid his agnum burgwarum on his agnum earde &t;onne he w&ae;s on &d;ara ryhtwisena gemanan. 
 Swa hwa &t;onne swa &t;&ae;s wyr&d;e bi&d; &t;&ae;t he on heora &t;eowdome beon mot  &t;onne bi&d; he on &d;am hehstan freodome. 
 Ne onscunige ic no &t;&ae;s neo&t;eran &amp; &t;&ae;s uncl&ae;nan stowe gif ic &t;e geradne gemete. ne me na ne lyst mid glase geworhtra waga ne heahsetla mid golde &amp; mid gimmum gerenodra  ne boca mid golde awritenra me swa swi&d;e ne lyst swa me lyst on &t;e rihtes willan. 
 Ne sece ic no her &t;a bec  ac &t;&ae;t &d;&ae;t &t;a bec forstent  &d;&ae;t is  &t;in gewit. 
 Swi&d;e rihte &t;u seofodest &t;a woon wyrd &ae;g&t;er ge on &d;ara unrihtwisra anwalda heanesse ge on minre unweor&t;nesse &amp; forsewennesse ge on &t;ara manfulra for&d;forl&ae;tnesse on &d;as weoruldspeda. 
 Ac for&t;on &t;e &t;e is swa micel unrotnes nu get getenge ge of &t;inum irre ge of &t;inre gnornunga  ic &t;e ne m&ae;g nu giet geandwyrdan &ae;r&t;on &d;&ae;s tiid wyr&d;; for&d;on eall &t;&ae;t mon untiidlice ungyn&d; n&ae;f&d; hit no &ae;lt&ae;wne ende. 
 &t;onne &d;&ae;re sunnan scima on Agustes mon&d;e hatost scin&d; &d;onne dysega&d; se &d;e &t;onne wile hwelc s&ae;d o&d;f&ae;stan &t;&ae;m drygum furum. 
 Swa de&d; eac se &d;e wintregum wederum wile blostman secan. 
 Ne meaht &t;u win wringan on midewinter  &t;eah &d;e wel lyste wearmes mustes. 
 &d;a clipode se Wisdom &amp; cw&ae;&d;: Mot ic nu cunnian hwon &t;inre f&ae;str&ae;dnesse  &t;&ae;t ic &t;onan ongietan m&ae;ge hwonon ic &t;in tilian scyle &amp; hu? 
 &d;a andwyrde &t;&ae;t Mod &amp; cw&ae;&d;: Cunna swa &t;u wille. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; seo Sceadwisnes: Gelefst &d;u &t;&ae;t sio wyrd wealde &t;isse worulde  o&d;&d;e auht godes swa geweor&d;an m&ae;ge butan &t;&ae;m wyrhtan? 
 &d;a andwyrde &t;&ae;t Mod &amp; cw&ae;&d;: Ne gelyfe ic no &t;&ae;t hit geweor&t;an meahte swa endebyrdlice  ac to so&d;um ic wat &d;&ae;tte God rihtere is his agenes weorces  &amp; ic no ne wear&d; of &t;am so&d;an geleafan. 
 &d;a andwyrde se Wisdom eft &amp; cw&ae;&d;: Ymb &t;&ae;t ilce &t;u giddodest nu hwene &ae;r &amp; cw&ae;de &t;&ae;t &ae;lc wuht from Gode wisse his rihttiman &amp; his rihtgesetnesse fuleode  butan men anum. 
 For&d;&ae;m ic wundrige swi&d;e ungemetlice hw&ae;t &t;e sy o&d;&d;e hw&ae;t &t;u m&ae;ne nu &t;u &d;one geleafan h&ae;fst. 
 Ac wit sculon &t;eah giet dioplicor ymb &d;&ae;t bion. 
 Ic nat ful geare ymb hw&ae;t &t;u giet tweost; gesege me  nu &t;u cwist &t;&ae;t &d;u noht ne tweoge &t;&ae;tte God &t;isse worulde rihtwisige  hu he &t;onne wolde &t;&ae;t heo w&ae;re. 
 &d;a andwyrde &t;&ae;t Mod &amp; cw&ae;&t;: Unea&t;e ic m&ae;g forstandan &t;ine acsunga  &amp; cwyst &t;eah &t;&ae;t ic &t;e andwyrdan scyle. 
 Se Wisdom &t;a cw&ae;&d;: Wenstu &t;&ae;t ic hyte &t;one dem &t;inre gedr&ae;fednesse &t;e &t;u mid ymbfangen eart? 
 ac s&ae;ge me hwelces endes &ae;lc angin wilnige. 
 &d;a andwirde &d;&ae;t Mod &amp; cw&ae;&d;: Ic hit gemunde gio  ac me h&ae;f&d; &t;ios gnornung &d;&ae;re gemynde benumen. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; se Wisdom: Wast &t;u hwonan &ae;lc wuht cume? 
 &d;a andwyrde &t;&ae;t Mod &amp; cw&ae;&d;: Ic wat &t;&ae;t &ae;lc wuht from Gode com. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; se Wisdom: Hu m&ae;g &t;&ae;t bion  nu &t;u &d;&ae;t angin wast  &t;&ae;t &d;u eac &d;one ende nyte; for&d;&ae;m sio gedrefednes m&ae;g &t;&ae;t mod onstyrian  ac hio hit ne m&ae;g his gewittes bereafian. 
 Ac ic wolde &t;&ae;t &t;u me s&ae;dest hw&ae;&t;er &d;u wisse hw&ae;t &t;u self w&ae;re. 
 Hit &t;a andwyrde &amp; cw&ae;&d;: Ic wat &t;&ae;t ic on libbendum men &amp; on gesceadwisum eom &amp; &t;eah on deadlicum. 
 &d;a andwyrde se Wisdom &amp; cw&ae;&d;: Wastu auht o&t;res bi &t;e selfum to secganne buton &t;&ae;t &t;u nu s&ae;dest? 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; &t;&ae;t Mod: Nat ic nauht o&d;res. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; se Wisdom: Nu ic h&ae;bbe ongiten &t;ine ormodnesse  nu &d;u self nast hw&ae;t &t;u self eart  ac ic wat hu &t;in man tilian sceal. 
 For&t;am &t;u s&ae;dest &t;&ae;t &t;u wr&ae;ccea w&ae;re &amp; bereafod &ae;lces godes for&d;on &t;u nestes hw&ae;t &t;u w&ae;re. 
 &t;a &t;u cyddest &t;&ae;t &d;u nystes hwelces endes &ae;lc angin wilnode  &t;a &d;u wendest &d;&ae;tte stiorlease men &amp; recelease w&ae;ren ges&ae;lie &amp; wealdendas &t;isse worulde. 
 &amp; &d;&ae;r &t;u cyddest eac &t;&ae;t &t;u nystes mid hwelcere gerece God wilt &d;isse worulde o&d;&t;e hu he wolde &t;&ae;t hio w&ae;re  &t;a &d;u s&ae;dest &t;&ae;t &d;u wende &t;&ae;t &t;ios sli&d;ne wyrd &d;as woruld wende buton Godes ge&t;eahte. 
 Eac &t;&ae;t w&ae;s swi&d;e micel pleoh &t;&ae;t &d;u swa wenan sceoldes; n&ae;s hit no &t;&ae;t an &t;&ae;t &t;u on ungemetlicum unges&ae;l&d;um w&ae;re  ac eac &t;&ae;t &t;u fulneah mid ealle forwurde. 
 &d;onca nu Gode &t;&ae;t he &d;e gefultumade &t;&ae;t ic &t;in gewit mid ealle ne forlet. 
 We habba&d; nu giet &t;one m&ae;stan d&ae;l &t;&ae;re tyndran &t;inre h&ae;le  nu &d;u gelief&ae;st &t;&ae;t sio wyrd &t;urh hie selfe butan Godes ge&t;eahte &t;as weoruld wendan ne m&ae;ge. 
 Nu &d;u ne &t;earft &t;e nauht ondr&ae;dan  for&d;&ae;m&t;e of &d;&ae;m lytlan spearcan &t;e &t;u mid &d;&ae;re tyndran gefenge lifes leoht &t;e onlyhte. 
 Ac hit nis giet se tima &t;&ae;t ic &t;e healicor m&ae;ge onbryrdan  for&d;&ae;m hit is &ae;lces modes wise &t;&ae;tte sona swa hit forl&ae;t so&d;cwidas  swa folga&t; hit leasspellunga. 
 Of &d;&ae;m &d;onne onginna&d; weaxan &t;a mistas &d;e &t;&ae;t mod gedrefa&d;  &amp; mid ealle fordwilma&d; &d;a so&d;an gesih&d;e swelce mistas swelce nu on &t;inum mode sindon. 
 Ac ic hi sceal &ae;r&ae;st ge&t;innian  &t;&ae;t ic si&d;&d;an &d;y e&d; m&ae;ge &t;&ae;t so&t;e leoht on &t;e gebringan. 
 Loca nu be &t;&ae;re sunnan &amp; eac be o&d;rum tunglum; &t;onne sweartan wolcnu him beforan ga&d; ne mahon hi &t;onne heora leoht sellan. 
 Swa eac se su&d;erna wind hwilum mid miclum storme gedrefe&d; &t;a s&ae; &t;e &ae;r w&ae;s smylte wedere gl&ae;shlutru on to seonne. 
 &t;onne heo &t;onne swa gemenged wyr&d; mid &d;an y&t;um  &t;onne wyr&d; heo swi&d;e hra&d;e ungladu  &t;eah heo &ae;r gladu w&ae;re on to locienne. 
 Hw&ae;t  eac se broc  &t;eah he swife of his rihtryne  &d;onne &t;&ae;r micel stan wealwiende of &t;am heohan munte oninnan feal&d; &amp; hine tod&ae;l&d; &amp; him his rihtrynes wi&d;stent. 
 Swa do&d; nu &d;a &t;eostro &t;inre gedrefednesse wi&d;standan minum leohtum larum. 
 Ac gif &d;u wilnige on rihtum geleafan &t;&ae;t so&d;e leoht oncnawan  afyr fram &t;e &d;a yfelan s&ae;l&t;a &amp; &t;a unnettan  &amp; eac &d;a unnettan unges&ae;l&t;a &amp; &t;one yflan ege &t;isse worulde  &t;&ae;t is &t;&ae;t &t;u &t;e ne anhebbe on ofermetto on &t;inre gesundfulnesse &amp; on &d;inre orsorgnesse  ne eft &t;e ne geortrywe nanes godes on nanre wi&d;erweardnesse. 
 For&d;am &t;&ae;t mod siemle bi&d; gebunden mid gedrefednesse  &t;&ae;r &t;issa twega yfela au&d;er ricsa&d;. 
 &d;a geswigode se Wisdom ane lytle hwile o&d; &t;&ae;t he ongeat &t;&ae;s Modes inge&t;oncas. 
 &d;a he hi &t;a ongieten h&ae;fde  &t;a cw&ae;&d; he: Gif ic &t;ine unrotnesse on riht ongieten h&ae;bbe  &t;onne nis &t;e noht swi&d;or &t;onne &d;&ae;t &t;&ae;t &t;u forloren h&ae;fst &t;a worulds&ae;l&d;a &t;e &t;u &ae;r h&ae;fdest  &amp; geomrast nu for&d;&ae;m &t;e hio onhwyrfed is. 
 Ic ongiete genoh sweotule &t;&ae;t &t;a worulds&ae;l&d;a mid swi&d;e monigre swetnesse swi&d;e lytelice olecca&d; &t;&ae;m modum &d;a hi on last willa&d; swi&t;ost beswican. 
 &amp; &t;onne &ae;t nihstan  &t;onne hy l&ae;st wena&d;  hi on ormodnesse forl&ae;ta&d; on &t;&ae;m m&ae;stan sare. 
 Gif &t;u nu witan wilt hwonan hi cuma&d;  &t;onne meaht &t;u ongietan &t;&ae;t hi cuma&d; of woruldgidsunga. 
 Gif &t;u &t;onne heora &t;eawas witan wilt  &t;onne meaht &t;u ongietan &t;&ae;t hie ne beo&d; nanum men getreowe. 
 Be &t;&ae;m &t;u meaht ongietan &d;&ae;t &t;u &t;&ae;r nane myrh&d;e on n&ae;fdest &d;a &t;a &t;u hie h&ae;fdest  ne eft nane ne forlure &t;a &d;a &t;u hi forlure. 
 Ic wende &t;&ae;t ic &t;e geo gel&ae;red h&ae;fde &t;&ae;t &t;u hi oncnawan cu&d;e  &amp; ic wisse &t;&ae;t &t;u hi onscunedest &d;a &d;a &t;u hi h&ae;fdest  &d;eah &t;u hiora bruce. 
 Ic wisse &t;&ae;t &d;u mine cwidas wi&d; hiora willan oft s&ae;dest  ac ic wat &t;&ae;t nan gewuna ne m&ae;g nanum men bion onwended &t;&ae;t &t;&ae;t mod ne sy be sumum d&ae;le onstyred. 
 For&d;&ae;m &t;u eart eac nu of &t;inre stilnesse ahworfen. 
 Eala Mod  hw&ae;t bewearp &t;e on &d;as care &amp; on &t;as gnornunga? 
 Wenst &t;u &t;&ae;t hit hw&ae;t niwes sie o&t;&t;e hw&ae;thwugu ungewunelices &t;&ae;t &t;e on becumen is  swelce o&t;rum monnum &ae;r &t;&ae;t ilce ne eglede? 
 Gif &t;u &t;onne wenst &t;&ae;t hit on &t;e gelong sie &t;&ae;t &d;a worulds&ae;l&d;a on &d;e swa onwenda sint  &t;onne eart &d;u on gedwolan  ac swylce hiora &t;eawas sint. 
 hi beheoldon on &d;e hiora agen gecynd  &amp; on hiora wandlunga hy gecy&d;don hiora unf&ae;str&ae;dnesse. 
 Swylce hi w&ae;ron rihte &d;e hi &d;a m&ae;st geolectan swilce hi nu sindon  &t;eah &d;e hi &d;e liolcen on &t;a leasan s&ae;l&d;a. 
 Nu &d;u h&ae;fst ongiten &d;a wanclan truwa &t;&ae;s blindan lustes. 
 &t;a triowa &t;e &t;e nu sindon opene hi sindon git mid manegum o&d;rum behelede. 
 Nu &t;u wast hwelce &t;eawas &t;a worulds&ae;l&d;a habba&d; &amp; hu hi hwearfia&d;. 
 Gif &t;u &t;onne heora &t;egen beon wilt &amp; &t;e heora &t;eawas licia&d;  to hwon myrnst &t;u swa swi&d;e? 
 Hwi ne hwearfost &t;u eac mid him? 
 Gif &t;u &t;onne heora untriowa onscunige  oferhoga hi &t;onne &amp; adrif hi fram &t;e; hi spana&d; &t;e to &t;inre un&d;earefe. 
 &d;a ilcan &t;e &t;e gedydon nu &t;as gnornunga for&d;&ae;m &t;e &t;u hi h&ae;fdest  &t;a ilcan &t;e w&ae;ren on stilnesse gif &t;u hi na ne underfenge. 
 &d;a ilcan &t;e habba&d; nu heora agnes &d;onces forl&ae;ten  nales &d;ines  &d;a &d;e n&ae;fre nanne mon buton sorge ne forl&ae;ta&d;. 
 &t;ynca&d; &t;e nu swi&d;e diore &amp; swi&d;e leofe &d;a &d;ing &d;a &d;e naw&d;er ne sint ne getrewe to habbanne  ne eac ie&d;e to forl&ae;tanne? 
 ac &d;onne hi hw&ae;m from hweorfende bio&d; he hi sceal mid &d;&ae;m m&ae;stan sare his modes forl&ae;tan? 
 Nu &d;u hi &d;onne &ae;fter &t;inum willan &t;e getrewe habban ne meaht  &amp; hy &t;e willa&d; on murcunga gebringan &t;onne hie &t;e fram hweorfa&d;  to hw&ae;m cuma&d; hi &t;onne elles butan to tacnunge sorges &amp; anfealdes sares? 
 Ne sindon &t;a worulds&ae;l&t;a ana ymb to &t;encenne &t;e mon &t;onne h&ae;f&d;  ac &ae;lc gleaw mod behealt hwelcne ende hi habba&d;  &amp; hit gewarena&d; &ae;g&d;er ge wi&d; heora &t;reaunga ge wi&d; olecunga. 
 Ac gif &t;u wilt beon heora &t;egn &t;onne scealt &t;u georne ge&d;olian gehw&ae;t &t;&ae;s &t;e to heora &t;enungum &amp; to hiora &t;eawum &amp; to heora willan belimpet. 
 Gif &t;u &t;onne wilnast &t;&ae;t hi for &t;inum &d;ingum o&t;re &d;eawas nimen o&d;er hiora willa &amp; heora gewuna is  hu ne unweor&t;ast &t;u &t;onne &d;e selfne  &t;&ae;t &d;u wins&d; wi&d; &t;am hlafordscipe &t;e &d;u self gecure  &amp; swa&d;eah ne meaht hiora sidu &amp; hiora gecynd onwendan. 
 Hw&ae;t  &t;u wast gif &t;u &t;ines scipes segl ongean &t;one wind tobr&ae;dest  &t;&ae;t &t;u &t;onne l&ae;t&ae;st eall eower f&ae;reld to &d;&ae;s windes dome. 
 Swa eac gif &t;u &t;e selfne to anwalde &t;&ae;m worulds&ae;l&d;um gesealdest hit is riht &t;&ae;t &t;u eac hiora &t;eawum fulgonge. 
 Wenst &t;u &t;&ae;t &d;u &t;&ae;t hwerfende hweol &t;onne hit on ryne wyr&d; m&ae;ge oncerran? 
 Ne miht &t;u &t;on ma &t;ara worulds&ae;l&d;a hwearfunga onwendan. 
 Ic wolde nu giet &d;&ae;t wit ma spr&ae;cen emb &d;a worulds&ae;l&d;a. 
 To hw&ae;m &ae;twite &d;u me &ae;r &t;&ae;t &t;u hi for minum &d;ingum forlure? 
 Hwi murcnast &d;u wi&d; min  swelce &t;u for minum &d;ingum sie &d;ines agnes benumen  &ae;g&t;er ge &t;inra welona ge &t;ines weor&t;scipes? 
 &ae;g&t;er &t;ara &t;e com &ae;r from me &t;a hi &t;e onl&ae;nde w&ae;ron. 
 Ute nu tellan beforan swilcum deman swilce &t;u wille; gif &d;u gese&t;an miht &t;&ae;t &ae;nig dea&d;lic man swelces hw&ae;t agnes ahte  ic hit &t;e eft eal agife &t;&ae;t &t;u gereccan miht &t;&ae;t &t;ines agnes w&ae;re. 
 Dysine &amp; ungel&ae;redne ic &t;e underfeng &t;a &t;u &ae;rest to monnum become  &amp; &t;a &t;e getydde &amp; gel&ae;rde  &amp; &t;e &t;a snyttro on gebrohte  &t;e &t;u &t;a woruld are mid begeate  &t;e &t;u nu sorgiende anforlete. 
 &t;u meaht &t;&ae;s habban &t;anc &t;&ae;t &t;u minra gifa wel bruce. 
 Ne miht &t;u no gereccan &t;&ae;t &t;u &t;ines auht forlure. 
 Hw&ae;t siofast &t;u wi&d; me? 
 Habbe ic &t;e awer benumen &t;inra gifena &t;ara &d;e from me comon? 
 &ae;lc so&t; wela &amp; so&t; weor&t;scipe sindan mine agne &t;eowas  &amp; swa hw&ae;r swa ic beo hie bio&d; mid me. 
 Wite &t;u for so&d;  gif &t;&ae;t &t;ine agne welan w&ae;ron &t;e &t;u m&ae;ndest &t;&ae;t &t;u forlure  ne meahtest &t;u hi na forleosan. 
 Eala  hu yfele me do&d; m&ae;nige weoruldmenn mid &t;&ae;m &t;&ae;t ic ne mot wealdan minra agenra &t;eawa. 
 Se heofen mot brengan leohte dagas &amp; eft &t;&ae;t leoht mid &t;eostrum behelian; &t;&ae;t gear mot brengan blostman &amp; &t;y ilcan geare eft geniman; seo s&ae; mot brucan smyltra y&t;a  &amp; ealle gesceafta motan hiora gewunan &amp; heora willan bewitigan  butan me anum. 
 Ic ana eom benumen minra &t;eawa &amp; eom getogen to fremdum &t;eawum &t;urh &t;a ungefylledan gitsunge woruldmonna. 
 &t;urh &d;a gidsunga hi me habba&d; benumen mines naman &t;e ic mid rihte habban sceolde. 
 &t;one naman ic scolde mid rihte habban &t;&ae;t ic w&ae;re wela &amp; weor&d;scipe  ac hy hine habba&d; on me genumen  &amp; hi me habba&d; gesealdne hiora wlencum &amp; getehhod to heora leasum welum  &t;&ae;t ic ne mot mid minum &d;eowum minra &t;egnunga fulgangan swa ealla o&t;ra gesceafta moton. 
 &d;a mine &t;eowas sindon wisdomas &amp; cr&ae;ftas &amp; so&d;e welan; mid &t;&ae;m &t;eowum w&ae;s on symbel min plega; mid &t;&ae;m &t;eowum ic eom ealne &t;one hefon ymbhweorfende  &amp; &t;a ni&d;emystan ic gebringe &ae;t &t;&ae;m hehstan  &amp; &t;a hehstan &ae;t &d;&ae;m ni&d;em&ae;stan; &d;&ae;t is &t;&ae;t ic gebringe eadmodnesse on heofonum  &amp; &d;a hefonlican god &ae;t &t;&ae;m ea&d;modum. 
 Ac &t;onne ic up gefere mid minum &t;eowum &t;onne forseo we &t;as styrmendan woruld swa se earn &d;onne he up gewit bufan &d;a wolcnu styrmendum wedrum  &t;&ae;t him &t;a stormas derigan ne m&ae;gen. 
 Swa ic wolde  la Mod  &t;&ae;t &t;u &t;e fore up to us gif &t;e lyste  on &t;a gerad &t;&ae;t &t;u eft mid us &t;a eor&d;an secan wille for godra manna &t;earfe. 
 Hu ne wastu mine &t;eawas  hu georne ic symle w&ae;s ymbe godra manna &t;earfe? 
 Wast &t;u hu ic gewand ymb Croeses &t;earfe Creca cyninges  &t;a &t;a hine Cirus P&ae;rsa cyning gefangen h&ae;fde &amp; hine forb&ae;rnan wolde? 
 &d;a hine mon on &t;&ae;t fyr wearp &t;a alysde ic hine mid heofonlicon rene. 
 Ac &t;u &d;e fortruwudest for &t;inre rihtwisnesse &amp; for &t;inum godan willan; wendest &t;&ae;t &t;e nanwuht unrihtlices on becuman ne meahte  swelce &t;u wolde &t;a lean eal &t;inra godena weorca on &t;isse weoruld habban. 
 Hu meahtest &t;u sittan on middum gem&ae;num rice &t;&ae;t &d;u ne sceolde &t;&ae;t ilce ge&t;olian &t;&ae;t o&d;re men? 
 Hu meahtes &t;u bion on midre &t;isse hwearfunga &t;&ae;t &d;u eac mid ne hwearfode? 
 Hw&ae;t singa&d; &t;a leo&d;wyrhtan o&d;res be &d;isse woruld buton mislica hwearfunga &t;isse worulde? 
 Hw&ae;t is &t;e &d;onne &t;&ae;t &t;u &t;&ae;rmid ne hwearfie? 
 Hw&ae;t recstu hu ge hwearfigen nu ic siemle mid &t;e beo? 
 &d;e w&ae;s &t;ios hwearfung betere for&d;&ae;m &t;&ae;t &d;e &d;issa worulds&ae;l&d;a to wel ne lyste  &amp; &t;&ae;t &d;u &t;e eac betre na gelefde. 
 &d;eah &t;&ae;m feohgitsere cume swa fela welena swa &t;ara sondcorna bi&d; be &t;isum s&ae;clifum o&t;&t;e &t;ara steorrena &d;e &t;iostrum nihtum scina&d;  ne forl&ae;t he &t;eah no &d;a seofunga &t;&ae;t he ne seofige his erm&d;a. 
 &t;eah nu God gefylle &t;ara weligra monna willan ge mid golde ge mid seolfre ge mid eallum deorwyr&d;nessum  swa&d;eah him ne beo&d; se &d;urst gefylled hiora gitsunga  ac sio grundlease swelgend h&ae;f&d; swi&d;e m&ae;negu westu holu on to gadrianne. 
 Hwa m&ae;g &t;&ae;m wedendan gietsere genoh forgifan? 
 Swa him mon mare sel&d;  swa hine ma lyst. 
 Hu wilt &t;u nu andwyrdan &t;&ae;m worulds&ae;l&d;um gif hi cwe&d;a&d; to &t;e: Hw&ae;t witst &t;u  la Mod  us? 
 Hwi yrsast &t;u wi&d; us? 
 On hw&ae;m abulgon we &t;e? 
 Hw&ae;t  &t;e ongan lystan ure  nales us &t;in; &t;u settest us on &t;&ae;t setl &d;ines sceoppendes &t;a &d;u wilnodest to us &t;&ae;s godes &d;e &d;u to him sceoldes. 
 &t;u cwist &d;&ae;t we h&ae;bban &t;e beswicenne  ac we magan cwe&t;an ma &t;&ae;t &t;u h&ae;bbe us beswicene  nu us &d;urh &t;ine lust &amp; &t;urh &t;ine gitsunga onscunian sceal ealra gesceafta sceppend. 
 Nu &t;u eart scyldigra &t;onne we  &ae;g&t;er ge for &t;inum agnum unrihtlustum ge eac for&d;&ae;m&t;e we ne motan for &d;e fulgan ures sceppendes willan. 
 for&d;&ae;m&d;e he ure &d;e onl&ae;nde &ae;fter his bebodum to brucanne  nallas &t;inre unrihtgitsunga gewill to fulfremmanne. 
 Andwyrde unc nu  cw&ae;&d; se Wisdom  swa swa &t;u wille; wit geanbidia&d; &t;inre ondswore. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; &t;&ae;t Mod: Ic me ongite &ae;ghwonan scyldigne  ac ic eom mid &t;&ae;s la&d;es sare swa swi&d;e of&d;rycced &t;&ae;t ic inc geandwyrdan ne m&ae;g. 
 &t;a cw&ae;&d; se Wisdom eft: &t;&ae;t is nu giet &t;inre unrihtwisnesse &t;&ae;t &d;u eart fulneah for&t;oht. 
 Ac ic nolde &t;&ae;t &t;u &t;e for&t;ohte  ac ic wolde &t;&ae;t &d;e sceamode swelces gedwolan; for&d;&ae;m se se &d;e hine for&t;enc&d; se bi&d; ormod  ac se se &d;e hine scamea&d; se bi&d; on hreowsunga. 
 Gif &t;u nu gemunan wilt ealra &d;ara arwyr&d;nessa &t;e &d;u for &t;isse weorulde h&ae;fdest si&d;&d;an &d;u &ae;rest geboren w&ae;re o&d; &d;isne d&ae;g: gif &t;u nu atelan wilt ealle &t;a bli&t;nessa wi&d; &t;am unrotnessum  ne meaht &d;u ful ea&t;e cwe&d;an &t;&ae;t &t;u earm sie &amp; unges&ae;lig. 
 for&t;am ic &d;e geongne underfeng untydne &amp; unl&ae;redne  &amp; me to bearne genom  &amp; to minum tyhtum getyde. 
 Hwa m&ae;g &t;onne auht o&d;res cwe&d;an butan &t;&ae;t &t;u w&ae;re se ges&ae;lgesta  &t;a &t;u me w&ae;re &ae;r leof &t;onne cu&t;  &amp; &ae;r &t;on &t;a &d;u cu&d;e minne tyht &amp; mine &t;eawas  &amp; ic &t;e giongne gel&ae;rde swylce snytro swelc manegum o&d;rum eldran gewittum oftogen is  &amp; ic &t;e gefyr&d;rede mid minum larum to &d;on &t;&ae;t &t;e mon to domere geceas? 
 Gif &t;u nu for&d;&ae;m cwist &t;&ae;t &t;u ges&ae;lig ne sie &t;e &t;u nu n&ae;fst &d;a hwilendlican awyr&d;nessa &amp; &d;a bli&t;nessa &t;e &t;u &ae;r h&ae;fdest  &t;onne neart &d;u &t;eah unges&ae;lig  for&d;&ae;m&d;e &t;a unrotnessa &t;e &t;u nu on eart swa ilce oferga&d; swa &d;u cwist &d;&ae;t &t;a blissa &ae;r dydon. 
 Wenstu nu &t;&ae;t &t;e anum &t;ellecu hwearfung &amp; &t;illecu unrotnes on becume &amp; nanum o&d;rum mode swelc ne on become  ne &ae;r &t;e ne &ae;fter &t;e? 
 O&t;&t;e wenst &t;u &t;&ae;tte on &ae;negum menniscum mode m&ae;ge auht f&ae;str&ae;dlices bion buton hwearfunga? 
 O&d;&d;e gif hit on &ae;negum &ae;nige hwile f&ae;stlice wuna&d;  se dea&t; hit huru aferre&d; &t;&ae;t hit bion ne m&ae;g &t;&ae;r hit &ae;r w&ae;s. 
 Hw&ae;t syndon &d;a worulds&ae;l&d;a o&d;res buton dea&d;es tacnung? 
 For&t;am se dea&d; ne cym&d; to nanum o&d;rum &d;ingu butan &t;&ae;t he &t;&ae;t lif afyrre; swa eac &t;a worulds&ae;l&d;a cuma&d; to &d;&ae;m mode to &d;am &t;&ae;t hi hit benimen &t;&ae;s &d;e him leofast bi&d; &d;isse weorulde; &t;&ae;t bi&d; &t;onne &t;onne hie him fram gewita&d;. 
 Gesege  la Mod  hw&ae;&d;er &t;e betere &t;ince  nu nanwuht woruldlices f&ae;stes &amp; unhwearfiendes bion ne m&ae;g? 
 Hw&ae;&d;er &d;e &d;u hi forseo  &amp; &t;ines agnes &t;onces hi forlete buton sare  &t;e &t;u gebide hwonne hi &d;e sorgiendne forl&ae;ten? 
 &d;a ongan se Wisdom singan &amp; giddode &t;us: &T;ONNE seo sunne on hadrum heofone beorhtost scine&d;  &t;onne a&t;eostria&d; ealle steorran  for&t;am&t;e heora beorhtnes ne beo&d; nan beorhtnes for hire. 
 &t;onne smylte blawe&d; su&t;anwestan wind  &t;onne weaxa&d; swi&d;e hra&d;e feldes blosman; ac &t;onne se stearca wind cym&d; nor&d;aneastan  &t;onne toweorp&d; he swi&d;e hra&t;e &t;&ae;re rosan wlite; swa oft &t;one to smylton s&ae; &t;&ae;s nor&d;anwindes yst onstyre&d;. 
 Eala &t;&ae;t nanwuht nis f&ae;ste stondendes weorces a wuniende on worulde. 
 &t;a cw&ae;&d; boetius: Eala  Wisdom  &t;u &t;e eart modor eallra m&ae;gena  ne m&ae;g ic na wi&d;cwe&d;an ne andsacigan &t;&ae;t he &t;u me &ae;r s&ae;dest  for&t;on&t;e hit is eall so&d;. 
 for&t;am ic nu h&ae;bbe ongiten &t;&ae;t &d;a mine s&ae;l&d;a &amp; sio orsorgnes  &t;e ic &ae;r wende &t;&ae;t ges&ae;l&d;a beon sceoldan  nane s&ae;l&d;a ne sint  for&d;am hi swa r&ae;dlice gewita&t;. 
 Ac &t;&ae;t me h&ae;f&d; eallra swi&d;ost gedrefed &t;onne ic ymbe swelc smealicost &t;ence  &t;&ae;t ic nu sweotole ongiten h&ae;bbe &t;&ae;t &t;&ae;t is seo m&ae;ste uns&ae;l&d; on &t;ys andweardan life &t;&ae;t mon &ae;rest weor&d;e ges&ae;lig  &amp; &ae;fter &t;am unges&ae;lig. 
 &t;a andsworede se Wisdom &amp; sio Gesceadwisnes  &amp; cw&ae;&d;: Ne meaht &t;u no mid so&d;e get&ae;lan &t;ine wyrd &amp; &t;ine ges&ae;l&d;a  swa swa &t;u wenst  for &t;am leasum unges&ae;l&t;um &t;e &t;u &d;rowast. 
 Hit is leasung &t;&ae;t &t;u wenst &d;&ae;t &d;u sie unges&ae;lig. 
 Ac gif &t;e nu &t;&ae;t swa swi&d;e gedrefed &amp; geunrotsad h&ae;f&d; &t;&ae;tte &t;u forlure &t;a leasan ges&ae;l&t;a  &t;onne m&ae;g ic &t;e openlice gereccan &t;&ae;t &d;u swutole ongits&d; &t;&ae;tte &t;u giet h&ae;fst &d;one m&ae;stan d&ae;l &t;ara ges&ae;l&d;a &t;e &t;u &ae;r h&ae;fdest. 
 Saga me nu hw&ae;&d;er &t;u mid rihte m&ae;ge siofian &t;ina uns&ae;l&d;a  swelce &d;u eallunga h&ae;bbe forloren &t;ina ges&ae;l&d;a; ac &d;u h&ae;fst get gesund gehealden eall &t;&ae;t deorwyr&d;oste &d;&ae;tte &t;u &d;e besorgost h&ae;fdes. 
 Hu meaht &t;u &t;onne m&ae;nan &t;&ae;t wyrse &amp; &t;&ae;t la&d;re nu &d;u &d;&ae;t leofre h&ae;fst gehealden? 
 Hw&ae;t  &t;u wast &t;&ae;t sio dugu&d; ealles moncynnes &amp; &d;e se m&ae;sta weor&d;scipe get leofa&d;  &t;&ae;t is Simachus &d;in swior. 
 Hw&ae;t  he is giet hal &amp; gesund  &amp; h&ae;f&d; &ae;lces godes genog. 
 for&d;on &d;e ic wat &t;&ae;t &d;u auht ne forslawode &t;&ae;tte &t;u &t;in agen feorh for hine ne sealdest gif &t;u hine gesawe on hwelcum earfo&d;um  for&d;&ae;m se wer is domes &amp; cr&ae;fta full  &amp; genog orsorg nu get &ae;lces eor&d;lices eges. 
 Se is swi&d;e sarig for &d;inum earfo&d;um &amp; for &d;inum wr&ae;csi&d;e. 
 Hu ne liofa&d; &t;in wif eac  &t;&ae;s ilcan Simaches dohtor? 
 &amp; sio is swi&d;e wel gerad &amp; swi&d;e gemetf&ae;st; sio h&ae;f&d; eall o&t;ru wif ofer&d;ungen mid cl&ae;nnesse. 
 Eall hire god ic &t;e m&ae;g mid feam wordum areccan; &t;&ae;t is &d;&ae;t hio is on ealum &t;eawum hiere f&ae;der gelic. 
 Sio liofa&d; nu &t;e  &t;e anum  for&d;&ae;m&d;e hio nanwuht elles ne lufa&d; buton &t;e. 
 &ae;lces godes hio h&ae;f&t; genoh on &d;ys andweardan life  ac heo hit h&ae;f&d; eall forsawen ofer &d;e anne; eall heo hit onscuna&d;  for&d;&ae;m&t;e heo &t;e &ae;nne n&ae;f&d;; &t;&ae;s anes hire is nu wana. 
 For &t;inre &ae;fweardnesse hire &t;inc&d; eall noht &t;&ae;t hio h&ae;f&d;  for&d;&ae;m hio is for &t;inum lufum ormod &amp; fulneah dead for tearum &amp; for unrotnesse. 
 Hw&ae;t wille we cwe&d;an be &t;inum twam sunum? 
 &d;a sint ealdormen &amp; ge&d;eahteras; on &t;&ae;m is swiotol sio gifu &amp; ealla &d;a dugu&t;a heora f&ae;der &amp; heora eldran f&ae;der  swa swa geonge men magon gelicoste beon ealdum monnum. 
 &t;y ic wundrige hwi &d;u ne m&ae;ge ongietan &t;&ae;t &d;u eart nu git swi&d;e ges&ae;lig  ne &d;u git liofost &amp; eart hal. 
 Hw&ae;t  &t;&ae;t is sio m&ae;ste ar dea&d;licra monna &t;&ae;t hie libban &amp; sien hale; &amp; &t;u h&ae;fst nu giet toeacan eall &t;&ae;t ic &d;e &ae;r tealde. 
 Hw&ae;t  ic wat &t;&ae;t &t;&ae;t is giet diorwyr&t;re &t;onne monnes lif  for&d;&ae;m m&ae;negum men is leofre &t;&ae;t he &ae;r self swelte &ae;r he gesio his wif &amp; his bearn sweltende. 
 Ac hwi tilast &t;u &t;onne to wepanne buton andweorce? 
 Ne meaht &d;u nu giet &t;inre wyrde nauht o&d;witan ne &t;in lif no get&ae;lan  ne eart &t;u no eallunga to nauhte gedon swa swa &t;u wenst. 
 Nis &t;e nu git nan unaberendlic broc getenge  for&d;on &d;in ancer is giet on eor&d;an f&ae;st; &t;&ae;t sint &d;a ealdormen &t;e we &ae;r ymb spr&ae;con. 
 &t;a &d;e ne laeta&d; geortrewan be &t;ys andweardan life; &amp; eft &t;in agna treowa &amp; seo godcunde lufu &amp; se tohopa  &t;a &d;reo &t;e ne l&ae;ta&d; geortrewan be &t;am ecan life. 
 &d;a andsworode &t;&ae;t unrote Mod &amp; cw&ae;&d;: Eala  w&ae;ran &t;a ancras swa trume &amp; swa &d;urhwuniende  ge for Gode ge for worulde  swa swa &t;u segst; &t;onne mihte we micle &t;y e&d; ge&t;olian swa hw&ae;t earfo&t;nessa swa us on become. 
 Eall hie us &t;ynca&d; &t;y leohtran &d;a hwile &t;e &t;a oncras f&ae;ste bio&d;. 
 Ac &t;u miht &t;eah ongitan hu &t;a mina s&ae;l&d;a &amp; se min weor&d;scipe her for worulde is oncerred. 
 &d;a andswarode se Wisdom &amp; seo Gesceadwisnes  &amp; cw&ae;&d;: Ic wene &t;eah &t;&ae;t ic hw&ae;thwugununges &t;e up ahofe of &t;&ae;re unrotnesse &amp; fulneah gebrohte &ae;t &t;am ilcan weor&d;scipe &t;e &t;u &ae;r h&ae;fdes  buton &t;u git to ful sy &t;&ae;s &t;e &t;e l&ae;fed is  &t;&ae;t &t;e for&d;y wlatige. 
 Ac ic ne m&ae;g adreohan &t;ine seofunga for &t;am lytlan &t;e &t;u forlure; for&t;am &t;u simle mid wope &amp; mid unrotnesse m&ae;nst gif &t;e &ae;nies willan wana bi&d;  &t;eah hit lytles hw&ae;t sie. 
 Hwa w&ae;s &ae;fre on &t;is andweardan life  o&d;&d;e hwa wyr&d; get &ae;fter us on &t;isse worulde  &t;&ae;t him nanwuht wi&d; his willan ne sie  ne lytles ne miceles? 
 Swi&d;e nearewe sent &amp; swi&d;e heanlice &t;a menniscan ges&ae;l&t;a  for&t;am o&t;er twega o&d;&d;e hie n&ae;fre to nanum men ne becuma&t;  o&d;&d;e hi &d;&ae;r n&ae;fre f&ae;stlice ne &d;urhwunia&d; swelca swelce hi &ae;r to coman. 
 &t;&ae;t ic wille her be&ae;ftan sweotolor gereccan. 
 We witon &t;&ae;t monige habba&d; &ae;lces woruldwelan genog  ac hi habba&d; sceame &t;&ae;s welan gif hi ne beo&d; swa &ae;&t;ele on gebyrdum swa hi woldon. 
 Sume beo&d; swi&d;e &ae;&t;ele &amp; widcu&d;e on heora gebyrdum  ac hi beo&t; mid w&ae;dle &amp; mid hen&d;e of&t;rycte &amp; geunrotsode  &t;&ae;t him w&ae;re leofre &t;&ae;t hie w&ae;ran un&ae;&t;ele &t;onne swa earme  gif hit on heora anwealde w&ae;re. 
 Manege beo&d; &t;eah &ae;g&d;er ge full &ae;&d;ele ge full welige  &amp; beo&d; &t;eah full unrote  &t;onne hi o&d;er twega o&d;&d;e wif habba&d; him gem&ae;c  o&d;&d;e him gemede nabba&d;. 
 Manige habba&d; genog ges&ae;lilice gewifod  ac for bearnleste eallne &t;one welan &t;e hi gegaderiga&d; hi l&ae;ta&d; fr&ae;mdum to brucanne  &amp; hi beo&t; for&t;am unrote. 
 Sume habba&d; bearn genoge  ac &t;a beo&t; hwilum unhale o&d;&d;e yfele &amp; unweor&t;e  o&d;&d;e hra&d;e gefara&d;  &t;&ae;t &t;a eldran for&d;am gnornia&d; ealle heora woruld. 
 For&t;am ne m&ae;g nan man on &t;ys andweardan life eallunga gerad beon wi&d; his wyrd. 
 &t;eah he nu nanwuht elles n&ae;bbe ymbe to sorgienne  &t;&ae;t him m&ae;g to sorge &t;&ae;t he nat hw&ae;t him toweard bi&d;  hw&ae;&d;er &t;e god &t;e yfel  &d;on ma &t;e &t;u wistest. 
 &amp; eac &t;&ae;t &t;&ae;t he &t;onne ges&ae;llice bryc&d; he ondr&ae;t &t;&ae;t he scyle forl&ae;tan. 
 Get&ae;c me nu sumne mann &t;ara &d;e &t;e ges&ae;legost &t;ince &amp; on his selfwille sy swi&d;ost gewiten. 
 ic &t;e gerecce swi&d;e hra&t;e &t;&ae;t &d;u ongitst &t;&ae;t he bi&d; for swi&d;e lytlum &t;ingum oft swi&d;e ungemetlice gedrefed  gif him &ae;nig wuht bi&d; wi&d; his willan o&d;&d;e wi&d; his gewunan  &t;eah hit nu lytles hw&ae;t sie  buton he to &ae;lcum men m&ae;ge gebecnan &t;&ae;t he irne on his willan. 
 Wundrum lytel m&ae;g gedon &t;one ealra ges&ae;lgostan mon her on worulde &t;&ae;t he wen&d; &d;&ae;t his ges&ae;l&d;a sien o&d;&d;e swi&d;e gewanode o&d;&d;e mid ealle forlorena. 
 &t;u wens&d; nu &t;&ae;t &t;u seo swi&d;e unges&ae;lig  &amp; ic wat &d;&ae;t monegum men &t;uhte &t;&ae;t he w&ae;re to hefonum ah&ae;fen gif he &ae;nigne d&ae;l h&ae;fde &t;ara &t;inra ges&ae;l&d;a &t;e &t;u nu giet h&ae;fst. 
 Ge fur&d;um sio stow &t;e &d;u nu on geh&ae;ft eart &amp; &t;u cwist &d;&ae;t &t;in wr&ae;cstow sie  hio is &t;&ae;m monnum e&t;el &t;e &d;&ae;ron geborene w&ae;ron  &amp; eac &t;am &t;e hiora willum &t;&ae;ron eardia&d;. 
 Ne nanwuht ne bi&d; yfel &ae;r mon wene &t;&ae;t hit yfel sie  &amp; &t;eah hit nu hefig sie &amp; wi&d;erweard  &t;eah hit bi&d; ges&ae;l&d; gif hit mon lustlice de&d; &amp; ge&t;yldelice ar&ae;fne&d;. 
 Feawe sint to &t;&ae;m gesceadwise  gif he wyr&d; on unge&d;ylde  &t;&ae;t he ne wilnige &t;&ae;t his s&ae;l&d;a weor&d;en onwende. 
 Wi&d; swi&d;e monige biternesse is gemenged sio swetnes &t;isse worulde; &d;eah hio hw&ae;m wynsumu &d;ynce  ne m&ae;g he hi no gehabban gif hio hine flion ongin&d;. 
 Hu ne is hit &t;&ae;r swi&d;e swiotol hu werelica &t;as worulds&ae;l&d;a sint  nu hi ne magon &t;one earman gefyllan  for&t;&ae;m he symle wilna&d; hw&ae;shwugu &t;&ae;s &d;e he &t;onne n&ae;f&d;; ne hi &t;&ae;m ge&t;yldegum &amp; &t;&ae;m gemetf&ae;stum symle ne wunia&d;. 
 Hwy sece ge &t;onne ymbutan eow &t;a ges&ae;l&d;a &t;e ge oninnan iow habba&d; &t;urh &t;a godcundan mieht geset? 
 Ac ge nyton hw&ae;t ge do&d;; ge sint on gedwolan. 
 Ac ic eow m&ae;g mid feawum wordum gereccan hw&ae;t se hrof is ealra ges&ae;l&d;a; wi&d; &t;as ic wat &t;u wilt higian &t;on &ae;r &t;e &d;u hine ongitest; &t;&ae;t is &t;onne good. 
 Meaht &t;u nu ongitan hw&ae;&d;er &t;u auht &t;e deorwyr&d;re h&ae;bbe &t;onne &t;e selfne? 
 Ic wene &t;eah &t;&ae;t &d;u wille cwe&t;an &t;&ae;t &t;u nauht deorwyr&d;re n&ae;bbe. 
 Ic wat  gif &t;u nu h&ae;fde fulne anweald &t;ines selfes  &t;onne h&ae;fde &t;u hw&ae;thwugu on &d;e selfum &t;&ae;s &d;e &t;u n&ae;fre &t;inum willum al&ae;t an noldes  ne sio wyrd &t;e on geniman ne meahte. 
 For&d;&ae;m ic &d;e mindgige &t;&ae;t &t;u ongite &t;&ae;tte nan ges&ae;l&d; nis on &t;is andweardan life &d;onne seo gesceadwisnes  for&d;&ae;m hio &t;urh nan &t;ing ne m&ae;g &t;&ae;m men losian; for&d;y is betere &t;&ae;t feoh &t;&ae;tte n&ae;fre losian ne m&ae;g &d;onne &t;&ae;tte m&ae;g &amp; sceal. 
 Hu ne is &t;e nu genoh sweotole ges&ae;d &t;&ae;t sio wyrd &t;e ne m&ae;g nane ges&ae;l&d;a sellan? 
 for&t;&ae;m&t;e &ae;g&t;er is unf&ae;st  ge seo wyrd ge seo ges&ae;l&d;; for&t;am sint swi&d;e tedre &amp; swidre hreosende &t;as ges&ae;l&t;a. 
 Hw&ae;t  &ae;lc &t;ara &t;e &t;as woruldges&ae;l&t;a h&ae;f&d; o&t;er twega o&d;&d;e he wat &t;&ae;t hi him fromwearde beo&d;  o&d;&d;e he hit &t;onne nat. 
 Gif he hit &t;onne nat  hwelce ges&ae;l&t;a h&ae;f&d; he &ae;t &t;am welan gif he bi&d; swa dysig &amp; swa ungewiss &t;&ae;t he &t;&ae;t witan ne m&ae;g? 
 Gif he hit &t;onne wat  &t;onne ondr&ae;t he him &t;&ae;t hi losien  &amp; eac geara wat &t;&ae;t he hi al&ae;tan sceal. 
 Se singala ege ne l&ae;t nonne mon ges&ae;linne bion. 
 Gif &t;onne hwa ne rec&d; hw&ae;&d;er he &t;a ges&ae;l&t;a h&ae;bbe &t;e n&ae;bbe &t;e he &t;onne h&ae;f&d;  hw&ae;t  &t;&ae;t &t;onne beo&d; for lytla s&ae;l&d;a o&t;&t;e nane  &t;&ae;t mon swa ea&d;e forl&ae;tan m&ae;g. 
 Ic wene nu &t;&ae;t ic &t;e h&ae;fde &ae;r genog sweotole gereaht be monegum tacnum &t;&ae;tte monna sawla sint undeadlica &amp; ece  &amp; &t;is is genog sweotol &t;&ae;tte n&ae;nne mon &t;&ae;s tweogan ne &t;earf &t;&ae;tte ealle men geendia&d; on &t;am dea&d;e  &amp; eac heora welan. 
 &t;i ic wundrige hwi men sien swa ungesceadwise &t;&ae;t hi wenen &t;&ae;t te &t;is andwearde lif maege &t;one monnan don ges&ae;ligne &t;a hwile &t;e he leofa&d;  &t;onne hit hine ne m&ae;g &ae;fter &t;ys life earmne gedon. 
 Hw&ae;t  we gewislice witon unrim &d;ara monna &t;e &t;a ecan ges&ae;l&d;a sohton nalles &t;urh &t;&ae;t an &t;&ae;t hi wilnodon &d;&ae;s lichomlican dea&d;es  ac eac manegra sarlicra wita hi gewilnodon wi&d; &t;&ae;m ecan life; &t;&ae;t w&ae;ron ealle &t;a halgan martiras. 
 &t;a ongan se Wisdom gliowian &amp; geoddode &t;us; ecte &t;&ae;t spell mid leo&d;e &t;&ae;t he &ae;r s&ae;de  &amp; cw&ae;&d;: Se &t;e wille f&ae;st hus timbrian ne sceal he hit no settan up on &d;one hehstan cnoll  &amp; se &d;e wille godcundne wisdom secan ne m&ae;g he hine wi&d; ofermetta. 
 &amp; eft se &t;e wille f&ae;st hus timbrian ne sette he hit on sondbeor has. 
 Swa eac gif &t;u wisdom timbrian wille  ne sete &t;u hine on uppan &t;a gitsunga  for&t;am swa swa sigende sond &t;one ren swylg&d;  swa swylg&d; seo gitsung &t;a dreosendan welan &t;isses middangeardes  for&t;am hio hiora simle bi&d; &t;urstegu. 
 Ne m&ae;g hus naht lange standan on &t;am hean munte gif hit full ungemetlic wind gestent; n&ae;f&d; &t;&ae;t &t;&ae;tte on &d;am sigendam sonde stent for swi&d;licum rene. 
 Swa eac &t;&ae;t mennisce mod bi&d; undereten &amp; aweged of his stede &t;onne hit se wind strongra geswinca astyro&d; o&d;&d;e se ren ungemetlices ymbhogan. 
 Ac se &t;e wille habban &t;a ecan ges&ae;l&d;a he sceal fleon &t;one frecnan wlite &t;ises middaneardes &amp; timbrian &t;&ae;t hus his modes on &t;am f&ae;stan stane ea&d;metta  for&t;am&d;e Crist earda&d; on &t;&ae;re dene eadmodnesse &amp; on &t;am gemynde wisdomes. 
 For&t;am simle se wisa mon eall his lif l&ae;t on gefean unonwendendlice &amp; orsorg  &t;onne he forsih&t; &ae;g&d;er ge &t;as eor&d;lican god ge eac &t;a yflu  &amp; hopa&d; to &t;am toweardan; &t;&ae;t sint &t;a ecan. 
 For&t;am&t;e God hine gehelt &ae;ghwonan singallice wuniendne on his modes ges&ae;l&d;um  &d;eah &t;e se wind &t;ara earfo&t;a &amp; seo singale gemen &t;issa worulds&ae;l&d;a him on blawe. 
 &d;a se Wisdom &t;a &amp; seo Gesceadwisnes &t;is leo&d; asungen h&ae;fde  &t;a ongon he eft secgean spel &amp; &t;us cw&ae;&d;: Me &t;inc&d; nu &t;&ae;t wit m&ae;gen smealicor sprecan &amp; diogolran wordum  for&t;am ic ongite &t;&ae;t min lar hw&ae;thwugu in g&ae;&d; on &t;in ondgit &amp; &t;u genoh wel understenst &t;&ae;t ic &t;e to sprece. 
 Ge&t;enc nu hw&ae;t &t;ines agnes sie ealra &d;issa woruld&ae;hta &amp; welena  o&d;&d;e hw&ae;t &t;u &t;&ae;ron age unandergildes  gif &t;u him sceadwislice &ae;fter spyrest. 
 Hw&ae;t h&ae;fst &t;u &ae;t &t;am gifum &t;e &t;u cwyst &t;&ae;t seo wyrd eow gife  &amp; &ae;t &d;&ae;m welan  &t;eah hy nu ece w&ae;ron? 
 S&ae;ge me nu hw&ae;&d;er se &t;in wela &t;ines &d;ances swa diore seo  &t;e for his agenre gecynde. 
 Hw&ae;&d;er ic &t;e secge &t;eah &d;&ae;t hit is of his agenre gecynde  n&ae;s of &t;inre. 
 Gif hit &t;onne his agenre gecynde is  nas of &t;inre  hwi eart &t;u &t;onne a &t;y betera for his gode? 
 Sege me nu hw&ae;t his &t;e deorast &t;ince  hw&ae;&d;er &t;e gold &t;e hw&ae;t. 
 Ic wat &t;eah gold. 
 Ac &t;eah hit nu god sie &amp; diore  &d;eah bi&d; hliseadigra &amp; leofwendra se &d;e hit sel&d; &t;onne se &d;e hit gadera&d; &amp; on o&d;rum reafa&d;. 
 Ge eac &t;a welan bio&d; hliseadigran &amp; leoft&ae;lran &t;onne &t;onne hi mon sel&d; &t;onne hi bion &d;onne hi mon gadra&d; &amp; hilt. 
 Hw&ae;t  sio gitsung gede&d; heore gitseras la&d;e &ae;g&t;er ge Gode ge monnum  &amp; &t;a cysta gedo&d; &t;a simle leoft&ae;le &amp; hliseadige &amp; weor&d;e &ae;g&t;er ge Gode ge monnum &d;e hie lufia&d;. 
 Nu &t;&ae;t feoh &t;onne &ae;g&t;er ne m&ae;g beon ge mid &t;am &t;e hit sel&d; ge mid &t;am &t;e hit mon sel&d;  nu is for&t;am &ae;lc feoh betere &amp; deorwyr&d;re geseald &t;onne gehealden. 
 Gif nu eall &t;ises middaneardes wela come to anum men  hu ne w&ae;ren &t;onne ealle o&t;re men w&ae;dlan buton him anum? 
 Genoh sweotol &t;&ae;t is &t;&ae;tte god word &amp; god hlisa &ae;lces monnes bi&d; betra &amp; deorra &t;onne &ae;nig wela; hw&ae;t  &t;&ae;t word gefyl&d; &ae;lces &t;ara earan &t;e hit geher&d;  &amp; ne bi&d; &t;eah na &t;y l&ae;sse mid &t;&ae;m &t;e hit spric&d;. 
 His heortan diegelnesse hit geopena&d;  &amp; &t;&ae;s o&d;res heortan belocena hit &t;urhf&ae;r&d;  &amp; on &t;am f&ae;relde &t;&ae;rbetwyx ne bi&d; hit no gewanod. 
 ne m&ae;g hit mon mid sweorde ofslean ne mid rape gebindan  ne hit n&ae;fre ne acwyl&d;. 
 Ac &t;a eowre welan  &t;eah hi ealne weg mid eow sien  ne &t;inc&d; eow no &t;y hra&d;or hiora genoh; &amp; &d;eah ge hi &t;onne o&t;rum monnum sellen  ne magon ge no &t;e ma mid &t;&ae;m hiora w&ae;dle &amp; heora gitsunge gefyllan. 
 &t;eah &d;u hi smale tod&ae;le swa dust  ne miht &t;u &d;eah ealle men emnlice mid gehealdan; &amp; &t;onne &t;u ealle ged&ae;lde h&ae;fst &t;onne bist &t;u &d;e self w&ae;dla. 
 Sint &t;&ae;t werilice welan &t;isses middangeardes  &t;onne hi nan mon fullice habban ne m&ae;g  ne hie nanne mon gewelegian ne magon  buton hie o&d;erne gedon to w&ae;dlan. 
 Hw&ae;&t;er nu gimma wlite eowre eagan to him getio hiora to wundriganne? 
 Swa ic wat &t;&ae;t hi do&d;. 
 Hw&ae;t  sio dugu&d; &t;onne &t;&ae;s wlites &t;e on &t;&ae;m gimmum bi&d;  bi&d; heora  n&ae;s eower. 
 &t;y ic eom swi&d;e ungemetlice ofwundrod hwi eow &t;ince &t;&ae;re ungesceadwisan gesceafte godweb betere &t;onne eower agen god; hwi ge swa ungemetlice wundrigen &t;ara gimma o&t;&t;e &ae;niges &t;ara deadlicena &d;inga &t;e gesceadwisnesse n&ae;f&d;; for&d;&ae;m hi mid nanum ryhte ne magon gearnigan &t;&ae;t ge heora wundrien. 
 &t;eah hi Godes gesceaftes sien  ne sint hi no wi&d; eow to metanne  for&d;&ae;m &t;e o&t;er twega o&d;&d;e hit nan god nis for eow selfe  o&d;&d;e &t;eah forlytel god wi&d; eow to metane. 
 To swi&d;e we herwa&d; us selfe &t;onne we &t;&ae;t ma lufia&d; &t;&ae;tte under us is on ussum anwalde  &t;onne us selfe o&d;&d;e &t;one drihten &t;e us gesceop  &amp; us eall &d;a god forgeaf. 
 Hw&ae;&t;er &t;e nu licien f&ae;gru lond? 
 &d;a andsworode &t;&ae;t Mod &t;aere Gesceadwisnesse &amp; cw&ae;&d;: Hwi ne sceolde me lician f&ae;ger lond? 
 Hu ne is &t;&ae;t se f&ae;geresta d&ae;l Godes gesceafta? 
 Ge  ful oft we fagenia&d; smyltre s&ae;  &amp; eac wundria&d; &t;&ae;s wlites &t;&ae;re sunnan &amp; &t;&ae;s monan &amp; ealra &t;ara steorrena. 
 &d;a andswarode se Wisdom &amp; seo Gesceadwisnes &t;&ae;m Mode &amp; &t;us cw&ae;&d;: Hw&ae;t belimp&d; &t;e to hiora f&ae;gernessa? 
 Hw&ae;&d;er &t;u dyrre gilpan &t;&ae;t hiora f&ae;gernes &t;in sie? 
 Nese  nese. 
 Hu ne wast &t;u &t;&ae;t &d;u hiora nan ne worhtest? 
 Ac gif &t;u gilpan wille  gilp Godes. 
 Hw&ae;&d;er &t;u nu f&ae;gerra blostm&ae;na f&ae;gnige on eastran  swelce &t;u hie gescope? 
 Hw&ae;&d;er &d;u nu swelces auht wyrcan m&ae;ge  o&d;&d;e geworhtes habbe? 
 Nese  nese. 
 Ne do &t;u swa. 
 Hw&ae;&t;er hit nu &t;ines gewealdes se &t;&ae;t se h&ae;rfest sie swa welig on w&ae;stmum? 
 Hu ne wat ic &t;&ae;t hit nis no &t;ines gewealdes? 
 Hwi eart &t;u &t;onne on&ae;led mid swa idele gefean  o&d;&d;e hwi lufast &t;u &d;a fremdan god swa ungemetlice  swelce hi sen &t;ine get nu? 
 Wenst &t;u m&ae;ge seo wyrd &t;e gedon &t;&ae;t &t;a &t;ing &t;in agnu sen &t;a &d;e heora agene gecynd &t;e gedon fremde? 
 Nese  nese. 
 Nis hit no &t;e gecynde &t;&ae;tte &t;u hi age; ne him nis gebyrde &t;&ae;t hi &d;e folgien. 
 Ac &t;a hefoncundan &t;ing &d;e sint gecynde  n&ae;s &t;&ae;s eor&d;lican. 
 &t;as eor&d;lican w&ae;stmas sint gesceapene netenum to andlifene; &amp; &t;a woruldwelan sint gesceapene to biswice &t;am monnum &t;e bio&d; neatum gelice  &t;&ae;t beo&d; unrihtwise &amp; ungemetf&ae;ste. 
 To &t;&ae;m hi eac becuma&d; oftost. 
 Gif &t;u &t;onne &t;&ae;t gemet habban wille  &amp; &t;a nyd&t;earfe witan wille  &t;onne is &t;&ae;t mete and drync &amp; cla&d;as &amp; tol to swelcum cr&ae;fte swelce &t;u cunne &t;&ae;t &t;e is gecynde &amp; &t;&ae;t &t;e is riht to habbenne. 
 Hwilc fremu is &t;e &t;&ae;t &t;&ae;t &t;u wilnige &t;issa andweardena ges&ae;l&t;a ofer gemet  &t;onne hie na&t;er ne magon ne &t;in gehelpan  ne heora selfra? 
 On swi&d;e lytlon hiera h&ae;f&d; seo gecynd genog; on swa miclum hio h&ae;f&d; genog swa we &ae;r spr&ae;con. 
 Gif &d;u heore mare selest  o&t;er twega o&d;&d;e hit &t;e dera&d;  o&d;&d;e hit &d;e &t;eah unwynsum bi&d;  o&d;&d;e unget&ae;se  o&d;&d;e frecenlic  eall &t;&ae;t &t;u nu ofer gemet dest. 
 Gif &d;u nu ofer gemet itst  o&d;&d;e drincst  o&d;&d;e cla&d;a &t;e ma on hehst &t;onne &t;u &t;urfe  seo oferinc &t;e wyr&d; o&d;&d;e to sare  o&d;&d;e to wl&ae;ttan  o&t;&t;e to ungerisenum  o&d;&d;e to plio. 
 Gif &t;u nu wenst &t;&ae;tte wundorlice gegerela hwelc weor&d;mynd sie  &t;onne telle ic &t;a weor&d;mynde &t;am wyrhtan &t;e hi worhte  nealles &t;e. 
 Se wyrhta is God; &t;&ae;s cr&ae;ft ic &t;&ae;r herige on. 
 Wenst &t;u &t;&ae;t sio menigo &d;inra monna &t;e m&ae;ge don ges&ae;ligne? 
 Nese nese. 
 Ac gif hi yfele sint &amp; lytige &t;onne sint hi &t;e pliolicran &amp; geswincfulran h&ae;fd &d;onne n&ae;fd; for&t;&ae;m yfele &t;egnas bio&d; simle heora hlafordes fiend. 
 Gif hi &t;onne gode beo&d; &amp; hlaford holde &amp; untwifealde  hu ne beo&d; &t;&ae;t &t;onne heora godes  n&ae;s &t;ines? 
 Hu miht &t;u &t;onne &t;e agnian heora god? 
 Gif &t;u nu &t;&ae;s gilpst  hu ne gilpst &t;u &t;onne heora godes  n&ae;s &t;ines? 
 Nu &t;e is genoh openlice gecy&t;ed &t;&ae;tte nan &t;ara goda &t;in nis  &t;e we &ae;r ymb spr&ae;con  &amp; &t;u teohhodest &t;&ae;t hi &d;ine bion sceolden. 
 Gif &d;onne &t;isse worulde wlites &amp; wela to wilnienne nis  hw&ae;t murcnast &t;u &t;onne &ae;fter &t;am &t;e &t;u forlure  o&d;&d;e to hwon fagnast &t;u &t;&ae;s &t;e &d;u &ae;r h&ae;fdest? 
 Gif hit f&ae;ger is  &t;&ae;t is of hiora agnum gecynde  n&ae;s of &t;inum  hiora f&ae;ger hit is  nas &t;in. 
 Hw&ae;t f&ae;gnast &t;u &t;onne heora f&ae;gres? 
 Hw&ae;t belimp&d; his to &t;e? 
 Ne &t;u hit ne gesceope  ne hi &t;ine agene ne sent. 
 Gif hi nu gode sint &amp; f&ae;gere  &t;onne w&ae;ron hi swa gesceapene; &amp; sw&ae;lce hi woldan bion  &t;eah &t;u hi n&ae;fre nahtest. 
 Wenst &t;u &t;&ae;t hi a &d;y deorwyr&d;ran seon &t;e hi to &t;inre note gel&ae;nde w&ae;ran? 
 Ac for&t;&ae;m&t;e heora dysige men wafia&d; &amp; hi him &t;inca&d; deore  for&t;am &t;u hi gaderast &amp; helst on &t;inum horde. 
 Hw&ae;t wilnast &t;u &t;onne &t;&ae;t &t;u h&ae;bbe &ae;t swelcere gelicnesse? 
 Gelef me  nu ic hit &t;e secge: n&ae;fst &t;u &t;&ae;r nauht &ae;t  buton &t;&ae;t &t;u tilas w&ae;dle to flionne  &amp; for&t;y g&ae;derast mare &t;onne &t;u &d;urfe. 
 Ac ic wat &t;eah swi&d;e geara &t;&ae;tte eall &t;&ae;t ic her sprece is wi&d; &t;inum willan. 
 Ac eowra ges&ae;l&d;a ne sint no &t;&ae;t ge wena&d; &t;&ae;t hi sen  for&t;am se &t;e micel innierfe &amp; mislic agan wile  he be&d;earf eac miceles fultumes. 
 Se ealda cwide is swi&d;e so&d; &t;e mon gefyrn cw&ae;&d;  &t;&ae;tte &t;a micles bedurfon &t;e micel agan willa&d;  &amp; &t;a &t;urfon swi&t;e lytles &t;e maran ne wilnia&d; &t;onne genoges. 
 Butan hi wilnien mid oferinge hiora gitsunga gefyllan  &t;&ae;t hi n&ae;fre ne gedo&d;. 
 Ic wat &t;&ae;t ge wena&d; &t;&ae;t ge nan gecundlic god ne ges&ae;l&t;a oninnan eow selfum n&ae;bben  for&d;&ae;m ge hi seca&d; butan eow to fremdum gesceaftum. 
 Swa hit is mishweorfed &t;&ae;t &t;&ae;m men &t;inc&d;  &t;eah he se godcundlice gesceadwis  &t;&ae;t he on him selfum n&ae;bbe s&ae;l&t;a genoge  buton he mare gegaderige &t;ara ungesceadwisene gesceafta &t;onne he be&t;urfe o&d;&d;e him gemetlicre sie. 
 &amp; &t;a ungesceadwisan neotena ne wilnia&d; nanes o&d;res feos  ac &t;inc&d; him genog on &t;am &t;e hi binnan heora &ae;genre hyde habba&d; toeacan &t;am fodre &t;e him gecyndelic bi&d;. 
 Hw&ae;t  ge &t;onne &t;eah hw&ae;thwega godcundlices on eowerre saule habba&d;  &t;&ae;t is andgit &amp; gemynd  &amp; se gesceadwislica willa &t;&ae;t hine &t;ara twega lyste. 
 Se &t;e &t;onne &t;as &d;reo h&ae;f&d;  &t;onne h&ae;f&d; he his sceoppendes onlicnesse swa for&d; swa swa &ae;negu gesceaft fyrmest m&ae;g hiere sceppendes onlicnesse habban. 
 Ac ge seca&d; &t;&ae;re hean gecynde ges&ae;l&t;a &amp; heora weor&d;scipe to &d;&ae;m ni&t;erlicum &amp; to &t;am hreosendlicum &t;ingum. 
 Ac ge ne ongita&d; hu micelne teonan ge do&d; Gode eowrum scippende  for&t;am&t;e he wolde &t;&ae;tte ealle men w&ae;ran ealra o&t;erra gesceafta wealdendas; ac ge under&t;eoda&d; eowre hehstan medemnesse under &t;a eallra ny&d;emestan gesceafta. 
 mid &t;am ge habba&d; gecy&d;ed &t;&ae;t &ae;fter eowrum agnum dome ge do&d; eow selfe wyrsan &t;onne eowra agne &ae;hta  nu ge wena&d; &t;&ae;t eowre nauht welan send eowre ges&ae;l&t;a  &amp; teohhia&d; &t;&ae;t eall eowre woruldgod sien dierran ge selfe. 
 Swa hit eac wyr&d; &t;onne ge swa willa&d;. 
 &t;&ae;s menniscan lifes gecynd is &t;&ae;t hi &t;y anan seon beforan eallum o&d;rum gesceaftum &t;y hi hie selfe ongiton hw&ae;t hie send &amp; hwonan hi send; &amp; &t;i hi send wyrsan &t;onne nytenu  &t;y hi nella&d; witan hw&ae;t hi sint  o&d;&d;e hwonan hi sint. 
 &t;am neatum is gecynde &t;&ae;t hi nyton hw&ae;t hie send; ac &t;&ae;t is &t;ara monna un&d;eaw &t;&ae;t hi niton hw&ae;t hie sen. 
 Nu &t;e is swi&t;e sweotol &t;&ae;t ge beo&t; on gedwolan  &t;onne ge wena&d; &t;&ae;t &ae;nig m&ae;g mid fremdum welum beon geweor&t;od. 
 Gif hwa nu bi&d; mid hwelcum welum geweor&t;od &amp; mid hwelcum deorwyr&t;um &ae;htum gegyrewod  hu ne belimp&d; se weor&d;scipe &t;onne to &t;am &t;e hine geweor&d;a&d;? 
 &t;&ae;t is to herianne hwene rihtlicor. 
 Ne &t;&ae;t ne beo&t; no &d;y f&ae;gerre &t;&ae;t mid elleshwam gerenod bi&d;  &t;eah &t;a gerenu f&ae;gru sien &t;e hit mid gerenod bi&d;. 
 Gif hit &ae;r scandlic w&ae;s  ne bi&d; hit no &d;y faegerre. 
 Wite &t;u for so&d; &t;&ae;t nan god ne dere&d; &t;&ae;m &t;e hit ah. 
 Hw&ae;t  &t;u wast nu &t;&ae;t ic &t;e ne leoge  &amp; eac wast &t;&ae;t &t;a welan oft deria&d; &t;am &t;e hi agon on manegum &t;ingum  &amp; on &d;&ae;m swi&d;ost &t;&ae;tte men weor&d;a&d; swa up ah&ae;fene for &d;&ae;m welan &t;&ae;t oft se ealra wyrresta &amp; se ealra unweor&d;esta mon wen&d; &t;&ae;t he sie ealles &t;&ae;s welan wyr&d;e &t;e on &t;isse worulde is  gif he wisse hu he him to cuman meahte. 
 Se &d;e micelne welan h&ae;f&d;  he him ondr&ae;t monige feond; gif he nane &ae;hta n&ae;fde  ne &t;orfte he him n&ae;nne ondr&ae;dan. 
 Gif &t;u nu w&ae;re wegferend &amp; h&ae;fdest micel gold on &d;e  &amp; &t;u &t;onne become on &t;iofscole  &t;onne ne wendes &t;u &t;e &t;ines feores. 
 &t;onne gif &d;u &t;onne swelces nanwuht n&ae;fde  &t;onne ne &d;orftes &t;u &d;e nanwuht ondr&ae;dan  ac meahtes &t;e gan singende &t;one ealdan cwide &t;e mon gefyrn sang  &t;&ae;t se nacoda wegferend him nanwuht ne ondrede. 
 &t;onne &t;u &t;onne orsorg w&ae;re  &amp; &t;a &t;eofas &t;e from gewiten w&ae;ron  &t;onne meahtes &t;u bismrian &t;&ae;s andweardan welan  &amp; meahtes cwe&t;an: Eala &t;&ae;t hit is god &amp; wynsum &t;&ae;t mon micelne welan h&ae;bbe  nu se n&ae;fre ne wyr&d; orsorg &t;e hine underfeh&d;. 
 &t;a seo Gesceadwisnes &t;a &t;is spell as&ae;d h&ae;fde  &t;a ongan heo singan &amp; &t;us cw&ae;&d;: Eala  hu ges&ae;lig seo forme eld was &t;ises midangeardes  &d;a &ae;lcum men &t;uhte genog on &t;&ae;re eor&t;an w&ae;stmum. 
 N&ae;ron &t;a welige hamas  ne mistlice swotmettas  ne drincas  ne diorwyr&d;ra hr&ae;gla hi ne girndan  for&t;am hi &t;a git n&ae;ran  ne hio nanwuht ne gesawon  ne ne geherdon. 
 Ne gemdon hie nanes fyrenlustes  buton swi&d;e gemetlice &t;a gecynd beeodan; ealne weg hi &ae;ton &ae;ne on d&ae;g  &amp; &t;&ae;t was to &ae;fennes. 
 Treowa w&ae;stmas hi &ae;ton &amp; wyrta  nalles scir win hi ne druncan  ne nanne w&ae;tan hi ne cu&t;on wi&d; hunige mengan; ne seolocenra hr&ae;gla mid mistlicum bleowum hi ne gimdon. 
 Ealne weg hi slepon ute on triowa sceadum; hluterra wella w&ae;ter hi druncon. 
 Ne geseah nan cepa ealand ne wero&d;  ne geherde non mon &t;a get nanne sciphere  ne fur&t;on ymbe nan gefeoht sprecan. 
 Ne seo eor&d;e &t;a get besmiten mid ofsl&ae;genes monnes blode  ne mon fur&d;um gewundod; ne monn ne geseah &t;a git yfelwillende men; n&ae;nne weor&d;scipe n&ae;fdon  ne hi non mon ne lufude. 
 Eala &t;&ae;t ure tida nu ne mihtan weor&t;an swilce. 
 Ac nu manna gitsung is swa byrnende swa &t;&ae;t fyr on &t;&ae;re helle  seo is on &t;am munte &t;e &ae;tne hatte  on &t;am ieglande &t;e Sicilia hatte. 
 se munt bi&d; simle swefle birnende  &amp; ealla &t;a neahstowa &t;&ae;rymbutan forb&ae;rn&d;. 
 &ae;ala  hw&ae;t se forma gitsere w&ae;re  &t;e &ae;rest &t;a eor&t;an ongan delfan &ae;fter golde  &amp; &ae;fter gimmum  &amp; &t;a frecnan deorwyr&d;nesse funde &t;e &ae;r behyd w&ae;s &amp; behelod mid &d;&ae;re eor&t;an. 
 &t;a se Wisdom &t;a &t;is leo&d; asungen h&ae;fde  &t;a ongan he eft spellian &amp; &t;us cw&ae;&t;: Hw&ae;t m&ae;g ic &t;y mare secgan be &t;&ae;m weor&d;scipe &amp; be &t;&ae;m anwealde &t;isse worulde? 
 For &d;&ae;m anwealde ge eow woldon ahebban up o&d; &d;one heofen  gif ge meahten. 
 &t;&ae;t is for&d;&ae;m&t;e ge ne gemunon ne eac ne ongita&d; &t;one heofoncundan anweald &amp; &t;one weor&d;scipe; se is eower agen  &amp; &t;onan ge comon. 
 Hw&ae;t  se eower wela &t;onne &amp; se eower anweald  &t;e ge nu weor&d;scipe hata&d;  gif he becym&d; to &t;am eallra wyrrestan men  &amp; to &t;am &t;e his eallra unweor&d;ost bi&d;  swa he nu dyde to &t;is ilcan &t;eodrice  &amp; iu &ae;r to Nerone &t;&ae;m casere  &amp; oft eac to m&ae;negum hiora gelicum  hu ne wile he &d;onne don swa hi dydon &amp; get do&d;  ealle &d;a ricu &t;e him under bio&d; o&d;&d;e awer on neaweste  forslean &amp; forheregian  sw&ae; swa fyres leg de&d; drigne h&ae;&d;feld  o&d;&d;e eft se byrnenda swefel &d;one munt b&ae;rn&d; &t;e we hata&d; Etne  se is on Sicilia &d;&ae;m ealonde; swi&d;e onlic &d;&ae;m miclan flode &d;e giu on Noes dagum w&ae;s. 
 Ic wene &d;&ae;t &t;u m&ae;ge gemunan &d;&ae;tte eowre eldran gio Romana witan on Torcwines dagum &t;&ae;s ofermodan cyninges for his ofermettum &t;one cynelican naman of Romebyrig &ae;res&d; adydon. 
 Ond eft swa ilce &t;a heretogan &d;e hine &ae;r ut adrifon hi wolden eft ut adrifan for hiora ofermettum. 
 ac hi ne meahton  for&d;&ae;m&t;e se &ae;ftera anweald &t;ara heretogena &t;&ae;m romaniscum witum get wyrs licode &t;onne se &ae;rra &t;ara cyninga. 
 Gif hit &t;onne &ae;fre gewir&d;  swa hit swi&d;e seldon gewyr&d;  &t;&ae;t se anweald &amp; se weor&d;scipe becume to godum men &amp; to wisum  hw&ae;t bi&d; &t;&ae;r &t;onne licwyr&d;es buton his god &amp; his weor&d;scipe  &t;&ae;s godan cyninges  n&ae;s &t;&ae;s anwealdes? 
 For&t;am&t;e se anwald n&ae;fre ne bi&d; good buton se god sie &t;e hine h&ae;bbe; &d;y hit bi&d; &t;&ae;s monnes god n&ae;s &t;&ae;s anwealdes  gif se anweald god bi&d;. 
 For&t;am hit bi&d; &t;&ae;tte nan man for his rice ne cym&d; to cr&ae;ftum &amp; to medemnesse  ac for his cr&ae;ftum &amp; for his medumnesse he cym&d; to rice &amp; to anwealde. 
 &t;i ne bi&d; nan man for his anwealde na &t;e betera  ac for his cr&ae;ftum he beo&d; good  gif he god bi&d;  &amp; for his cr&ae;ftum he bi&d; anwealdes weor&d;e  gif he his weor&d;e bi&d;. 
 Leornia&d; for&d;&ae;m wisdom  &amp; &t;onne ge hine geleornod h&ae;bben  ne forhycga&d; hine &t;onne. 
 &t;onne secge ic eow buton &ae;lcum tweon &t;&ae;t ge magon &t;urh hine becuman to anwealde  &t;eah ge no &t;&ae;s anwealdes ne wilnigan. 
 Ne &t;urfon ge no hogian on &t;am anwealde  ne him &ae;fter &t;ringan. 
 Gif ge wise beo&d; &amp; gode  he wile folgian eow  &t;eah ge his no ne wilnigen. 
 Ac sege me nu hw&ae;t eower deorwyr&d;esta wela &amp; anwald sie  &t;e ge swi&d;ost girna&t;. 
 Ic wat &t;eah &t;&ae;t hit is &t;is andwearde lif &amp; &d;es brosnienda wela &d;e we &ae;r ymbe spr&ae;con. 
 Eala  hw&ae;&d;er ge netenlican men ongiten hwilc se wela sie  &amp; se anwald  &amp; &d;a worulds&ae;l&d;a? 
 &t;a sint eowere hlafordas &amp; eowere waldendas  n&ae;s ge heora. 
 Gif ge nu gesawan hwelce mus &t;&ae;t w&ae;re hlaford ofer o&d;re mys  &amp; sette him domas  &amp; nedde hie &ae;fter gafole  hu wunderlic wolde eow &d;&ae;t &t;incan. 
 hwelce cehhettunge ge woldan &t;&ae;s habban  &amp; mid hwelce hleatre ge woldon bion astered. 
 Hu micle mare is &d;onne &t;&ae;s monnes lichoma to metenne wi&d; &t;&ae;t mod &t;onne seo mus wi&d; &d;one mon. 
 Hw&ae;t  ge &t;onne magon ea&d;e ge&t;encan  gif ge hit georne ymbe smeagan willa&d; &amp; &ae;fter spyrigan  &t;&ae;t nanre wuhte lichoma ne beo&d; &t;onne tederra &t;onne &t;&ae;s monnes. 
 &t;&ae;m magon derian &t;a l&ae;stan fleogan  ge &d;a gn&ae;ttas mid swy&d;e lytlum sticelum him deria&d;  &amp; eac &d;a smalan wyrmas &d;e &d;one mon &ae;g&d;er ge innan ge utan wyrda&d;  &amp; hwilum fulneah deadne gedo&d;; ge fur&d;um &t;ios lytle loppe hine deadne gede&d;. 
 Swilca wuhta him deriga&d; &ae;g&d;er ge innan ge utan. 
 On hw&ae;m m&ae;g &ae;nig mon o&d;rum derian buton on his lichoman  o&d;&d;e eft on hiora welum  &t;e ge hata&d; ges&ae;l&d;a ? 
 Ne nan mon ne m&ae;g &d;&ae;m gesceadwisan mode gederian  ne him gedon &t;&ae;t hit sie &d;&ae;t &d;&ae;t hit ne bi&d;. 
 &d;&ae;t is swi&d;e sweotol to ongitanne be sumum romaniscum &ae;&t;elinge  se w&ae;s haten Liberius. 
 se w&ae;s to manegum witum geworht  for&d;&ae;m&t;e he nolde meldian on his geferan &t;e mid him siredon ymb &d;one cyning &t;e hie &ae;r mid unrihte gewunnen h&ae;fdon. 
 &t;a he &d;a beforan &d;one graman cyning gel&ae;d w&ae;s  &amp; he hine het secgan hw&ae;t his geferan w&ae;ron &d;e mid him ymbe sieredon  &t;a forceaw he his tungan &amp; wearp hine mid &d;&ae;re tungan on &t;&ae;t neb foran. 
 For&d;&ae;m hit gewear&d; &t;&ae;t &d;&ae;m wisan men com to lofe &amp; to wyr&d;scipe &t;&ae;t se unrihtwisa cyning him tiohhode to wite. 
 Hw&ae;t is &t;&ae;t &d;emma &d;&ae;t &ae;nig mon m&ae;ge o&d;rum don  &t;&ae;t he ne m&ae;ge him don &d;&ae;t ilce? 
 Gif he ne m&ae;g  o&d;er mon m&ae;g. 
 We leornodon eac be &d;&ae;m w&ae;lreowan Bosiridem  se w&ae;s on Egyptum. 
 &d;&ae;s leodhatan gewuna w&ae;s &t;&ae;t he wolde &ae;lcne cuman swi&d;e arlice underfoon &amp; swi&d;e sw&ae;slice wi&d; geb&ae;ran  &d;onne he &ae;res&d; him to com. 
 Ac eft  &ae;r he him from cerde  he sceolde bion ofsl&ae;gen. 
 Ond &d;a geberede hit &d;&ae;t Erculus Iobes sunu com to him. 
 &t;a wolde he don ymbe hine swa swa he ymbe manigne cuman &ae;r dyde; wolde hine adrencan on &t;&ae;re ea &d;e Nilus hatte. 
 &d;a wear&d; he strengra  &amp; adrencte hine swi&d;e rihte be Godes dome  swa swa he manigne o&d;erne &ae;r dyde. 
 Hw&ae;t  eac Regulus  se forem&ae;ra heretoga  &t;a he feaht wi&d; Africanas  he h&ae;fde fulneah unasecgendlicne sige ofer &t;a Africanas. 
 &t;a he hi &t;a swi&d;ost forslagen h&ae;fde  &d;a het he hi bindan &amp; on balcan lecgan. 
 &d;a gebyrede hit swi&d;e hra&d;e &t;&ae;t he wear&d; gebunden mid hira racentum. 
 Hw&ae;t wenst &t;u &t;onne hw&ae;t godes se anweald sie  &t;onne he on nane wisan his agenes cr&ae;ftes ne m&ae;g forbugan &t;&ae;t he &d;&ae;t ilce yfel ne ge&d;afige o&d;rum monnum &t;&ae;t he &ae;r o&d;rum dyde? 
 Hu ne is se anweald &t;onne &t;&ae;r nauht? 
 Hw&ae;t wenst &t;u? 
 gif se weor&d;scipe &amp; se anweald his agnes &t;onces god w&ae;re &amp; his selfes anweald h&ae;fde  hw&ae;&d;er he wolde &t;am forcu&d;estum monnum folgian swa he nu hwilum de&d;? 
 Hu ne wast &t;u &t;&ae;t hit nis nauht gecynde ne nauht gewunelic &t;&ae;t &ae;nig wi&d;erweard &t;ing bion gemenged wi&d; o&d;rum wi&d;erweardum  o&d;&d;e &ae;nige geferr&ae;denne wi&d; habban? 
 Ac seo gecynd hit onscuna&d; &t;&ae;t hi ne magon weor&d;an tog&ae;dere gemenged  &t;e ma &d;e &t;&ae;t good &amp; &d;&ae;t yfel magon &ae;tg&ae;dere bion. 
 Nu &t;e is swi&d;e openlice gecy&d;ed &t;&ae;t &t;is andwearde rice &amp; &t;as weoruldges&ae;l&t;a &amp; &t;es anweald of heora agnum gecynde &amp; heora agnes gewealdes nauht gode ne sient  ne heora selfra nanne anwald nabba&d;  nu hi willa&d; clifian on &t;am wyrrestan monnum  &amp; him ge&t;afia&d; &t;&ae;t hi bio&d; hiora hlafordas. 
 Nis &d;&ae;s nu nan tweo &d;&ae;t oft &t;a eallra forcu&t;estan men cuma&d; to &t;am anwealde &amp; to &t;am weor&d;scipe. 
 Gif se anweald &d;onne of his agenre gecynde &amp; his agnes gewealdes god w&ae;re  ne underfenge he n&ae;fre &t;a yfelan ac &t;a godan. 
 &t;&ae;s ilcan is to wenanne to eallum &d;&ae;m ges&ae;l&t;um &t;e seo wyrd breng&d; &t;isses andweardan lifes ge on cr&ae;ftum ge on &ae;htum; for&t;&ae;m&t;e hi hwilum becuma&d; to &t;am forcu&d;estum. 
 Hw&ae;t  we genog georne witon &d;&ae;t nanne mon &t;&ae;s ne tweo&d; &t;&ae;t se sie strong on his m&ae;gene &t;e mon gesih&d; &t;&ae;t stronglic weorc wyrc&d;; ne &t;onne ma  gif he hw&ae;t bi&d;  ne tweo&d; n&ae;nne mon &t;&ae;t he hw&ae;t ne sie. 
 Her enda&d; sio forme boc Boetius &amp; onginne&d; sio &ae;ftere. 
 Swa m&ae;g eac se dreamcr&ae;ft &d;&ae;t se mon bi&d; dreamere  &amp; se l&ae;cecr&ae;ft &t;&ae;t he bi&d; l&ae;ce  &amp; seo racu de&d; &t;&ae;t he bi&d; reccere. 
 Swa de&d; eac se gecynda cr&ae;ft &ae;lcum men &d;&ae;t &t;&ae;t god ne m&ae;g beon wi&d; &d;&ae;t yfel gemenged  ne &t;&ae;t yfel wi&d; &t;&ae;t god; &t;eah hie buta on anum men sien  &t;eah bi&d; &ae;g&d;er him onsundran. 
 &t;&ae;t gecynd nyle n&ae;fre nanwuht wi&d;erweardes l&ae;tan gemengan  for&d;&ae;m heora &ae;g&d;er onscuna&d; o&d;er  &amp; &ae;g&d;er wile bion &t;&ae;t &d;&ae;t hit bi&d;. 
 Ne m&ae;g se wela gedon &t;&ae;t se gitsere ne sie gitsere  ne &d;a grundleasan gitsunga gefyllan; ne se anweald ne m&ae;g gedon his waldend wealdendne. 
 Nu &t;onne nu &ae;lc gesceaft onscuna&d; &d;&ae;t &d;&ae;t hire wi&d;erweard bi&d;  &amp; swi&d;e georne tiola&d; &t;&ae;t hit him &t;&ae;t from ascufe  hwylce twa sint &t;onne wi&d;erweardran betwuh him &t;onne god &amp; yfel? 
 Ne weor&t;a&d; hi n&ae;fre tosomne gefeged. 
 Be &t;&ae;m &t;u meaht ongitan  gif &t;a ges&ae;l&t;a &d;ises andweardan lifes &t;urh hie selfe heora selfra geweald ahton  &amp; of heora agnum gecynde gode w&ae;ron  &t;onne woldon hi simle on &t;am clifian &t;e him god mid worhte  nal&ae;s yfel. 
 Ac &d;&ae;r &d;&ae;r hi gode beo&d;  &t;onne beo&d; hi &t;urh &t;&ae;s godan monnes god gode &t;e him god mid wyrc&d;  &amp; se bi&d; &t;urh God god. 
 Gif hine &t;onne yfel mon h&ae;f&d;  &t;onne bi&d; he yfel &t;urh &t;&ae;s monnes yfel &t;e him yfel mid de&d;  &amp; &t;urh dioful. 
 Hw&ae;t godes is se wela &d;onne  &d;onne he ne m&ae;g &t;a grundleasan gitsunga afyllan &t;&ae;s gitseres; o&d;&d;e se anweald  &d;onne he ne m&ae;g his waldend waldendne gedon? 
 Ac hine gebinda&d; &t;a won welnunga mid hiora unabindendlicum racentum. 
 &d;eah mon nu yfelum men anwald selle  ne gede&d; se anwald hine godne ne medomne  gif he &ae;r n&ae;s  ac geopena&d; his yfel  gif he &ae;r yfel w&ae;s  &amp; gede&d; hit &d;onne sweotol  gif hit &ae;r n&ae;s. 
 For&d;&ae;m &t;eah he &ae;r yfel wolde  &t;onne nysste he hu he hit swa fullice acy&d;de  &ae;r he fullne anweald h&ae;fde. 
 &t;&ae;t gewyr&d; for &t;am dysige &t;e ge f&ae;gnia&d; &t;&ae;t ge moton sceppan &t;one naman  hatan &t;&ae;t s&ae;l&t;a &t;&ae;t nane ne beo&d;  &amp; &t;&ae;t medumnes &t;&ae;t nan medomnes ne beo&d;. 
 for&t;am hi gecy&d;a&d; on heora endunge  &t;onne hie endia&d;  &t;&ae;t hie nau&d;er ne bio&d;  for&t;&ae;m naw&d;er ne se wela ne se anweald ne se weor&d;scipe ne beo&d; to wenanne &t;&ae;t hit seo so&t;e ges&ae;l&d; sie. 
 Swa hit is nu hra&d;ost to secganne be eallum &t;am woruldges&ae;l&d;um &t;e seo wyrd breng&d;  &t;&ae;t nan wuht on nis &d;&ae;s &t;&ae;r to wilnianne seo  for&t;am&d;e &t;&ae;r nan wuht gecyndelices godes on nis &t;&ae;s &d;e of him cume. 
 &t;&ae;t is on &d;&ae;m sweotol &t;&ae;t hi hi symle to &d;&ae;m godum ne &d;eoda&d;  ne &d;a yfelan gode ne gedo&d; &t;e hi hie oftos&d; to ge&t;ioda&d;. 
 &d;a se Wisdom &d;a &t;is spell &d;us areaht h&ae;fde  &d;a ongan he eft giddian &amp; &t;us cw&ae;&d;: Hw&ae;t  we witon hwelce w&ae;lriownessa &amp; hwilce hryras &amp; unryhth&ae;medu &amp; hwilc man &amp; hwilce arleasnesse se unrihtwisa kasere Neron weorhte. 
 Se het &ae;t sumum cyrre forb&ae;rnan &ae;alle Romeburg on anne si&d; &ae;fter &t;&ae;re bisene &t;e gio Trogiaburg barn. 
 Hine lyste eac geseon hu seo burne  hu lange  &amp; hu leohte be &t;&ae;re o&d;erre. 
 &amp; eft he het ofslean ealle &t;a wisestan witan Romana  ge fur&d;on his agene modor  &amp; his agene bro&d;or; ge fur&d;om his agen wif he ofslog mid sweorde; &amp; for &d;yllecum n&ae;s he nanwuht geunrotsod  ac w&ae;s &t;y bli&t;ra &amp; fagenode &t;&ae;s. 
 Ond &t;eah betwuh &t;yllecum unrihtum w&ae;s him no &t;y l&ae;s under&t;eod eall &t;es middangeard from easteweardum o&t; westeweardne  &amp; eft from su&d;eweardum o&d; nor&d;eweardne; eall he was on his anwealde. 
 Wenst &d;u &t;&ae;t se godcunda anweald ne mihte afyrran &t;one anweald &t;am unrihtwisan kasere  &amp; him &t;&ae;re wuhhunge gesteoran  gif he wolde? 
 Gise  la  gese; ic wat &t;&ae;t he mihte  gif he wolde. 
 Eala  eaw  hu hefig geoc he beslepte on eall&ae; &t;am &t;&ae; on his tidum libbende w&ae;ron on eor&d;an; &amp; hu oft his sweord w&ae;ron besyled on unscyldegum blode. 
 Hu ne was &t;&ae;r genog sweotol &t;&ae;t se anweald his agenes &d;onces god n&ae;s  &t;a se god n&ae;s &t;e he to com? 
 &d;a se Wisdom &d;a &t;is leo&d; asungen h&ae;fde  &d;a gesugode he; &amp; &t;a andswarode &t;&ae;t Mod &amp; &t;us cw&ae;&d;: Eala  Gesceadwisnes hw&ae;t  &t;u wast &t;&ae;t me n&ae;fre seo gitsung &amp; seo gem&ae;g&d; &t;isses eor&d;lican anwealdes forwel ne licode  ne ic ealles forswi&d;e ne girnde &t;isses eor&d;lican rices  buton tola ic wilnode &t;eah &amp; andweorces to &t;am weorce &t;e me beboden was to wyrcanne; &t;&ae;t was &t;&ae;t ic unfracodlice &amp; gerisenlice mihte steoran &amp; reccan &t;one anwald &t;e me bef&ae;st w&ae;s. 
 Hw&ae;t  &t;u wast &t;&ae;t nan mon ne m&ae;g n&ae;nne cr&ae;ft cy&d;an ne n&ae;nne anweald reccan ne stioran butun tolum &amp; andweorce. 
 &t;&ae;t bi&d; &ae;lces cr&ae;ftes andweorc &t;&ae;t mon &t;one cr&ae;ft buton wyrcan ne m&ae;g. 
 &t;&ae;t bi&d; &t;onne cyninges andweorc &amp; his tol mid to ricsianne  &t;&ae;t he h&ae;bbe his lond fullmonnad; he sceal habban gebedmen &amp; fyrdmen &amp; weorcmen. 
 Hw&ae;t  &t;u wast &t;&ae;tte butan &t;issan tolan nan cyning his cr&ae;ft ne m&ae;g cy&d;an. 
 &t;&ae;t is eac his ondweorc  &t;&ae;t he habban sceal to &d;&ae;m tolum &t;am &t;rim geferscipum biwiste. 
 &t;&ae;t is &t;onne heora biwist: land to bugianne  &amp; gifta  &amp; w&ae;pnu  &amp; mete  &amp; ealo  &amp; cla&t;as  &amp; gehw&ae;t &t;&ae;s &d;e &t;a &t;re geferscipas behofia&d;. 
 Ne m&ae;g he butan &t;isum &t;as tol gehealdan  ne buton &t;isum tolum nan &t;ara &t;inga wyrcan &t;e him beboden is to wyrcenne. 
 For&t;y ic wilnode andweorces &t;one anweald mid to reccenne  &t;&ae;t mine cr&ae;ftas &amp; anweald ne wurden forgitene &amp; forholene. 
 For&t;am &ae;lc cr&ae;ft &amp; &ae;lc anweald bi&d; sona forealdod &amp; forsugod  gif he bi&d; buton wisdome; for&d;&ae;m ne m&ae;g non mon n&ae;nne cr&ae;ft bringan buton wisdome. 
 for&d;&ae;m&t;e swa hw&ae;t swa &t;urh dysig gedon bi&d;  ne m&ae;g hit mon n&ae;fre to cr&ae;fte gerecan. 
 &t;&ae;t is nuhra&d;ost to secganne  &t;&ae;t ic wilnode weor&d;fullice to libbanne &t;a hwile &t;e ic lifde  &amp; &ae;fter minum life &t;&ae;m monnum to l&ae;fanne &t;e &ae;fter me w&ae;ren min gemyndig on godum weorcum. 
 &d;a &d;is &t;a gesprecen was  &t;a gesugode &t;&ae;t Mod  &amp; seo Gesceadwisnes ongon sprecan &amp; &t;us cw&ae;&t;: Eala  Mod  eala; an yfel is swi&d;e to anscunianne. 
 &t;&ae;t is &t;&ae;t &t;&ae;tte swi&d;e singallice &amp; swi&d;e hefiglice beswic&d; ealra &t;ara monna mod &t;e beo&d; on heora gecynde gecorene  &amp; &t;eah ne beo&d; to &t;am hrofe &t;onne git cumen fulfremedra m&ae;gena; &t;&ae;t is &t;onne wilnung leases gilpes &amp; unryhtes anwealdes &amp; ungemetlices hlisan godra weorca ofer eall folc. 
 For&t;am wilniga&d; monige men anwealdes &t;e hie woldon habban godne hlisan  &t;eah hi his unwyr&d;e sien; ge fur&d;um se ealra forcu&t;esta wilna&d; &t;&ae;s ilcan. 
 Ac se &t;e wile wislice &amp; geornlice &ae;fter &t;am hlisan spyrian  &t;onne ongit he swi&d;e hr&ae;&d;e hu lytel he bi&d;  &amp; hu l&ae;ne  &amp; hu tedre  &amp; hu bed&ae;led &ae;lces godes. 
 Gif &t;u nu geornlice smeagan wilt &amp; witan wilt ymb ealr&ae; &t;isse eor&d;an ymbhwyrft from easteweardan &d;isses middangeardes o&d; westeweardne  &amp; from su&d;eweardum o&d; nor&d;eweardne  swa swa &t;u liornodest on &t;&ae;re bec &t;e Astralogium hatte  &d;onne meaht &t;u ongetan &t;&ae;t he is eal wi&d; &t;one heofon to metanne swilce an lytlu price on bradum brede  o&d;&t;e rondbeag on scelde  &ae;fter wisra monna dome. 
 Hu ne wast &t;u &t;&ae;t &d;u leornodest on Ptolomeus bocum  se towrat ealles &t;ises middangeardes gemet on anre bec? 
 &t;&ae;r &t;u miht on geseon &t;&ae;t eall moncynn &amp; ealle netenu ne notiga&d; nawer neah feor&d;an d&ae;les &t;isse eor&d;an &d;&ae;s &t;e men gefaran magan  for&t;&ae;m&t;e hy hit ne magon eall gebugian  sum for h&ae;to  sum for cile; &amp; &t;one m&ae;stan d&ae;l his h&ae;f&d; s&ae; oferseten. 
 Do nu of &d;am feor&d;an d&ae;le an &t;inum mode eall &t;&ae;t seo s&ae; his ofseten h&ae;f&d;  &amp; eal &t;a sceard &t;e hio him on genumen h&ae;f&d;  &amp; eall &t;&ae;t his fennas &amp; moras genumen habba&d;  &amp; eall &t;&ae;t on eallum &t;iodum westes lige&d;  &t;onne meaht &t;u ongitan &t;&ae;tte &t;&ae;s ealles nis monnum &t;onne mare l&ae;fed to bugianne  buton swelce on lytel cauertun. 
 Is &t;&ae;t &t;onne fordyslic geswinc &t;&ae;t ge winna&d; eowre woruld to &d;on &t;&ae;t ge wilnia&d; eowerne hlisan ungemetlice to br&ae;danne ofer swelcne cauerton. 
 swelce &t;&ae;t is &d;&ae;tte men bugia&d; &t;isse worulde fulneah swilce an prica for &t;&ae;t o&d;er. 
 Ac hw&ae;t rumedlices o&d;&d;e micellices o&d;&d;e weor&d;fullices h&ae;f&d; se eower gilp &t;e ge &t;&ae;r bogia&d; on &t;am fiftan d&ae;le healfum londes &amp; unlondes  mid s&ae;  mid f&ae;nne  mid ealle  swa hit is generwed. 
 To hwon wilnige ge &t;onne to ungemetlice &t;&ae;t ge eowerne naman tobr&ae;dan ofer &t;one teo&d;an d&ae;l  nu his mare nis mid s&ae;  mid f&ae;nne  mid ealle? 
 Ge&d;enca&d; eac &t;&ae;t on &d;isum lytlan pearroce &t;e we &ae;r ymb spr&ae;con bugia&d; swi&d;e manega &t;eoda &amp; swi&d;e mislica  &amp; swi&d;e ungelica &ae;g&t;er ge on spr&ae;ce ge on &t;eawum ge on eallum sidum  ealra &t;ara &t;eoda &t;e ge nu wilnia&d; swi&d;e ungemetlice &t;&ae;t ge scylon eowerne naman ofer tobr&ae;dan. 
 &t;&ae;t ge n&ae;fre gedon ne magon  for&d;on hiora spr&ae;c is tod&ae;led on twa &amp; on hundseofontig  &amp; &ae;lc &t;ara spr&ae;ca is tod&ae;led on manega &t;ioda  &amp; &t;a sint tolegena &amp; tod&ae;lda mid s&ae; &amp; mid wudum &amp; mid muntum &amp; mid fennum  &amp; mid manegum &amp; mid mislicum westenum &amp; ungeferum londum  &t;&ae;t hit fur&d;um cepemen ne gefara&d;. 
 Ac hu mag &d;&ae;r &t;onne synderlice anes rices monnes nama cuman  &t;onne &t;&ae;r mon fur&d;um &t;&ae;re burge naman ne geher&d; ne &t;&ae;re &t;eode &t;e he on hamf&ae;st bi&d;? 
 &t;y ic nat for hwilcon dysige ge girna&d; &t;&ae;t ge woldon eowerne naman tobr&ae;dan geond ealle eor&t;an; &t;&ae;t ge n&ae;fre gedon ne magon  ne fur&d;um nawer neah. 
 Hw&ae;t  &t;u wast hu micel Romana rice w&ae;s on Marcuses dagum &t;&ae;s heretogan; se w&ae;s o&d;re naman haten Tullius  &amp; &t;riddan Cicero. 
 Hw&ae;t  he cy&d;de on sumre his boca &d;&ae;tte &t;a get Romana nama ne come ofer &t;a muntas  &t;a we hata&d; Caucaseas  ne &d;a Sci&d;&d;eas &t;e on o&d;re healfe &t;ara munta bugia&d; fur&d;um &t;&ae;re burge naman ne &t;&ae;s folces ne geherdon  ac &t;a he com &ae;rest to Par&d;um  &amp; w&ae;s &t;&ae;r swi&d;e niwe. 
 ac he w&ae;s &t;eah &t;&ae;rymbutan manegum folce swi&d;e egeful. 
 Hu ne ongite ge nu hu nearo se eower hlisa bion wile &t;e ge &t;&ae;r ymb swinca&d; &amp; unrihtlice tiolia&d; to gebr&ae;danne? 
 Hw&ae;t wenstu hu micelne hlisan &amp; hu micelne weor&d;scipe an romanisc man m&ae;ge habban on &t;am lande &t;&ae;r mon fur&d;um &d;&ae;re burge naman ne geherde  ne ealles &d;&ae;s folces hlisa ne com? 
 &t;eah nu hwelc mon ungemetlice &amp; ungedafenlice wilnige &t;&ae;t he scyle his hlisan tobr&ae;dan ofer ealle eor&t;an  he ne m&ae;g &t;&ae;t for&d;bringan  for&t;am&t;e &t;ara &d;eoda &t;eawas sint swi&d;e ungelice  &amp; hiora gesetenessa swi&d;e mislica  swa &d;&ae;tte &t;&ae;t on o&d;rum lande betst lica&d; &t;&ae;tte &t;&ae;t bi&d; hwilum on &d;&ae;m o&d;rum t&ae;lwyr&d;licos&d;  &amp; eac micles wites wyr&d;e. 
 For&d;&ae;m ne m&ae;g nan mon habban gelic lof on &ae;lcum londe  for&t;on&d;e on &ae;lcum londe ne lica&d; &t;&ae;t on o&d;rum lica&d;. 
 For&d;y sceolde &ae;lc mon bion on &d;&ae;m wel gehealden &t;&ae;t he on his agnum earde licode. 
 &t;eah he nu maran wilnige  he ne m&ae;g fur&d;um &t;&ae;t for&d;bringan  for&t;&ae;m&t;e seldhwonne bi&d; &t;&ae;tte auht monegum monnum anes hw&ae;t licige. 
 for&t;y wyr&d; oft godes monnes lof alegen inne on &t;&ae;re ilcan &t;eode &t;e he on hamf&ae;st bi&d;  &amp; eac for&t;am&t;e hit oft swi&d;e sarlice gebyrede &t;urh &t;a heards&ae;l&t;a &t;ara writera &d;&ae;t hi for heora sl&ae;w&d;e &amp; for gimeleste &amp; eac for recceleste forleton unwriten &t;ara monna &d;eawas &amp; hiora d&ae;da  &t;e on hiora dagum form&ae;roste &amp; weor&d;geornuste w&ae;ron. 
 &amp; &t;eah hi nu eall hiora lif &amp; hira d&ae;da awriten h&ae;fdon  swa swa hi sceoldon gif he dohton  hu ne forealdodon &t;a gewritu &t;eah &amp; losodon &t;onecan &t;e hit w&ae;re  swa some swa &t;a writeras dydon  &amp; eac &t;a &d;e hi ymb writon. 
 &amp; eow &t;inc&d; &t;eah &t;&ae;t ge h&ae;bben ece are gif ge m&ae;gen on ealre eowerre worulde geearnigan &t;&ae;t ge h&ae;bben godne hlisan &ae;fter eowrum dagum. 
 Gif &t;u nu getelest &t;a hwila &t;isses andweardan lifes &amp; &t;isses hwilendlican wi&d; &t;&ae;s ungeendodan lifes hwila  hw&ae;t bi&d; hit &t;onne? 
 Tele nu &t;a lengu &t;&ae;re hwile &t;e &t;u &t;in eage on beprewan m&ae;ge wi&d; ten &d;usend wintra; &t;onne habba&d; &t;a hwila hw&ae;thwugu onlices  &t;eah hit lytel sie; &t;&ae;t is &t;onne &t;&ae;t heora &ae;g&t;er h&ae;f&d; ende. 
 Tele nu &t;on &t;&ae;t ten &t;usend geara  ge &t;eah &t;u ma wille  wi&d; &t;&ae;t ece &amp; &t;&ae;t ungeendode lif. 
 &t;onne ne finst &t;u &t;&ae;r nauht angelices  for&d;am &t;&ae;t ten &d;usend geara  &t;eah hit lang &d;ince  ascorta&t;  &amp; &t;&ae;s o&d;res n&ae;fre ne cym&d; nan ende. 
 For&t;&ae;m hit nis no to metanne &t;&ae;t geendodlice wi&d; &d;&ae;t ungeendodlice.
