 &t;eah &t;u nu telle from &t;ises middangeardes fruman o&d; &d;one ende  &amp; mete &t;onne &t;a gear wi&d; &t;&ae;t &d;e n&ae;nne ende n&ae;f&d;  &t;onne ne bi&d; &t;&ae;r nauht anlices. 
 Swa bi&d; eac se hlisa &t;ara forem&ae;rena monna; &t;eah he hwilum lang sie  &amp; fela geara &t;urhwunige  he bi&d; &t;eah swi&d;e scort to metanne wi&d; &d;one &t;e n&ae;fre ne geenda&d;. 
 &amp; ge ne recca&d; &d;eah hwe&d;er ge auht to gode don wi&d; &ae;negum o&t;rum &t;ingum buton wi&d; &t;am lytlan lofe &t;&ae;s folces  &amp; wi&d; &t;&ae;m scortan hlisan &t;e we &ae;r ymb spr&ae;con. 
 Earnia&d; &t;&ae;s  &amp; forsio&d; &t;a cr&ae;ftas eoweres inge&d;onces &amp; eowres andgietes &amp; eowre gescead wisnesse  &amp; woldon habban eowerra godena weorca mede &ae;t fremdra monna cwiddunge. 
 Wilniga&d; &t;&ae;rto &t;&ae;re mede &t;e ge to Gode sceolden. 
 Hw&ae;t  &t;u gehyrdest &t;&ae;tte gio dagum gelomp &t;&ae;t an swi&d;e wis mon &amp; swi&d;e rice ongan fandigan anes u&d;witan &amp; hine bismrode  for&d;&ae;m he hine swa orgellice up ahof  &amp; bodode &t;&ae;s &t;&ae;t he u&d;wita w&ae;re. 
 ne cy&d;de he hit mid n&ae;num cr&ae;ftum  ac mid leasum &amp; ofermodlicum gelpe. 
 &t;a wolde se wisa mon his fandian  hw&ae;&d;er he swa wis w&ae;re swa he self wende &t;&ae;t he w&ae;re. 
 Ongon hine &t;a hyspan  &amp; hearmcwidian. 
 &t;a geherde se u&d;wita swi&d;e ge&t;yldelice &t;&ae;s wisan monnes word sume hwile. 
 ac si&d;&d;an he his hispinge gehered h&ae;fde  &t;a scylde he ongean swi&d;e unge&t;yldelice  &t;eah he &ae;r licette &t;&ae;t he u&d;wita w&ae;re. 
 Ahsode hine &t;a eft hw&ae;&d;er him &t;uhte &t;&ae;t he u&t;wita w&ae;re &t;e n&ae;re. 
 &d;a andswarode se wisa mon him &amp; cw&ae;&d;: Ic wolde cwe&t;an &t;&ae;t &t;u u&d;wita w&ae;re  gif &t;u ge&d;yldig w&ae;re &amp; gesugian meahte. 
 Hu langsum w&ae;s him se hlisa  &t;a he &ae;r mid leasungum wilnode. 
 Hu ne forb&ae;rst he &t;a &t;&ae;rrihte for &d;&ae;m anum andwyrde. 
 Hw&ae;t forstod &t;onne &t;&ae;m betstum monnum &t;e &ae;r us w&ae;ron &t;&ae;t hi swa swi&d;e wilnodon &t;&ae;s idelan gilpes &amp; &t;&ae;s hlisan &ae;fter heora dea&t;e? 
 o&d;&d;e hw&ae;t forstent hit &t;&ae;m &t;e nu sindon? 
 &t;y w&ae;re &ae;lcum men mare &t;earf &t;&ae;t he wilnode godra cr&ae;fta &t;onne leases hlisan. 
 Hw&ae;t h&ae;f&d; he &ae;t &t;am hlisan &ae;fter &t;&ae;s lichoman gedale &amp; &t;&ae;re sawle? 
 Hu ne witon we &t;&ae;t ealle men lichomlice swelta&d;  &amp; &t;eah sio sawl bi&d; libbende ? 
 Ac sio sawl f&ae;r&d; swi&d;e friolice to hefonum  si&d;&d;an hio ontiged bi&d;  &amp; for &t;&ae;m carcerne &t;&ae;s lichoman onlesed bi&d;. 
 Heo forsih&d; &t;onne eall &d;as eor&d;lican &t;ing  &amp; f&ae;gna&d; &t;&ae;s &t;&ae;t hio mot brucan &t;&ae;s heofonlican  si&d;&d;an hio bi&d; abrogden from &d;&ae;m eor&d;lican. 
 &t;onne &t;&ae;t mod him selfum gewita bi&d; Godes willan. 
 &d;a se Wisdom &t;a &t;is spel areaht h&ae;fde  &d;a ongan he gyddian &amp; &d;us singende cw&ae;&d;: Swa hwa swa wilnige to habbenne &t;one idelan hlisan &amp; &t;one unnyttan gilp  behealde he on feower healfe his hu widgille &t;&ae;s heofones hwealfa bi&d;  &amp; hu neara &t;&ae;re eor&d;an stede is  &t;eah heo us rum &t;ince. 
 &t;onne m&ae;g hine scamigan &t;&ae;re br&ae;dinge his hlisan  for&t;am he hine ne m&ae;g fur&d;um tobr&ae;dan ofer &t;a nearwan eor&d;an ane. 
 &ae;ala  ofermodan  hwi ge wilnigen &t;&ae;t ge underlutan mid eowrum swiran &t;&ae;t dea&d;lice geoc? 
 o&d;&d;e hwi ge seon on swa idelan geswince &t;&ae;t ge woldon eowerne hlisan tobr&ae;dan ofer swa manega &t;eoda? 
 &t;eah hit nu gebyrige &t;&ae;t &d;a utemestan &d;ioda eowerne naman up ahebban  &amp; on manig &t;eodisc eow herigen  &amp; &t;eah hwa wexe mid micelre &ae;&t;elcundnesse his gebyrda  &amp; &t;eo on eallum welum &amp; eallum wlencum  ne se dea&t; &t;eah swelces ne rec&d;. 
 Ac he forsieh&d; &t;a &ae;&t;elo  &amp; &t;one rican gelice &amp; &t;one heanan ofswelg&d;  &amp; swa geemnet &t;a rican &amp; &t;a heanan. 
 Hw&ae;t synt nu &t;&ae;s foremeran &amp; &t;&ae;s wisan goldsmi&d;es ban Welondes? 
 For&t;i ic cw&ae;&d; &t;&ae;s wisan for&t;y &t;am cr&ae;ftegan ne m&ae;g n&ae;fre his cr&ae;ft losigan  ne hine mon ne m&ae;g &t;onne e&d; on him geniman &d;e mon m&ae;g &t;a sunnan awendan of hiere stede. 
 Hw&ae;r synt nu &t;&ae;s Welondes ban  o&d;&d;e hwa wat nu hw&ae;r hi w&ae;ron? 
 o&d;&d;e hw&ae;r is nu se forem&ae;ra &amp; se ar&ae;da Romwara heretoga  se w&ae;s haten Brutus  o&d;re naman Cassius? 
 O&d;&d;e se wisa &amp; f&ae;str&ae;da Cato  se w&ae;s eac Romana heretoga; se w&ae;s openlice u&d;wita. 
 Hu ne w&ae;ron &t;as gefyrn for&d;gewitene? 
 &amp; nan mon nat hw&ae;r hi nu sint. 
 Hw&ae;t is heora nu to lafe  butan se lytla hlisa &amp; se nama mid feaum stafum awriten? 
 &amp; &t;&ae;t git wyrse is  &t;&ae;t we witon manige forem&ae;re &amp; gemyndwyr&t;e weras for&d;gewitene &t;e swi&d;e feawa manna a ongit. 
 Ac manige licgga&d; deade mid ealle forgitene  &t;&ae;t se hlisa hie fur&d;um cu&t;e ne gede&d;. 
 &t;eah ge nu wenen &amp; wilnian &t;&ae;t ge lange libban scylan her on worulde  hw&ae;t bi&d; eow &t;onne &t;y bet? 
 Hu ne cym&d; se dea&d; &t;eah  &t;eah he late cume  &amp; ade&d; eow of &d;isse worulde? 
 &amp; hw&ae;t forstent eow &t;onne se gilp  huru &t;am &t;e se &ae;fterra dea&d; gegrip&d; &amp; on ecnesse geh&ae;f&d;? 
 &d;a se Wisdom &t;a &t;is leo&d; asungen h&ae;fde  &d;a ongan he spillian &amp; &d;us cw&ae;&d;: Ne wen &d;u no &t;&ae;t ic to anwillice winne wi&d; &d;a wyrd. 
 for&d;&ae;m ic hit no self nauht ne ondr&ae;de  for &t;am hit oft gebyre&d; &t;&ae;t sio lease wyrd nau&t;er ne m&ae;g &t;&ae;m men don ne fultum ne eac n&ae;nne dem. 
 For&t;am hio nis nanes lofes wyr&d;e  for&t;am hio hire self gecy&d; &t;&ae;t heo nanwuht ne bi&d;; ac heo onwrih&d; hire &ae;welm &t;onne heo geo&t;ena&d; hiore &t;eawas. 
 Ic wene &d;eah &t;&ae;t &d;u ne forstande nu get hw&ae;t ic &t;e to cwe&d;e. 
 for&t;am hit is wundorlic &t;&ae;t ic secgan wille  &amp; ic hit m&ae;g unea&d;e mid wordum areccan swa swa ic wolde; &t;&ae;t is &d;&ae;t ic wat &d;&ae;tte sio wi&d;erwearde wyrd bi&d; &ae;lcum men nytwyr&d;re &t;onne sio orsorge. 
 For&d;&ae;m seo orsorge simle lih&d; &amp; licet &t;&ae;t mon scyle wenan &t;&ae;t hio is sio so&d;e ges&ae;l&d;; ac sio wi&d;erwearde is sio so&d;e ges&ae;l&t;  &t;eah hw&ae;m swa ne &t;ynce  for&d;&ae;m heo is f&ae;str&ae;d &amp; geh&ae;t simle &t;&ae;tte so&d; bi&d;. 
 Sio o&d;ru is leas &amp; beswic&d; ealle hire geferan  for&d;&ae;m hio hit gecy&d; self mid hire hwurfulnesse &t;&ae;t hio bi&d; swi&d;e wancol; ac sio wi&d;erwearde gebet &amp; gel&ae;re&d; &ae;lcne &t;ara &t;e hio hi to ge&t;iet. 
 Sio o&d;ru gebin&d; &ae;lc &d;ara moda &d;e hire bryc&d; mid &d;&ae;re hiwunga &t;e hio licet &t;&ae;t hio sie god. 
 sio wi&d;erwearde &t;onne onbin&d; &amp; gefreo&d; &ae;lc &t;ara &t;e hio to ge&d;iet  mid &d;&ae;m &t;e hio him geopena&d; hu tiedre &t;&ae;s andweardan ges&ae;l&d;a sint. 
 Ac seo orsorhnes g&ae;&d; scyrm&ae;lum sw&ae;&d;er windes pyf; sio wi&d;erweardnes &t;onne bi&d; simle unt&ae;lu &amp; w&ae;ru  ascirped mid &t;&ae;re styringe hire agenre frecennesse. 
 Ac sio lease ges&ae;l&d; hio tih&d; on last neadinga &t;a &t;e hiere to ge&d;eoda&d; from &t;&ae;m so&d;um ges&ae;l&d;um mid hiere oliccunge. 
 sio wi&d;erweardnes &t;onne ful oft ealle &d;a &d;e hiere under&t;eodde bio&d; neadinga getyh&d; to &d;am so&d;um ges&ae;l&d;um  swa swa mid angle fisc gefangen bi&d;. 
 &d;inc&d; &d;e nu &t;&ae;t lytel gestreon &amp; lytel eaca &t;inra ges&ae;l&d;a &t;&ae;tte &d;eos re&d;e &amp; &t;ios egeslice wi&d;erweardnes &t;e bring&d;? 
 &t;&ae;t is &t;&ae;t hio swi&d;e hra&d;e &d;a mod &t;e geopena&d; &t;inra getreowra freonda &amp; eac &t;inra fionda  &t;&ae;t &t;u hi miht swi&d;e sweotole tocnawan? 
 Ac &t;&ae;s leasan ges&ae;l&d;a  &t;onne hi &d;e from gewita&d;  &t;onne nima&d; hi hiora men mid him  &amp; l&ae;ta&d; &t;ine feawan getreowan mid &d;e. 
 Hu woldes &d;u nu gebycggan &t;a &t;u ges&ae;legost w&ae;re &amp; &t;e &t;uhte &t;&ae;t seo wyrd swi&d;ost on &t;inne willan wode? 
 mid hu micelan feo woldest &t;u &t;a habban geboht &t;&ae;t &d;u switole mihtest tocnawan &t;ine frind &amp; &d;ine fynd? 
 Ic wat &d;eah &t;&ae;t &d;u hit woldest habban mid miclan feo geboht &t;&ae;t &d;u hi cu&d;est wel toscadan. 
 &t;eah &t;e nu &t;ince &t;&ae;t &d;u deorwyr&d;e feoh forloren habbe  &t;u h&ae;fst &t;eah micle diorwyr&d;re mid geboht; &t;&ae;t sint getreowe friend; &t;a &d;u miht nu tocnawan  &amp; wast hw&ae;t &t;u hiora h&ae;fst. 
 Hw&ae;t. &t;&ae;t is &t;&ae;t eallra deorweor&d;oste fioh. 
 &d;a se Wisdom &t;a &d;is spell as&ae;d h&ae;fde  &t;a ongan he giddigan &amp; &t;us singende cw&ae;&d;: An sceppend is buton &ae;lcum tweon  &amp; se is eac wealdend heofones &amp; eor&d;an &amp; ealra gesceafta  gesewenlicra &amp; eac ungesewenlicra; &t;&ae;t is God &ae;lmihtig. 
 &t;am &d;eowia&d; ealle &t;a &t;e &d;eowia&d;  ge &d;a &t;e cunnon ge &t;a &t;e ne cunnon  ge &t;a &d;e hit witon &t;&ae;t hie him &d;eowia&d; ge &t;a &d;e hit nyton. 
 Se ilca gesette unawendendlicne sido &amp; &t;eawas &amp; eac gecyndelice sibbe eallum his gesceaftum  &d;a &t;a he wolde  &amp; swa swa he wolde  &amp; swa lange swa he wolde; &t;a nu sculon standan to worulde. 
 &d;ara unstillena gesceafta styring ne m&ae;g no weor&d;an gestilled  ne eac onwend of &t;am ryne &amp; of &t;&ae;re endebyrdnesse &t;e him geset is. 
 ac se anwealda h&ae;f&d; ealle his gesceafta swa mid his bridle befangene &amp; getogene &amp; gemanode swa &t;&ae;t hi nau&t;er ne gestillan ne moton  ne eac swi&d;or styrian &t;onne he him &t;&ae;t gerum his wealdle&d;eres to forl&ae;t. 
 Swa h&ae;f&d; se &ae;lmihtiga God gehea&d;orade ealle his gescefta mid his anwealde &t;&ae;t heora &ae;lc win&d; wi&d; o&d;er  &amp; &t;eah wr&ae;&d;e&d; o&d;er  &t;&ae;t hie ne moton toslupan  ac bio&d; gehwerfde eft to &t;am ilcan ryne &t;e hie &ae;r urnon  &amp; swa weor&d;a&d; eft geedniwade. 
 Swa hi hit fagia&d; &t;&ae;t &t;a wi&d;erweardan gesceafta &ae;g&d;er ge hie betwux him winna&d;  ge eac f&ae;ste sibbe betwux him healda&d;. 
 Swa nu fyr de&d;  &amp; w&ae;ter &amp; s&ae; &amp; eor&d;e  &amp; manega o&d;ra gesceafta &t;e beo&d; a swa unge&d;w&ae;ra betwux him swa swa hi beo&d;. 
 &amp; &t;eah hi beo&d; swa ge&t;w&ae;ra &t;&ae;tte no &t;&ae;t an &t;&ae;t hi magon geferan beon  ac &t;y fur&d;or &t;&ae;t heora fur&d;um nan buton o&d;rum beon ne m&ae;g. 
 Ac a sceal &t;&ae;t wi&d;erwearde &t;&ae;t o&d;er wi&d;erwearde gemetgian. 
 Swa nu h&ae;f&d; se &ae;lmihtega God swi&d;e gesceadwislice &amp; swi&d;e limplice geset &t;&ae;t gewrixle eallum his gesceaftum. 
 Swa nu lencten &amp; h&ae;rfest: on lencten hit grew&d;  &amp; on h&ae;rfest hit wealwa&d;. 
 &amp; eft sumer &amp; winter: on sumera hit bi&d; wearm  &amp; on wintra ceald. 
 Swa eac sio sunne bring&d; leohte dagas  &amp; se mona liht on niht  &t;urh &t;&ae;s ilcan Godes miht. 
 Se ilca forwyrn&d; &t;&ae;r&ae; s&ae; &t;&ae;t heo ne mot &t;one &t;eorscwold oferst&ae;ppan &t;&ae;re eor&t;an. 
 Ac he h&ae;f&d; heora mearce swa gesette &t;&ae;t hie ne mot heore mearce gebr&ae;dan ofer &t;a stillan eor&t;an. 
 Mid &t;am ilcan gerece is gereaht swi&d;e anlic gewrixle &t;&ae;s flodes &amp; &t;&ae;s ebban. 
 &t;a gesetennesse &t;a he l&ae;t standan &t;a hwile &t;e he wile. 
 Ac &t;onne &ae;r &t;e he &t;&ae;t gewealdle&d;er forl&ae;t &t;ara bridla &t;e he &d;a gesceafta nu mid gebridlode h&ae;f&d;: &t;&ae;t is seo wi&d;erweardnes &t;e we &ae;r ymbe spr&ae;con: gif he &t;a l&ae;t toslupan  &t;onne forl&ae;ta&d; hi &t;a sibbe &d;e hi nu healda&d;  &amp; win&d; heora &ae;lc on o&d;er &ae;fter his agenum willan  &amp; forl&ae;ta&d; heora geferr&ae;denne  &amp; fordo&d; ealne &d;ysne middaneard  &amp; weor&d;a&d; him selfe to nauhte. 
 Se ilca God gefeg&d; mid freondr&ae;denne folc tog&ae;dere  &amp; sinhigscipas gesamna&d; mid cl&ae;nlicre lufe. 
 He geg&ae;dera&d; frind &amp; geferan &t;&ae;t hie getreowlice heora sibbe &amp; heora freondr&ae;denne healda&d;. 
 Eala &t;&ae;tte &t;is moncyn w&ae;re ges&ae;lig  gif heora mod w&ae;re swa riht &amp; swa gesta&d;elod &amp; swa geendebyrd swa swa &t;a o&d;re gesceafta sindon. 
 Her enda&d; nu seo &ae;ftre froferboc Boeties  &amp; ongin&d; sio &t;ridde. 
 Se Boetius w&ae;s o&d;re naman haten Seuerinus; se w&ae;s heretoga Romana. 
 &d;a se Wisdom &t;a &d;is lio&d; asungen h&ae;fde  &t;a h&ae;fde he me gebundenne mid &t;&ae;re wynsumnesse his sanges  &t;&ae;t ic his w&ae;s swi&d;e wafiende &amp; swi&d;e lustb&ae;re hine to geheranne mid innewearde mode  &amp; &t;a fulhr&ae;&d;e &d;&ae;s ic cleopode to him &amp; &t;us cw&ae;&d;: Eala  Wisdom  &t;u &d;e eart sio hehste frofer ealra werigra moda; hu &t;u me h&ae;fst afrefredne &ae;g&t;er ge mid &t;inre smealican spr&ae;ce  ge mid &t;inre wynsumnesse &t;ines sanges. 
 To &t;&ae;m &t;u me h&ae;fst nu aretne &amp; ofercumene mid &t;inre gesceadwisnesse  &t;&ae;t me nu &d;inc&d; &d;&ae;tte no &t;&ae;t an &t;&ae;t ic &d;as unwyrd ar&ae;fnan m&ae;g &d;e me on becumen is  ac &t;eah me giet mare frecenes on becume  ne cwi&d;e ic n&ae;fre ma &t;&ae;t hit butan gewyrhtum sie. 
 for&d;&ae;m ic wat &t;&ae;t ic maran &amp; hefigran wyr&d;e w&ae;re. 
 Ac ic wolde ymbe &t;one l&ae;cedom &t;ara &t;inra lara hwene mare geheran. 
 &t;eah &t;u nu hwene &ae;r s&ae;de &t;&ae;t &t;u wende &t;&ae;t hi woldon me swi&d;e bitere &t;incan  ne ondr&ae;de ic hi me nu nauht. 
 ac ic heora eom swi&d;e gifre &ae;g&d;er ge to geheranne ge eac to gehealdenne  &amp; &t;e swi&d;e georne bidde &t;&ae;t &t;u hi me gel&ae;ste  swa swa &d;u me nu lytle &ae;r gehete. 
 &t;a cw&ae;&d; se Wisdom: Ic ongeat sona &t;a &d;u swa wel geswugodes &amp; swa lustlice geherdest mina lara  &t;&ae;t &t;u woldest mid innewearde mode hi ongiton &amp; smeagean. 
 For&d;&ae;m ic geanbidode swi&d;e wel o&t; ic wisse hw&ae;t &t;u woldest &amp; hu &t;u hit understandan woldest  &amp; eac &t;y fur&d;ur ic tiolode swi&d;e geornfullice &t;&ae;t &t;u hit forstandan meahte. 
 Ac ic &t;e nu wille secgan hwilc se l&ae;cecr&ae;ft is minre lare &t;e &t;u me nu bitst. 
 He is swi&d;e biter on mu&d;e  &amp; he &t;e tir&d; on &d;a &t;rotan &t;onne &d;u his &ae;rast fandast; ac he wereda&d; si&d;&d;an he innan bi&d; &amp; swi&d;e li&d;e on &d;&ae;m inno&d;e  &amp; swi&d;e swi&d;e swete to bealcetenne. 
 Ac &t;&ae;r &d;u ongeate hwider ic &d;e nu tiohige to l&ae;denne  ic wat &d;&ae;t &t;u woldest swi&d;e georne &t;ider fundian &amp; swi&d;e swi&d;lice beon on&ae;led mid &t;&ae;re gitsunge  for&t;am ic geherde &t;&ae;t &d;u &ae;r s&ae;dest &t;&ae;t &t;u swi&d;e geornfull w&ae;re hit to gehyranne. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; &t;&ae;t Mod: Hwider wilt &d;u me nu swi&d;ost l&ae;dan? 
 &d;a andwyrde sio Gesceadwisnes &amp; cw&ae;&d;: To &t;&ae;m so&d;um ges&ae;l&d;um ic tiohige &d;&ae;t ic &t;e l&ae;de  &t;&ae;r &t;in mod oft ymb r&ae;swe&d; &amp; eac m&ae;t. 
 &amp; &t;u ne meahtes gyt ful rihtne weg aredian to &d;&ae;m so&d;um gesael&d;um  for&d;on &t;in mod w&ae;s abisgod mid &d;&ae;re ansene &t;issa leasena ges&ae;l&d;a. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; &t;&ae;t Mod: Ic &t;e healsige &t;&ae;t &t;u me o&d;ewe butan &ae;lcum tweon hw&ae;t sio so&d;e ges&ae;l&d; sie. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; sio Gesceadwisnes: Ic wille forlustlice for &d;inum lufum. 
 ac ic sceal be sumre bysene sume anlicnesse &t;&ae;re wisan &d;e get&ae;can  o&d; &d;e &t;&ae;t &t;ing cu&d;re sie  to &d;&ae;m &t;&ae;t &t;u &t;a bisne sweotole gesceawige  &amp; &t;onne be &t;&ae;re anlicnesse &t;ara so&d;ena ges&ae;l&t;a &d;u m&ae;ge ongitan &t;a so&d;an ges&ae;l&d;a  &amp; forl&ae;tan &t;&ae;tte him wi&d;erweard bi&d;; &t;&ae;t sint &t;a leasan gesael&d;a. 
 &amp; &t;onne mid ealles modes geornfullan inge&d;once higie &t;&ae;t &t;u m&ae;ge becuman to &t;am ges&ae;l&d;um &t;e ece &t;urhwunia&d;. 
 &d;a se Wisdom &d;a &d;is spell ar&ae;d h&ae;fde  &t;a ongan he eft giddian  &amp; &d;us cw&ae;&d;: Swa hwa swa wille sawan westmb&ae;re land  atio &ae;rest of &d;a &t;ornas &amp; &t;a fyrsas &amp; &t;&ae;t fearn &amp; ealle &t;a weod &t;e he gesio &t;&ae;t &t;am &ae;cerum derigen  &t;&ae;t se hw&ae;te m&ae;ge &t;y bet weaxan. 
 Eac is &d;eos bisen to ge&d;encenne  &t;&ae;t is &t;&ae;t &ae;lcum men &t;inc&d; huniges biobread &t;y weorodra gif he hwene &ae;r biteres onbirig&d;. 
 &amp; eft smylte weder bi&d; &t;y &t;ancwyr&d;re gif hit hwene &ae;r bi&d; stearce stormas &amp; nor&d;anwindas &amp; micle renas &amp; snawas. 
 &amp; &t;ancwyr&d;re bi&d; eac &t;as d&ae;ges leoht for &t;&ae;re egeslican &t;iostro &t;&ae;re nihte  &t;onne hit w&ae;re gif nan niht n&ae;re. 
 Swa bi&d; eac micle &t;e winsumre sio so&d;e ges&ae;l&d; to habbenne efter &t;am eorm&d;um &t;isses andweardan lifes. 
 &amp; eac micle &d;i e&d; &t;u miht &t;a so&d;an ges&ae;l&d;a gecnawan &amp; to hiora cy&d;&d;e becuman  gif &d;u &ae;rest awyrtwalast of &t;inum mode &d;a leasan ges&ae;l&d;a  &amp; hi of atiht o&d; &d;one grund. 
 Si&d;&d;an &t;u hi &t;onne gecnawan miht  &d;onne wat ic &t;&ae;t &d;u ne wilnast nanes o&d;res &t;inges ofer &t;a. 
 &t;a he &t;a &t;is leo&d; asungen h&ae;fde  &t;a forlet he &t;one sang  &amp; geswugode ane hwile  &amp; ongann smealice &t;encan on his modes inge&t;ance  &amp; &d;a cw&ae;&d;: &ae;lc dea&d;lic man swenc&d; hine selfne mid mistlicum &amp; m&ae;nigfealdum ymbhogum  &amp; &t;eah wilnia&d; ealle &d;urh mislice pa&d;as cuman to anum ende. 
 &t;&ae;t is &t;&ae;t hi wilnia&d; &t;urh ungelice earnunga cuman to anre eadignesse; &t;&ae;t is &t;onne God; se is fruma &amp; ende &ae;lces goodes  &amp; he is sio hehste ges&ae;l&d;. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; &d;&ae;t Mod: &d;&ae;t me &d;inc&d; sie &t;&ae;t hehste good  &t;&ae;tte mon ne &d;urfe nanes o&d;res godes  ne eac ne recce ofer &t;&ae;t  si&d;&d;an he &t;&ae;t h&ae;bbe &t;&ae;t is hrof eallra o&d;erra gooda. 
 for&t;am hit eall o&d;ru god utan befeh&d;  &amp; eall oninnan him h&ae;f&d;. 
 N&ae;re hit no &t;&ae;t hehste god gif him &ae;nig butan w&ae;re  for&t;&ae;m hit &t;onne h&ae;fde to wilnian ne sumes goodes &t;e hit self n&ae;fde. 
 &t;a andswarode sio Gesceadwisnes &amp; cw&ae;&d;: &d;&ae;t is swi&d;e sweotol &t;&ae;t &d;&ae;t is sio hehste ges&ae;l&d;  for&d;&ae;m hit is &ae;g&d;er ge hrof ge flor ealles goodes. 
 Hw&ae;t is &d;&ae;t &t;onne buton sio seleste ges&ae;l&d;  &t;e &d;a o&d;ra ges&ae;l&d;a ealla oninnan him gegadera&d;  &amp; hi utan ymbh&ae;f&d;  &amp; oninnan him gehelt  &amp; him nanes ne bi&d; wana  ne he nanes ned&t;earfe n&ae;f&d;  ac hi cuma&d; eall of him  &amp; eft eall to him  swa swa eall w&ae;tru cuma&d; of &d;&ae;re s&ae;  &amp; eft cuma&d; ealle to &d;&ae;re s&ae;? 
 Nis nan to &d;&ae;s lytel &ae;wylm &t;&ae;t he &t;a s&ae; ne gesece; &amp; eft of &d;&ae;re s&ae; he gelent in on &t;a eor&d;an  &amp; swa he bi&d; smugende geond &t;a eor&d;an o&d; he eft cym&d; to &d;&ae;m ilcan &ae;welme &t;e he &ae;r ut fleow  &amp; swa eft to &t;&ae;re s&ae;. 
 &d;is is nu bysen &t;ara so&t;ena ges&ae;l&d;a; &t;ara wilnia&d; ealle dea&d;lice men to begitanne  &t;eah hi &d;urh mislice wegas &d;encan to cumanne. 
 For&t;am &ae;ghwelc man h&ae;f&d; gecyndelic god on him selfum  for&t;am &ae;lc mod wilna&d; so&d;es godes to begitanne; ac hit bi&d; amerred mid &t;am l&ae;num godum  for&d;&ae;m hit bi&d; ofd&ae;lre &d;&ae;rto. 
 For&d;am sume menn wena&d; &t;&ae;t &t;&ae;t se seo seleste ges&ae;l&d; &t;&ae;t mon seo swa welig &t;&ae;t he nanes &d;inges maran ne &d;urfe  &amp; wilnia&d; hiora woruld &ae;fter &t;am. 
 Sume men wena&d; &t;&ae;t &t;&ae;t sie &t;&ae;t hehte god &t;&ae;t he sie his geferum his geferena weor&d;ost  &amp; eallon maegene &d;&ae;s tiola&d;. 
 Sume wena&d; &t;&ae;t &d;&ae;t hehste good sie on &t;am hehstan anwalde; &t;a wilnia&d; o&d;er twega  o&d;&d;e him selfe ricsian  o&d;&d;e hi to &d;&ae;ra ricena freondscipe ge&t;iodan. 
 Sume &t;onne tiohia&d; &t;&ae;t &d;&ae;t betst sie &t;&ae;t mon sie forem&ae;re &amp; widm&ae;re  &amp; h&ae;bbe godne hlisan; tilia&d; &t;onne &t;&ae;s &ae;g&d;er ge on sibbe ge on gewinne. 
 Manege tella&d; &t;&ae;t to m&ae;stum goode &amp; to m&ae;stere ges&ae;l&d;e &t;&ae;t mon sie simle bli&d;e on &t;is andweardan life  &amp; fulga eallum his lustum. 
 Sume &t;onne &t;a &t;e &d;as welan wilnia&d;  hi his wilnia&d; for&t;am &t;&ae;t hi woldean &d;y maran anweald habban  &t;&ae;t he mihte &t;y orsorglicor &d;issa woruldlusta brucan  &amp; eac &t;as welan. 
 Manega sint &t;ara &t;e for&t;i wilnia&d; anwaldes &t;e hie woldon orm&ae;te feoh gegaderian; o&d;&d;e eft &t;one hlisan heora naman hi wilnia&d; &t;&ae;t hi gebr&ae;dan. 
 On swilcum &amp; on o&d;rum swelcum l&ae;num &amp; hreosendum weor&d;scipum &ae;lces mennisces modes inge&t;anc bi&d; geswenced mid &d;&ae;re geornfulnesse &amp; mid &d;&ae;re tiluncga. 
 wen&d; &t;onne &t;&ae;t hit h&ae;bbe sum healic god gestryned &t;onne hit h&ae;f&d; genumen &t;&ae;s folces olecunga; &amp; me &t;inc&d; &t;&ae;t hit h&ae;bbe geboht sume swi&d;e leaslice m&ae;r&d;e. 
 Sume tilia&d; mid micelre geornfulnesse wifa  for&d;&ae;m &t;&ae;t he &t;urh &d;&ae;t m&ae;ge m&ae;st bearna begitan  &amp; eac wynsumlice libban. 
 &d;a getriewan friend &t;onne ic secgge sie &d;&ae;t deorwyr&d;este &d;ing ealra &t;issa weoruldges&ae;l&d;a. 
 &t;a ne sint fur&d;um to woruldgodum to tellanne  ac to godcundum; for&t;am seo lease wyrd hi na for&d; ne bring&d;  ac se God &t;e hi gecyndelice gesceop to gemagum. 
 For&t;am&d;e &ae;lces o&d;res &t;inges on &t;isse worulde mon wilna&d;  o&d;&d;e for&t;am&t;e he m&ae;g &t;urh &t;&ae;t to anwealde cuman  o&d;&d;e to sumum woruldluste  butan &t;&ae;s getreowan freondes. 
 &t;one mon lufa&d; hwilum for lufum &amp; for triowum  &t;eah he him nanra o&d;erra l&ae;na ne wene. 
 &t;&ae;t gecynd gef&ae;g&d; &amp; gelim&d; &t;a friend togadre mid swi&d;e untodeledlicre lufe. 
 Ac mid &t;issum woruldges&ae;l&d;um &amp; mid &t;is andweardan welan mon wyrc&d; oftor fiond &d;onne freond. 
 Be &d;isan &amp; be m&ae;negum &t;illicum m&ae;g beon eallum monnum cu&d; &d;&ae;tte ealle &t;a licumlican good bio&d; forcu&d;ran &d;onne &d;&ae;re sawle cr&ae;ftas. 
 Hw&ae;t  we wena&d; &d;&ae;t mon bio &t;y strencra &t;e he bi&d; micel on his lichoman. 
 Seo f&ae;gernes &d;onne &amp; sio hw&ae;tnes &t;aes lichoman geblissa&d; &d;one mon &amp; aret  &amp; sio h&ae;lo hine gede&d; lus&d;b&ae;rne. 
 On eallum &d;issum licumlicum ges&ae;lignessum men seca&d; anfealde eadignesse &d;&ae;s &d;e him &d;inc&d;  for&t;am &t;e &ae;ghwelc man swa hw&ae;t swa he ofer ealle o&d;re &t;ing swi&d;ost lufa&d;  &t;&ae;t he teohha&d; &t;&ae;t him sie betst  &amp; &t;&ae;t bi&d; his hehste god. 
 &t;onne he &t;&ae;t &d;onne begiten h&ae;f&d;  &t;onne tihha&d; he &t;&ae;t he m&ae;ge beon swi&d;e ges&ae;lig. 
 Ne onsace ic nauht &t;&ae;t &d;a ges&ae;l&d;a &amp; seo eadignes sie &t;&ae;t hehste god &t;ises andweardan lifes; for&t;am &d;e &ae;ghwilc mon tiohha&d; &t;&ae;t &t;&ae;t &d;ing betst sie &t;&ae;t he swi&d;ust ofer o&d;re &t;ing lufa&d;. 
 &amp; &t;onne he tiohha&d; &t;&ae;t he sie swi&d;e ges&ae;lig gif he &t;&ae;t begitan m&ae;g &d;&ae;t he &t;onne swi&t;ust willna&d;. 
 Hu ne is &t;&ae;t nu genoh openlice geeowad &t;ara leasena ges&ae;l&d;a anlicnes &t;&ae;t is &t;onne &ae;hta &amp; weor&d;scipe &amp; anweald &amp; gielp &amp; woruldlust? 
 Be &t;am woruldluste Epeccurus se u&d;wita s&ae;de  &t;a he ymb ealle &t;as o&d;ra ges&ae;l&d;a smeade &t;e we &ae;r nemdon. 
 &t;a s&ae;de he &t;&ae;t se lust w&ae;re &t;&ae;t hehste good  for&d;&ae;m ealle &t;a o&d;ru good &t;e we &ae;r nemdon olecca&d; &t;am mode &amp; hit reta&d;; se lust &d;onne ana olec&d; &d;&ae;m lichoman anum swi&d;ost. 
 Ac we willa&d; nu giet sprecan ymbe manna gecynd &amp; ymbe heora tilunga. 
 &t;a nu &t;eah heora mod &amp; heora gecynd sie adimmad  &amp; hi sien on &t;&ae;t ofd&ae;le asigen to yfele &amp; &t;ider healde  &t;eah hi wilnia&d; &t;&ae;s &d;e hi cunnon &amp; magon &t;&ae;s hehstan godes. 
 Swa swa oferdruncen man wat &t;&ae;t he sceolde to his huse &amp; to his r&ae;ste  &amp; ne m&ae;g &t;eah &d;ider aredian  swa bi&d; eac &t;am mode &t;onne hit bi&d; ahefigad mid &d;&ae;m ymhogum &t;isse worulde. 
 hit bi&d; mid &t;am hwilum oferdrenced &amp; gedwelod to &t;am &t;&ae;t hit ne m&ae;ge full rihte aredian to gode. 
 Ne &t;inc&d; &t;eah &t;&ae;m monnum &t;&ae;t hi auht mearrigen &t;e &t;&ae;s wilnia&d; to begitanne  &t;&ae;t hi maran ne &d;urfon tilian; ac wena&d; &t;&ae;t hi m&ae;gen ealle &t;as good gegadrian tog&ae;dere  &t;&ae;tte nan butan &t;&ae;re gesomnunga ne sie. 
 Nyton &t;onne nan herre good &t;onne eallra &t;ara deorwyr&d;estena &d;inga gegadrunga to hiora anwealde &d;&ae;t he nanes &d;inges buton &t;&ae;m ne &t;yrfe. 
 Ac &d;&ae;t nis nan man &t;&ae;tte sumes eacan ne &d;yrfe  buton Gode anum; he h&ae;f&d; on his agenum genog  ne &d;earf he nanes &t;inges buton &d;&ae;s &t;e he on him selfum h&ae;f&d;. 
 Wenst &t;u nu &t;&ae;t &d;a dysegian &t;e wena&d; &t;&ae;tte &t;&ae;t &d;ing sie &ae;lces weor&d;scipes betst wyr&d;e &t;&ae;tte hi medemast ongiton magon? 
 Nese  nese. 
 Ic wat &t;&ae;t hit nis no to forseone. 
 Hu m&ae;g &t;&ae;t yfel beon &t;&ae;tte &ae;lces monnes inge&t;anc wen&d; &t;&ae;tte good sie  &amp; &ae;fter higa&d;  &amp; wilna&d; to begitanne? 
 Nese  nis hit na yfel; &t;&ae;t is &t;&ae;t hehste good. 
 Hwi nis nu anweald to tellanne to sumum &t;ara hehstena goda &t;isses anweardan lifes? 
 Hw&ae;&d;er &t;&ae;t nu sie to talianne waclic &amp; unnyt &d;&ae;tte nytwyr&d;ost is eallra &t;issa woruld&t;inga  &t;&ae;t is anweald? 
 Hw&ae;&d;er nu good hlisa &amp; forem&ae;rnes seo for nauht to tellenne? 
 Nese  nese; nis hit nan cyn &t;&ae;t mon &d;&ae;t for nauht telle  for&d;&ae;m&d;e &ae;lc mon wen&d; &t;&ae;t &t;&ae;t betst sie &t;&ae;t he swi&d;ost lufa&d;. 
 Hu ne witon we &t;&ae;t nan nearones ne nan earfo&d;u ne nan unrotnes ne nan sar ne nan hefignes nis nan ges&ae;l&d;? 
 Hw&ae;t &t;urfon we nu ma ymbe &t;a ges&ae;l&d;a sprecan? 
 Hu ne wat &ae;lc mon hw&ae;t &d;a bio&d;  &amp; eac wat &t;&ae;t hi bio&d; &t;&ae;t hehste good? 
 &amp; &t;eah sec&d; fulneah &ae;lc mon on swi&d;e lytlum &t;ingum &d;a selestan ges&ae;l&d;a; for&t;&ae;m he wen&d; &t;&ae;t he hi &t;onne ealle h&ae;bbe  gif he h&ae;f&d; &t;&ae;t &t;&ae;t he &t;onne swi&d;ost wilna&d; to begitanne. 
 &t;&ae;t is &d;onne &t;&ae;t hi swi&d;ost wilnia&d; to begitanne: wela &amp; weor&d;scipe &amp; rice &amp; &t;isse worulde wuldor &amp; gilp &amp; woruldlust. 
 &D;isses ealles hi wilnia&d;  for&t;am&t;e hi wena&d; &t;&ae;t hie &t;urh &t;a &t;ing scylon begitan &t;&ae;t him ne seo nanes willan wana  na&d;er ne weor&d;scipes ne anwealdes ne forem&ae;rnesse ne blisse. 
 &d;&ae;s ealles hi wilnia&d;  &amp; wel do&t; &t;&ae;t hi &t;&ae;s wilnia&d;  &t;eah hi mistlice his wilnigen. 
 Be &t;am &t;ingum mon m&ae;g sweotole ongitan &t;&ae;t &ae;lc mon &t;&ae;s wilna&d; &t;&ae;t he m&ae;ge &t;&ae;t hehste god begitan &t;&ae;r hi hit gecnawan meahtan  o&d;&d;e on riht secan cu&d;en. 
 ac hi hit ne seca&d; on &t;one rihtestan weg; hit nis on &t;isse worulde. 
 &d;a se Wisdom &t;a &d;is spel as&ae;d h&ae;fde  &t;a ongan he eft singan &amp; &t;us cw&ae;&d;: Ic wille nu mid giddum gecy&d;an hu wundorlice Drihten welt eallra gesceafta mid &t;am bridlum his anwealdes  &amp; mid hwilcere endebyrdnesse he gesta&d;ola&d; &amp; gemetga&d; ealle gesceafta. 
 &amp; hu he hi h&ae;f&d; gehea&d;orade &amp; geh&ae;fte mid his unanbindendlicum racentum  &t;&ae;t &ae;lc gesceaft bi&d; healdon locen wi&d; hire gecynde  &t;&ae;re gecynde &t;e heo to gesceapen wes  buton monnum &amp; sumum englum; &t;a weor&d;a&d; hwilum of hiora gecynde. 
 Hw&ae;t  seo leo  &t;eah hio wel tam se  &amp; f&ae;ste racentan habbe &amp; hire magister swi&d;e lufige &amp; eac ondr&ae;de  gif hit &ae;fre gebyre&d; &t;&ae;t heo blodes onbirig&d;  heo forgit sona hire niwan taman  &amp; gemon&d; &t;&ae;s wildan gewunan hire eldrana. 
 Ongin&d; &t;onne ryn &amp; hire racentan brecan  &amp; abit &ae;rest hire ladteow  &amp; si&d;&d;an &ae;ghw&ae;t &t;&ae;s &t;e heo gefon m&ae;g  ge monna ge neata. 
 Swa do&d; eac wudufuglas; &t;eah hi beon wel atemede  gif hi on &t;am wuda weor&d;a&d;  hi forseo&d; heora lareowas &amp; wunia&d; on heora gecynde. 
 &t;eah heora lareowas him &t;onne biodan &t;a ilcan mettas &t;e hi &ae;r tame mid gewenedon  &d;onne ne recca&d; hi &t;ara metta  gif hi &t;&ae;s wuda benugon; ac &t;inc&d; him wynsumre &t;&ae;t him se weald oncwe&d;e &amp; hi gehiran o&d;erra fugla stemne. 
 Swa bi&d; eac &t;am treowum &t;e him gecynde bi&d; up heah to standanne. 
 &t;eah &t;u teo hwelcne boh ofdune to &t;&ae;re eor&d;an swelce &t;u began m&ae;ge  swa &t;u hine al&ae;tst  swa sprinc&d; he up &amp; wriga&d; wi&d; his gecyndes. 
 Swa de&d; eac seo sunne; &t;eah heo ofer midne d&ae;g onsige &amp; lute to &t;&ae;re eor&t;an  eft heo sec&d; hire gecynde &amp; stig&d; on &t;a d&ae;glan wegas wi&d; hire upryn&ae;s  &amp; swa hie ufor &amp; ufor o&d;&d;e hio cym&d; swa up swa hire yfemest gecynde bi&d;. 
 Swa de&d; &ae;lc gesceaft; wriga&d; wi&d; his gecyndes  &amp; gefagen bi&d; gif hit &ae;fre to cuman m&ae;g. 
 Nis nan gesceaft gesceapen &d;ara &t;e ne wilnige &t;&ae;t hit &t;ider cuman m&ae;ge &t;onan &t;e hit &ae;r com  &t;&ae;t is to r&ae;ste &amp; to orsorgnesse. 
 Seo r&ae;st is mid Gode  &amp; &t;&ae;t is God. 
 Ac &ae;lc gesceaft hwearfa&d; on hire selfre swa swa hweol; &amp; to &t;am heo swa hwearfa&d; &t;&ae;t heo eft cume &t;&ae;r heo &ae;r w&ae;s  &amp; beo &t;&ae;t ilce &t;&ae;t heo &ae;r w&ae;s  &d;onecan &d;e heo utan behwerfed sie &t;&ae;t &t;&ae;t hio &ae;r w&ae;s  &amp; do &t;&ae;t &t;&ae;t heo &ae;r dyde. 
 &D;a se Wisdom &d;a &d;is leo&d; asungen h&ae;fde  &t;a ongan he eft spellian &amp; &t;us cw&ae;&d;: Eala  hw&ae;t  ge eor&d;lican men  &d;eah ge eow selfe nu don neatum gelice for eowre dysige  hw&ae;t  ge &t;eah magon hw&ae;thwugu ongitan swelce eow m&ae;te be eowrum frumsceafte  &t;&ae;t is God. 
 &d;one so&d;an fruman &amp; &t;one so&d;an ende &ae;lcre ges&ae;l&d;e ge ongita&d;  &t;eah ge hine fullice ne oncnawen; &amp; swa&d;eah sio gecynd eow tih&d; to &d;&ae;m andgite  ac eow teoh&d; swi&d;e manigfeald gedwola of &t;am andgite. 
 Ge&d;enca&d; nu hw&ae;&d;er men m&ae;gen cuman to &t;am so&t;um ges&ae;l&d;um &t;urh &t;a andweardan ges&ae;l&d;a; for&t;am&d;e fullneah ealle men cwe&d;a&d; &t;&ae;t se seo se ges&ae;lgosta se &t;e &t;as eor&d;lican ges&ae;l&d;a ealla h&ae;f&d;. 
 Hw&ae;&d;er nu micel feoh o&d;&d;e weor&d;scipe o&d;&d;e eall &t;es andwearda wela m&ae;ge &ae;nigne mon don swa ges&ae;ligne &t;&ae;t he nanes &t;inges maran ne &t;yrfe? 
 Nese  nese; ic wat &t;&ae;t &t;&ae;t hi ne magon. 
 Hwy nis hit &t;onne on &t;y swi&d;e sweotol &t;&ae;t &t;as andweardan good ne sint no &t;a so&d;an god  for&d;&ae;m&t;e hi ne magon sellan &t;&ae;t hi gehata&d;? 
 Ac licetta&d; &t;&ae;t hi gel&ae;stan ne magon  &t;onne hi gehata&d; &t;&ae;m &t;e hi lufian willa&d; &d;a so&d;an ges&ae;l&t;a; &amp; aleoga&t; him &t;eah ma &d;onne hi him gel&ae;sten  for&d;&ae;m&d;e hi heora nabba&t; ma &t;onne hi heora h&ae;bben. 
 Ge&t;enc &t;u nu be &d;e selfum  la  Boetius  hw&ae;&d;er &t;u &ae;fre auht unrot w&ae;re &t;a &t;a &t;u ges&ae;legost w&ae;re  o&d;&d;e hw&ae;&d;er &t;e &ae;fre &ae;niges welan wana w&ae;re &t;a &d;u m&ae;stne welan h&ae;fdest  o&d;&d;e hw&ae;&d;er &t;in woruld &t;a eall w&ae;re &ae;fter &t;inum willan? 
 &t;a andsworode Boetius &amp; cw&ae;&d;: Nese  la  nese; n&ae;s ic n&ae;fre git nane hwile swa emnes modes  &t;&ae;s &t;e ic gemunan m&ae;ge  &t;&ae;t ic eallunga w&ae;re orsorg  &t;&ae;t ic swa orsorg w&ae;re &t;&ae;t ic nane gedrefednesse n&ae;fde. 
 ne me n&ae;fre git ne licode eall &t;&ae;t ic wisste  ne me n&ae;fre n&ae;s ealles swa ic wolde  &t;eah ic his mi&d;e. 
 &d;a andsworode se Wisdom &amp; cw&ae;&d;: Hwi n&ae;re &d;u &d;onne genog earm &amp; genog unhydig  &t;eah &t;e &d;uhte &t;&ae;t &d;u welig w&ae;re  &t;onne &d;u o&d;er twega  o&d;&d;e h&ae;fdest &t;&ae;t &d;u noldes o&d;&d;e n&ae;fdest &t;&ae;t &d;u woldest? 
 &d;a andswarode Beotius &amp; cw&ae;&d;: Eall me w&ae;s swa swa &d;u s&ae;dest. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; se Wisdom: hu ne bi&d; &ae;lc mon genog earm &t;&ae;s &d;e he n&ae;f&d;  &t;onne hit hine lyst habban? 
 &t;&ae;t is so&d;  cw&ae;&d; Beotius. 
 &t;a cw&ae;&d; se Wisdom: Gif he &t;onne earm bi&d;  ne he &t;onne ne bi&d; eadig; for&d;i he eac wilna&d; &t;&ae;t he habbe &t;&ae;t he n&ae;f&d;  &t;y he wolde genog habban. 
 &t;a cw&ae;&d; Boetius: &t;&ae;t is eall so&d; &t;&ae;t &d;u segst. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; se Wisdom: Hu ne h&ae;fdest &t;u &t;onne &t;a yrm&d;e  &d;a &d;a &d;u welgost w&ae;re? 
 &d;a andswarode ic &amp; cw&ae;&d;: Ic wat &t;&ae;t &t;u so&d; segst  &t;&ae;t ic hi h&ae;fde. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; se Wisdom: Hu ne &t;inc&d; me &d;onne nu &t;&ae;t ealle &t;a welan &t;isses middaneardes ne m&ae;gon gedon &ae;nne mon weligne  swa weligne &t;&ae;t he genog h&ae;bbe &amp; no maran ne &d;yrfe? 
 &amp; swa&d;eah hi hit gehata&d; &ae;lcum &d;ara &t;e hi h&ae;f&d;. 
 &t;a cw&ae;&d; ic: Nis nan &t;ing so&d;re &t;onne &t;&ae;t &d;u segst. 
 &t;a cw&ae;&d; se Wisdom: Ac hwi ne eart &t;u &t;onne his ge&d;afa? 
 Hu ne miht &t;u geseon &ae;lce d&ae;g &t;&ae;t &d;a strengran nima&d; &t;a welan of &t;am unstrengum? 
 Hwi bi&d; elles &ae;lce d&ae;g swelc seofung &amp; swelce geflitu &amp; gemot &amp; domas  buton &t;&ae;t &ae;lc bit &t;&ae;s reaflaces &t;e him on genumen bi&d;  o&d;&d;e eft o&d;res gitsa&d;? 
 &t;a andswarode ic &amp; cw&ae;&d;: Genoh ryhte &t;u spyrast; swa hit is swa &t;u segst. 
 &t;a cw&ae;&d; he: For &d;isum &t;ingum be&d;earf &ae;lc mon fultumes toeacan him selfum  &t;&ae;t he m&ae;ge gehealdan his welan. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; ic: Hwa o&d;s&ae;c&d; &t;&ae;s? 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; he: Gif he nauht n&ae;fde &t;&ae;s &d;e he ondrede &t;&ae;t he forleosan &t;orfte  &t;onne ne &d;orfte he no maran fultomes &t;onne his selfes. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; ic: So&d; &t;u segst. 
 &d;a onsac se Wisdom sarlice &amp; cwae&d;: Eala  &t;&ae;t me &t;ync&d; wi&d;erweard &t;ing &ae;lces monnes gewunan &amp; &ae;lces monnes willan  &t;e ic nu secgan wille. 
 &t;&ae;t is &t;&ae;tte &t;onan &t;e hi tiohhia&d; &t;&ae;t hi scylan eadigran weor&d;an  &t;&ae;t hi weor&d;a&d; &t;onan earmran &amp; eargran. 
 For&d;&ae;m gif hi lytles hw&ae;t habba&d;  &t;onne be&t;urfon hi &t;&ae;t hi oleccen &t;&ae;m &ae;fter fri&d;e &t;e &ae;nigre wuhte mare habba&d;; sam hi &t;yrfen  sam hi ne &t;urhfon  hi willa&d; &t;eah. 
 Hw&ae;r is &t;onne seo gemetgung  o&d;&d;e hwa h&ae;f&d; hi  o&d;&d;e hwonne cym&d; heo  &t;&ae;t heo m&ae;ge adrifan &t;a yrm&d;a from &d;&ae;m welegum eallunga? 
 Swa he mare h&ae;f&d;  swa he ma monna oleccan sceal. 
 Hw&ae;&d;er &t;a welegan nu n&ae;fre ne hingrige ne ne &t;yrste  ne ne cale? 
 Ic wene &t;eah &t;&ae;t &t;u wille nu cwe&d;an &t;&ae;t &d;a welgan h&ae;bben mid hwam hi m&ae;gen &t;&ae;t eall gebetan. 
 Ac &t;eah &d;u nu swa cw&ae;de  hit ne magon &d;a welan ellunga gebetan  &t;eah hi sume hwile m&ae;gen. 
 For&d;&ae;m&t;e hi sculon &ae;lce d&ae;g ycan &t;&ae;t mon &ae;lce d&ae;g wana&d;. 
 for&t;am&t;e sio mennisce w&ae;dl &d;e n&ae;fre gefylled ne bi&d; wilna&d; &ae;lce d&ae;g hw&ae;shwugu &t;ysses woruldwelan  &ae;g&d;er ge hr&ae;gles ge metes ge drynces ge monegra &t;inga toeacan &t;am. 
 For&d;&ae;m nis nan mon swa welig &t;&ae;t he maran ne &t;yrfe. 
 Ac sio gitsung ne con gemet  ne n&ae;fre ne bi&d; gehealden on &d;&ae;re ned&d;earfe  ac wilna&d; symle maran &t;onne he &t;urfe. 
 Ic nat hwi ge fultruwia&d; &d;&ae;m hreosendan welan  nu hy ne magon eowre w&ae;dle eow from adon; ac ge eca&d; eowre w&ae;dle mid &d;&ae;m &d;e hi eow to cuma&d;. 
 &d;a se Wisdom &d;a &t;is spel as&ae;d h&ae;fde  &t;a ongan he eft giddian  &amp; &t;us singende cw&ae;&d;: Hwelc fremu by&d; &t;am welgan gitsere &t;&ae;t he gegaderige ungerim &t;issa welena &amp; &ae;lces gimcynnes genog begite? 
 &amp; &t;eah he erige his land mid &t;usend sula  &amp; &t;eah eall &d;es middaneard sie his anwealde under&d;eoded  ne l&ae;t he his nanwuht of &t;is middanearde mid him mare &t;onne he brohte hider. 
 &d;a se Wisdom &d;a &d;is lio&d; asungen h&ae;fde  &d;a ongan he eft spellian &amp; cw&ae;&d;: Tu &t;ing m&ae;g se weor&d;scipe &amp; se anwald gedon  gif he becym&d; to &t;&ae;m dysgan; he m&ae;g hine gedon weor&d;ne &amp; andrysne o&d;rum dysegum. 
 Ac &t;onecan &t;e he &d;one anwald forl&ae;t  o&d;&d;e se anweald hine  &t;onne ne bi&d; he nau&d;er &t;am dysegan ne weor&d; ne andrysne. 
 Hw&ae;&d;er nu se anwald h&ae;bbe &t;one &t;eaw &d;&ae;t he astificige un&d;eawas &amp; awyrtwalige of ricra monna mode  &amp; plantige &d;&ae;r cr&ae;ftas on? 
 Ic wat &d;eah &t;&ae;t se eor&d;lica anweald n&ae;fre ne s&ae;w&d; &t;a cr&ae;ftas  ac lis&d; &amp; gadra&d; un&d;eawas; &amp; &t;onne hi gegadrad h&ae;f&d;  &t;onne eowa&d; he hi  nallas ne hil&d;. 
 for&t;am &d;ara ricra monna un&d;eawas manige men geseo&d;  for&t;am&d;e hi manige cunnon  &amp; manege him mid beo&d;. 
 For&d;&ae;m we symle seofia&d; ymbe &d;one anwald &amp; hine eac forseo&d;  &t;onne we geseo&d; &t;&ae;t he cym&d; to &t;am wyrrestum &amp; to &t;am &t;e us unweor&t;oste bio&d;. 
 For &d;&ae;m &t;ingum w&ae;s gio &t;&ae;t se wisa Catulus hine gebealg &amp; swa ungefr&ae;glice forcw&ae;&d; Nonium &t;one rican  for&d;&ae;m he hine gemette sittan on gerenedum scridw&ae;ne. 
 for&d;&ae;m hit w&ae;s &d;a swi&d;e micel sido mid Romwarum &t;&ae;t &t;&ae;r nane o&d;re an ne s&ae;ton buton &t;a weor&d;estan. 
 &t;a forseah se Catulus hine  for&d;y he &t;&ae;ran sittan sceolde; for&d;&ae;m he hine wiste swi&d;e ungesceadwisne &amp; swi&d;e ungemetf&ae;stne. 
 &t;a ongan se Catulus him spigettan on; se Catulus w&ae;s heretoga on Rome  swi&d;e gesceadwis mon. 
 Ne forsawe he no &t;onne o&d;erne swa swi&d;e gif he nan rice ne n&ae;nne anwald naefde. 
 Hw&ae;&t;er &t;u nu mage ongitan hu micelne unweor&d;scipe se anwald breng&d; &t;am unmedeman gif he hine underfeh&d;? 
 for&d;&ae;m &ae;lces monnes yfel bi&d; &t;y openre gif he anwald h&ae;f&d;. 
 Ac gesege me nu  ic ascige &d;e  &t;u Boetius  hwi &t;u swa manigfeald yfel h&ae;fde &amp; swa micele une&d;nesse on &t;&ae;m rice  &t;a hwile &t;e &d;u hit h&ae;fdest  o&d;&d;e forhwy &t;u hit eft &t;inum unwillum forlete? 
 Hu ne was&d; &t;u &t;&ae;t hit n&ae;s for nanum o&d;rum &d;ingum buton for&d;&ae;m&t;e &t;u noldest on eallum &d;ingum bion ge&t;w&ae;re &t;&ae;s unrihtwisan cyninges willan &T;iodrices? 
 for&d;&ae;m&d;e &d;u hine ongeate on eallum &t;ingum unwyr&d;ne &t;&ae;s anwealdes  swi&d;e sceamleasne &amp; unge&t;w&ae;rne  buton &ae;lcum godum &t;eawe. 
 For&t;am we ne magon nauht ea&d;e secgan &t;&ae;t &t;a yfelan sien gode  &t;eah hi anweald habban. 
 Ne wurde &t;u &d;eah na adrifen from &d;eodrice  ne he &d;e na ne forsawe  gif &t;e licode his dysig &amp; his unrihtwisnes swa wel swa his dysegum deorlingum dyde. 
 Gif &t;u nu gesawe sumne swi&d;e wisne man &t;e h&ae;fde swi&d;e gooda oferhyda  &amp; w&ae;re &t;eah swi&d;e earm &amp; swi&d;e unges&ae;lig  hw&ae;&d;er &d;u wolde cwe&d;an &t;&ae;t he w&ae;re unwry&d;e anwealdes &amp; weor&d;scipes? 
 &d;a andswarode Boetius &amp; cw&ae;&d;: Nese  la  nese; gif ic hine swilcne gemete ne cw&ae;&d;e ic n&ae;fre &d;&ae;t he sie unweor&d;e anwaldes &amp; weor&d;scipes  ac &ae;lces me &d;inc&d; &t;&ae;t he sie wyr&d;e &t;e on &t;isse worulde is. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; se Wisdom: &ae;lc cr&ae;ft h&ae;f&d; his sundorgife  &amp; &t;a gife &amp; &t;one weor&d;scipe &t;e he h&ae;f&d; he forgif&d; swi&d;e hr&ae;&d;e &t;&ae;m &t;e hine lufa&d;. 
 Swa swa wisdom is se hehsta cr&ae;ft &amp; se h&ae;f&d; on him feower o&d;re cr&ae;ftas; &d;ara is an w&ae;rscipe  o&d;er gemetgung  &d;ridde is ellen  feor&d;e rihtwisnes. 
 Se Wisdom gede&d; his lufiendas wise &amp; weor&d;e &amp; gemetf&ae;ste &amp; ge&t;yldige &amp; rihtwise  &amp; &ae;lces godes &t;eawes he gefyll&d; &t;one &t;e hine lufa&d;. 
 &t;&ae;t ne magon don &t;a &d;e &t;one anweald habba&d; &t;isse worulde; ne magon hi nanne cr&ae;ft forgifan &t;am &d;e hine lufia&d; of hiora welan  gif hi hine on heora gecynde nabba&d;. 
 Be &t;&ae;m is swi&d;e sweotol &t;&ae;t &d;a rican on &t;&ae;m woruldwelan nabba&d; n&ae;nne sundorcr&ae;ft; ac him bi&d; se wela utane cumen  &amp; he ne m&ae;g utane nauht agnes habban. 
 Ge&d;enc nu hw&ae;&d;er &ae;nig mon bio a &d;e unweor&d;ra &t;e hine manige men forseon; gif &t;onne &ae;nig mon a &t;e unweor&d;ra bi&d;  &t;onne bi&d; &ae;lc dysig man &t;y unweor&d;ra &t;e he mare rice h&ae;f&d; &ae;lcum wisum men. 
 Be &t;&ae;m is genoh sweotol &t;&ae;t se anweald &amp; se wela ne m&ae;g his wealdend gedon no &d;y weor&d;ran  ac he hine gede&d; &d;y unweor&d;ran &t;e he him to cym&d;  gif he &ae;r ne dohte. 
 Swa bi&d; eac se wela &amp; se anwald &t;i wyrsa  gif se ne deah &t;e hine ah; &ae;g&d;er hiora bi&d; &t;y forcu&d;ra gif hi hi gemeta&d;. 
 Ac ic &t;e m&ae;g ea&t;e gereccan be sumere bisne  &t;&ae;t &d;u miht genoh sweotole ongiton &t;&ae;t &d;is andwearde lif is swi&d;e anlic sceade  &amp; on &t;&ae;re sceade nan mon ne m&ae;g begitan &t;a so&d;an ges&ae;l&d;a. 
 Hu wenst &d;u nu? 
 gif hwelc swi&d;e rice mon wyr&d; adrifen of his earde o&d;&d;e on his hlafordes &ae;rende f&ae;r&d;  cym&d; &t;onne on &ae;l&d;eodig folc &t;&ae;r &t;&ae;r hine nan man ne can ne he ne &ae;nne mon  ne fur&d;um &t;&ae;t ge&d;eode ne can  wenstu m&ae;ge his rice hine &t;&ae;r on londe wyr&d;ne gedon? 
 Ac ic wat &t;&ae;t he ne m&ae;g. 
 Gif &t;onne se weor&d;scipe &t;&ae;m welan gecynde w&ae;re  &amp; he his agen w&ae;re  o&d;&d;e eft se wela &d;&ae;s welegan agen w&ae;re  &t;onne ne meahte he hine no forl&ae;tan. 
 W&ae;re se mon on swelcum lande swelce he w&ae;re &t;e hi ahte  &d;onne w&ae;re his wela &amp; his weor&d;scipe mid him. 
 Ac for&t;&ae;m&t;e se wela &amp; se anwald his agene ne bio&d;  for&d;y hi hine forl&ae;ta&d;; &amp; for&d;y&t;e hi nan gecyndelic good on him selfum nabba&d;  for&d;y hi losia&d; swa swa sceadu o&d;&d;e smec. 
 &t;eah se leasa wena &amp; sio r&ae;delse &t;ara dysigena monna tiohhige &t;&ae;t se anwald &amp; se wela sie &t;&ae;t hehste good  ac hit bi&d; eall o&d;er. 
 &t;onne &t;a rican beo&d; o&d;er twega  o&d;&d;e on &ae;l&d;eode o&d;&d;e on hiora agenre gecy&d;&d;e mid gesceadwisum monnum  &t;onne bi&d; &ae;g&d;er ge &t;am wisan ge &t;am &ae;l&d;eodegan his wela for nauht  si&d;&d;an hi ongita&d; &t;&ae;t hi n&ae;ron for nanum cr&ae;fte gecorene  buton for dysges folces heringe. 
 Ac &t;&ae;r hi &ae;nige wuht agnes o&d;&d;e gecyndelices godes an heora anwealde h&ae;fdon  &t;onne h&ae;fden hi &t;&ae;t mid him  &t;eah hi &t;&ae;t rice forleten. 
 ne forleton hi no &t;&ae;t gecyndelice good  ac simle him wolde &t;&ae;t fylgean &amp; hi symle weor&d;e gedon  w&ae;ron hi on swelcum lande swylce hi w&ae;ron. 
 Nu &d;u meaht ongitan &t;&ae;t se weta &amp; se anwald n&ae;nne mon ne magon on ellende weor&d;ne gedon. 
 Ic nat &t;eah &d;u wene &t;&ae;t hi on hiora agenre cy&d;&d;e ealneweg m&ae;gen; ac &d;eah &t;u his wene  ic wat &t;&ae;t hi ne magon. 
 Hit w&ae;s gio giond ealle Romana mearce &t;&ae;t heretogan &amp; domeras  &amp; &t;a ma&d;mhirdas &t;e &t;&ae;t fioh hioldon &t;e mon &t;am ferdmonnum on geare sellan sceolde  &amp; &t;a wisestan witan  h&ae;fdon m&ae;stne weor&d;scipe. 
 nu &t;onne o&d;er twega  o&d;&d;e &t;ara nan nis  o&d;&d;e hi n&ae;nne weor&t;scipe nabba&d;  gif hiora &ae;nig is. 
 Swa hit bi&d; be &ae;lcum &t;ara &t;inga &d;e agen god &amp; gecyndelic nabba&d; on him selfum; o&d;re hwile hit bi&d; to t&ae;lenne  o&d;re hwile hit bi&d; to heriganne. 
 Ac hw&ae;t &t;inc&d; &t;e &t;onne on &t;am welan &amp; on anwealde wynsumes o&d;&d;e nytwyr&t;es  nu hi nanes &d;inges genog nabba&t;  ne hi nauht agnes goodes nabba&d;  ne nauht &t;urhwunigendes hiora wealdendum sellan na magon? 
 &d;a se Wisdom &t;a &d;is spell as&ae;d h&ae;fde  &d;a ongan he eft giddigan &amp; &t;us cw&ae;&d;: &d;eah nu se unrihtwisa cyning Neron hine gescyrpte mid eallum &t;am wlitegestum w&ae;dum &amp; mid &ae;lces cynnes gimmum geglengde  hu ne wes he &t;eah &ae;lcum witum la&d; &amp; unweor&d;  &amp; &ae;lces un&d;eawes &amp; firenlustes full? 
 Hw&ae;t  he &t;eah weor&d;ode his deorlingas mid miclum welum; ac hw&ae;t was him &d;y bet? 
 Hwelc gesceadwis mon mihte cwe&t;an &t;&ae;t he a &d;y weor&d;ra w&ae;re &t;eah he hine weor&d;ode? 
 &d;a se Wisdom &t;a &t;is leo&d; asungen h&ae;fde  &t;a ongan he eft spelligan &amp; &t;us cw&ae;&d;: Hwe&d;er &t;u nu wene &t;&ae;t &t;&ae;s cyninges geferr&ae;den &amp; se wela &amp; se anweald &t;e he gif&d; his deorlingum m&ae;ge &ae;nigne mon gedon weligne o&d;&d;e wealdendne? 
 &d;a andsworede ic &amp; cw&ae;t: Forhwi ne magon hi? 
 Hw&ae;t is on &d;is andweardan life wynsumre &amp; betere &t;onne &t;&ae;s cyninges folga&d; &amp; his neawest  &amp; si&d;&d;an wela &amp; anweald? 
 &d;a andswarode se Wisdom &amp; cw&ae;&d;: Sege me nu hw&ae;&d;er &t;u &ae;fre gehyrdest &t;&ae;t he &ae;ngum &d;ara &t;e &ae;r us w&ae;re eallunga &t;urhwunode; o&d;&d;e wenstu hw&ae;&d;er hine &ae;nig &t;ara ealne weg habban m&ae;ge &t;e hine nu h&ae;f&d;? 
 Hu ne was&d; &d;u &t;&ae;tte ealle bec sind fulla &t;ara biesena &t;ara monna &t;e &ae;r us w&ae;ren? 
 &amp; &ae;lc mon wat &t;ara &t;e nu leofa&d; &d;&ae;tte manegum cyninge onhwearf se anweald &amp; se wela o&d; &d;&ae;t he eft wear&d; w&ae;dla. 
 Eala ea  is &t;&ae;t &t;onne forweor&d;fullic wela &t;&ae;t nau&t;er ne m&ae;g ne hine selfne gehealdan ne his hlaford  to &t;on &t;&ae;t he ne &t;yrfe maran fultumes  o&d;&d;e hi bio&d; begen forhealden? 
 Hu ne is &t;&ae;t &t;eah sio eowru hehste ges&ae;l&d; &t;ara cyninga anweald? 
 &amp; &t;eah gif &t;am cyninge &ae;niges willan wana bi&d;  &t;onne lytla&d; &d;&ae;t his anweald  &amp; ec&d; his erm&d;a; for&d;y bio&d; simle &t;a eowra ges&ae;l&d;a on sumum &t;ingum uns&ae;l&d;a. 
 Hw&ae;t  &t;a cyningas  &t;eah hi m&ae;nig ger &t;ioda wealden  ne wealda&d; hi &t;eah ealra &t;ara &t;e hi wealdan woldan  ac bio&d; for&d;&ae;m swi&d;e earme on hiora mode for&d;y hi nabba&d; sume &t;ara &t;e hi habban wolden. 
 for&d;&ae;m ic wat &t;&ae;t se cyning &t;e gitsere bi&d;  &t;&ae;t he h&ae;f&d; maran erm&d;e &t;onne anwald. 
 For&d;&ae;m cw&ae;&d; gio sum cyning &t;e unrihtlice feng to rice: Eala  hw&ae;t &d;&ae;t bi&d; ges&ae;lig mon &t;e him ealne weg ne hanga&d; nacod sweord ofer &d;&ae;m heafde be smale &t;r&ae;de  swa swa me git symle dyde? 
 Hu &t;inc&d; &t;e nu  hu &t;e se wela &amp; se anwald licige  nu hi n&ae;fre ne bio&d; buton ege &amp; earfo&d;um &amp; sorgum? 
 Hw&ae;t  &t;u w&ae;st &t;&ae;t &ae;lc cyninc wolde bion butan &t;issum  &amp; habban &t;eah anwald gif he meahte; ac ic wat &t;&ae;t he ne m&ae;g; &t;y ic wundrige forhwy hi gilpen swelces anwaldes. 
 Hw&ae;&d;er &t;e nu &t;ince &t;&ae;t se mon micelne anwald h&ae;bbe &amp; sie swi&d;e ges&ae;lig &t;e simle willna&d; &t;&ae;s &t;e he begitan ne m&ae;g? 
 O&d;&d;e wenstu &t;&ae;t se sie swi&d;e ges&ae;lig &t;e symle mid micle werede f&ae;r&d;  o&d;&d;e eft se &d;e &ae;g&d;er ondr&ae;d ge &t;one &t;e hine ondr&ae;t ge &t;one &t;e hine no ne ondr&ae;t? 
 Hw&ae;&d;er &t;e nu &t;ince &t;&ae;t se mon micelne anwald h&ae;bbe &t;e him selfum &d;inc&d; &t;&ae;t he n&ae;nne n&ae;bbe  swa swa nu manegum men &d;inc&d;  &t;&ae;t he n&ae;nne n&ae;bbe buton he h&ae;bbe m&ae;nigne man &t;e him here? 
 Hw&ae;t wille we ma nu sprecan be &d;&ae;m cininge &amp; be his folgerum  butan &t;&ae;t &ae;lc gesceadwis man m&ae;g witan &t;&ae;t hi bio&d; full earme &amp; ful unmihtige? 
 Hu magon &t;a cyningas o&d;sacan o&d;&d;e forhelan heora unmeahte  &t;onne hi ne magon n&ae;nne weor&d;scipe for&d;brengan buton hiora &t;egna fultume? 
 Hw&ae;t wille we nu elles secggean be &d;&ae;m &t;egnum buton &t;&ae;t &t;&ae;t &d;&ae;r oft gebyre&d; &t;&ae;t hi weor&d;a&d; bereafode &ae;lcre are  ge fur&d;um &t;&ae;s feores  from hiora leasan cyninges? 
 Hw&ae;t  we witon &t;&ae;t se unrihtwisa cyning Neron wolde hatan his agenne magister &amp; his fostorf&ae;der acwellan  &t;&ae;s nama w&ae;s Seneca; se w&ae;s u&d;wita. 
 &t;a he &t;a onfunde &t;&ae;t he dead bion sceolde  &t;a bead he ealla his &ae;hta wi&d; his feore; &t;a nolde se cyning &t;&ae;s onfon  ne him his feores geunnan. 
 &d;a he &t;a &t;&ae;t ongeat  &t;a geceas he hi &t;one dea&d; &d;&ae;t hine mon oflete blodes on &d;&ae;m earme; &amp; &d;a dyde mon swa. 
 Hw&ae;t  we eac geherdon &t;&ae;t Papinianus w&ae;s Antoniose &d;&ae;m casere ealra his dyrlinga besorgost  &amp; ealles his folces m&ae;stne anwald h&ae;fde; ac he hine het gebindan &amp; si&d;&d;an ofslean. 
 Hw&ae;t  ealle men witan &t;&ae;t se Seneca w&ae;s Nerone &amp; Papinianus Antonie &t;a weor&d;estan &amp; &t;a leofostan  &amp; M&ae;stne anwald h&ae;fdon ge on hiora hirede ge buton  &amp; &t;eah buton &ae;lcre scylde wurdon fordone. 
 Hw&ae;t  hi wilnedon begen eallon m&ae;gene &t;&ae;t &d;a hlafordas naman swa hw&ae;t swa hi h&ae;fden  &amp; leten hi libban. 
 ac hi ne meahten &t;&ae;t begitan  for&d;&ae;m &t;ara cyninga w&ae;lhreownes w&ae;s to &d;&ae;m heard &t;&ae;t hiora ea&d;metto ne meahton nauht forstandan  ne huru heora ofermetto dydon; swa hw&ae;&d;er swa hi dydon ne dohte him &d;a naw&d;er  &t;eah hi scoldon &t;&ae;t feorh &ae;l&ae;tan. 
 For&d;&ae;m se &d;e his &ae;r tide ne tiola&d;  &t;onne bi&d; his on tid untilad. 
 Hu lica&d; &t;e nu se anwald &amp; se wela  nu &d;u gehered h&ae;fst &t;&ae;t hine mon naw&d;er ne butan ege habban ne m&ae;g ne forl&ae;tan ne mot  &t;eah he wille? 
 O&d;&d;e hw&ae;t forstod seo menigu &t;ara freonda &t;am deorlingum &t;ara cyninga? 
 o&d;&d;e hw&ae;t forstent hio &ae;negum men? 
 For&d;on &t;a frend cuma&d; mid &t;&ae;m welum &amp; eft mid &d;&ae;m welan gewita&d; buton swi&d;e feawa. 
 Ac &d;a frend &t;e hine &ae;r for &d;&ae;m welan lufia&d; &t;a gewita&d; eft mid &t;&ae;m welan  &amp; weor&d;a&d; &d;onne to feondum  buton &t;a feawan &d;e hine &ae;r for lufum &amp; for treowum lufedon. 
 &t;a hine woldon &t;eah lufian &d;eah he earm w&ae;re; &t;a him wunia&d;. 
 Hwylc is wirsa wol o&d;&d;e &ae;negum men mare daru &t;onne he h&ae;bbe on his geferr&ae;denne &amp; on his neaweste feond &amp; freondes anlicnesse? 
 &d;a se Wisdom &d;a &d;is spell areaht h&ae;fde  &t;a ongan he eft singan &amp; &t;us cw&ae;&d;: Se &t;e wille fullice anweald agan  he sceal tiligan &ae;rest &t;&ae;t he h&ae;bbe anweald his agenes modes  &amp; ne sie to ungerisenlice under&d;eod his un&t;eawum  &amp; ado of his mode ungerisenlice ymbhogan  &amp; forl&ae;te &t;a seofunga his eorm&t;a. 
 &t;eah he nu ricsige ofer eallne middangeard from easteweardum o&d; westeweardne  from Indeum  &t;&ae;t is se su&d;eastende &t;isses middaneardes  o&d; &d;&ae;t iland &t;e we hata&d; Tyle  &t;&ae;t is on &t;am nor&d;westende &t;isses middaneardes  &t;&ae;r ne bi&d; naw&t;er ne on sumera niht  ne on wintra d&ae;g. 
 &t;eah he nu &t;&ae;s ealles wealde  n&ae;f&d; he no &t;e maran anweald gif he his inge&t;ances anweald n&ae;f&d; &amp; gif he hine ne warena&d; wi&d; &t;a un&t;eawas &t;e we &ae;r ymb spr&ae;con. 
 &d;a se Wisdom &t;a &t;as fitte asungen h&ae;fde  &t;a ongon he eft seggan spell &amp; cw&ae;&d;: Is &t;&ae;t ungerisenlic wuldor &t;isse worulde &amp; swi&d;e leas; be &d;&ae;m w&ae;s gio singende sum sceop. 
 &t;a he forseah &t;is andwearde lif  &d;a cw&ae;&d; he: Eala  wuldur &t;isse weorulde  ea  forhwy &t;e haten dysige men mid leasre stemne wuldor  nu &d;u nane neart? 
 For&d;&ae;m&d;e ma manna h&ae;f&d; micelne gielp &amp; micel wuldor &amp; micelne weor&d;scipe for dysiges folces wenan  &t;onne he haebbe for his gewyrhtum. 
 Ac sege me nu hw&ae;t ungerisenlicre sie &d;onne &t;&ae;t  o&d;&d;e forhwy hi ne m&ae;gen hiora ma scamian &t;onne f&ae;gnian  &t;onne hi gehera&d; &t;&ae;t him man on lih&d;? 
 &t;eah mon nu hwone godra mid rihte herige &amp; so&d; an segge  ne sceal he na &t;e hr&ae;&t;or to ungemetlice f&ae;gnian &d;&ae;s folces worda; ac &t;&ae;s he sceal f&ae;gnian &d;&ae;t hi him so&d; an segga&d;. 
 &t;eah he nu &t;&ae;s f&ae;gnige &t;&ae;t hi his naman br&ae;den  ne bi&d; he no &t;y hr&ae;&d;or swa brad swa hi tihha&d;  for&d;&ae;m hi hine ne magon tobr&ae;dan geond ealle eor&d;an  &t;eah hi on sumum lande m&ae;gen. 
 for&d;&ae;m &t;eah he sie anum gehered  &t;onne bi&d; he o&d;rum unhered; &t;eah he on &t;am lande sie m&ae;re  &t;onne bi&d; he on o&d;rum unm&ae;re. 
 For&d;&ae;m is &t;&ae;s folces hlisa &ae;lcum men for nauht to habbanne for&d;&ae;m he to &ae;lcum men ne cym&d; be his gewyrhtum  ne huru nanum ealne weg ne wuna&d;. 
 Ge&t;enc nu &ae;rest be &t;&ae;m gebyrdum  gif hwa &t;&ae;s gilp&d;  hu idel &amp; hu unnet se gylp bi&d;; for&d;am &t;e &ae;lc mon wat &t;&ae;t ealle men of anum f&ae;der comon &amp; of anre meder. 
 O&d;&d;e eft be &t;&ae;s folces hlisan &amp; be hiora heringe; ic nat hw&ae;s we &t;&ae;r f&ae;gnia&d;. 
 &t;eah &d;a nu forem&ae;re sien &t;e folcisce men heria&d;  &t;eah bio&d; &t;a forem&ae;rran &amp; rihtlicran to herianne &t;a &t;e bio&d; mid cr&ae;ftum geweor&d;ode. 
 for&d;&ae;m&t;e nan mon ne bi&d; mid rihte for o&d;res gode ne for his cr&ae;ftum no &t;y m&ae;rra ne no &t;y geheredra  gif he hine self n&ae;f&d;. 
 Hw&ae;&d;er &t;u beo a &t;y f&ae;gerra for o&d;res mannes f&ae;gere? 
 Bi&d; men ful lytle &t;y bet &t;eah he godne f&ae;der h&ae;bbe  gif he self to nauhte ne m&ae;g. 
 For&t;am ic l&ae;re &t;&ae;t &d;u f&ae;genige o&d;erra monna goodes &amp; heora &ae;&d;elo to &t;on swi&d;e &t;&ae;t &t;u ne tilige &d;e selfum agnes  for&d;&ae;m&t;e &ae;lces monnes god &amp; his &ae;&t;elo bio&d; ma on &t;am mode &t;onne on &t;&ae;m fl&ae;sce. 
 &t;&ae;t an ic wat &t;eah godes on &t;a &ae;&d;elo  &t;&ae;t m&ae;nigne mon sceama&t; &t;&ae;t he wior&d;e wyrsa &t;onne his eldran w&ae;ron  &amp; for&d;&ae;m higa&d; eallon m&ae;gne &d;&ae;t he wolde &t;ara betstena sumes &t;eawas &amp; his cr&ae;ftas gefon. 
 &t;a se Wisdom &d;a &t;is spell areaht h&ae;fde  &t;a ongan he singan ymb &t;&ae;t ilce &amp; cw&ae;&d;: Hw&ae;t  ealle men h&ae;fdon gelicne fruman  for&t;am hi ealle coman of anum f&ae;der &amp; of anre meder  &amp; ealle hi beo&d; git gelice acennede. 
 Nis &t;&ae;t nan wundor  for&t;am&t;e an God is f&ae;der eallra gesceafta for&t;am he hi ealle gesceop &amp; ealra welt. 
 Se sel&d; &t;&ae;re sunnan leoht  &amp; &t;am monan  &amp; ealle tungla geset. 
 He gesceop men on eor&t;an; gegaderode &t;a saula &amp; &t;one lichoman mid his &t;am anwealde  &amp; ealle menn gesceop emn&ae;&t;ele on &t;&ae;re fruman gecynde. 
 Hwi ofermodige ge &t;onne ofer o&d;re men for eowrum gebyrdum buton anweorce  nu ge nanne ne magon metan un&ae;&t;elne? 
 ac ealle sint emn&ae;&t;ele  gif ge willa&d; &t;one fruman sceaft ge&t;encan  &amp; &t;one scippend  &amp; si&d;&d;an eoweres &ae;lces acennednesse. 
 Ac &t;a ryht&ae;&t;elo bi&d; on &t;am mode  n&ae;s on &t;am fl&ae;sce  swa swa we &ae;r s&ae;don. 
 Ac &ae;lc mon &t;e allunga under&t;eoded bi&d; un&t;eawum forl&ae;t his sceppend &amp; his fruman sceaft &amp; his &ae;&d;elo  &amp; &t;onan wyr&d; an&ae;&t;elad o&d; &d;&ae;t he wyr&d; un&ae;&d;ele. 
 &d;a se Wisdom &t;a &t;is lio&d; asungen h&ae;fde  &t;a ongan he eft seggan spell &amp; &t;us cw&ae;&d;: Hw&ae;t godes magon we seggan on &t;a fl&ae;sclican un&t;eawas? 
 For&t;am swa hwa swa hi forl&ae;tan wile  he sceal ge&t;olian micle nearanesse &amp; manige gearfo&d;u; for&t;am seo oferfyll simle fet un&t;eawas  &amp; &t;a un&t;eawas habba&d; ofer&d;earfe hreowsunga  &amp; seo hreowsung ne beo&d; na butan sorge &amp; butan nearonesse. 
 Eala  eaw  hu manega adla &amp; hu micel sar &amp; hu micele w&ae;ccan &amp; hu micle unrotnesse se h&ae;f&d; &t;e &d;one won willan h&ae;f&d; on &t;isse worulde. 
 &amp; hu micele ma wenst &d;u &t;&ae;t hi scylon habban &ae;fter &t;isse worulde edlean hiora earnunga; swa swa bearneacen wif acen&d; bearn &amp; &d;rowa&d; micel earfo&d;u  &ae;fter &t;am &t;e hio &ae;r micelne lust &t;urhteah. 
 For &t;y ic nat hw&ae;t &t;a woruldlustas myrges bringa&d; hiora lufigendum. 
 Gif nu hwa cwi&d; &t;&ae;t se sie ges&ae;lig se &t;e his woruldlustum eallu fulg&ae;&d;  hwi nele he cwe&d;an eac &t;&ae;t &d;a netenu seon ges&ae;legu  for&d;&ae;m&d;e hiora willa to nanum o&d;rum &d;ingum nis a&t;enod buton to gifernesse &amp; to wr&ae;nnesse? 
 Swi&d;e gewynsum hit bi&d; &t;&ae;t mon wif h&ae;bbe &amp; bearn; ac &d;eah manige bearn bio&d; gestrined to hiora eldrena forwirde  for&d;&ae;m&t;e manig wif forswilt for hire bearne &ae;r heo hit brengan m&ae;ge. 
 &amp; we leornodon eac &t;&ae;t hwilum geberede swi&d;e ungewunelic &amp; ungecyndelic yfel  &t;&ae;t &d;a bearn getreowedon betwuh him &amp; sieredon ymbe &t;one f&ae;der. 
 ge fur&d;on &t;&ae;t wyrse w&ae;s  we geheordon geo geara on ealdum spellum &t;&ae;t sum sunu ofsloge his f&ae;der; ic nat humeta  buton we witon &t;&ae;t hit unmennisclic d&ae;d w&ae;s. 
 Hw&ae;t  &ae;lc mon m&ae;g witan hu hefig sorg men beo&d; seo gemen his bearna; ne &t;earf ic &t;e &t;eah &t;&ae;t secgan  for&d;&ae;m &t;u hit h&ae;fst afunden be &t;e selfum. 
 Be &t;&ae;re h&ae;fegan gemenne his bearna cw&ae;&d; min m&ae;gister Eurupides &t;&ae;t hwilum gebyrede &t;am heards&ae;lgan &t;&ae;t him w&ae;re betere &t;&ae;t he bearn n&ae;fde &t;onne he h&ae;fde. 
 &t;a se Wisdom &d;a &t;is spel areht h&ae;fde  &t;a ongan he eft giddian &amp; &t;us singende cw&ae;&d;: Hw&ae;t  se yfela willa unrihth&ae;medes gedref&d; fulneah &ae;lces libbendes monnes mod. 
 Swa swa seo beo sceal losian &t;onne heo hw&ae;t irringa sting&d;  swa sceal &ae;lc sawl forweor&d;an &ae;fter &t;am unrihth&ae;mede  buton se mon hweorfe to gode. 
 &d;a se Wisdom &t;a &t;is leo&d; asungen h&ae;fde  &t;a ongan he eft spellian &amp; &t;us cw&ae;&d;: For&d;&ae;m nis nan tweo &t;&ae;t &t;es andwearda wela myr&d; &amp; let &t;a men &t;e bio&d; atehte to &t;am so&d;um ges&ae;l&d;um. 
 &amp; he n&ae;nne ne m&ae;g gebringan &t;&ae;r he him gehet  &t;&ae;t is &ae;t &t;&ae;m hehstan goode. 
 Ac ic &t;e m&ae;g mid feaum wordum gesecgan hu manegra yfela &t;a welan sint gefylde. 
 Hw&ae;t &t;u &t;onne m&ae;ne mid &t;&ae;re gidsunge &t;&ae;s feos  nu &t;u hit nahu elles begitan ne miht buton &t;u hit forstele o&d;&d;e gereafige o&d;&d;e abe&t;ecige  &amp; &t;&ae;r &t;&ae;r hit &t;e wex&d;  &t;onne wana&d; hit o&t;rum? 
 &d;u woldest nu bion forem&ae;re on weor&d;scipe; ac gif &t;u &t;&ae;t habban wilt  &t;onne scealt &d;u oleccan swi&d;e earmlice &amp; swi&t;e eadmodlice &t;&ae;m &d;e &t;e to &t;&ae;m gefulteman m&ae;ge. 
 Gif &t;u &t;e wilt don manegra beteran &amp; weor&d;ran  &t;onne scealt &t;u &t;e l&ae;tan anes wyrsan. 
 Hu ne is &t;&ae;t &t;onne sum d&ae;l yrm&d;a &t;&ae;t mon swa werelice scyle culpian to &t;&ae;m &t;e him gifan scyle? 
 Anwaldes &d;u wilnast? 
 Ac &t;u hine n&ae;fre orsorgne ne begitst for &ae;l&d;eodegum &amp; git ma for &d;inum agnum monnum &amp; m&ae;gum. 
 Gilpes &t;u girnst? 
 Ac &t;u hine ne meaht habban orsorgne  for&t;am &d;u scealt habban simle hw&ae;thweg wi&d;erweardes &amp; unget&ae;ses. 
 &t;u woldest nu brucan ungemetlicre wr&ae;nnesse? 
 Ac &d;e willa&d; &t;onne forsion goode Godes &t;eowas  for&d;&ae;m&t;e &t;in werie fl&ae;sc hafa&d; &t;in anwald  nales &t;u his. 
 Hu m&ae;g mon earmlicor geb&ae;ron &t;onne mon hine under&d;iede his weregan fl&ae;sce  &amp; nelle his gesceadwisan saule? 
 Hw&ae;&t;er ge nu sien maran on eowrum lichoman &t;onne elpend  o&d;&d;e strengran &t;onne leo o&d;&d;e fear  o&d;&d;e swiftran &t;onne tigris? 
 &t;eah &d;u nu w&ae;re mara &t;onne elpend &amp; strengra &t;onne leo o&d;&d;e fear and swiftra &d;onne tigris &t;&ae;t deor  &amp; &t;eah &t;u w&ae;re eallra manna f&ae;grost on wlite  &amp; &t;onne woldest geornlice &ae;fter wisdome spyrian o&d;&d;&ae;t &t;u fullice riht ongeate  &t;onne meahtes &d;u sweotole ongiton &d;&ae;t ealle &t;a m&ae;gno &amp; &t;a cr&ae;ftas &t;e we &ae;r ymb spr&ae;con ne sint to metanne wi&d; &t;&ae;re sawle cr&ae;fta &ae;nne. 
 Hw&ae;t nu  wisdom is an anlepe cr&ae;ft &t;&ae;re sawle  &amp; &t;eah we witon ealle &t;&ae;t he is betera &d;onne ealle &t;a o&d;re cr&ae;ftas &t;e we &ae;r ymbe spr&ae;con. 
 Behealda&d; nu &t;a widgielnesse &amp; f&ae;stnesse &amp; &t;a hr&ae;dfernesse &t;isses heofenes; &d;onne magon ge ongitan &t;&ae;t he is ealles nauht wi&d; his sceppend to metanne &amp; wi&d; his wealdend. 
 Ac hwi ne l&ae;te ge eow &t;onne a&t;reotan &t;&ae;t ge ne wundrigen &amp; ne herigen &t;&ae;tte unnyttre is  &t;&ae;t is &t;es eor&d;lica wela? 
 Swa swa se heofon is betera &amp; healicra &amp; f&ae;gerra &t;onne eall his innung buton monnum anum  swa is &t;&ae;t monnes lichoma betera &amp; deorwyr&d;ra &t;onne ealle his &ae;hta. 
 Ac hu micele &t;inc&d; &t;e &t;onne sio sawl betere &amp; deorwyr&d;re &t;onne se lichoma? 
 &ae;lc gesceaft is to arianne be hire andefne  &amp; symle sio hehste swi&d;ost; for&d;&ae;m is se godcunda anwald to arianne &amp; to wyndrianne &amp; to weor&d;ianne ofer ealla o&d;ra gesceafta. 
 Se wlite &t;&ae;s lichoman is swi&d;e flionde &amp; swi&d;e tedre &amp; swi&d;e anlic eor&d;an blostmum. 
 &d;eah nu hwa sie swa f&ae;ger swa swa Alcibiadis se &ae;&t;elincg w&ae;s; gif hwa bi&d; swa scearpsiene &t;&ae;t he m&ae;ge hine &t;urhsion  swa swa Aristotelis se u&d;wita s&ae;de &t;&ae;t an dior w&ae;re &d;e meahte &ae;lc wuht &t;urhsion ge treowu ge fur&d;um stanas: &t;&ae;t dior we hata&d; lox. 
 gif &t;onne hwa w&ae;re swa scearpsiene &t;&ae;t he mihte &t;one cniht &t;urhsion &t;e we &ae;r ymbe spr&ae;con  &t;onne ne &d;uhte he him no innon swa f&ae;ger swa he utan &t;uhte. 
 &t;eah &t;u nu hw&ae;m f&ae;ger &d;ince  ne bi&d; hit no &t;y hr&ae;&d;or swa; ac sio ungesceadwisnes hiora eagena hi myr&d; &t;&ae;t hi ne magon ongiton &t;&ae;t hi &d;e sceawia&d; utan  n&ae;s innan. 
 Ac ge&t;enca&d; nu swi&d;e geornlice  &amp; gesceadwislice smeag&d; hwelc &t;&ae;s fl&ae;slican good sien  &amp; &t;a ges&ae;l&d;a &t;e ge nu ungemetlice wilnia&d;. 
 &t;onne magan ge sweotole ongeotan &t;&ae;t &t;&ae;s lichoman f&ae;ger &amp; his strengo &t;a magon beon afyrred mid &t;reora daga fefre. 
 For&d;&ae;m ic &t;e recce eall &t;&ae;t ic &t;e &ae;r reahte for&d;&ae;m ic &d;e wolde openlice gereccan on &d;&ae;m ende &t;isses capitulan &t;&ae;tte eall &t;as andweardan good ne magon gel&ae;stan hiora lufiendum &t;&ae;t hi him gehata&d;; &t;&ae;t is &t;&ae;t hehste good &t;&ae;t hi him gehata&d;. 
 &t;eah hi nu gegaderien ealle &t;as andweardan good  nabba&d; hi no &d;y hra&t;or fulfremed good on &d;&ae;m  ne hi ne magon gedon hiora lufiendas swa welige swa swa hi woldon. 
 &d;a se Wisdom &d;a &t;is spell areaht h&ae;fde  &t;a ongon he eft gieddigan &amp; &t;us singinde cw&ae;&d;: Eala wa  hu hefig &amp; hu frecendlic &t;&ae;t dysig is &t;e &d;a earman men gedwela&d; &amp; al&ae;t of &t;am rihtan wege. 
 Se weg is God. 
 Hw&ae;&d;er ge nu secan gold on treowum? 
 ic wat &t;eah &t;&ae;t ge hit &t;&ae;r ne seca&d;  ne finde ge hit no  for&t;am&d;e ealle men witon &t;&ae;t hit &t;&ae;r ne weax&d; &t;e ma &d;e gimmas weaxa&d; on wingeardum. 
 Hw&ae;&d;er ge nu settan eower nett on &t;a hehstan dune  &t;onne ge fiscian willa&d;? 
 Ic wat &t;eah &t;&ae;t ge hit &t;&ae;r ne setta&d;. 
 Hw&ae;&d;er ge nu eower hundas &amp; eower net ut on &t;a s&ae; l&ae;don  &t;onne ge huntian willa&d;? 
 Ic wene &t;eah &t;&ae;t ge hi &t;onne setton up on dunum &amp; innon wudum. 
 Hw&ae;t  &t;&ae;t is wundorlic &t;&ae;t geornfulle men witon &t;&ae;t hi sculon secan be s&ae; waro&d;e &amp; be &ae; aofrum &ae;g&d;er ge hwite gimmas ge reade &amp; &ae;lces cynnes gimcyn; &amp; hi witon eac on hwelcum w&ae;terum &amp; on &ae;ghwelcra ea mu&t;um hi sculon secan fiscas. 
 &amp; ealne &t;isne andweardan welan hi witon hw&ae;r hi secan sculon  &amp; &t;one swi&d;e una&d;rotenlice seca&d;. 
 Ac hit is swi&d;e earmlic &t;ing &t;&ae;t &d;a dysegan men sint &ae;lces domes swa blinde &t;&ae;t hi nyton hw&ae;r &t;a so&d;an ges&ae;l&t;a sint gehydde  ne fur&d;um nane lustb&ae;rnesse nabba&d; hi to secanne. 
 ac wena&d; &t;&ae;t hi m&ae;gon on &t;issum l&ae;nan &amp; on &d;isum deadlicum &t;ingum findan &t;a so&d;an ges&ae;l&d;a  &t;&ae;t is God. 
 Ic nat nu hu ic m&ae;ge heora dysig eall swa sweotole areccan &amp; swa swi&d;e get&ae;lan swa ic wolde  for&t;am hi sint earmran &amp; dysigran &amp; unges&ae;ligran &t;onne ic hit arecan m&ae;ge. 
 Welan &amp; weor&d;scipes hi willnia&d;  &amp; &t;onne hi hine habba&d; &t;onne wena&d; hi swa ungewitfulle &t;&ae;t hi habban &t;a so&d;an ges&ae;l&d;a. 
 &t;a se Wisdom &t;a &t;is leo&d; asungen h&ae;fde  &d;a ongan he eft spellian &amp; &t;us cw&ae;&d;: Genog ic &t;e h&ae;bbe nu gereaht ymb &d;a anlicnessa &amp; emb &d;a sceaduwa &t;&ae;re so&d;an ges&ae;l&d;e. 
 Ac gif &t;u nu sweotole gecnawan meaht &t;a anlicnesse &t;&ae;re so&d;an ges&ae;l&d;e &t;onne is si&d;&d;an &d;earf &t;&ae;t ic &t;e hi selfe get&ae;ce. 
 &t;a andwyrde ic &amp; cw&ae;&d;: Nu ic ongite genog openlice &t;&ae;tte &ae;lces goodes genog nis on &d;issum woruldwelum  ne &ae;lt&ae;we anwald nis on nanum weoruldrice  ne se so&d;a weor&d;scipe nis on &t;isse weorulde  ne &t;a m&ae;stan m&ae;r&d;a ne sint on &d;ysse woruldgype  ne sio hehste blis nis on &t;am fl&ae;sclicum lustum. 
 &d;a andsworede se Wisdom &amp; cw&ae;&d;: Hw&ae;&t;er &t;u nu fullice ongite forhwy hit &t;onne swa sie? 
 &d;a andswarede ic &amp; cw&ae;&d;: &t;eah ic his nu hw&ae;thwugu ongite  ic wolde hit &t;eah fullicor &amp; openlicor of &d;e ongitan. 
 &d;a andsworode se Wisdom &amp; cw&ae;&d;: Genog sweotol his is &t;&ae;tte God is anfeald &amp; untod&ae;lendlic  &t;eah hine dysige men on m&ae;nig tod&ae;len  &t;onne hi dwoliende seca&d; &t;&ae;t hehste god on &d;a s&ae;mran gesceafta. 
 Hw&ae;&t;er &t;u nu wene &t;&ae;t se nauhtes maran ne &t;yrfe se &t;e m&ae;stne anwald h&ae;f&d; &t;isse worulde? 
 &t;a andsworede ic eft &amp; cw&ae;&d;: Ne secge ic no &t;&ae;t he nauhtes maran ne &d;yrfe  for&d;&ae;m ic wat &t;&ae;t nan nis &t;&ae;s welig &t;&ae;t he sumes eacan ne &t;yrfe. 
 &d;a andswarode se Wisdom &amp; cw&ae;&d;: Genog rihte &t;u s&ae;gst; &t;eah hwa anwald h&ae;bbe  gif o&d;er h&ae;f&d; maran  &t;onne be&t;earf se unstrengra &t;&ae;s strengran fultumes. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; ic: Eall hit is swa &t;u s&ae;gst. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; se Wisdom: &t;eah mon nu anweald &amp; genyht to tw&ae;m &t;ingum nemne  &t;eah hit is an. 
 &t;a cw&ae;&d; ic: Swa me &t;inc&d;. 
 &d;a he cw&ae;&d;: Wenstu nu &t;&ae;t se anwald &amp; &t;&ae;t geniht sie to forseonne o&d;&d;e eft swi&d;or to weor&d;ianne &t;onne o&d;re good? 
 &t;a cw&ae;&d; ic: Ne m&ae;g n&ae;nne mon &t;&ae;s tweogan &t;&ae;tte anwald &amp; genyht is to weor&d;ianne. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; he: Uton nu  gif &d;e swa &t;ince  ecan &t;one anwald &amp; &t;&ae;t geniht  don &t;&ae;r weor&d;scipe to  &amp; gereccan &t;onne &t;a &t;reo to anum. 
 &d;a andswarode ic &amp; cw&ae;&d;: Uton &t;&ae;s  for&d;&ae;m hit is so&d;. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; he: Hwe&t;er &t;e &t;onne &t;ince unweor&d; &amp; unm&ae;rlic sio gegaderunc &t;ara &d;riora &t;inga &t;onne &t;a &t;rio bio&d; to anum gedon  o&d;&d;e hw&ae;&d;er hit &t;e eft &t;ince eallra &t;inga weor&t;licos&d; &amp; m&ae;rlicost? 
 Gif &t;u nu &ae;nigne mon cu&d;e &t;ara &t;e h&ae;fde &ae;lces &t;inces anwald &amp; &ae;lcne weor&d;scipe h&ae;fde  swa for&d; &t;&ae;t he na maran ne &d;orfte  ge&t;enc nu hu weor&d;lic &amp; hu forem&ae;rlic &t;e wolde se man &t;incan. 
 &amp; &t;eah he nu &t;a &t;reo h&ae;fde  gif he n&ae;re hliseadig  &t;onne w&ae;re him &t;eah sumes weor&d;scipes wana. 
 &t;a cw&ae;&d; ic: Ne m&ae;g ic &t;&ae;s o&d;sacan. 
 &t;a cw&ae;&d; he: Hu ne is &t;&ae;t &d;onne genog sweotol &t;&ae;t we sculon don &t;a hliseadignesse to &t;&ae;m &t;rim  &amp; don &t;a feower to anum? 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; ic: &t;&ae;t is cyn. 
 &t;a cw&ae;&d; he: Hw&ae;&t;er &t;u nu wene &t;&ae;t se auht bli&d;e sie &d;e ealle &t;as feower h&ae;f&d;? 
 Fifte bi&d; seo blis  &amp; m&ae;g don eall &t;&ae;t he wile  &amp; nanes &t;inges maran ne be&t;earf &t;onne he h&ae;f&d;. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; ic: Ne m&ae;g ic n&ae;fre ge&t;encan  gif he swylc w&ae;re &amp; &t;&ae;t eall h&ae;fde  hwonan him &ae;nig unrotnes cuman sceolde. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; he: Swa&t;eah is to ge&t;encanne &t;&ae;t &d;a fif &t;ing &t;e we &ae;r ymb spr&ae;con  &t;eah hi tonemde sien mid wordum  &t;&ae;t hit is eall an &t;ing  &t;onne hi gegaderede bio&d;; &t;&ae;t is anwald &amp; genyht &amp; forem&ae;rnes &amp; weor&d;scipe &amp; blis. 
 &t;a fif &d;ing  &t;onne hi ealle gegaderade bio&d;  &t;onne bi&d; &t;&ae;t God; for&d;&ae;m &t;a fif eall nan mennisc man fullice habban ne m&ae;g &d;a hwile &t;e he on &t;isse worulde bi&d;. 
 Ac &t;onne &t;a fif &t;ing  swa we &ae;r cw&ae;don  eall gegadorede bio&d;  &t;onne bi&d; hit eall an &t;ing  &amp; &t;&ae;t an &d;ing bi&d; God; &amp; he bi&d; anfeald untod&ae;led  &t;eah he &ae;r on m&ae;nig tonemned w&ae;re. 
 &d;a andsworede ic &amp; cw&ae;&d;: &t;isses ic eom ealles ge&t;afa. 
 &t;a cw&ae;&d; he: &t;eah nu God anfeald sie &amp; untod&ae;led  swa swa he is  se mennisca gedwola hine tod&ae;le&d; on m&ae;nig mid heora unnyttum wordum. 
 &ae;lc mon tiohha&d; him &t;&ae;t to selestum goode &d;&ae;t &t;&ae;t he swi&d;ust lufa&d;; &t;onne lufa&d; sum &d;&ae;t  sum elles hw&ae;t. 
 &t;&ae;t bi&d; &t;onne his god &t;&ae;t he &t;&ae;r swi&d;ost lufa&d;. 
 &t;onne hi &t;onne heora God on swa monige d&ae;las to d&ae;la&d;  &t;onne meta&d; hi nau&t;er ne God selfne ne &t;one d&ae;l godes &d;e hi swi&d;or lufia&d;. 
 &t;onne hi hine selfne don ealne &ae;tg&ae;dere  nabba&d; &t;onne nau&d;er ne hine ealne ne &t;one d&ae;l &t;e hi &t;&ae;rof dydon. 
 For&d;y ne fint &ae;lc mon &t;&ae;t he sec&d; for&d;y he hit on riht ne sec&d;. 
 Ge seca&d; &t;&ae;t ge findan ne magon  &t;onne ge seca&d; eal good on anum goode. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; ic: &t;&ae;t is so&d;. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; he: &t;onne se mon w&ae;dla bi&d; ne wilna&d; he nanes anwealdes  ac he wilna&d; welan &amp; flih&d; &t;a w&ae;dle; ne swinc&d; he nauht &ae;fter &t;&ae;m hu he forem&ae;rost sie  ne nan man eac ne begit &t;&ae;t he &ae;fter ne swinc&d;. 
 He &t;onne win&d; ealle his weoruld &ae;fter &t;&ae;m welan  &amp; forl&ae;t m&ae;nigne weoruldlust wi&d; &t;&ae;m &t;e he &t;one welan begete &amp; gehealde  for&t;&ae;m &t;e his hine lyst ofer eal o&d;ru &t;ing. 
 Gif he hine &t;onne beget  &t;onne &t;inc&d; him &t;&ae;t he n&ae;bbe genog buton he h&ae;bbe eac anwald &t;&ae;rto  for&t;&ae;m&t;e him &t;inc&d; &t;&ae;t he ne m&ae;ge &t;one welan buton anwalde gehealdan. 
 Ne him eac n&ae;fre genog ne &t;inc&d; &ae;r he h&ae;bbe eal &t;&ae;t hine lyst  for&d;on &t;e &t;one welan lyst anwaldes  &amp; &t;one anwald lyst weor&d;scipes  &amp; &t;one weor&d;scipe lyst m&ae;r&d;a. 
 Si&d;&d;an he &t;&ae;s welan full bi&d;  &t;onne &t;inc&d; him &t;&ae;t he h&ae;bbe &ae;lcne willan gif he h&ae;bbe anwald. 
 &amp; ges&ae;l&t; ealne &t;one welan &ae;fter &t;&ae;m anwalde  buton he hine mid l&ae;ssan begitan m&ae;ge; &amp; forl&ae;t &ae;lcne o&d;erne weor&d;scipe wi&d; &d;&ae;m &t;e he m&ae;ge to &d;&ae;m anwealde cuman. 
 &amp; &t;onne gebyre&d; oft  &t;onne he eall wi&d; anwalde geseald h&ae;f&d; &t;&ae;t &t;&ae;t he h&ae;fde  &t;&ae;t he n&ae;f&d; nau&d;er ne &t;one anwald ne eac &t;&ae;t &t;&ae;t he wi&d; sealde  ac wyr&d; &t;onne swa earm &t;&ae;t he n&ae;f&d; fur&t;um &t;a ned&t;earfe ane; &t;&ae;t is wist &amp; w&ae;da. 
 Wilna&d; &t;eah &t;onne &t;&ae;re ned&d;earfe  n&ae;s &t;&ae;s anwaldes. 
 We spr&ae;con &ae;r be &t;&ae;m fif ges&ae;l&t;um; &t;&ae;t is wela &amp; anwald &amp; weor&d;scipe &amp; form&ae;rnes &amp; willa. 
 Nu h&ae;bbe we gereaht be welan &amp; be anwalde  &amp; &t;&ae;t ilce we magon reccan be &t;&ae;m &t;rim &d;e we unareht habba&d;; &t;&ae;t is weor&d;scipe &amp; forem&ae;rnes &amp; willa. 
 &t;a &t;rio &t;incg  &amp; &t;a tu &t;e we &ae;r nemdon  &t;eah hwa wene &t;&ae;t he on hiora anra hwylcum m&ae;ge habban fulla ges&ae;l&d;a  ne bi&d; hit no &d;y hr&ae;&t;or swa  &d;eah hi his wilnigen  buton hi &t;a fif ealle habben. 
 &d;a andsworede ic &amp; cw&ae;&d;: Hw&ae;t sculon we &t;onne don  nu &t;u cwist &t;&ae;t we ne m&ae;gen on &d;ara anra hwylcum &t;&ae;t hehste good habban &amp; &t;a fullan ges&ae;l&d;a  ne we huru ne wena&d; &t;&ae;t ure anra hwelc &t;a fif eall &ae;tg&ae;dre begite? 
 &d;a andsworede he &amp; cw&d;: Gif hwa wilna&d; &t;&ae;t he &t;a fif eall h&ae;bbe  &t;onne wilna&d; he &t;ara hehstena ges&ae;l&d;a. 
 ac he ne m&ae;g &d;a fullice begitan on &d;isse weorulde  for&d;&ae;m &t;eah he ealle &t;a fif ges&ae;l&d;a begite  &t;onne ne bi&d; hit &t;eah &t;&ae;t hehste good ne &t;a selestan ges&ae;l&d;a; for&d;&ae;m hi ne bio&d; ece. 
 &t;a andswarode ic &amp; cw&ae;&d;: Nu ic ongite genog sweotole &t;&ae;t &d;a selestan ges&ae;l&d;a ne sint on &t;isse weorulde. 
 &t;a cw&ae;&d; he: Ne &t;earf nan mon on &d;ys andweardan life spyrian &ae;fter &t;&ae;m so&d;um ges&ae;l&d;um  ne &t;&ae;s wenan &d;&ae;t he &ae;r m&ae;ge good genog findan. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; ic: So&d; &t;u s&ae;gst. 
 &T;a cw&ae;&d; he: Ic wene nu &t;&ae;t ic &t;e h&ae;bbe genog ges&ae;d ymb &d;a leasan ges&ae;l&d;a  ac ic wolde nu &t;&ae;t &d;u wende &t;in inge&t;onc from &t;&ae;m leasum ges&ae;l&d;um; &t;onne ongitst &t;u swi&d;e hr&ae;&d;e &t;a so&d;an ges&ae;l&d;a &t;e ic &d;e &ae;r gehet &t;&ae;t ic &t;e eowian wolde. 
 &t;a cw&ae;&t; ic: Ge fur&d;um &t;a dysegan men ongita&d; &t;&ae;tte fulla ges&ae;l&d;a sint  &t;eah hi &t;&ae;r ne sien &t;&ae;r hi heora wena&d;. 
 &t;u me gehete nu lytle &ae;r &t;&ae;t &d;u hi wolde me get&ae;can. 
 ac &t;&ae;s me &t;inc&d; &d;&ae;t &t;&ae;t bio sio so&d;e &amp; sio fulfremede ges&ae;l&d; &d;e m&ae;g &ae;lcum hire folgera sellan &d;urhwunigendne welan &amp; ecne anwald &amp; singalne weor&d;scipe &amp; ece m&ae;r&d;a &amp; fulle geniht. 
 Ge fur&d;um &t;&ae;t ic cwe&d;e sie sio so&d;e ges&ae;l&d; &t;e an &d;issa fifa m&ae;g fullice forgifan  for&d;&ae;m&t;e on &ae;lcum anum hi sint eall. 
 For&d;&ae;m ic secge &t;as word &d;e for&t;y ic wille &t;&ae;t &d;u wite &d;&ae;t se cwide swi&d;e f&ae;st is on minum mode  swa f&ae;st &t;&ae;t his me nan mon gedwellan ne m&ae;g. 
 &t;a cw&ae;&d; he: Eala  cniht  &t;y &t;u eart ges&ae;lig &t;&ae;t &t;u hit swa ongiten h&ae;fst; ac ic wolde &t;&ae;t wyt spyredon get &ae;fter &t;&ae;m &t;e &t;e wana is. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&t; ic: Hw&ae;t is &t;&ae;t &d;onne? 
 &t;a cw&ae;&d; he: Wenst &d;u hw&ae;&d;er &ae;nig &t;issa andweardana gooda &t;e m&ae;g sellan fulle ges&ae;l&d;a? 
 &d;a andswarode ic &amp; cw&ae;&d;: Nat ic nan wuht on &d;ys andweardan life &t;e swilc gifan m&ae;ge. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; he: &t;as andweardan good sint anlicnessa &t;&ae;s ecan goodes  n&ae;s ful goode  for&t;am hi ne magon so&d; good &amp; ful good forgifan hiora folgerum. 
 &t;a cw&ae;&d; ic: Ic eom genog wel ge&t;afa &t;&ae;s &t;e &t;u s&ae;gst. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; he: Nu &d;u &t;onne wast hw&ae;t &d;a leasan ges&ae;l&d;a sint &amp; hw&ae;t &t;a so&t;an ges&ae;l&d;a sint  nu ic wolde &t;&ae;t &t;u leornodest hu &t;u mihtest becuman to &t;am so&t;um ges&ae;l&d;um. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; ic: Hu ne gehete &t;u me gefyrn &ae;r &t;&ae;t &d;u hit wolde me get&ae;can  &amp; me lyste nu &t;&ae;t swi&d;e georne geheran. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; he: Hw&ae;t sculon we nu don to &t;on &t;&ae;t we m&ae;gen cuman to &t;&ae;m so&d;um ges&ae;l&d;um? 
 Hw&ae;&t;er we scylen biddan &t;one godcundan fultum &ae;g&d;er ge on l&ae;ssan ge on maran  swa swa ure u&d;wita s&ae;de  Plato? 
 &t;a cw&ae;&d; ic: Ic wene &t;&ae;t we scylen biddan &t;one f&ae;der ealra &t;inga; for&d;&ae;m se &d;e hine biddan nyle &t;onne ne gemet he hine  ne fur&t;um ryhtne weg wi&d; his ne areda&d;. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; he: Swi&d;e rihte &t;u s&ae;gst; &amp; ongan &d;a singan &amp; &t;us cw&ae;&d;: Eala  Dryhten  hu micel &amp; hu wunderlic &t;u eart  &t;u &d;e ealle &t;ine gesceafta gesewenlice &amp; eac ungesewenlice wunderlice gesceope &amp; gesceadwislice heora weltst; &d;u &d;e tida fram middaneardes fruman o&d; &d;one ende endebyrdlice gesettest  swa &t;&ae;tte hi &ae;g&t;er ge for&d; fara&d; ge eft cuma&d;; &t;u &d;e ealle &t;a unstillan gesceafta to &t;inum willan astyrast  &amp; &t;u self simle stille &amp; unawendedlic &t;urhwunast. 
 for&t;am &d;e nan mihtigra &t;e nis  ne nan &t;in gelica  ne &t;e nan neod&t;earf ne l&ae;rde to wyrcanne &t;&ae;t &t;&ae;t &d;u worhtest; ac mid &t;inum agenum willan &amp; mid &t;inum agenum anwealde &t;u ealle &t;ing geworhtest  &d;eah &d;u heora nanes ne be&t;orfte. 
 Swi&d;e wunderlic is &t;&ae;t gecynd &t;ines godes  for&t;am&d;e hit is eall an  &t;u &amp; &t;in godnes; &t;&ae;t god na uton cumen to &t;e  ac hit is &d;in agen. 
 Ac eall &t;&ae;t we godes habba&d; on &t;isse worulde  &t;&ae;t us is uton cumen; &t;&ae;t is from &t;e. 
 N&ae;fst &t;u nanne andan to nanum &t;inge  for&t;am&t;e nan cr&ae;ftigra nis &t;onne &t;u  ne nan &t;in gelica; for&t;am &d;u ealle god mid &d;ines anes ge&t;eahte ge&t;ohtest &amp; geworhtest. 
 Ne bisnode &t;e nan man  for&t;am&t;e nan &ae;r &t;e n&ae;s &t;ara &t;e auht o&d;&d;e nauht worhte. 
 Ac &t;u ealle &t;ing geworhtest swi&d;e gode &amp; swi&d;e f&ae;gere  &amp; &t;u self eart &t;&ae;t hehste god &amp; &t;&ae;t f&ae;gereste. 
 Swa swa &t;u self ge&t;ohtest &t;u geworhtest &t;isne middangeard  &amp; his weltst swa swa &t;u wilt  &amp; &t;u self d&ae;lst eall god swa swa &t;u wilt. 
 &amp; ealle gesceafta &t;u gesceope him gelice  &amp; eac on sumum &d;ingum ungelice. 
 &t;eah &t;u &t;a ealle gesceafta ane naman genemde  elle &t;u nemdest togedere &amp; hete woruld; &amp; &t;eah &t;one anne noman &t;u tod&ae;ldest on feower gesceafta; an &t;&ae;ra is eor&d;e  o&d;er w&ae;ter  &d;ridde lyft  feor&t;e fyr. 
 &ae;lcum &t;ara &t;u gesettest his agene sunderstowe  &amp; &t;eah &ae;lc is wi&d; o&d;re genemned &amp; sibsumlice gebunden mid &t;inum bebode  swa &t;&ae;t heora nan o&d;res mearce ne ofereode  &amp; se cile ge&t;rowode wi&d; &d;a h&ae;to  &amp; &t;&ae;t w&ae;t wi&d; &t;am drygum. 
 Eor&d;an gecynd &amp; w&ae;teres is ceald; sie eor&d;e is dryge &amp; ceald  &amp; &t;&ae;t w&ae;ter w&ae;t &amp; ceald. 
 Sie lyft &t;onne is genemned &t;&ae;t hio is &ae;g&t;er ge ceald ge w&ae;t ge wearm. 
 Nis hit nan wunder  for&t;am &d;e hio is gesceapen on &t;am midle betwux &t;&ae;re drygan &amp; &t;&ae;re cealdan eor&t;an &amp; &t;am hatam fyre. 
 &t;&ae;t fyr is yfemest ofer ellum &t;issum woruldgesceaftum. 
 wundorlic is &t;&ae;t &t;in ge&d;eaht  &t;&ae;t &d;u h&ae;fst &ae;g&t;er gedon: ge &t;a gesceafta gem&ae;rsode betwux him  ge eac gemengde &t;a drigan eor&d;an &amp; &t;a cealdan under &t;am cealdan w&ae;tere &amp; &t;am w&ae;tan  &t;&ae;t &t;&ae;t hnesce &amp; flowende w&ae;ter h&ae;bbe flor on &t;&ae;re f&ae;stan eor&d;an; for&t;am&t;e hit ne m&ae;g on him selfum gestandan 
 Ac seo eor&d;e hit helt &amp; be sumum d&ae;le swilg&d;  &amp; for &t;am sype heo bi&d; geleht &t;&ae;t hio grew&d; &amp; blew&d; &amp; westmas bring&d;. 
 for&t;am gif &t;&ae;t w&ae;ter hi ne ge&d;w&ae;nde  &t;onne drugode hio &amp; wurde todrifen mid &t;am winde swa swa dust o&d;&d;e axe. 
 Ne mihte nanwuht libbendes &t;&ae;re eor&t;an brucan ne &t;&ae;s w&ae;teres  ne on nau&d;rum eardigan for cile  gif &t;u hi hw&ae;thwegununga wi&d; fir ne gemengdest. 
 Wundorlice cr&ae;fte &t;u hit h&ae;fst gesceapen &t;&ae;t &t;&ae;t fyr ne forb&ae;rn&d; &t;&ae;t w&ae;ter &amp; &t;a eor&t;an  nu hit gemenged is wi&d; &ae;g&d;er; ne eft w&ae;ter &amp; seo eor&d;e eallunga ne adw&ae;sce&d; &t;&ae;t fyr. 
 &t;&ae;s w&ae;teres agnu cy&d; is on eor&t;an  &amp; eac on lyfte  &amp; eft bufan &t;am rodore. 
 Ac &t;&ae;s fyres agen stede is ofer eallum woruldgesceaftum gesewenlicum  &amp; &t;eah hit is gemenged wi&d; ealle gesceafta; &amp; &t;eah ne m&ae;g nane &t;ara gesceafta eallunga forcuman  for&t;am&t;e hit n&ae;f&d; leafe &t;&ae;s &ae;lmihtigan. 
 Sio eor&t;e &t;onne is hefigre &amp; &t;iccre &t;onne o&d;ra gesceafta  for&t;am hio is nio&d;or &t;onne &ae;nig o&d;ru gesceaft buton &t;am rodore. 
 for&t;am se rodor hine h&ae;f&d; &ae;lce d&ae;g utane  &t;eah he hire nawer ne geneal&ae;ce; on &ae;lcere stowe he is hire emnneah  ge ufan ge neo&d;on.
