 &ae;lc &t;ara gesceafta &t;e we gefyrn &ae;r ymbe spr&ae;con h&ae;f&d; his agenne eard onsundron; &amp; &t;eah is &ae;lc wi&d; o&d;er gemenged  for&d;am&t;e nan &d;ara gesceafta ne m&ae;g bion buton o&d;erre  &d;eah hio unsweotol sie on &t;&ae;re o&d;erre. 
 Swa swa nu eor&d;e is &amp; w&ae;ter sint swi&d;e earfo&d;e to geseonne o&d;&d;e to ongitonne dysgum monnum on fyre  &amp; swa&t;eah hi sint &d;&ae;rwi&d; gemengde. 
 Swa is eac &t;&ae;r fyr on &d;am stanum &amp; on &d;am w&ae;tere  swi&d;e earfo&d;hawe  ac hit is &t;eah &t;ara. 
 &t;u gebunde &t;&ae;t fyr mid swi&d;e unanbindendlicum racentum  &t;&ae;t hit ne m&ae;g cuman to his agenum earde  &t;&ae;t is to &t;am m&ae;stan fyre &d;e ofer us is  &t;yl&ae;s hit forl&ae;te &t;a eor&d;an. 
 &amp; ealle o&d;re gesceafta aswinda&d; for ungemetlicum cile  gif hit eallunga from gewite. 
 &d;u gesta&d;oladest eor&d;an swi&d;e wundorlice &amp; f&ae;stlice  &t;&ae;t heo ne helt on nane healfe ne on nanum eor&d;licum &t;inge ne stent. 
 ne nanwuht eor&d;lices hi ne healt &t;&ae;t hio ne sige  &amp; nis hire &t;eah &t;onne e&d;re to feallanne ofdune &t;onne up. 
 &t;u eac &t;a &d;riefealdan sawla on ge&d;w&ae;rum limum styrest  swa &t;&ae;t &d;&ae;re sawle &t;y l&ae;sse ne bi&d; on &d;am l&ae;stan fingre &d;e on eallum &t;am lichoman. 
 For&t;i ic cw&ae;&d; &t;&ae;t sio sawul w&ae;re &t;reofeald  for&t;am&t;e u&d;witan secga&d; &t;&ae;t hio h&ae;bbe &t;rio gecynd. 
 An &d;ara gecynda is &t;&ae;t heo bi&d; wilnigende  o&d;er &t;&ae;t hio bi&d; irsiende  &t;ridde &t;&ae;t hio bi&d; gesceadwis. 
 Twa &t;ara gecynda habba&d; netenu swa same swa men; o&d;er &t;ara is wilnung  o&d;er is irsung. 
 Ac se mon ana h&ae;f&d; gesceadwisnesse  nalles nan o&d;ru gesceaft; for&d;i he h&ae;f&d; ofer&t;ungen ealle &t;a eor&d;lican gesceafta mid ge&d;eahte &amp; mid andgite. 
 For&t;am seo gesceadwisnes sceal wealdan &ae;g&d;er ge &t;&ae;re wilnunga ge &t;&ae;s yrres  for&t;am hio is synderlic cr&ae;ft &t;&ae;re saule. 
 Swa &d;u gesceope &t;a saule &t;&ae;t hio sceolde ealne weg hwearfian on hire selfre  swa swa eall &t;es rodor hwerf&d;  o&d;&d;e swa swa hweol onhwerf&d;  smeagende ymb hire sceoppend  o&d;&d;e ymbe hi selfe  o&d;&d;e ymbe &t;as eor&d;lican gesceafta. 
 &t;onne hio &t;onne ymbe hire scippend smea&d;  &t;onne bi&d; hio ofer hire selfre; ac &t;onne hio ymbe hi selfe smea&d;  &t;onne bi&d; hio on hire selfre; &amp; under hire selfre hio bi&d; &t;onne &d;onne hio lufa&d; &t;as eor&d;lican &t;ing  &amp; &t;ara wundra&d;. 
 Hw&ae;t &t;u  Drihten  forgeafe &t;am sawlum eard on hiofonum  &amp; him &t;&ae;r gifst weor&d;lice gifa  &ae;lcere be hire geearnunge; &amp; gedest &t;&ae;t hi scina&d; swi&d;e beorhte  &amp; &t;eah swi&d;e mistlice birhtu  sume beorhtor sume unbyrhtor  swa swa steorran  &ae;lc be his geearnunga. 
 Hw&ae;t &t;u  Drihten  geg&ae;derast &t;a hiofonlican sawla &amp; &t;a eor&d;lican lichoman  &amp; hi on &d;isse worulde gemengest. 
 Swa swa hi from &t;e hider comon  swa hi eac to &t;e hionan fundia&d;. 
 &t;u fyldest &d;as eor&d;an mid mistlicum cynrenum netena  &amp; hi si&d;&d;an aseowe mistlicum s&ae;de treowa &amp; wyrta. 
 Forgif nu  Drihten  urum modum &t;&ae;t hi moton to &t;e astigan &t;urh &t;as earfo&d;u &t;isse worulde  &amp; of &t;issum bisegum to &t;e cuman  &amp; openum eagum ures modes we moten geseon &t;one &ae;&t;elan &ae;welm ealra goda; &t;&ae;t eart &d;u. 
 Forgif us &t;onne hale eagan ures modes  &t;&ae;t we hi &t;onne moton af&ae;stnian on &t;e; &amp; todrif &d;one mist &t;e nu hanga&d; beforan ures modes eagum  &amp; onliht &t;a eagan mid &d;inum leohte. 
 for&t;am &d;u eart sio birhtu &d;&ae;s so&d;an leohtes  &amp; &t;u eart sio sefte r&ae;st so&d;f&ae;stra  &amp; &d;u gedest &t;&ae;t hi &d;e gesio&d;. 
 &t;u eart ealra &t;inga fruma &amp; ende. 
 &d;u brist ealle &t;ing buton geswince. 
 &t;u eart &ae;g&d;er ge weg  ge lad&t;eow  ge sio stow &d;e se weg to lig&d;; &d;e ealle men to fundia&d;. 
 &D;a se Wisdom &t;a &d;is leo&d; &amp; &t;is gebed asungen h&ae;fde  &t;a ongan he eft spellian &amp; &t;us cw&ae;&d;: Ic wene &t;&ae;t hit sie nu &ae;rest &t;earf &t;&ae;t ic &d;e gerecce hw&ae;r &t;&ae;t hehste good is  nu ic &d;e &ae;r h&ae;fde gereaht hw&ae;t hit w&ae;s  o&d;&d;e hwylc &t;&ae;t medeme good w&ae;s  hwylc &t;&ae;t unmedeme. 
 Ac anes &t;inges ic &t;e wolde &ae;rest acsian: Hw&ae;&d;er &t;u wene &t;&ae;t &ae;nig &t;ing on &t;isse worulde swa good sie &t;&ae;t hit &d;e m&ae;ge forgifan fulla ges&ae;l&d;a? 
 &d;e ic &d;e ascige &t;y ic nolde &t;&ae;t unc beswice &ae;negu leas anlicnes for so&d;a ges&ae;l&d;a. 
 For&d;y nan mon ne m&ae;g o&d;sacan &t;&ae;t sum good ne sie &t;&ae;t hehste  swa swa sum micel &ae;welm &amp; diop  &amp; irnen m&ae;nege brocas &amp; ri&d;a of. 
 For&d;y mon cwi&d; be sumum goode &t;&ae;t hit ne sie ful good  for&d;&ae;m him bi&d; hw&ae;shwugu wana; &amp; &t;eah ne bi&d; ealles butan  for&d;&ae;m &t;e &ae;lc &t;ing wyr&d; to nauhte gif hit nauht goodes on him n&ae;f&d;. 
 Be &t;y &d;u meaht ongitan &t;&ae;t of &t;am m&ae;stan goode cuma&d; &d;a l&ae;ssan god  n&ae;s of &d;&ae;m l&ae;ssan &t;&ae;t m&ae;ste  &t;on ma &t;e sio ea m&ae;g weor&d;an to &ae;welme. 
 Ac se &ae;welm m&ae;g weor&d;an to ea  &amp; &t;eah sio ea cym&d; eft to &d;&ae;m &ae;welme; swa cym&d; &ae;lc good of Gode &amp; eft to him  &amp; he is &t;&ae;t fulle god &amp; &t;&ae;t fullfremede  &t;&ae;t nanes willan wana ne bi&d;. 
 Nu &t;u meaht sweotole ongitan &t;&ae;t &t;&ae;t is good self. 
 Hwi ne meaht &d;u ge&t;encan  gif nanwuht full n&ae;re  &t;onne n&ae;re nan wuht wana  &amp; gif nan wuht wana n&ae;re  &t;onne n&ae;re nan wuht full? 
 For&t;y bi&d; &ae;nig &t;ing full &t;e sum bi&d; wana  &amp; for&d;y bi&d; &ae;nig &t;ing wana &d;e sum bi&d; full; &ae;lc &t;ing bi&d; fullost on his agnum earda. 
 Hwy ne meaht &t;u &t;onne ge&d;encan  gif on &ae;negum &t;issa eor&d;licena gooda &ae;niges willan &amp; &ae;niges goodes wana is  &t;onne is sum good full &ae;lces willan  &amp; nis nanes goodes wana? 
 &d;a andsworede ic &amp; cw&ae;&d;: Swi&d;e rihtlice &amp; swi&d;e gesceadwislice &t;u h&ae;fst me ofercumen &amp; gefangen  &t;&ae;t ic ne m&ae;g no wi&d;cwe&d;an ne fur&d;um ongean &d;&ae;t &t;encan  buton &t;&ae;t hit is eall swa swa &t;u s&ae;gst. 
 &t;a cw&ae;&d; se Wisdom: Nu ic wolde &t;&ae;t &d;u &d;ohte geornlice o&d; &t;&ae;t &d;u ongeate hw&ae;r sio fulle ges&ae;l&d; sie. 
 Hu ne wast &t;u nu &d;&ae;tte eall moncyn is anmodlice ge&t;afa &t;&ae;t God is fruma ealra gooda &amp; waldend ealra gesceafta? 
 He is &t;&ae;t hehste good  ne n&ae;nne mon nu &t;&ae;s ne tweo&d;; for&d;&ae;m &t;e hi nauht niton betere  ne fur&d;um nauht emngoodes. 
 For&d;&ae;m us s&ae;g&d; &ae;lc gesceadwisnes &amp; ealle men &t;&ae;t ilce andetta&d; &t;&ae;t God sie &t;&ae;t hehste good  for&t;&ae;m&t;e hi tacnia&d; &t;&ae;tte eall good on him sien. 
 for&d;&ae;m gif hit swa n&ae;re  &t;onne n&ae;re he &t;&ae;t &t;&ae;t he gehaten is; o&d;&d;e &ae;nig &t;ing &ae;r w&ae;re o&d;&d;e &ae;lt&ae;wre  &t;onne w&ae;re &t;&ae;t betere &t;onne he. 
 Ac for&d;&ae;m&t;e nan &t;ing n&ae;s &ae;r &t;onne he ne &ae;lt&ae;wre &t;onne he ne diorwyr&d;re &t;onne he  for&d;&ae;m he is fruma &amp; &ae;welm &amp; hrof eallra gooda. 
 Genog sweotol hit is &d;&ae;t &t;&ae;t fulle good w&ae;s &ae;r&d;&ae;m &t;e &t;&ae;t wana. 
 &t;&ae;t is to gelefanne &t;&ae;t se hehsta God sie &ae;lces godes fullast  &t;yl&ae;s we leng sprecen ymb &t;onne we ne &t;yrfen. 
 Se ilca God is  swa swa we &ae;r s&ae;don  &t;&ae;t hehste good &amp; &t;a selestan ges&ae;l&d;a  nu hit is openlice cu&d; &t;&ae;t &d;a selestan ges&ae;l&d;a on nanum o&d;rum gesceaftum ne sint buton on Gode. 
 &t;a cw&ae;&d; ic: Ic eom ge&t;afa. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; he: Ic &t;e healsige &t;&ae;t &d;u gesceadwislice &t;&ae;t ongite &t;&ae;tte God is full &ae;lcere fullfremednesse &amp; &ae;lces godes &amp; &ae;lcere ges&ae;l&d;e. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&t; ic: Ic ne m&ae;g fullice ongitan forhwy &d;u eft s&ae;gst &t;&ae;t ilce &t;&ae;t &d;u &ae;r s&ae;dest. 
 &t;a cw&ae;&d; he: For&d;y ic hit &t;e secge eft  &t;y ic nolde &t;&ae;t &d;u wende &t;&ae;t se God &t;e f&ae;der is and fruma eallra gesceafta  &t;&ae;t him ahwonan utan come his sio hea goodnes &t;e he full is. 
 Ne ic eac nolde &t;&ae;t &d;u wende &t;&ae;tte o&d;er w&ae;re his god &amp; his ges&ae;l&d;  o&d;er he self. 
 for&d;&ae;m gif &d;u wenst &t;&ae;t him ahwonan utan come &t;a good &t;e he h&ae;f&d;  &t;onne w&ae;re &t;&ae;t &d;ing betre &t;e hit him from come &t;onne he  gif hit swa w&ae;re. 
 Ac &t;&ae;t is swi&d;e dyslic &amp; swi&d;e micel syn &t;&ae;t mon &t;&ae;s wenan scyle be Gode  o&d;&d;e eft wenan &t;&ae;t &ae;nig &t;ing &ae;r him w&ae;re o&d;&d;e betre &d;onne he o&d;&d;e him gelic. 
 Ac we sculon bion ge&t;afan &t;&ae;tte se God sie ealra &t;inga betst. 
 Gif &t;u nu gelyfst &t;&ae;tte an God sie  swa swa on monnum bi&d;: o&d;er bi&d; se mon  &t;&ae;t bi&d; saul &amp; lichoma  o&d;er bi&d; his godnes. 
 &t;a gegadera&d; God &amp; eft  &ae;tg&ae;dre gehelt &amp; gemetga&d;: gif &t;u &t;onne gelefst &t;&ae;t hit swa sie on Gode  &t;onne scealt &t;u nede gelefan &t;&ae;t sum anwald sie mara &t;onne his  &t;&ae;t &t;onne his swa gesomnige swa he &t;one urne de&d;. 
 Hw&ae;t  &ae;lc &t;ing &t;e tosceaden bi&d; from o&d;rum bi&d; o&d;er  o&t;er &t;&ae;t &t;ing  &t;eah hi &ae;tg&ae;dre sien; gif &t;onne hwylc &t;ing tosceaden bi&d; from &t;&ae;m hehstan goode  &t;onne ne bi&d; &t;&ae;t no &t;&ae;t hehste good. 
 &t;&ae;t is &t;eah micel syn to ge&d;encanne be Gode  &t;&ae;tte &ae;nig god sie buton on him  o&d;&d;e &ae;nig from him ad&ae;led  for&d;&ae;m&t;e nan wuht nis betere &t;onne he  ne emngod him. 
 Hwilc &t;ing m&ae;g beon betre &t;onne his sceppend? 
 For&d;&ae;m ic secge mid ryhtre gesceadwisnesse &t;&ae;t &t;&ae;t sie &t;&ae;t hehste good on his agenre gecynde &t;&ae;tte fruma is eallra &t;inga. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; ic: Nu &t;u h&ae;fst me nu swi&d;e rihte oferreahtne. 
 &t;a cw&ae;&d; he: Hw&ae;t  ic &t;onne &ae;r s&ae;de &t;&ae;t &t;&ae;t hehste good &amp; sio hehste ges&ae;l&d; an w&ae;re. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; ic: Swa hit is. 
 &t;a cw&ae;&d; he: Hw&ae;t  wille we &t;onne secgan hw&ae;t &t;&ae;t sie elles buton God? 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; ic: Ne m&ae;g ic &d;&ae;s o&d;sacan  for&d;&ae;m &t;e ic his w&ae;s &ae;r ge&t;afa. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; he: Hw&ae;&d;er &t;u hit a sweotolor ongitan m&ae;ge gif ic &t;e sume bisne get ma secge? 
 Gif nu tu good w&ae;ren &t;e ne meahton &ae;tsomne bion  &amp; w&ae;ren &t;eah buto goode  hu ne w&ae;re hit &t;onne genog sweotol &t;&ae;t hiora n&ae;re nau&d;er &t;&ae;t o&d;er? 
 for&d;y ne m&ae;g &t;&ae;t fulle god bion no tod&ae;led. 
 Hu m&ae;g hit bion &ae;g&t;er ge full ge wana? 
 For&d;&ae;m we cwe&d;a&d; &t;&ae;t sio fulle ges&ae;l&d; &amp; god &t;&ae;t hi sien an good  &amp; &t;&ae;t sie &t;&ae;t hehste; &t;a ne magon n&ae;fre weor&d;an tod&ae;lede. 
 Hu ne sculon we &t;onne nede bion ge&t;afan &t;&ae;tte sio hehste ges&ae;l&d; &amp; sio hea godcundnes an sie? 
 &t;a cw&ae;&d; ic: Nis nan &t;ing so&d;re &t;onne &t;&ae;t; ne magon we nanwuht findan betere &t;onne God. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; he: Ac ic wolde giet mid sumre bisne &t;e behwerfan utan &t;&ae;t &t;u ne mihtst n&ae;nne weg findan ofer. 
 swa swa u&d;witena gewuna is &t;&ae;t hi willa&d; simle hw&ae;thwugu niwes &amp; seldcu&t;es eowian  &t;&ae;t hi m&ae;gen mid &t;y aweccan &t;&ae;t mod &t;ara geherendra. 
 Hu ne h&ae;fdon we &ae;r gereaht &t;&ae;t &d;a ges&ae;l&t;a &amp; sio godcundnes an w&ae;re? 
 Se &t;e &t;onne &t;a ges&ae;l&d;a h&ae;f&d;  &t;onne h&ae;f&d; he &ae;g&t;er  se &t;e &t;one &ae;g&t;er h&ae;f&d;. 
 Hu ne bi&d; se &t;onne full eadig? 
 Hu ne wast &t;u nu &t;&ae;t we cwe&d;a&d; &t;&ae;t se bio wis &t;e wisdom h&ae;f&d;  &amp; rihtwis &t;e rihtwisnesse h&ae;f&d;? 
 Swa we cwe&d;a&d; eac &t;&ae;t &t;&ae;t sie God &t;e &t;a godcundnesse h&ae;f&d; &amp; &d;a ges&ae;l&d;a  &amp; &ae;lc ges&ae;lig mon bi&d; God. 
 &amp; &t;eah is an God  se is stemn &amp; sta&d;ol eallra goda; of &t;&ae;m cuma&d; eall good  &amp; eft hi fundia&d; to him  &amp; he welt ealra. 
 &t;eah he nu sie se fruma &amp; se sta&d;ol ealra goodra &amp; ealra gooda  &t;eah is m&ae;nig good &t;e of him cym&d;; swa swa ealle steorran weor&d;a&d; onlihte &amp; gebirhte of &t;&ae;re sunnan  sume &t;eah beorhtor  sume unbeorhtor. 
 Swa eac se mona  swa miclum he lyht swa sio sunne hine gescin&d;; &t;onne hio hine ealne geondscin&d;  &t;onne bi&d; he eall beorht. 
 &d;a ic &t;a &t;is spell ongeat  &t;a wear&d; ic ag&ae;lwed &amp; swi&d;e af&ae;red  &amp; cw&ae;&d;: Is &t;is la wundorlic &amp; wynsum &amp; gesceadwislic spell &t;&ae;t &d;u nu s&ae;gst. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; he: Nis nan wuht wynsumre ne gewisre &t;onne &t;&ae;t &d;ing &t;&ae;t &t;is spell ymbe is &amp; we nu embe sprecan willa&d;; for&d;&ae;m me &t;inc&d; good &t;&ae;t we hit gemengen to &d;&ae;m &ae;rran. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; ic: Hw&ae;t is &t;&ae;t  la? 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; he: Hw&ae;t  &t;u wast &d;&ae;t ic &t;e &ae;r s&ae;de &t;&ae;t sio so&d;e ges&ae;l&d; w&ae;re good  &amp; of &t;&ae;re so&d;an ges&ae;l&d;e cuma&d; eall &d;a o&d;ru good &t;e we &ae;r embe spr&ae;con  &amp; eft to. 
 swa swa of &t;&ae;re s&ae; cym&d; &t;&ae;t w&ae;ter innon &d;a eor&d;an  &amp; &t;&ae;r afersca&d;; cym&d; &t;onne up &ae;t &t;&ae;m &ae;welme  wyr&d; &t;onne to broce  &t;onne to ea  &t;onne andlang ea  o&d; hit wyr&d; eft to s&ae;. 
 Ac ic wolde &t;e nu ascian hu &t;u &t;is spell understanden h&ae;fdest; hw&ae;&t;er &t;u wene &t;&ae;t &t;a fif god &t;e we oft &ae;r ymbe spr&ae;can  &t;&ae;t is anwald &amp; weor&d;scipe &amp; forem&ae;rnes &amp; genyht &amp; blis  ic wolde witan hw&ae;&d;er &t;u wende &t;&ae;t &t;as good w&ae;ren limu &t;&ae;re so&t;an ges&ae;l&t;e  swa swa monegu limu beo&d; on anum men  &amp; weor&d;a&d; &t;eah ealle to anum lichoman. 
 o&d;&d;e &t;u wendest &t;&ae;t hwylc an &t;ara fif goda worhte &t;a so&d;an ges&ae;l&d;e  &amp; si&t;&t;an &d;a feower good w&ae;ren hire good. 
 swa swa nu saul &amp; lichoma wyrca&d; anne mon  &amp; se an mon h&ae;f&d; m&ae;nig lim  &amp; &t;eah to &t;&ae;m tw&ae;m  &t;&ae;t is to &t;&ae;re saule &amp; to &t;&ae;m lichoman  belimpa&d; ealle &t;as &t;&ae;s monnes good ge gastlicu ge lichomlicu. 
 &t;&ae;t is nu &t;&ae;s lichoman good &t;&ae;t mon sie f&ae;ger &amp; strang &amp; lang &amp; brad  &amp; manegu o&t;ru good to eac &t;&ae;m; &amp; ne bi&d; hit &t;eah se lichoma self  for&d;&ae;m &t;eah he &t;ara gooda hwylc forleose  &t;eah he bi&d; &t;&ae;t he &ae;ror w&ae;s. 
 &t;onne is &d;&ae;re saule good w&ae;rscipe &amp; gemetgung &amp; ge&t;yld &amp; rihtwisnes &amp; wisdom  &amp; manege swelce cr&ae;ftas; &amp; swa&t;eah bi&d; o&t;er sio saul  o&d;er bio&d; hire cr&ae;ftas. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; ic: Ic wolde &t;&ae;t &d;u me s&ae;dest get sweotolor ymb &t;a o&d;ru good &t;e to &d;&ae;re so&d;an ges&ae;l&d;e belimpa&d;. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; he: Ne s&ae;de ic &t;e &ae;r &t;&ae;t sio ges&ae;l&d; good w&ae;re? 
 Gyse  cw&ae;&d; ic  ge &t;u &t;&ae;t s&ae;dest &t;&ae;t hio &t;&ae;t hehste good w&ae;re. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; he: Eart &t;u nu get ge&t;afa &t;&ae;tte anweald &amp; weor&d;scipe &amp; forem&ae;rnes &amp; genyht &amp; blis &amp; sio eadignes &amp; &t;&ae;t hehste god  &t;&ae;t &d;a sien eall an  &amp; &t;&ae;t an &t;onne sie god? 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; ic: Hu wille ic nu &t;&ae;s o&d;sacan? 
 &t;a cw&ae;&d; he: Hw&ae;&t;er &t;inc&d; &t;e &t;onne &t;&ae;t &t;a &t;incg sien  &d;e &d;ara so&d;ena ges&ae;l&d;a limu  &t;e sio ges&ae;l&d; self? 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; ic: Ic wat nu hw&ae;t &t;u woldest witan; ac me lyste bet &t;&ae;t &d;u me s&ae;de sume hwile ymb &t;&ae;t  &t;onne &t;u me ascode. 
 &t;a cw&ae;&d; he: Hu ne meaht &t;u ge&d;encan? 
 gif &t;a good w&ae;ron &t;aere so&t;an ges&ae;l&d;e limu  &t;onne w&ae;ron hi hw&ae;thwegu tod&ae;led; swa swa monnes lichoman limu bio&d; hw&ae;thwugu tod&ae;led. 
 Ac &t;ara lima gecynd is &t;&ae;t hi gewerca&d; &ae;nne lichoman  &amp; &t;eah ne bio&d; eallunga gelice. 
 &t;a cw&ae;&d; ic: Ne &t;earft &t;u ma swincan ymbe &t;&ae;t; genog sweotole &d;u h&ae;fst me ges&ae;d &t;&ae;t &d;a good ne sint nanwuht tod&ae;led from &d;&ae;re so&d;an ges&ae;l&d;e. 
 &t;a cw&ae;&d; he: Genog rihte &t;u hit ongitst  nu &t;u ongitst &t;&ae;t &t;a good ealle sint &t;&ae;t ilce &t;&ae;t ges&ae;l&d; is  &amp; sio ges&ae;l&d; is &d;&ae;t hehste good  &amp; &t;&ae;t hehste good is God  &amp; se God is semle on anum untod&ae;led. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; ic: Nis &t;&ae;s nan tweo; ac ic wolde nu &t;&ae;t &d;u me s&ae;dest hw&ae;thwugu uncu&d;es. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; he: &t;&ae;t is nu sweotol &t;&ae;tte eall &t;a good &t;e we &ae;r ymbe spr&ae;con belimpa&d; to &d;&ae;m hehstan goode  &amp; &t;i men seca&t; god genog &t;e hi wena&d; &t;&ae;t &d;&ae;t sie &t;&ae;t hehste good. 
 &t;y hi seca&d; anwald &amp; eac eall o&d;ru good &t;e we &ae;r ymb spr&ae;con  &d;y hi wena&t; &t;&ae;t hit sie &t;&ae;t hehste good. 
 Be &t;y &t;u meaht witan &t;&ae;t &t;&ae;t hehste good is hrof eallra &d;ara o&d;ra gooda &t;e men wilnia&d; &amp; hi lyst  for&d;&ae;m&t;e n&ae;nne mon ne lyst nanes &t;inges buton goodes o&d;&d;e hw&ae;shwugu &t;&ae;s &d;e goode gelic bi&d;. 
 Maniges &t;inges hi wilnia&t; &t;&ae;s &d;e full good ne bi&d;  ac hit h&ae;f&d; &t;eah hw&ae;thwugu gelices goode. 
 For&d;&ae;m we cwe&d;a&d; &t;&ae;t &t;&ae;t hehste good sie se hehsta hrof eallra gooda &amp; sio hior &d;e eall good on hwearfa&d;  &amp; eac &d;&ae;t &t;ing &t;e mon eall good fore de&d;; for &d;&ae;m &t;inge men lyst &ae;lces &t;ara gooda &t;e hi lyst. 
 &t;&ae;t &t;u meaht swi&d;e sweotole ongitan be &t;&ae;m &t;e n&ae;nne mon ne lyst &t;&ae;s &t;inges &t;e hine lyst ne &t;&ae;s &t;e he de&d;  ac &t;&ae;s &t;e he mid &d;&ae;m earna&d;. 
 for&d;&ae;m&d;e he wen&d;  gif he &t;onne lust begite &amp; &t;&ae;t &t;urhtio &t;&ae;t he &t;onne getiohhad h&ae;f&d;  &t;&ae;t he &t;onne h&ae;bbe fulle ges&ae;l&d;a. 
 Hu ne wast &t;u &t;&ae;t nan mon for&d;y ne rit &t;e hine ridan lyst  ac rit for &d;y &t;e he mid &d;&ae;re rade earna&d; sume earnunga? 
 Sume mid &t;&ae;re rade earna&d; sume &t;&ae;t hie sien &t;y halran  sume earnia&d; &t;&ae;t hie sien &d;y cafran  sume &t;&ae;t hy woldon cuman to sumre &t;ara stowa &t;e hi &d;onne to fundia&d;. 
 Hu ne is &d;e &t;onne genog sweotol &t;&ae;tte men nanwuht swi&d;or ne lufia&d; &t;onne hi do&d; &t;&ae;t hehste god? 
 for&d;&ae;m&t;e &ae;lc wuht &t;&ae;s &d;e hi wilnia&d; o&d;&d;e do&d; hi do&d; for&t;y&t;e hi woldon habban &t;&ae;t hehste good on &d;&ae;m. 
 Ac hi dwolia&d; sume on &d;&ae;m &t;e hi wena&d; &d;&ae;t hi m&ae;gen habban full god &amp; fulla ges&ae;l&d;a on &t;isum andweardum godum; ac &t;a fullan ges&ae;l&d;a &amp; &t;&ae;t hehste good is God self  swa swa we oft &ae;r s&ae;don. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; ic: Ne m&ae;g ic no ge&t;encan hu ic &t;&ae;s o&d;sacan m&ae;ge. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; he: Uton l&ae;tan &t;onne bion &t;a spr&ae;ce  &amp; bion unc &d;&ae;s orsorge  nu &d;u swa fullice ongiten h&ae;fst &t;&ae;tte God simle bi&d; untod&ae;ledlic &amp; full good  &amp; &t;&ae;t his good &amp; sio his ges&ae;l&d; him nahwonan utane ne com  ac w&ae;s symle on him selfum  &amp; nu is  &amp; a bi&d;. 
 &d;a se Wisdom &t;a &d;is spell as&ae;d h&ae;fde  &t;a ongan he eft singan &amp; &t;us cw&ae;&d;: Wella  men  wel; &ae;lc &t;ara &d;e freo sie fundige to &t;am goode &amp; to &t;am ges&ae;l&d;um. 
 &amp; se &d;e nu geh&ae;ft sie mid &t;&ae;re unnyttan lufe &t;isses middaneardes sece him freodom hu he m&ae;ge becuman to &t;am ges&ae;l&d;um  for&t;am &t;&ae;t is sio an r&ae;st eallra urra geswinca; sio an hy&d; bi&d; simle smyltu &ae;fter eallum &t;am ystum &amp; &t;am y&d;um urra geswinca. 
 &t;&ae;t is seo an fri&d;stow &amp; sio an frofer erminga &ae;fter &t;am erm&d;um &d;isses andweardan lifes. 
 Ac &t;a gyldenan stanas  &amp; &t;a seolfrenan  &amp; &ae;lces cynnes gimmas  &amp; eall &t;es andwearda wela  ne onlihta&d; hi nauht &t;&ae;s modes eagan  ne heora scearpnesse nauht gebeta&d; to &t;&ae;re sceawunga &t;&ae;re so&d;an ges&ae;l&d;e; ac get swi&d;or hi ablenda&d; &t;&ae;s modes eagan &t;onne hi hi ascirpan. 
 For&t;am ealle &t;a &d;ing &t;e her licia&d; on &t;isum andweardum life sint eor&d;lice  for&t;y hi sint fleonde. 
 Ac sio wundorlice beorhtnes &t;e ealle &d;ing gebirht &amp; eallum welt  nyle &t;&ae;t &d;a sawla forweor&d;an  ac wile hi onlihtan. 
 Gif &t;onne hwelc mon m&ae;ge gesion &t;a birhtu &t;&ae;s heofenlican leohtes mid hluttrum eagum his modes  &t;onne wile he cwe&d;an &t;&ae;t sio beorhtnes &t;&ae;re sunnan sciman sie &t;esternes to metanne wi&d; &d;a ecan birhtu Godes. 
 &d;a se Wisdom &d;a &d;is leo&d; asungen h&ae;fde  &t;a cw&ae;&d; ic: Ic eom ge&t;afa &t;&ae;s &t;e &t;u s&ae;gst  for&d;&ae;m&t;e &t;u hit h&ae;fst gese&d;ed mid gesceadwislicere race. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; he: Mid hu micle feo woldest &t;u nu habban geboht &t;&ae;t &t;u meahte ongitan hw&ae;t &t;&ae;t so&d;e god w&ae;re  &amp; hwylc hit w&ae;re. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; ic: Ic wolde f&ae;gnian mid swi&d;e ungemetlice gefean  &amp; ic wolde mid unarimedum feo gebycgan &t;&ae;t ic hit moste gesion. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; he: Ic hit &t;e &t;onne wille get&ae;can; ac &t;&ae;t an ic &t;e bebiode  &t;&ae;t &t;u &t;eah for &d;&ae;re t&ae;cinge ne forgite &t;&ae;t &t;&ae;t ic &d;e &ae;r t&ae;hte. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; ic: Nese  ne forgite ic hit no. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; he: Hu ne s&ae;don we &t;e &ae;r &t;&ae;t &t;is andwearde lif &t;e we her wilnia&d; n&ae;re no &t;&ae;t hehste good  for&d;&ae;m hit w&ae;re mislic &amp; on swa manigfeald tod&ae;led  &t;&ae;t hit nan mon ne m&ae;g eall habban &t;&ae;t him ne sie sumes &t;inges wana? 
 Ic &d;e t&ae;hte &t;a &t;&ae;t &t;&ae;r w&ae;re &d;&ae;t hehst&ae; god &t;&ae;r &t;&ae;r &t;a good ealle gegadrade bio&d;  swelce hi sien to anum wegge gegoten. 
 &t;onne &t;&ae;r bi&d; full good &t;onne &t;a good ealle &t;e we &ae;r ymb spr&ae;con beo&d; to anum gode gegadrad; &t;onne ne bi&t; &d;&ae;r nanes goodes wana; &t;onne &t;a good ealle on annesse bio&d;  &amp; sio annes bi&d; on ecnesse. 
 Gif hi on ecnesse n&ae;ren  &t;onne n&ae;re hiora swa swi&d;e to girnanne. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; ic: &t;&ae;t is ges&ae;d; ne m&ae;g ic no &t;&ae;s twiogean. 
 &t;a cw&ae;&d; he: &ae;r ic &t;e h&ae;fde ges&ae;d &t;&ae;t &t;&ae;t n&ae;re full good &t;&ae;t eall &ae;tg&ae;dere n&ae;re  for&d;&ae;m is &t;&ae;t fulle good &t;&ae;t eall &ae;tg&ae;dre is untod&ae;led. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; ic: Sw&ae; me &d;inc&d;. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; he: Wenstu nu &t;&ae;t eall &d;a &t;ing &d;e gode sint on &t;isse weorulde for&d;y goode sien &t;e hi h&ae;bben hw&ae;thwugu goodes on him? 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; ic: Hw&ae;s m&ae;g ic elles wenan? 
 hu ne is hit swa? 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; he: &t;u scealt &t;eah gelyfan &d;&ae;t sio annes &amp; sio goodnes an &d;ing sie. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; ic: Ne m&ae;g ic &t;&ae;s o&d;sacan. 
 &t;a cw&ae;&d; he: Hu ne meaht &t;u ge&t;encan &t;&ae;t &ae;lc &t;ing m&ae;g bion  ge on &t;isse weorulde ge on &t;&ae;re toweardan  &t;a hwile &t;e hit untod&ae;led bi&d;? 
 &t;onne ne bi&d; hit eallunga swa swa hit &ae;r w&ae;s. 
 &t;a cw&ae;&d; ic: Sege me &t;&ae;t sweotolor; ne m&ae;g ic fullice ongitan &ae;fter hwam &t;u spyrast. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; he: Wast &t;u hw&ae;t mon sie? 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; ic: Ic wat &t;&ae;t hit bi&d; sawl &amp; lichoma. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; he: Hw&ae;t  &t;u wast &t;&ae;t hit bi&d; mon  &t;a hwile &t;e sio saul &amp; se lichoma untod&ae;lde bio&d;; ne bi&d; hit nan mon si&d;&d;an hi tod&ae;lde bio&d;. 
 Swa eac se lichoma bi&d; lichoma &t;a hwile &t;e he his limu ealle h&ae;f&d;; gif he &t;onne hwilc lim forlyst  &t;onne ne bi&d; he eall swa he &ae;r w&ae;s. 
 &t;&ae;t ilce &t;u meaht ge&t;encan be &ae;lcum &t;inge  &t;&ae;t nan &t;ing ne bi&d; swilce hit w&ae;s si&d;&d;an hit wanian ongin&d;. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; ic: Nu ic hit wat. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; he: Wenst &t;u hw&ae;&d;er &ae;nig gesceaft sie &t;e hire willum nylle ealne weg bion  ac wille hire agnum willum forweor&d;an? 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; ic: Ne m&ae;g ic nane cwuce wuht ongitan &t;ara &t;e wite hw&ae;t hit wille  o&d;&d;e hw&ae;t hit nylle  &t;e ungened lyste forweor&d;an. 
 for&d;&ae;m&t;e &ae;lc wuht wolde bion hal &amp; libban  &t;ara &t;e me cwuco &d;inc&d;; bute ic nat be treowum &amp; be wyrtum  &amp; be swelcum gesceaftum swelce nane sawle nabba&d;. 
 &d;a smearcode he &amp; cw&ae;&d;: Ne &t;earft &t;u no be &t;&ae;m gesceaftum tweogan &t;on ma &t;e be &d;&ae;m o&d;rum. 
 Hu ne meaht &t;u gesion &t;&ae;t &ae;lc wyrt &amp; &ae;lc wudu wile weaxan on &t;&ae;m lande selest &t;e him betst gerist &amp; him gecynde bi&d; &amp; gewunlic  &amp; &t;&ae;r &t;&ae;r hit gefret &t;&ae;t hit hra&d;ost weaxan m&ae;g &amp; latost wealowian? 
 Sumra wyrta o&d;&d;e sumes wuda eard bi&d; on dunum  sumra on merscum  sumra on morum  sumra on cludum  sumra on barum sondum. 
 Nim &d;onne swa wuda swa wyrt  swa hw&ae;&d;er swa &t;u wille  of &t;&ae;re stowe &t;e his eard &amp; &ae;&t;elo bi&d; on to wexanne  &amp; sete on ungecynde stowe him; &t;onne ne gegrew&d; hit &t;&ae;r nauht  ac forseara&d;. 
 for&d;&ae;m &ae;lces landes gecynd is &t;&ae;t hit him gelica wyrta &amp; gelicne wudu tydre  &amp; hit swa de&d;. 
 Fri&d;a&d; &amp; fyr&d;ra&d; swi&d;e georne  swa lange swa hiora gecynd bi&d; &t;&ae;t hi growan moton. 
 Hw&ae;t wenst &t;u  forhwy &ae;lc s&ae;d creope inon &t;a eor&d;an  &amp; to ci&d;um &amp; to wyrtrumum weor&d;e on &t;&ae;re eor&d;an  buton for&d;y &t;e hi tiohhia&d; &t;&ae;t se stemn &amp; se helm mote &t;y f&ae;stor &amp; &t;e leng stondan? 
 Hwy ne meaht &t;u ongitan  &t;eah &t;u hit gesion ne m&ae;ge  &t;&ae;t eall se d&ae;l se &d;e &t;&ae;s treowes on twelf mon&d;um gewex&d;  &t;&ae;t he ongin&d; of &t;&ae;m wyrtrumum &amp; swa upweardes grew&d; o&d; &d;one stemn  &amp; si&d;&d;an andlang &t;&ae;s pi&d;an  &amp; andlang &t;&ae;re rinde o&d; &d;one helm  &amp; si&d;&d;an &ae;fter &t;&ae;m bogum  o&d;&d;&ae;t hit ut aspringe&d; on leafum &amp; on blostmum &amp; on bledum? 
 Hwi ne meaht &t;u ongitan &t;&ae;tte &ae;lc wuht cwuces bi&d; innanweard hnescost &amp; unbrocheardost? 
 Hw&ae;t  &t;u meht gesion hu &t;&ae;t treow bi&d; utan gescerped &amp; bew&ae;fed mid &t;&ae;re rinde wi&d; &d;one winter &amp; wi&d; &d;a stearcan stormas &amp; eac wi&d; &t;&ae;re sunnan h&ae;to on sumera. 
 Hwa m&ae;g &t;&ae;t he ne wundrie swelcra gesceafta ures scyppendes  &amp; huru &t;&ae;s scyppendes? 
 &amp; &t;eah we his nu wundrigen  hwilc ure m&ae;g areccan medemlice ures scyppendes willan &amp; anwald  hu his gesceafta wexa&d; &amp; eft wania&d;  &t;onne &t;&ae;s tima cym&d;  &amp; of hiora s&ae;de wior&d;a&d; eft geedniwode  swylce hi &t;onne weor&d;en to edsceafte? 
 Hw&ae;t  hi &t;onne eft bio&d;  &amp; eac hw&ae;thwugu anlice bio&d; swilce hi a bion  for&d;&ae;m hi &ae;lce geare weor&d;a&d; to edsceafte. 
 Hw&ae;&t;er &t;u giet ongite &t;&ae;t &d;a uncwe&d;endan gesceafta wilnodon to bionne on ecnesse swa ilce swa men  gif hi meahten? 
 Hw&ae;&d;er &t;u nu ongite forhwy &t;&ae;t fyr fundige up  &amp; sio eor&d;e ofdune? 
 Forhwy is &t;&ae;t buton for&t;y&d;e God gesceop his eard up &amp; hire ofdune; for&d;y fundia&d; &ae;lc gesceaft &t;ider swi&d;ost &t;ider his eard &amp; his h&ae;lo swi&d;ost bio&d;  &amp; flih&d; &t;&ae;tte him wi&d;erweard bi&d; &amp; ungebyrde &amp; ungelic. 
 Hw&ae;t  &t;a stanas  for&d;&ae;m hi sint stillre gecynde &amp; heardre  bio&d; earfo&d;e to ted&ae;lenne; &amp; eac unea&d;e tosomne cuma&d;  gif hi tod&ae;lde weor&t;a&d;. 
 Gif &t;u &t;onne &ae;nne stan toclifst  ne wyr&d; he n&ae;fre gegadrod swa he &ae;r w&ae;s; ac &t;&ae;t w&ae;ter &amp; sio lyft bio&d; hwene hnescran gecynde; hi bio&d; swi&d;e e&d;e to ted&ae;lenne  ac hi bio&d; eft sona &ae;tg&ae;dre. 
 &t;&ae;t fyr &t;onne ne m&ae;g n&ae;fre weor&d;an tod&ae;led. 
 Ic s&ae;de &t;eah nu hwene &ae;r &t;&ae;tte nanwuht his agenum willum nolde forweor&d;an; ac ic eom nu ma ymb &t;&ae;t gecynd &t;onne ymb &t;one willan  for&d;&ae;m hi hwilum willa&d; on tu. 
 &t;u meaht witan be manegum &t;ingum &t;&ae;t &t;&ae;t gecynd is swi&d;e micel; is &t;&ae;t formicel gecynd &d;&ae;t urum lichoman cym&d; eall his m&ae;gen of &d;&ae;m mete &t;e we &t;igga&d;  &amp; &t;eah f&ae;r&d; se mete ut &t;urh &t;one lichoman. 
 ac his sw&ae;c &d;eah &amp; his cr&ae;ft gecym&d; on &ae;lcre &ae;dre  swa swa mon meolo seft; &d;&ae;t meolo &d;urgcryp&d; &ae;lc &d;yrel  &amp; &t;a syfe&d;a weor&d;a&d; asyndred. 
 Swa eac ure gast bi&d; swi&d;e wide farende urum unwillum &amp; ures ungewealdes for his gecynde  nalles for his willan; &t;&ae;t bi&d; &t;onne &t;onne we slapa&d;. 
 Hw&ae;t  &t;a nytenu &d;onne &amp; eac &t;a o&d;ra gesceafta ma wilnia&d; &t;&ae;s &t;e hi wilnia&d; for gecynde &d;onne for willan. 
 Ungecyndelic is &ae;lcre wuhte &t;&ae;t hit wilnige frecennesse o&d;&d;e dea&d;es  ac &t;eah m&ae;nig &t;ing bi&d; to &t;&ae;m gened &t;&ae;t hit wilna&d; &t;ara &ae;g&d;res; for&d;&ae;m se willa bi&d; &t;onne strengra &t;onne &t;&ae;t gecynd. 
 Hwilum bi&d; se willa swi&d;ra &t;onne &t;&ae;t gecynd  hwilum &t;&ae;t gecynd ofercym&d; &t;one willan. 
 Swa nu wr&ae;nnes de&d;; sio bi&d; &ae;lcum men gecynde  &amp; hwilum &t;eah hire bi&d; forwerned hire gecyndes &t;urh &t;&ae;s monnes willan. 
 Eall sio lufu &t;&ae;s h&ae;med&t;inges bi&d; for gecynde  nallas for willan. 
 Be &t;&ae;m &t;u meaht openlice witan &t;&ae;t se sceppend ealra gesceafta h&ae;f&d; forgifen &ae;nne lust &amp; an gecynd eallum his gesceaftum; &t;&ae;t is &t;&ae;t hi woldon a bion. 
 &ae;lcre wuhte is gecynde &t;&ae;t hit wilnige &t;&ae;t hit a sie be &t;&ae;m d&ae;le &t;e hit his gecynde healdan mot &amp; m&ae;g. 
 Ne &t;earft &d;u no tweogan ymbe &t;&ae;t &t;e &t;u &ae;r tweodest  &t;&ae;t is be &t;am gesceaftum &t;e nane sawle nabba&d;; &ae;lc &t;ara gesceafta &t;e sawle h&ae;f&d;  ge eac &t;a &t;e nabba&d;  willnia&d; simle to bionne. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; ic: Nu ic ongite &t;&ae;t &d;&ae;t ic &ae;r ymbe tweode; &t;&ae;t is &d;&ae;t &ae;lc gesceaft wilna&d; symle to bionne; &t;&ae;t is swi&d;e sweotol on &d;&ae;re tidringe. 
 &t;a cw&ae;&d; he: Hw&ae;&t;er &t;u &t;onne ongite &t;&ae;t &ae;lc &t;ara wuhta &t;e him beon &t;enc&d;  &t;&ae;t hit &t;enc&d; &ae;tg&ae;dere bion  gehal  untod&ae;led? 
 for&d;&ae;m gif hit tod&ae;led bi&d;  &t;onne ne bi&d; hit no hal. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; ic: &t;&ae;t is so&d;. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; he: &t;&ae;t is  eall &t;ing habba&t; &t;eah &ae;nne willan  &d;&ae;t is &d;&ae;t hi woldon a bion; &t;urh &t;one &ae;nne willan hi wilnia&d; &d;&ae;s anes goodes &t;e a bi&d;  &t;&ae;t is God. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; ic: Swa hit is swa &d;u s&ae;gst. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; he: Hw&ae;t  &t;u miht openlice ongitan &t;&ae;t &d;&ae;t is for inlice good &t;ing &t;e ealra wuhta &amp; ealle gesceafta wilnia&d; to habbanne. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; ic: Ne m&ae;g nan mon so&d;re secgan  for&d;&ae;m ic ongite &t;&ae;t ealla gesceafta toflowen swa swa w&ae;ter  &amp; nanne sibbe ne nane endebyrdnesse ne heolden  ac swi&d;e ungereclice toslupen &amp; to nauhte wurden  swa swa we lange &ae;r s&ae;don on &d;isse ilcan bec  gif hi n&ae;fdon &ae;nne God &t;e him eallum stiorde &amp; racode &amp; r&ae;dde. 
 Ac nu for&t;am&d;e we witon &t;&ae;t an wealdend is eallra &t;inga  we sceolon beon nede ge&t;afan  sam we willan sam we nyllan  &t;&ae;t he sie se hehsta hrof eallra goda. 
 &d;a smercode he wi&d; min &amp; cw&ae;&d;: Eala  min cild  ea; hw&ae;t  &t;u eart swi&d;e ges&ae;lig  &amp; ic swi&d;e bli&d;e  for minum andgite. 
 Swi&d;e neah &t;u ongeate &t;a &t;&ae;t riht  &amp; &t;&ae;t ilce &t;&ae;t &t;u &ae;r s&ae;dest &t;&ae;t &d;u ongiton ne mihtest  &t;&ae;s &t;u w&ae;re nu ge&t;afa. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; ic: Hw&ae;t w&ae;s &t;&ae;t &t;&ae;t ic &ae;r s&ae;de &t;&ae;t ic nysste? 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; he: Nu &t;u s&ae;dest &t;&ae;t &d;u nystest &ae;lcre gesceafte ende; ac wite nu &t;&ae;t &t;&ae;t is &ae;lcre gesceafte ende &t;&ae;t &d;u self &ae;r nemdest  &t;&ae;t is God; to &t;am fundia&d; ealle gesceafta. 
 Nabba&d; hi nan god ofer &t;&ae;t to secanne  ne hi nanwuht ne magon ne ufor ne utor findan. 
 &d;a he &t;a &t;is spell as&ae;d h&ae;fde  &t;a ongan he eft singan &amp; &t;us cw&ae;&d;: Swa hwa swa wille dioplice spirigan mid inneweardan mode &ae;fter ryhte  &amp; nylle &t;&ae;t hine &ae;nig mon o&d;&d;e &ae;nig &t;ing mage amerran  onginne &t;onne secan oninnan him selfum  &t;&ae;t he &ae;r ymbuton hine sohte  &amp; forl&ae;te unnytte ymbhogan swa he swi&d;ost m&ae;ge. 
 &amp; geg&ae;derige to &t;am anum  &amp; gesecge &t;onne his anum mode &t;&ae;t hit m&ae;g findan oninnan him selfum ealle &t;a god &t;e hit ute sec&d;. 
 &t;onne m&ae;g he swi&d;e ra&t;e ongitan eall &t;&ae;t yfel &amp; &t;&ae;t unnet &t;&ae;t he &ae;r on his mode h&ae;fde. 
 swa sweotole swa &d;u miht &t;a sunnan geseon  &amp; &t;u ongitst &t;in agen inge&t;anc  &t;&ae;t hit bi&d; micele beorhtre &amp; leohtre &t;onne seo sunne. 
 For&t;am nan h&ae;fignes &t;&ae;s lichoman ne nan un&d;eaw ne m&ae;g eallunga ation of his mode &t;a rihtwisnesse  swa &t;&ae;t he hire hw&ae;thwegu nabbe on his mode; &t;eah sio sw&ae;rnes &d;&ae;s lichoman &amp; &t;a un&t;eawas oft abisegien &t;&ae;t mod mid ofergiotulnesse  &amp; mid &t;am gedwolmiste hit fortio &t;&ae;t hit ne m&ae;ge swa beorhte scinan swa hit wolde. 
 &amp; &t;eah bi&d; simle corn &t;&ae;re so&d;f&ae;stnesse s&ae;d on &t;&ae;re sawle wunigende  &t;a hwile &t;e sio sawl &amp; se lichoma gederode bio&d;. 
 &t;&ae;t corn sceal bion aweht mid ascunga &amp; mid lare  gif hit growan sceal. 
 Hu m&ae;g &t;onne &ae;nig man ryhtwislice &amp; gesceadwislice acsigan  gif he nan grot rihtwisnesse on him n&ae;f&d;? 
 Nis nan swa swi&d;e bed&ae;led ryhtwisnesse &t;&ae;t he nan ryht andwyrde nyte  gif mon acsa&d;. 
 For&t;am hit is swi&d;e ryht spell &t;&ae;t Plato se u&d;wita s&ae;de; he cw&ae;&d;: swa hwa swa ungemyndig sie rihtwisnesse  gecerre hine to his gemynde. 
 &t;onne fint he &t;&ae;r &t;a ryhtwisnesse gehydde mid &t;&ae;s lichoman h&ae;fignesse &amp; mid his modes gedrefednesse &amp; bisgunga. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; ic: Ic eom ge&d;afa &t;&ae;t &t;&ae;t was so&d; spell &t;&ae;t Plato s&ae;de. 
 Hu ne mynegodest &t;u me eac nu tuwa &t;&ae;re ilcan spr&ae;ce? 
 &ae;rest &t;u cw&ae;de &t;&ae;t ic h&ae;fde forgiten &t;&ae;t gecyndelice god &t;&ae;t ic oninnan me selfum h&ae;fde  for &d;&ae;s lichoman hefignesse. 
 &ae;t o&d;rum cerre &t;u me s&ae;dest &t;&ae;t &d;u h&ae;fdest ongiten &t;&ae;t me selfum &t;uhte &t;&ae;t ic h&ae;fde eallunga forloren &t;&ae;t gecyndelice god &t;&ae;t ic oninnan me selfum sceolde habban  for &t;&ae;re ungemetlican unrotnesse &t;e ic h&ae;fde for &d;am forl&ae;tenan welan. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; he: &t;&ae;r &t;u gemyndest &t;a word &t;e ic &t;e s&ae;de on &t;&ae;re forman bec  &t;onne miht &t;u be &t;am wordum genog sweotole ongitan &t;&ae;t &t;&ae;t &d;u &ae;r s&ae;dest &t;&ae;t &d;u nysstest. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; ic: Hw&ae;t was &t;&ae;t  hw&ae;t s&ae;de ic &t;&ae;t ic nyste? 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; he: &d;u s&ae;dest on &t;&ae;re ilcan bec &t;&ae;t &d;u ongeate &t;&ae;tte God weolde &t;isses middangeardes  ac &t;u s&ae;dest &t;&ae;t &t;u ne mihte witan humeta he his weolde  o&d;&d;e hu he his weold. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; ic: Ic geman genog geara min agen dysig  &amp; ic his w&ae;s &ae;r &t;e ge&t;afa. 
 &d;eah ic hit &d;a be sumum d&ae;le ongeate  ic wolde giet his mare &ae;t &t;e geheran. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; he: Ne &d;e nauht &ae;r ne tweode &d;&ae;tte God r&ae;dde &amp; wiolde ealles middangeardes. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; ic: Ne me giet nauht ne tweo&d;  ne nu n&ae;fre ne twio&d;; ic &d;e wille eac sona secgan be hw&ae;m ic hit &ae;rest ongeat. 
 Ic ongeat &t;&ae;t &d;es middangeard w&ae;s of swi&d;e manegum &amp; mislicum &t;ingum gegaderod  &amp; swi&d;e f&ae;ste tosomne gelimed &amp; gefangod. 
 N&ae;ren &d;e hi gegaderode &amp; geradode  swa wi&d;erwearda gesceafta  &t;onne ne wurdon hi n&ae;fre ne geworhte ne eac gegaderod. 
 &amp; gif he hi ne gebunde mid his unanbindendlicum racentum  &d;onne toslupen hi ealla; &amp; n&ae;re no swa gewislice ne swa endebyrdlice ne swa gemetlice hiora stede &amp; hiora ryne funden on hiora stowum &amp; on hiora tidum  gif an unanwendendlic God n&ae;re &t;e heora weolde. 
 &t;one God  &d;&ae;t &t;&ae;t he is  &t;&ae;t ic hate God  swa swa ealle gesceafta hata&d;. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; he: Nu &d;u &t;&ae;t swa openlice ongiten h&ae;fst  ne &d;earfe ic nu nauht swi&d;e ymb &d;&ae;t swincan &t;&ae;t ic &d;e ma be Gode recce. 
 for&t;am &t;u eart nu fulneah cumen in on &d;a ceastre &t;&ae;re so&d;an ges&ae;l&d;e  &t;e &t;u lange &ae;r ne meahtest aredian. 
 Ac wit sculon swa&t;eah secan &t;&ae;t &t;&ae;t wit &ae;r mynton. 
 &t;a cw&ae;&d; ic: Hw&ae;t is &d;&ae;t? 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; he: Hu ne tealdon wit &ae;r &t;&ae;tte genyht w&ae;ren ges&ae;l&d;a  &amp; &t;a ges&ae;l&d;a w&ae;ren God? 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; ic: Swa hit is swa &t;u s&ae;gst. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; he: God ne be&t;earf nanes o&d;res fultomes buton his selfes his gesceafta mid to wealdanne  &t;e ma &t;e he &ae;r &t;orfte to &t;am weorce. 
 for&d;&ae;m gif he &ae;niges fultomes on &ae;negum &t;ingum be&d;orfte  &t;onne n&ae;fde he no self genog. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; ic: Swa hit is swa &d;u segst. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; he: &t;urg hine selfne he gesceop eall &d;ing &amp; ealra wylt. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; ic: Ne m&ae;g ic &t;&ae;s o&d;sacan. 
 &d;a cwae&d; he: &ae;r we &t;e h&ae;fdon &t;&ae;t gereaht &t;&ae;t God w&ae;re &t;urh hine selfne good. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; ic: Ic geman &t;&ae;t &d;u swa s&ae;dest. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; he: &t;urg good God gesceop eal &d;ing  for&d;&ae;m he wilt &t;urh hine selfne ealles &t;&ae;s &t;e we &ae;r cw&ae;don &d;&ae;t good w&ae;re. 
 &amp; he is ana sta&d;olf&ae;st wealdend &amp; stiora &amp; steorro&d;er &amp; helma  for&d;&ae;m he riht &amp; r&ae;t eallum gesceaftum  swa swa good stiora anum scipe. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; ic: Nu ic &d;e andette &t;&ae;t ic h&ae;bbe funden duru &t;&ae;r &t;&ae;r ic &ae;r geseah ane lytle cinan  swa &d;&ae;t ic unea&d;e mihte gesion swi&d;e lytelne sciman leohtes of &t;issum &t;iostrum. 
 &amp; &t;eah &t;u me t&ae;htest &ae;r &t;a duru  ac ic hire ne meahte mare aredian  buton &t;&ae;t ic hire grapode ymbutan &t;&ae;t &t;e ic &t;&ae;t lytle leoht geseah twinclian. 
 Ic &t;e s&ae;de gefyrn &ae;r on &t;isse ilcan bec &t;&ae;t ic nysse hw&ae;t se fruma w&ae;re ealra gesceafta; &t;a gerehtest &t;u me &t;&ae;t hit w&ae;s God. 
 &d;a nysse ic eft ymb &t;one ende  &ae;r &t;u me eft gereahtes &t;&ae;t &d;&ae;t w&ae;re eac God. 
 &d;a s&ae;de ic &t;e &t;&ae;t ic nysse hu he ealra &t;ara gesceafta wiolde; ac &t;u hit me h&ae;fst nu swi&d;e sweotole gereht swylce &t;u h&ae;bbe &t;a duru abroden &t;e ic &ae;r sohte. 
 &d;a andswarode he me &amp; cw&ae;&d;: Ic wat &t;&ae;t ic &d;e &ae;r myndgode &d;&ae;re ilcan spr&ae;ce  &amp; nu me &d;inc&t; &t;&ae;t &t;u ongite swa swa leng swa bet ymbe &t;a so&d;f&ae;stnesse. 
 ac ic wolde git &t;e eowian sume bysne  ac swa sweotole swa sio w&ae;s &t;e ic &t;e &ae;r s&ae;de. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; ic: Hw&ae;t is sio? 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; he: Ne m&ae;g n&ae;nne mon &t;&ae;s twiogean &t;&ae;tte ealra gesceafta agnum willum God ricsa&d; ofer hi  &amp; ea&d;modlice hiora willan wenda&d; to his willan. 
 Be &t;am is swi&d;e sweotol &d;&ae;tte God &ae;ghw&ae;s wealt mid &t;&ae;m helman &amp; mid &d;&ae;m stioro&d;re his goodnesse. 
 for&d;&ae;m&t;e ealla gesceafta gecyndelice hiora agnum willum fundia&d; to cumanne to Gode  swa swa we oft &ae;r s&ae;don on &d;isse ilcan bec. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; ic: Hwi ne m&ae;g ic &t;&ae;s twiogan; for&t;am Godes anweald n&ae;re full eadiglic gif &t;a gesceafta hiora unwillum him herden. 
 &amp; eft &t;a gesceafta n&ae;ren nanes &t;onces ne nanes weor&d;scipes wyr&d;e gif hi hiora unwillum hlaforde herden. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; he: Nis nan gesceaft &t;e tiohhie &t;&ae;t hio scyle winnan wi&d; hire scippendes willan gif hio hire cynd healdan wille. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; ic: Nis nan gecynd &t;e wi&d; hire scippendes willan winne buton dysig mon  o&d;&d;e eft &t;a wi&d;erweardan englas. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; he: Hw&ae;t wenst &d;u? 
 gif &ae;negu gesceaft tiohhode &t;&ae;t hio wi&d; his willan sceolde winnan  hw&ae;t hio meahte wi&d; swa mihtigne swa we hine gereahtne habba&d;? 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; ic: Ne magon hi nauht  &t;eah hi willon. 
 &d;a wundrode he &amp; cw&ae;&d;: Nis nanwuht &t;e m&ae;ge o&d;&d;e wille swa heaum Gode wi&d;cwe&d;an. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; ic: Ne wene ic &t;&ae;t &ae;nig wuht sie &d;e wi&d; winne  buton &d;&ae;t wit &ae;r spr&ae;con. 
 &d;a smearcade he &amp; cw&ae;&d;: Wite geare &d;&ae;t &d;&ae;t is &t;&ae;t hehste god  &d;&ae;t hit eall swa mihtiglice maca&d; &amp; eall &d;ing gesceop &amp; eallum swa gereclice raca&d; &amp; swa e&d;elice buton &ae;lcum geswince hit eall set. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; ic: Wel me licode &d;&ae;t &t;u &ae;r s&ae;des  &amp; &t;ises me lyst nu giet bet; ac me sceama&d; nu &d;&ae;t ic hit &ae;r ne ongeat. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; he: Hw&ae;t  ic wat &t;&ae;t &d;u geherdest oft reccan on ealdum leasum spellum &t;&ae;tte Iob Saturnes sunu sceolde bion se hehsta god ofer ealle o&d;re godu  &amp; he sceolde bion &t;&ae;s heofenes sunu  &amp; sceolde ricsian on heofenum. 
 &amp; sceolden gigantes bion eor&d;an suna  &amp; &d;a sceolden ricsian ofer eor&t;an; &amp; &t;a sceolden hi bion swelce hi w&ae;ren geswysterna bearn  for&d;&ae;m&t;e he sceolde beon heofones sunu  &amp; hi eor&d;an. 
 &amp; &t;a sceolde &t;&ae;m gigantum of&t;incan &t;&ae;t he h&ae;fde hiera rice; woldon &t;a tobrecan &t;one heofon under him; &t;a sceolde he sendan &t;unras &amp; ligeta &amp; windas  &amp; toweorpan eall hira geweorc mid  &amp; hi selfe ofslean. 
 &d;yllica leasunga hi worhton  &amp; meahton ea&d;e seggan so&d;spell  gif him &t;a leasunga n&ae;ren swetran  &amp; &t;eah swi&d;e gelic &d;isum. 
 Hi meahton seggan hwylc dysig Nefrod se gigant worhte; se Nefrod w&ae;s Chuses sunu; Chus w&ae;s Chames sunu  Cham Noes. 
 Se Nefrod het wyrcan &ae;nne tor on &d;&ae;m felda &d;e Nensar hatte  &amp; on &d;&ae;re &t;iode &d;e Deira hatte  swi&d;e neah &t;&ae;re byrig &t;e mon nu h&ae;t Babilonia. 
 &t;&ae;t hi dydon for &t;am &d;ingum &t;e hi woldon witan hu heah hit w&ae;re to &d;&ae;m heofone  &amp; hu &d;icce se hefon w&ae;re &amp; hu f&ae;st  o&d;&d;e hw&ae;t &t;&ae;r ofer w&ae;re. 
 Ac hit gebyrede  swa hit cynn was  &t;&ae;t se godcunda wald hi tostencte &ae;r hi hit fullwyrcan mosten  &amp; towearp &d;one tor  &amp; hiora monigne ofslog  &amp; hiora spr&ae;ce tod&ae;lde on tu &amp; hund seofontig ge&t;ioda. 
 Swa gebyre&d; &ae;lcum &t;ara &t;e win&d; wi&d; &d;&ae;m godcundan anwalde; ne gewyx&d; him nan weor&d;scipe on &d;&ae;m  ac wyr&d; se gewanod &t;e hi &ae;r h&ae;fdon. 
 Ac loca nu hw&ae;&d;er &t;u wille &d;&ae;t wit giet spyrigen &ae;fter &ae;nigre gesceadwisnesse fur&d;ur  nu wit &d;&ae;t funden habba&d; &t;&ae;t wit &ae;r sohton. 
 Ic wene &t;eah  gif wit giet uncru word tosomne slea&d;  &t;&ae;t &d;&ae;r asprunge sum spearca up so&d;f&ae;stnesse &t;ara &t;e wit &ae;r ne gesawon. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; ic: Do swa swa &d;u wille. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; he: Hw&ae;t  n&ae;nne mon nu ne tweo&d; &t;&ae;t God sie swa mihtig &t;&ae;t he m&ae;ge wyrcan &t;&ae;t &t;&ae;t he wille. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; ic: Ne tweo&d; &d;&ae;s n&ae;nne mon &d;e auht wat. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; he: Hw&ae;&d;er &ae;nig mon wene &t;&ae;t auht sie &t;&ae;s &t;e God don ne m&ae;ge. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; ic: Ic hit wat &d;&ae;t nauht nis &t;&ae;s &t;e he don ne m&ae;ge. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; he: Wenstu hw&ae;&d;er he m&ae;ge &ae;nig yfel don? 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; ic: Ic wat &t;&ae;t he ne m&ae;g. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; he: So&d; &t;u s&ae;gst  for&d;&ae;m hit is nauht; &t;&ae;r yfel auht w&ae;re  &t;onne meahte hit God wyrcan; for&d;y hit is nauht. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; ic: Me &t;inc&d; &t;&ae;t &d;u me dwelle &amp; dydre  swa mon cild de&d;; l&ae;dst me hidres &amp; &d;idres on swa &t;icne wudu &d;&ae;t ic ne m&ae;g ut aredian. 
 For&d;&ae;m &d;u a ymbe sticce fehst eft on &d;a ilcan spr&ae;ce &t;e &t;u &ae;r spr&ae;ce  &amp; forl&ae;tst eft &d;a &ae;r &d;u hi geendod h&ae;bbe  &amp; fehst on uncu&d;e; &t;y ic nat nu hw&ae;t &t;u wilt. 
 Me &t;inc&d; &t;&ae;t &d;u hwerfe ymbeutan sume wundorlice &amp; seldcu&t;e spr&ae;ce ymbe &d;a anfealdnesse &t;&ae;re godcundnesse. 
 Ic geman &t;&ae;t &d;u me &ae;r reahtes sum wundorlic spell be &d;am &t;a &d;u me reahtes &t;&ae;t hit w&ae;re eall an ges&ae;l&d;a &amp; &t;&ae;t hehste god  &amp; cw&ae;de &t;&ae;t &d;a ges&ae;l&d;a w&ae;ren on &d;&ae;m hehste goode f&ae;ste  &amp; &t;&ae;t hehste good w&ae;re God self  &amp; he w&ae;re full &ae;lcre ges&ae;l&d;e; &amp; &t;u cw&ae;de &t;&ae;t &ae;lc ges&ae;lig mon w&ae;re God. 
 &amp; eft &t;u s&ae;des &t;&ae;t Godes goodnes &amp; his ges&ae;lignes &amp; he self &d;&ae;t &d;&ae;t w&ae;re eall an  &amp; &t;&ae;t &d;onne w&ae;re se hehsta God; &amp; to &d;&ae;m gode ealla &t;a gesceafta fundia&d; &d;e hiora gecynd healda&d;  &amp; wilnia&d; &t;&ae;t hy to cumon. 
 &amp; eac &t;u s&ae;des &d;&ae;tte God wiolde eallra his gesceafta mid &d;&ae;m stiorro&d;re his goodnesse; &amp; eac s&ae;des &t;&ae;t ealla gesceafta hiora agnum willum ungenedde him w&ae;ren under&d;iodde. 
 &amp; nu on last &t;u s&ae;des &t;&ae;t yfel n&ae;re nauht. 
 &amp; eall &t;is &t;u gereahtes to so&d;e swi&d;e gesceadwislice  buton &ae;lcre leasre r&ae;delsan. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; he: &t;u s&ae;des &ae;r &t;&ae;t ic &d;e dwealde; ac me &d;inc&d; selfum &t;&ae;t ic &t;e nauht ne dwelle  ac &d;e s&ae;de swi&d;e lang spell &amp; wundorlic  &amp; swi&d;e gesceadlice be &d;&ae;m Gode &d;e wit unc gefyrn to geb&ae;don. 
 &amp; nu giet ic tiohhie &t;&ae;t ic &d;e hw&ae;thwugu uncu&d;es gerecce be &d;&ae;m ilcan Gode. 
 Hit is gecynd &t;&ae;re godcundnesse &t;&ae;t hio m&ae;g bion ungemenged wi&d; o&d;re gesceafta buton o&d;erra gesceafta fultome  swa swa nan o&d;er gesceaft ne m&ae;g. 
 Ne m&ae;g nan o&d;ru gesceaft be him selfum bion  swa swa gio Parmenides se sciop giddode &amp; cw&d;: Se &ae;lmihtega God is eallra &t;inga reccend  &amp; he ana unanwendendlic wuna&d;  &amp; ealra &d;ara anwendendlicra welt. 
 For&d;&ae;m &d;u ne &t;earft nauht swi&t;e wundrian &d;eah we spyrien &ae;fter &d;&ae;m &d;e we ongunnon  swa mid l&ae;s worda swa mid ma  sw&ae;&d;er we hit gereccan magon. 
 &d;eah we nu scylen manega &amp; mislica bisna &amp; bispell reccan  &d;eah hanga&d; ure mod ealne weg on &t;&ae;m &t;e we &ae;fterspyria&d;. 
 Ne fo we no on &d;a bisna &amp; on &d;a bispel for &d;ara leasena spella lufan  ac for&d;&ae;m&d;e we woldon mid gebecnan &t;a so&d;f&ae;stnesse  &amp; woldon &d;&ae;t hit wurde to nytte &d;am geherendum. 
 Ic gemunde nu ryhte &t;&ae;s wisan Platones lara suma  hu he cw&ae;&d; &d;&ae;t te se mon se &d;e bispell secgan wolde  ne sceolde fon on to ungelic bispell &d;&ae;re spr&ae;ce &t;e he &d;onne sprecan wolde. 
 Ac geher nu ge&d;yldelice hw&ae;t ic nu sprecan wille  &d;eah hit &t;e gefyrn &ae;r unnyt &t;uhte  hw&ae;&d;er &t;e se ende a bet lician wille. 
 Ongon &d;a singan &amp; cw&ae;&d;: Ges&ae;lig bi&d; se mon &t;e m&ae;g geseon &t;one hluttran &ae;wellm &t;&ae;s hehstan godes  &amp; of him selfum aweorpan m&ae;g &t;a &t;iostro his modes. 
 We sculon get of ealdum leasum spellum &d;e sum bispell reccan. 
 Hit gelamp gio &d;&ae;tte an hearpere w&ae;s on &d;&ae;re &d;iode &d;e &d;racia hatte  sio w&ae;s on Creca rice; se hearpere w&ae;s swi&d;e ungefr&ae;glice good  &d;&ae;s nama w&ae;s Orfeus; he h&ae;fde an swi&d;e &ae;nlic wif  sio w&ae;s haten Eurudice. 
 &d;a ongon mon secgan be &d;am hearpere &t;&ae;t he meahte hearpian &t;&ae;t se wudu wagode  &amp; &t;a stanas hi styredon for &d;y swege  &amp; wildu dior &d;&ae;r woldon to irnan &amp; stondan swilce hi tamu w&ae;ren  swa stille  &d;eah him men o&d;&d;e hundas wi&d; eoden  &d;&ae;t hi hi na ne onscunedon. 
 &d;a s&ae;don hi &t;&ae;t &d;&ae;s hearperes wif sceolde acwelan  &amp; hire saule mon sceolde l&ae;dan to helle. 
 &d;a sceolde se hearpere weor&d;an swa sarig &t;&ae;t he ne meahte ongemong o&d;rum monnum bion  ac teah to wuda  &amp; s&ae;t on &d;&ae;m muntum &ae;g&d;er ge d&ae;ges ge nihtes. 
 weop &amp; hearpode &d;&ae;t &d;a wudas bifedon &amp; &t;a ea stodon  &amp; nan heort ne onscunode nanne leon  ne nan hara n&ae;nne hund  ne nan neat nyste n&ae;nne andan ne n&ae;nne ege to o&d;rum for &d;&ae;re merg&d;e &d;&ae;s sones. 
 &d;a &d;&ae;m hearpere &d;a &d;uhte &d;&ae;t hine &t;a nanes &d;inges ne lyste on &d;isse worulde  &d;a &d;ohte he &d;&ae;t he wolde gesecan helle godu  &amp; onginnan him oleccan mid his hearpan  &amp; biddan &t;&ae;t hi him ageafan eft his wif. 
 &t;a he &d;a &d;ider com  &d;a sceolde cuman &d;&ae;re helle hund ongean hine  &t;&ae;s nama w&ae;s Ceruerus  se sceolde habban &t;rio heafdu; &amp; ongan onf&ae;gnian mid his steorte  &amp; plegian wi&d; hine for his hearpunga. 
 &d;a w&ae;s &d;&ae;r eac swi&d;e egeslic geatweard  &d;&ae;s nama sceolde bion Caron; se h&ae;fde eac &t;rio heafdu  &amp; se w&ae;s swi&d;e oreald. 
 &d;a ongon se hearpere hine biddan &t;&ae;t he hine gemundbyrde &d;a hwile &t;e he &d;&ae;r w&ae;re  &amp; hine gesundne eft &d;onan brohte. 
 &d;a gehet he him &d;&ae;t  for&d;&ae;m he w&ae;s oflyst &d;&ae;s seldcu&d;an sones. 
 &d;a eode he fur&d;ur  o&d; he gemette &d;a graman metena &d;e folcisce men hata&d; Parcas  &d;a hi secga&d; &d;&ae;t on nanum men nyton nane are  ac &ae;lcum men wrecen be his gewyrhtum; &t;a hi secga&d; &d;&ae;t walden &ae;lces mannes wyrde. 
 &d;a ongon he biddan heora blisse; &d;a ongunnon hi wepan mid him. 
 &d;a eode he fur&d;ur  &amp; him urnon ealle hellwaran ongean  &amp; l&ae;ddon hine to hiora cininge  &amp; ongunnon ealle sprecan mid him &amp; biddan &t;&ae;s &d;e he b&ae;d. 
 &amp; &t;&ae;t unstille hweol &d;e Ixion w&ae;s to gebunden Leuita cyning for his scylde  &d;&ae;t o&d;stod for his hearpunga. 
 &amp; Tantulus se cyning &d;e on &d;isse worulde ungemetlice gifre w&ae;s  &amp; him &d;&ae;r &d;&ae;t ilce yfel filgde &d;&ae;re gifernesse  he gestilde. 
 &amp; se ultor sceolde forl&ae;tan &d;&ae;t he ne slat &d;a lifre Sticces &t;&ae;s cyninges &d;e hine &ae;r mid &d;y witnode. 
 &amp; eall hellwara witu gestildon &d;a hwile &t;e he beforan &d;am cyninge hearpode. 
 &d;a he &d;a longe &amp; longe hearpode  &d;a cleopode se hellwara cyning &amp; cw&ae;&d;: Wutun agifan &d;&ae;m esne his wif  for&d;&ae;m he hi h&ae;f&d; geearnad mid his hearpunga. 
 Bebead him &d;a &t;&ae;t he geare wisse &t;&ae;t he hine n&ae;fre underb&ae;c ne besawe  si&d;&d;an he &d;onanweard w&ae;re; &amp; s&ae;de gif he hine underb&ae;c besawe &t;&ae;t he sceolde forl&ae;tan &d;&ae;t wif. 
 Ac &d;a lufe mon m&ae;g swi&d;e unea&d;e o&d;&d;e na forbeodan; weilawei  hw&ae;t  Orpheus &d;a l&ae;dde his wif mid him o&d; he com on &t;&ae;t gem&ae;re leohtes &amp; &d;iostro. 
 &t;a eode &t;&ae;t wif &ae;fter him. 
 &d;a he fur&d;um on &d;&ae;t leoht com  &d;a beseah he hine underb&ae;c wi&d; &d;&ae;s wifes; &d;a losade hio him sona. 
 &d;as leasan spell l&ae;ra&d; gehwylcne mon &d;ara &d;e wilna&d; helle &d;iostro to flionne &amp; to &d;&ae;s so&d;an godes liohte to cumanne  &t;&ae;t he hine ne besio to his ealdan yflum  swa &d;&ae;t he hi eft swa fullice fullfremme swa he hi &ae;r dyde. 
 For&d;&ae;m swa hwa swa mid fulle willan his mod went to &d;&ae;m yflum &d;e he &ae;r forlet  &amp; hi &d;onne fullfreme&d;  &amp; hi him &t;onne fullice licia&d;  &amp; he hi n&ae;fre forl&ae;tan ne &t;ence&d;  &d;onne forlyst he eall his &ae;rran good  buton he hit eft gebete. 
 Her enda&d; nu sio &t;ridde boc Boeties  &amp; onginne&d; sio fior&d;e. 
 &d;a se Wisdom &d;a &d;is leo&d; swi&d;e lustb&ae;rlice &amp; gesceadwislice asungen h&ae;fde  &d;a h&ae;fde ic &d;a giet hwylchwugu gemynd on minum mode &d;&ae;re unrotnesse &t;e ic &ae;r h&ae;fde  &amp; cw&ae;&d;: Eala Wisdom  &d;u &t;e eart boda &amp; forerynel &d;&ae;s so&d;an leohtes  hu wundorlic me &d;inc&d; &t;&ae;t &d;&ae;t &t;u me recst. 
 for&d;&ae;m ic ongite &t;&ae;tte eall &d;&ae;t &t;u me &ae;r reahtes me reahte God &t;urh &d;e  &amp; ic hit wisse eac &ae;r be sumum d&ae;le; ac me h&ae;fde &t;ios unrotnes amerredne  &t;&ae;t ic hit h&ae;fde mid ealle forgiten. 
 &amp; &t;&ae;t is eac minre unrotnesse se m&ae;sta d&ae;l  &t;&ae;t ic wundrige forhwy se gooda God l&ae;te &ae;nig yfel bion  o&d;&d;e gif hit &t;eah bion scyle  &amp; he hit ge&t;afian wille  forhwy he hit &t;onne sona ne wrece. 
 Hw&ae;t  &t;u meaht &d;e self ongitan &t;&ae;t &d;&ae;t is to wundrianne  &amp; eac o&d;er &d;incg me &d;inc&d; giet mare wundor; &t;&ae;t is &t;&ae;tte dysig &amp; unrithwisnes nu rixsa&d; ofer eallne middangeard  &amp; se wisdom &amp; eac o&d;re cr&ae;ftas nabba&d; nan lof ne n&ae;nne weor&d;scipe on &d;isse worulde  ac licga&d; forsewene swa swa miox under feltune. 
 &amp; yfele men on &ae;lcum lande sindon nu weor&t;e &amp; &t;a goodan habba&d; manigfeald witu. 
 Hwa m&ae;g forberan &t;&ae;t he &t;&ae;t ne siofige &amp; swelcre w&ae;f&d;e ne wundrige  &d;&ae;t te &ae;fre swylc yfel geweor&d;an sceolde under &d;&ae;s &ae;lmihtgan Godes anwalde  nu we witon &t;&ae;t he hit wat &amp; &ae;lc good wile? 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; he: Gif hit swa is swa &d;u s&ae;gst  &d;onne is &t;&ae;t egeslicre &d;onne &ae;nig o&d;er broga  &amp; is endeleas wundor  &d;&ae;m gelicost &d;e on sumes cyninges hirede sien gyldenu fatu &amp; selfrenu forsewen  &amp; treowenu mon weor&d;ige. 
 Nis hit no swa swa &d;u wenst; ac gif &d;u eall &d;&ae;t gemunan wilt &t;&ae;t we &ae;r spr&ae;con  mid &d;&ae;s Godes fultume &d;e we nu embe spreca&d;  &d;onne meaht &d;u ongitan &t;&ae;t &d;a godan beo&d; symle waldende  &amp; &t;a yfelan nabba&d; n&ae;nne anwald; &amp; &d;&ae;t &t;a cr&ae;ftas ne bio&d; n&ae;fre buton heringe ne buton edleane  ne &t;a un&d;eawas n&ae;fre ne bio&d; unwitnode  ac &d;a goodan bio&d; symle ges&ae;lie  &amp; &t;a yfelan unges&ae;lige. 
 Ic &d;e m&ae;g eowian &d;&ae;s swi&d;e manega bisena  &d;a &d;e magon getrymian to &d;on &t;&ae;t &t;u nast hw&ae;t &t;u leng siofige. 
 Ac ic &t;e wille nu giet get&ae;can &d;one weg &d;e &d;e gel&ae;t to &t;&ae;re heofonlican byrig &t;e &d;u &ae;r of come  si&d;&d;an &d;u ongitst &t;urh mine lare hw&ae;t sio so&d;e ges&ae;l&d; bi&d;  &amp; hw&ae;r hio bi&d;. 
 Ac ic sceal &ae;rest &d;in mod gefe&d;eran  &d;&ae;t hit m&ae;ge hit &d;e y&d; up ahebban &ae;r &d;on hit fleogan onginne on &d;a heanesse  &t;&ae;t hit m&ae;ge hal &amp; orsorh fleogan to his earde  &amp; forl&ae;tan &ae;lce &d;ara gedrefednessa &d;e hit nu &d;rowa&d;. 
 Sitte him on minum hr&ae;dw&ae;ne; &d;ocrige him on minne weg; ic bio his lad&d;eow. 
 &d;a se Wisdom &d;a &t;is spell areaht h&ae;fde  &d;a ongon he singan &amp; cw&ae;&d;: Ic h&ae;bbe swi&d;e swifte fe&t;era  &t;&ae;t ic m&ae;g fliogan ofer &t;one hean hrof &t;&ae;s heofones. 
 Ac &t;&ae;r ic nu moste &t;in mod gefi&d;erigan mid &t;am fi&d;erum  &t;&ae;t &d;u mihtest mid me fliogan  &t;onne miht &t;u ofersion ealle &t;as eor&d;lican &t;ing. 
 Gif &t;u mihtest &t;e fligon ofer &t;am rodore  &t;onne mihtest &t;u gesion &t;a wolcnu under &t;e  &amp; mihtest &t;e fliogan ofer &t;am fyre &t;e is betwux &t;am rodore &amp; &t;&ae;re lyfte. 
 &amp; mihtest &t;e feran mid &t;&ae;re sunnan betwyx &t;am tunglum  &amp; &t;onon weor&t;an on &t;am rodore  &amp; si&d;&d;an to &t;am cealdan stiorran &t;e we hata&d; Saturnes steorra. 
 Se is eall isig; se wandra&d; ofer o&d;rum steorrum ufor &t;onne &ae;nig o&d;er tungol. 
 Si&d;&d;on &t;u &t;onne for&d; ofer &t;one bist aferod  &t;onne bist &t;u bufan &t;am swiftan rodore  &amp; l&ae;tst &t;onne behindan &t;e &t;one hehstan heofon. 
 Si&d;&d;an &t;u miht habban &t;inne d&ae;l &t;&ae;s so&d;an leohtes. 
 &t;&ae;r ricsa&d; an cyning; se h&ae;f&d; anweald eallra o&d;ra cyninga; se gemetga&d; &t;one bridel &amp; &t;&ae;t gewealdle&t;er ealles ymbhweorftes hiofenes &amp; eor&t;an; se an dema is  gest&ae;&d;&d;ig &amp; beorht; se stior&d; &t;am hr&ae;dw&ae;ne eallra gesceafta. 
 Ac gif &t;u &ae;fre cymst on &t;one weg &amp; to &t;&ae;re stowe &t;e &d;u nu geot forgiten hafst  &t;onne wilt &d;u cwe&t;an: &t;is is min riht e&d;el; hionan ic was &ae;r cumen  &amp; hionan ic was acenned; her ic wille nu standan f&ae;ste; nelle ic nu n&ae;fre hionon. 
 Ic wat &t;eah  gif &t;e &ae;fre gewyr&d; &t;&ae;t &d;u wilt o&d;&d;e most eft fandian &t;ara &t;iostra &t;isse worulde  &t;onne gesihst &t;u nu &t;a unrihtwisan cyningas &amp; ealle &t;a ofermodan rican bion swi&d;e unmihtige &amp; swi&d;e earme wreccan  &t;a ilcan &t;e &t;is earme folc nu heardost ondr&ae;t. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; ic: Eala  Wisdom  micel is &d;&ae;t &amp; wundorlic &t;&ae;t &d;u geh&ae;tst  &amp; ic eac nauht ne tweoge &d;&ae;t &d;u hit m&ae;ge gel&ae;stan. 
 Ac ic &t;e halsige &d;&ae;t &d;u me no leng ne lette  ac get&ae;c me &t;one weg; for&d;&ae;m &t;u meaht ongitan &t;&ae;t me lyst &d;&ae;s weges. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; he: &t;u scealt &ae;rest ongitan &t;&ae;t &d;a goodan habba&d; symle anweald  &amp; &t;a yfelan n&ae;fre nanne  ne n&ae;nne cr&ae;ft; for&d;&ae;m hiora nan ne ongit &t;&ae;tte good &amp; yfel bio&d; symle gewinnan. 
 Gif &d;a goodan &d;onne symle habba&d; anwald  &t;onne nabba&d; &t;a yflan n&ae;fre n&ae;nne; for&d;&ae;m &t;&ae;t good &amp; &t;&ae;t yfel sint swi&d;e unsamwr&ae;de. 
 Ac ic &d;e wolde giet be &ae;g&d;rum &d;ara hw&ae;thwugu sweotolor gereccan  &t;&ae;t &d;u m&ae;ge &d;y bet gelefan &d;e ic &d;e o&d;re hwile recce be &d;&ae;m o&d;rum  o&d;re hwile be &d;&ae;m o&d;rum. 
 Twa &d;ing sindon &d;e &ae;lces monnes inge&d;onc to funda&d;  &t;&ae;t is &d;onne willa &amp; anwald. 
 Gif &d;onne hw&ae;m &d;ara twega hw&ae;&d;res wana bi&d;  &t;onne ne m&ae;g he mid &d;&ae;m o&d;rum nanwuht fullfremman. 
 For&d;&ae;m nan nyle onginnan &t;&ae;t &t;&ae;t he nyle  buton he nede scyle; &amp; &d;eah he eall wille  he ne m&ae;g  gif he &d;&ae;s &d;inges anwald n&ae;f&d;. 
 Be &d;&ae;m &d;u meaht sweotole ongitan  gif &d;u &ae;nigne mon gesihst wilnian &d;&ae;s &d;e he n&ae;f&d;  &d;&ae;t &t;am bi&d; anwaldes wana. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; ic: &t;&ae;t is so&d;; ne m&ae;g ic &t;&ae;s o&d;sacan. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; he: Gif &d;u &d;onne hwone gesihst &d;e m&ae;g don &t;&ae;t &t;&ae;t he don wile  ne &d;e &d;onne nauht ne tweo&d; &t;&ae;t se h&ae;bbe anwald. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; ic: Ne tweo&d; me &d;&ae;s nauht. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; he: &ae;lc mon bi&d; waldend &d;&ae;s &d;e he welt; n&ae;f&d; he nanne anweald &t;&ae;s &d;e he ne welt. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; ic: &t;&ae;s ic eom ge&d;afa. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; he: Hw&ae;&d;er &t;u nu giet m&ae;ge gemunan &t;&ae;t ic &d;e &ae;r reahte; &t;&ae;t w&ae;s &t;&ae;tte &ae;lces monnes inge&d;anc wilna&d; to &t;&ae;re so&d;an ges&ae;l&d;e to cumanne  &d;eah hi ungelice hiora earnien. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; ic: &t;&ae;t ic geman; genog sweotole me is &d;&ae;t ges&ae;d. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; he: Gemunst &d;u &t;&ae;t ic &d;e &ae;r s&ae;de &t;&ae;t hit w&ae;re eall an good &amp; ges&ae;l&d;a; se &t;e ges&ae;l&d;a sec&d;  he sec&d; good. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; ic: &t;&ae;t ic h&ae;bbe genog f&ae;ste on gemynde. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; he: Ealle men ge goode ge yfele wilnia&d; to cumanne to goode  &t;eah hi his mislice wilnien. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; ic: &t;&ae;t is so&d; &t;&ae;t &t;u s&ae;gst. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; he: Genog sweotol &t;&ae;t is &d;&ae;t te for&d;y sint gode men goode  &d;e hi god gemeta&d;. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; ic: Genog open hit is. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; he: &t;a goodan begita&d; &t;&ae;t good &t;&ae;t hi wilnia&d;. 
 &t;a cw&ae;&d; ic: Swa me &d;ync&d;. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; he: &t;a yfelan n&ae;ron na yfele gif hi gemetten &d;&ae;t good &d;&ae;t hi wilnia&d;; ac for&d;y hi sint yfle &t;e hi hit ne meta&d;  &amp; for&d;y hi hit ne meta&d; &d;e hi hit on riht ne seca&d;. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; ic: Swa hit is swa &d;u s&ae;gst. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; he: For&d;&ae;m hit is nan tweo &t;&ae;t &d;a goodan beo&d; symle waldende  &amp; &t;a yflan nabba&d; n&ae;nne anwald; for&d;y &d;a goodan &d;&ae;t god on riht seca&d;  &amp; &d;a yflan on woh. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&t;&d; ic: Se &d;e ne wen&d; &t;&ae;t &d;is so&d; sie  &d;onne ne gelyf&d; he nanes so&d;es. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; he: Hw&ae;&d;er wenstu nu? 
 gif twegen men fundia&d; to anre stowe  &amp; habba&d; emnmicelne willan to to cumenne  &amp; o&d;er h&ae;f&d; his fota anweald &t;&ae;t he m&ae;g gan &d;&ae;r he wile  swa swa eallum monnum gecynde w&ae;re &t;&ae;t hi meahten  o&d;er n&ae;f&d; his fota geweald &t;&ae;t he m&ae;ge gan  &amp; wilna&d; &d;eah to feranne  &amp; ongin&d; creopan on &t;one ilcan weg. 
 hw&ae;&d;er &d;ara twega &t;inc&d; &d;e mehtigra? 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; ic: Nis &t;&ae;t gelic; se bi&d; mehtigra se &d;e g&ae;&d; &t;onne se &d;e criep&d;  for&d;&ae;m he m&ae;g cuman e&d; &d;ider &d;e he wile &t;onne se o&d;er; saga elles &t;&ae;t &d;u wille  &d;&ae;t wat &ae;lc mon. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; he: Swa ilce bi&d; &d;&ae;m goodum &amp; &d;&ae;m yflum; &ae;g&t;er heora wilna&d; for gecynde &t;&ae;t he cume to &d;&ae;m hehstan goode. 
 Ac se gooda m&ae;g cuman &d;ider he wilna&d;  for&d;&ae;m he his on riht wilna&d;  &amp; se yfla ne m&ae;g cuman to &d;&ae;m &t;e he wilna&d;  for&d;&ae;m hi hit on wog seca&d;. 
 Ic nat &d;eah &t;e elles hw&ae;t &d;ince. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; ic: Ne &d;inc&d; me nauht o&d;res of &d;inum spellum. 
 &t;a cw&ae;&d; he: Genog rihte &d;u hit ongitst  &amp; &t;&ae;t is eac tacn &t;inre h&ae;lo; swa swa l&ae;ca gewuna is &t;&ae;t hi cwe&d;a&d; &d;onne hi siocne mon gesio&d;  gif hi hwilc ungef&ae;glic tacn on him gesio&d;. 
 Me &d;inc&d; nu &t;&ae;t &t;in gecynd &amp; &d;in gewuna flite swi&d;e swi&d;lice wi&d; &d;&ae;m dysige. 
 Ic h&ae;bbe nu ongiten &t;&ae;t &d;u eart gearo to ongitanne mina lara; for&d;y ic &d;e wolde gegaderian manigu spell &amp; manega bisna be &d;&ae;m &t;&ae;t &d;u meahte &d;y e&d; ongitan hw&ae;t ic secgan wille. 
 Ongit nu hu unmehtige &t;a yflan men bio&d;  nu hi ne magon cuman &d;ider &d;ider &d;a ungewittigan gesceafta wilnia&d; to to cumanne; &amp; hu micle unmihtegran hi w&ae;ren gif hi his nan gecynde n&ae;fden. 
 Beheald nu mid hu hefigre racentan dysiges &amp; unges&ae;l&d;a hi sint gebundene. 
 Hw&ae;t  &t;a cild  &d;onne hi fur&d;um gan magon  &amp; eac &d;a ealdan ceorlas  &t;a hwile &t;e hi gan magon  wilnia&d; sumes weor&d;scipes &amp; sumre m&ae;r&d;e. 
 &d;a cild rida&d; on hiora stafum &amp; manigfealde plegan plegia&d; &d;&ae;r hi hyria&d; ealdum monnum. 
 &amp; &d;a dysegan nanwuht nella&d; onginnan &d;&ae;s &d;e hi him aw&d;er m&ae;gen to wenan o&d;&d;e lofes o&d;&d;e leana  ac do&d; &t;&ae;t wyrse is. 
 irna&d; hidres &d;idres dwoligende under &t;&ae;m hrofe eallra gesceafta; &amp; &t;&ae;tte &d;a ungewittegan gesceafta witon  &t;&ae;t niton &d;a dysegan men. 
 For&d;y sint &t;a cr&ae;ftas beteran &d;onne &t;a un&d;eawas  for&d;&ae;m&t;e &ae;lc mon sceal bion ge&t;afa  sam he wille sam he nylle  &t;&ae;t se sie anwaldegost &d;e m&ae;g becuman to &t;am hehstan hrofe eallra gesceafta  &t;&ae;t is God. 
 &t;am nis nanwuht beufan ne nanwuht beny&t;an ne ymbutan  ac ealle &t;ing sint binnan him on his anwalde. 
 Se God is swi&d;e to lufianne. 
 Hu ne cw&ae;de &t;u &ae;r &t;&ae;t se w&ae;re an fe&d;e mihtigost se &t;e meahte gan &t;eah he wolde o&d; &d;isse eor&t;an ende  swa &t;&ae;tte nan d&ae;l &t;isse eor&t;an ofer &t;&ae;t n&ae;re? 
 &t;&ae;t ilce &t;u meaht ge&d;encan be Gode  swa swa we &ae;r cw&ae;don  &t;&ae;t se bi&d; meahtegost &t;e to him cuman m&ae;g  for&d;&ae;m he nohwider ofer &t;&ae;t cuman ne m&ae;g. 
 Be eallum &d;issum racum &t;u meaht ongitan &t;&ae;t &d;a goodan bio&d; simle mihtige  &amp; &d;a yflan beo&d; &ae;lces m&ae;gnes &amp; &ae;lces cr&ae;ftes bed&ae;lde. 
 Hwy wenstu &d;onne &t;&ae;t hi forl&ae;ten &d;a cr&ae;ftas &amp; folgien &d;&ae;m un&d;eawum? 
 Ic wene &d;eah &t;&ae;t &d;u wille secgan &t;&ae;t hit sie for dysige &t;&ae;t hi hi ne cunnen tocnawan . 
 Ac hw&ae;t s&ae;gst &d;u &t;onne &t;&ae;t sie forcu&d;re &t;onne sio ungesceadwisnes? 
 hwy ge&d;afia&d; hi &d;&ae;t hi bio&d; dysige? 
 hwy nylla&d; hy spyrian &ae;fter cr&ae;ftum &amp; &ae;fter wisdome? 
 Ic wat &t;eah &d;&ae;t swongornes hi ofsit &amp; hi mid sl&ae;w&d;e ofercym&d;  &amp; gitsung hi ablent. 
 Wit cw&ae;don &t;eah &ae;r &t;&ae;t nanwuht n&ae;re wyrse &t;onne ungesceadwisnes. 
 Ac hw&ae;t willa&d; wit nu cwe&d;an  gif &t;a gesceadwisan habba&d; un&d;eawas &amp; nylla&d; spyrian &ae;fter wisdome &amp; &ae;fter cr&ae;ftum? 
 Ic wat &t;eah &t;&ae;t &d;u wilt cwe&d;an &t;&ae;t wr&ae;nnes &amp; ungemetf&ae;stnes hi ofsitte. 
 ac hw&ae;t is &t;onne unstrengra &d;onne se mon &t;e bi&d; to ungemetlice oferswi&d;ed mid &d;&ae;m tedran fl&ae;sce  buton he eft geswice &amp; winne wi&d; &t;a un&d;eawas swa he swi&d;ost m&ae;ge? 
 Ac hw&ae;t wilt &d;u &t;onne cwe&d;an  gif hwa nanwuht nyle wi&d; winnan  ac mid fulle willan forl&ae;t &ae;lc good &amp; fulg&ae;&d; &d;&ae;m yfle  &amp; bi&d; &d;eah gesceadwis? 
 Ic secge sie unmehtig &amp; eac ealles nauht; for&d;&ae;m swa hwa swa &d;one gem&ae;nan God eallra goda forl&ae;t  buton tweonne ne bi&d; se nauht. 
 Ac hwa swa willna&d; &t;&ae;t he cr&ae;ftig sie  he wilna&d; &t;&ae;t he wis sie; swa hwa swa &d;onne cr&ae;ftig bi&d;  he bi&d; wis  &amp; se &d;e wis bi&d;  he bi&d; good. 
 se &t;e &t;onne good bi&d; se bi&d; ges&ae;lig  &amp; se &d;e ges&ae;lig bi&d;  se bi&d; eadig  &amp; se &t;e eadig bi&d;  se bi&d; god  be &d;&ae;m d&ae;le &d;e we &ae;r reahton on &d;isse ilcan bec. 
 Ac ic wene nu hwonne &t;&ae;t dysige men willen wundrian &t;&ae;s &d;e ic &ae;r s&ae;de; &d;&ae;t w&ae;s &d;&ae;tte yfle men n&ae;ren nauhtas  for&d;&ae;m &t;e &d;ara is ma &t;onne &t;ara o&d;ra. 
 Ac &d;eah hi his nu n&ae;fre ne gelefen  &d;eah hit is swa; ne magon we n&ae;fre gereccan &d;one yflan mon cl&ae;nne &amp; untwifealdne  &d;on ma &d;e we magon hatan o&d;&d;e habban deadne mon for cwucone. 
 ne bi&d; se cwuca &d;onne nyttra &d;e se deada  gif him his yfel ne hreow&d;; ac se &t;e ungereclice liofa&d; &amp; his gecynd nyle healdan  ne bi&d; se nauht. 
 Ic wene &t;eah &t;&ae;t &d;u wille cwe&d;an &t;&ae;t hit ne sie ealles swa gelic  &d;&ae;t se yfla m&ae;ge don yfel &d;eah he good ne m&ae;ge  &amp; se deada ne m&ae;ge nau&d;er don. 
 ac ic &d;e secge &t;&ae;t se anwald &d;ara yflena ne cym&d; of nanum cr&ae;fte  ac of un&d;eawum; ac gif &d;a yflan symle goode w&ae;ren  &t;onne ne dyden hi nan yfel. 
 Ne bio&d; &d;&ae;t nane mehta &t;&ae;t mon m&ae;ge yfel don  ac bio&d; unmeahta; gif &t;&ae;t so&d; is &t;&ae;t we &ae;r gefyrn reahton  &t;&ae;t &t;&ae;t yfel nauht ne sie  &d;onne ne wyrc&d; se nauht  se &d;e yfel wyrc&d;. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; ic: Genog so&d; &t;&ae;t is &t;&ae;t &d;u s&ae;gst. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; he: Hu ne reahton we &ae;r &t;&ae;t nanwuht n&ae;re mehtigra &d;onne &t;&ae;t hehste good? 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; ic: Swa hit is swa &d;u s&ae;gst. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; he: Ne hit &t;eah ne m&ae;g nan yfel don. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; ic: &d;&ae;t is so&d;. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; he: Hw&ae;&d;er &ae;ni mon wene &t;&ae;t &ae;nig mon sie swa meahtig &t;&ae;t he m&ae;ge don eall &d;&ae;t &d;&ae;t he wille? 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; ic: Ne wen&d; &d;&ae;s nan mon &t;e his gewit h&ae;f&d;. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; he: Hw&ae;t  yfle men magon &d;eah yfel don. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; ic: Eala  &d;&ae;r hi ne meahton. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; he: Hit is sweotol &t;&ae;t hi magon don yfel  &amp; ne magon nan good; &t;&ae;t is for&d;&ae;m&t;e &t;&ae;t yfel nis nauht; ac &t;a goodan  gif hi fulne anwald habba&d;  hi magon don to goode &t;&ae;t &t;&ae;t hi willa&d;. 
 For&d;y is se fulla anwald to tellanne to &d;&ae;m hehstum goodum  for&d;&ae;m &ae;g&t;er ge se anwald ge &t;a o&d;ru good &amp; &d;a cr&ae;ftas &d;e we longe &ae;r nemdon sindon f&ae;ste on &d;&ae;m hehstan goode. 
 Swa swa &ae;lces huses wah bi&d; f&ae;st &ae;g&d;er ge on &d;&ae;re flore ge on &d;&ae;m hrofe  swa bi&d; &ae;lc good on Gode f&ae;st; for&d;&ae;m he is &ae;lces godes &ae;g&d;er ge hrof ge flor. 
 &d;y is a to wilnianne &t;&ae;s anwaldes &t;&ae;t mon m&ae;ge good don; for&d;&ae;m &d;&ae;t is se betsta anwald &t;&ae;t mon m&ae;ge &amp; wille wel don  swa l&ae;ssan spedum swa maran  sw&ae;&d;er he h&ae;bbe. 
 For&d;&ae;m swa hwa swa wilna&d; good to donne  he wilna&d; good to habbanne &amp; mid goode to bionne. 
 For&d;y is se Platones cwide genog so&d; &t;e he cw&ae;&d;: &d;a wisan ane magon don to goode &t;&ae;t hi wilnia&d;; &d;a yflan magon onginnan &t;&ae;t hi willa&d;. 
 Ic nat nu &d;eah &d;u wille cwe&d;an &t;&ae;t &t;a goodan onginnen hwilum &t;&ae;t hi ne magon for&d;brengan; ac ic cwe&d;e &t;&ae;t hi hit bringa&d; symle for&d;. 
 &d;eah hi &d;&ae;t weorc ne m&ae;gen fullfremman  hi habba&d; &d;eah fullne willan  &amp; se untweofealda willa bi&d; to tellanne for fullfremed weorc. 
 For&d;&ae;m he n&ae;fre ne forlist &d;&ae;m leanum o&d;&d;e her o&d;&d;e &d;&ae;r o&d;&d;e &ae;g&d;er. 
 &t;eah willa&d; &d;a yflan wircan &t;&ae;t &t;&ae;t hi lyst  &d;eah hit nyt ne sie; ne forleosa&d; hi eac &d;one willan  ac habba&t; his wite o&d;&d;e her o&d;&d;e elleshw&ae;r o&d;&d;e &ae;g&d;er; se yfla willa to donne hiora welt. 
 For&d;y hi ne magon begitan &t;&ae;t good &t;&ae;t hi wilnia&d;  for&d;y hi hit &d;urg &d;one willan seca&d;  nales &t;urg rihtne weg. 
 Se yfla willa n&ae;f&d; n&ae;nne geferscipe wi&d; &t;a ges&ae;l&d;a. 
 &d;a se Wisdom &d;a &d;is spell areaht h&ae;fde  &d;a ongan he eft singan &amp; &t;us cw&ae;&d;: Geher nu an spell be &t;am ofermodum &amp; &t;am unrihtwisum cyningum. 
 &t;a we gesio&d; sittan on &t;am hehstan heahsetlum; &t;a scina&d; on manegra cynna hr&ae;glum  &amp; beo&d; uton ymbstandene mid miclon geferscipe hiora &t;egna. 
 &amp; &t;a bio&d; mid fetlum &amp; mid gyldenum hyltsweordum &amp; mid manigfealdum heregeatwum gehyrste  &amp; &t;reatia&d; eal moncynn mid hiora &t;rymme. 
 &amp; se &t;e hiora welt ne myrn&d; nau&t;er ne friend ne fiend &t;e ma &t;e wedende hund  ac bio&d; swi&d;e ungefr&ae;glice up ahafen on his mode for &t;am ungemetlican anwealde. 
 Ac gif him mon &t;onne awint of &t;a cla&t;as  &amp; him oftih&d; &t;ara &t;enunga &amp; &t;&ae;s anwealdes  &t;onne miht &t;u geseon &t;&ae;t he bio&d; swi&d;e anlic &t;ara his &t;egna sumum &t;e him &t;ar &t;enia&d;  buton he forcu&d;ra sie. 
 &amp; gif him nu weas gebyre&d; &t;&ae;t him wyr&d; sume hwile &t;ara &t;enunga oftohen  &amp; &t;ara cla&t;a  &amp; &t;as anwealdes  &t;onne &t;inc&d; him &t;&ae;t he sie on carcerne gebroht  o&d;&d;e on racentum. 
 For&t;am of &t;am unm&ae;tan &amp; &t;am ungemetlican gegerelan  of &t;am swetmettum &amp; of mistlicum dryncum &t;&ae;s li&t;es onw&ae;cna&d; sio wode &t;rag &t;&ae;re wr&ae;nnesse  &amp; gedref&d; hiora mod swi&d;e swi&d;lice. 
 &t;onne weaxa&d; eac &t;a ofermetta &amp; unge&t;w&ae;rnes; &amp; &t;onne hi weor&d;a&d; gebolgen  &t;onne wyr&d; &t;&ae;t mod beswungen mid &t;am welme &t;&ae;re hatheortnesse  o&d;&d;&ae;t hi weor&t;a&d; ger&ae;pte mid &t;&ae;re unrotnesse  &amp; swa geh&ae;fte. 
 Si&d;&d;an &t;&ae;t &t;onne gedon bi&d;  &d;onne ongin&d; him leogan se tohopa &t;&ae;re wr&ae;ce  &amp; swa hw&ae;s swa his irsung wilna&d;  &t;onne gehet him &t;&ae;s his reccelest. 
 Ic &t;e s&ae;de gefyrn &ae;r on &t;isse ilcan bec &t;&ae;t ealle gesceafta willnodon sumes godes for gecynde; ac &t;a unrithwisan cyngas ne magon nan god don  for&t;am ic &t;e nu s&ae;de. 
 Nis &t;&ae;t nan wundor  for&t;am hi hi under&t;ioda&d; eallum &t;am un&t;eawum &t;e ic &t;e &ae;r nemde. 
 Sceal &d;onne nede to &t;ara hlaforda dome &t;e he hine &ae;r under&t;eodde  &amp; &t;&ae;tte wyrse is  &t;&ae;t he him nyle fur&d;um wi&d; winnan. 
 &t;&ae;r he hit a anginnan wolde  &amp; &t;onne on &t;am gewinne &t;urhwunian ne mihte  &t;onne n&ae;fde he his nane scylde. 
 &D;a se Wisdom &d;a &d;is leo&d; asungen h&ae;fde  &t;a ongon he eft spellian &amp; &t;us cw&ae;&d;: Gesihst &t;u nu on hu miclum &amp; on hu diopum &amp; on hu &t;iostrum horosea&d;a &t;ara un&d;eawa &d;a yfelwillendan sticia&d;  &amp; hu &d;a goodan scina&d; beorhtor &t;onne sunne? 
 For&d;&ae;m &t;a goodan n&ae;fre ne beo&d; bed&ae;lde &t;ara edleana hiora goodes  ne &d;a yflan n&ae;fre &t;ara wita &d;e hi geearniga&d;. 
 &ae;lc &d;ing &d;e on &t;isse worulde gedon bi&d; h&ae;f&d; edlean; wyrce hwa &t;&ae;t &d;&ae;t he wyrce  o&d;&d;e do &t;&ae;t he do  a he h&ae;f&d; &t;&ae;t &t;&ae;t he geearna&d;. 
 Nis &t;&ae;t eac nauht unriht; swa swa gio Romana &t;eaw w&ae;s  &amp; giet is on manegum &t;iodum  &t;&ae;t mon heh&d; &ae;nne heafodbeag gyldenne &ae;t sumes &ae;rneweges ende. 
 f&ae;r&d; &d;onne micel folc to  &amp; yrna&d; ealle endemes  &d;a &d;e hiora &ae;rninge trewa&d;. 
 &amp; swa hwelc swa &ae;rest to &t;&ae;m beage cym&d;  &t;onne mot se hine habban him. 
 &ae;lc wilna&d; &t;&ae;t he scyle &ae;rest to cuman &amp; hine habban  ac anum he &t;eah gebyre&d;. 
 Swa de&d; eall moncyn on &d;is andweardan life; irna&d; &amp; onetta&d; &amp; wilnia&d; ealle &t;&ae;s hehstan goodes; ac hit nis nanum anum men getiohhod  ac is eallum monnum. 
 For&d;&ae;m is &ae;lcum &d;earf &t;&ae;t he higie ealle m&ae;gene &ae;fter &d;&ae;re mede; &d;&ae;re mede ne wyr&d; n&ae;fre nan good man bed&ae;led. 
 Ne m&ae;g hine mon no mid rihte hatan se gooda  gif he bi&d; &d;&ae;s hehstan goodes bed&ae;led  for&d;&ae;m nan good &d;eaw ne bi&d; buton goodum edleanum. 
 Don &t;a yflan &t;&ae;t &t;&ae;t hi don  symle bi&d; se beag goodes edleanes &d;&ae;m godum gehealden on ecnesse. 
 Ne m&ae;g &t;ara yflena yfel &t;a goodan beniman heora goodes &amp; hiora wlites; ac gif hi &d;&ae;t good buton him selfum h&ae;fden  &d;onne meahte hi mon his beniman  o&d;er twega  o&d;&d;e se &t;e hit &ae;r sealde  o&d;&d;e o&d;er mon. 
 Ac &d;onne forlyst good man his leanum &d;onne he his good forl&ae;t. 
 Ongit nu &t;&ae;tte &ae;lcum men his agen good gif&d; good edlean  &t;&ae;t good &t;&ae;tte oninnan him selfum bi&d;. 
 Hwa wisra manna wile cwe&d;an &t;&ae;t &ae;nig god man sie bed&ae;led &t;&ae;s hehstan goodes  for&d;&ae;m he symle &ae;fter &t;&ae;m swinc&d;? 
 Ac gemun &d;u symle &t;&ae;s miclan &amp; &t;&ae;s f&ae;gran edleanes  for&d;&ae;m &t;&ae;t edlean is ofer eal o&d;ru lean to lufianne; &amp; do &d;&ae;s lean to &d;&ae;m forsprecenan goodum &t;e ic &t;e &ae;r tealde on &t;&ae;re &t;riddan bec. 
 &t;onne hi &t;onne gegaderudu bio&d;  &d;onne meaht &t;u &t;onne ongitan &t;&ae;t &d;a ges&ae;l&d;a &amp; &t;&ae;t hehste good bi&d; eall an  &amp; &t;&ae;t bi&d; God.

 &amp; swa swa &d;&ae;s godan godnes bi&d; his agen good  &amp; his agen edlean  swa bi&d; eac &d;&ae;s yfelan yfel his agen yfel &amp; his edlean &amp; his agen wite. 
 Ne tweo&d; n&ae;nne mon  gif he wite h&ae;f&d;  &t;&ae;t he n&ae;bbe yfel. 
 Hw&ae;t wena&d; &t;a yfelan &t;&ae;t hi bion bed&ae;lde &d;ara wita  &amp; sint fulle &ae;lces yfles?

 Gif eac hwylc good man from gode gewit  &t;onne ne bi&d; he &t;on ma fullice good  gif he eallunga from gewit; &t;onan hit gebere&d; &t;&ae;t &d;a yflan forl&ae;ta&d; &t;&ae;t &t;&ae;t hi &ae;r &d;a dydon  &amp; ne beo&d; &t;&ae;t &t;&ae;t hi &ae;r w&ae;ron.

 Hit gebyrede gio on Troiana gewinne &t;&ae;t &t;&ae;r w&ae;s an cyning &t;&ae;s nama Aulixes; se h&ae;fde twa &t;ioda under &t;am kasere.

 &d;a se Aulixes mid &t;am kasere to &t;am gefiohte for  &t;a h&ae;fde he sume hundred scipa; &t;a w&ae;ron hi sume ten gear on &t;am gewinne.

 &d;a gestod hine heah weder &amp; storms&ae;. 
 Wear&d; &t;a fordrifen on an iglond ut on &d;&ae;re Wendels&ae;. 
 &t;a w&ae;s &t;&ae;r Apollines dohtor Iobes suna; se Iob was hiora cyning  &amp; licette &t;&ae;t he sceolde bion se hehsta god; &amp; &t;&ae;t dysige folc him gelyfde  for&t;am&d;e he was cynecynnes; &amp; hi nyston n&ae;nne o&d;erne god on &t;&ae;ne timan  buton hiora cyningas hi weor&t;odon for godas.

 &t;a was hiora an se Apollinus &t;e we &ae;r ymb spr&ae;con.

 &t;&ae;t gewit was swi&d;e sorgiende for &t;am erm&d;um &d;e hi drogan.
