 Ac ic &d;e healsige giet &d;&ae;t &t;u me secge hw&ae;&d;er &d;u wene &t;&ae;t &t;a yflan habban &ae;nig wite &ae;fter &t;isse weorulde; o&d;&d;e &t;a godan &ae;nig edlean hiora goodes. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; he: Hu ne s&ae;de ic &d;e &ae;r &t;&ae;t &d;a goodan habba&d; edlean heora goodes &ae;g&t;er ge her ge on ecnesse  &amp; &d;a yflan eac habba&d; edlean hiora yfles  &ae;g&t;er ge her ge eft on ecnesse. 
 Ac ic wille d&ae;lan &t;a yflan &t;am yfelum nu on twua; for&d;&ae;m&t;e o&d;er d&ae;l &t;ara yflena h&ae;f&d; ece wite  for&d;&ae;m hi nane mildheortnesse ne geearnodon; o&d;er d&ae;l sceal beon gecl&ae;snod  &amp; &t;a amered on &d;&ae;m heofonlican fyre  swa her bi&d; seolfor  for&d;&ae;m he h&ae;f&d; sume geearnung&ae; sumre mildheortnesse. 
 for&d;&ae;m he mot cuman &ae;fter &d;&ae;m earfo&d;um to ecre are. 
 Giet ic &t;e meahte mare reccan &ae;g&d;er ge be &d;&ae;m goodum ge be &t;&ae;m yflum  &t;&ae;r ic nu &ae;mettan h&ae;fde. 
 Ac ic ondr&ae;de &t;&ae;t ic forl&ae;te &t;&ae;t wyt &ae;r &ae;fterspyredon; &t;&ae;t w&ae;s &t;&ae;t wit woldon gereccan &t;&ae;t &t;u ongeate &t;&ae;t &d;a yflan n&ae;fden n&ae;nne anwald ne n&ae;nne weor&d;scipe ne on &t;isse weorulde ne on &t;&ae;re toweardan. 
 For&d;&ae;m &t;e &t;uhte &ae;r &t;&ae;t eallra &d;inga wyrrest &t;&ae;t &d;u wendes &t;&ae;t hi h&ae;fden to micelne; &amp; &d;&ae;t eallneg siofodes &t;&ae;t hi eallneg n&ae;ron on wite. 
 &amp; ic &d;e s&ae;de eallne weg &t;&ae;t hi n&ae;fre ne bio&d; buton wite  &d;eah &t;e swa ne &t;ince. 
 Ac ic wat &t;eah &t;&ae;t &d;u wilt siofian &d;&ae;t hi swa longne fyrst habba&d; leafe yfel to donne; &amp; ic &d;e s&ae;de ealne weg &t;&ae;t se fyrst bi&d; swi&d;e lytle hwile. 
 &amp; ic &t;e secge giet  swa swa he lengra bi&d; swa hi bio&d; unges&ae;ligran; &t;&ae;t him w&ae;re eallra m&ae;st uns&ae;l&d; &t;&ae;t &t;&ae;t se fyrst w&ae;re o&d; domes d&ae;g. 
 &amp; ic &t;e s&ae;de eac &t;&ae;t &d;a w&ae;ren unges&ae;ligran &t;e him unrihtlice hiora yfel forboren w&ae;re &t;onne &t;a w&ae;ren &t;e him heora yfel rihtlice on gewrecen w&ae;re. 
 Git hit gebyre&d; &t;&ae;t &d;e &d;inc&d; &d;&ae;t &t;a orsorgan bio&d; unges&ae;ligran &t;onne &t;onne &t;a gewitnodan. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; ic: Ne &t;inc&d; me n&ae;fre nanwuht swa so&d;lic swa me &t;inca&d; &t;ine spell &d;&ae;m tidum &d;e ic &d;a gehere. 
 Ac gif ic me wende to &t;ises folces dome  &t;onne nis hit no &d;&ae;t an &t;&ae;t hi nylla&d; &t;isse &t;inre race gelefan  ac hi hit nylla&d; fur&d;um geheran. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; he: Nis &t;&ae;t nan wundor; hw&ae;t  &t;u wast &t;&ae;t &t;a men &t;e habba&d; unhale eagan ne magon full ea&d;e locian ongean &t;a sunnan &t;onne hio beortost scin&d;  ne fur&d;um on fyr ne on nanwuht beortes hi ne lyst locian  gif se &ae;ppel lef bi&d;. 
 Swa beo&d; &d;a synfullan mod ablend mid heora yflan willan &t;&ae;t hi ne magon gesion &t;&ae;t leoht &t;&ae;re beorhtan so&d;f&ae;stnesse  &t;&ae;t is se hehsta wisdom. 
 Ac him bi&d; swa &t;&ae;m fuglum &amp; &t;&ae;m diorum &d;e magon bet locian on niht &t;onne on d&ae;g; se d&ae;g blent &amp; &t;iostra&d; heora eagan  &amp; &t;&ae;re nihte &d;iostro hi onlyhta&d;. 
 For&d;y wena&d; &d;a ablendan mod &t;&ae;t &t;&ae;t sie sio m&ae;ste ges&ae;l&d; &t;&ae;t men sie alefed yfel to donne  &amp; sio d&ae;d him mote bion unwitnod. 
 For&d;&ae;m hi ne lyst spyrian &ae;fter &ae;lcre spr&ae;ce swa longe o&d; hi &t;&ae;t riht witen  ac wena&d; on hiora unnettan willan &amp; spyria&d; &ae;fter &d;&ae;m. 
 &t;e ic nat hu nyt &t;u me t&ae;hst to &d;&ae;m dysegum monnum  &t;a n&ae;fre &ae;fter me ne spyria&d;. 
 ic ne sprece n&ae;fre to &d;&ae;m  ac ic sprece to &t;e  for&d;&ae;m &t;u tiohhast &t;&ae;t &t;u spyrie &ae;fter me  &amp; swi&d;or swincst on &d;&ae;m spore &t;onne hi don. 
 Ne recce ic hw&ae;t hi demen; ic l&ae;te nu to &t;inum dome ma &t;onne to hiora  for&d;&ae;m hi eall locia&d; mid b&ae;m eagum on &t;as eor&d;lican &d;incg  &amp; hi him licia&d; eallunga &t;&ae;r  ge on &t;&ae;s modes eagum ge on &t;&ae;s lichoman. 
 Ac &t;u ana hwilum bescylst mid o&d;re eagan on &t;a heofonlican &t;incg  mid o&d;re &t;u locast nu giet on &t;as eor&d;lican. 
 For&d;&ae;m wena&d; &t;a dysegan &t;&ae;t &ae;lc mon sie blind swa hi sint  &amp; &t;&ae;t nan mon ne m&ae;ge gesion &t;&ae;t hi gesion ne magon. 
 &t;&ae;t dysi is anlicost &t;e sum cild sie full hal &amp; ful &ae;lt&ae;we geboren  &amp; swa fullice &d;ionde on eallum cystum &amp; cr&ae;ftum &t;a hwile &t;e hit on cnihthade bi&d;. 
 &amp; swa for&d; eallne giogo&d;had  o&d; he wyr&d; &ae;lces cr&ae;ftes medeme  &amp; &d;onne lytle &ae;r his midferh&d;e weor&d;e b&ae;m eagum blind  &amp; eac &t;&ae;s modes eagan weor&d;an swa ablende &t;&ae;t he nanwuht ne gemune &t;&ae;s &d;e he &ae;fre &ae;r geseah o&d;&d;e geherde  &amp; wene &t;eah &d;&ae;t he sie &ae;lces &t;inges swa medeme swa he &ae;fre medomest w&ae;re  &amp; wen&d; &t;&ae;t &ae;lcum men sie swa swa him si  &amp; &ae;lcum men &d;ince swa swa him &t;inc&d;. 
 &t;eah &d;e he &t;onne swa dysig sie &t;&ae;t he &t;&ae;s wene  hw&ae;&d;er we &d;onne willen ealle wenan &t;&ae;s &d;e he wen&d;? 
 Ic wene &d;eah &t;&ae;t we nyllen; ac ic wolde witan hu &t;e &t;uhte be &t;&ae;m monnum &d;e wit &ae;r cw&ae;don &t;&ae;t unc &d;uhte &t;&ae;t w&ae;ren wildiorum gelicran &t;onne monnum  hu micelne wisdom &t;a h&ae;fden; me &t;inc&d; &t;eah &d;e hi n&ae;bben n&ae;nne. 
 Ic &d;e wolde giet reccan sume swi&d;e rihte raca; ac ic wat &t;&ae;t &t;is folc his nele gelyfan; &t;&ae;t is &t;&ae;t &d;a bio&d; ges&ae;lig ran &t;e mon witna&d;  &t;onne &t;a bion &t;e hi witnia&d;. 
 &d;a wundrode ic &d;&ae;s &amp; cw&ae;&d;: Ic wolde &t;&ae;t &t;u me gereahte hu hit swa bion meahte. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; he: Hw&ae;&d;er &t;u ongite &t;&ae;t &ae;lc yfelwillende mon &amp; yfelwyrcende sie wites wyr&d;e? 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; ic: Genog sweotole ic &t;&ae;t ongite. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; he: Hu ne is se &d;onne yfelwillende &amp; yfelwyrcende &d;e &t;one unscyldigan witna&d;? 
 &d;a cw&d; ic: Swa hit is swa &d;u s&ae;gst. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; he: Hw&ae;&d;er &t;u wene &t;&ae;t &d;a sien earme &amp; unges&ae;lige &t;e wites wyr&d;e bio&d;? 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; ic: Ne wene ic his no  ac wat geare. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; he: Gif &t;u nu deman moste  hw&ae;&d;erne woldes &t;u deman wites wyr&d;ran  &t;e &d;one &t;e &d;one unscyldgan witnode  &d;e &d;one &t;e &t;&ae;t wite &t;olade? 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; ic: Nis &t;&ae;t gelic; ic wolde helpan &t;&ae;s &d;e &d;&ae;r unscyldig w&ae;re  &amp; henan &t;one &t;e hine yflode. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; he: &t;onne &t;e &d;inc&d; se earmra se &t;&ae;t yfel de&d; &d;onne se &t;e hit &t;afa&d;. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; ic: &t;&ae;s ic gelefe &t;&ae;tte &ae;lc unriht witnung sie &t;&ae;s yfel &t;e hit de&d;  n&ae;s &t;&ae;s &d;e hit &d;af&ae;&d;  for&d;&ae;m his yfel hine gede&d; earmne. 
 &amp; ic ongite &d;&ae;t &t;is is swi&d;e riht racu &t;&ae;t &t;u nu recst  &amp; swi&d;e anlic &t;&ae;m &t;e &t;u &ae;r reahtes; ac ic wat &t;eah &t;&ae;t &t;is folce swa ne &t;inc&d;. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; he: Wel &t;u hit ongitst; ac &d;a &t;ingeras &t;ingia&d; nu hwilum &t;&ae;m &t;e l&ae;ssan &t;earfe ahton; &t;ingia&d; &t;&ae;m &t;e &t;&ae;r man yfla&d;  &amp; ne &t;ingia&d; &t;&ae;m &t;e &t;&ae;t yfel do&d;. 
 &t;&ae;m w&ae;re mare &d;earf &t;e &t;a o&d;re unscyidige yfla&d; &t;&ae;t him mon &t;ingode to &t;&ae;m ricum  &amp; b&ae;de &t;&ae;t him mon dyde swa micel wite swa hi &t;&ae;m o&d;rum unscyldgum dydon. 
 Swa swa se sioca ah &t;earfe &t;&ae;t hine mon l&ae;de to &t;&ae;m l&ae;ce  &t;&ae;t he his tilige  swa ah se &t;e &d;&ae;t yfel de&d; &t;&ae;t hine mon l&ae;de to &t;&ae;m ricum  &t;&ae;t mon &t;&ae;r m&ae;ge sni&d;an &amp; b&ae;rnan his un&t;eawas. 
 Ne cwe&d;e ic na &t;&ae;t &t;&ae;t yfel sie &t;&ae;t mon helpe &t;&ae;s unscyldgan &amp; him fore&t;ingie; ac ic cwe&d;e &t;&ae;t hit is betere &t;&ae;t mon wrege &t;one scyldgan. 
 &amp; ic secge &t;&ae;t sio forespr&ae;c ne dyge nau&d;er ne &t;&ae;m scyldgan ne &d;&ae;m &t;e him fore&t;inga&d;  gif hi &t;&ae;s wilnia&d; &t;&ae;t him heora yfel unwrecen sie be &d;&ae;s gyltes andefne. 
 Ac ic wat gif &d;a scyldgan &ae;nigne spearcan wisdomes h&ae;fden &amp; be &ae;negum d&ae;le ongeaten &t;&ae;t hi meahten heora scylda &t;urg &t;&ae;t wite gebetan  &t;e him her on weorulde on become  &t;onne noldon hi na cwe&d;an &t;&ae;t hit w&ae;re wite  ac woldan cwe&d;an &t;&ae;t hit w&ae;re heora cl&ae;nsung  &amp; heora betrung. 
 &amp; noldon n&ae;nne &t;ingere gesecan  ac lustlice hi woldon l&ae;tan &t;a rican hi tucian &ae;fter hiora agnum willan. 
 For&d;&ae;m ne scyle nan wis man n&ae;nne mannan hatian; ne hata&d; nan mon &t;one godan  butan se eallra dysgosta; ne &t;&ae;t nis nan riht &t;&ae;t mon &t;one yflan hatige  ac hit is rihtre &t;&ae;t him mon miltsige. 
 &T;&ae;t is &t;onne hiora mildsung &t;&ae;t mon wrece hiora un&d;eawas be hiora gewyrhtum. 
 Ne scyle nan mon siocne monnan &amp; gesargodne swencan  ac hine mon scel l&ae;dan to &t;&ae;m l&ae;ce &t;&ae;t he his tilige. 
 &d;a se Wisdom &t;a &t;is spell areaht h&ae;fde  &d;a ongan he eft singan &amp; &t;us cw&d;: Forhwi drefe ge eowru mod mid unrihtre fiounge  swa swa y&d;a for winde &t;a s&ae; hrera&d;? 
 o&d;&d;e forhwy &ae;twite ge eowerre wyrde &t;&ae;t hio nan geweald nah? 
 o&d;&d;e hwy ne magon ge gebidan gecyndelices dea&d;es  nu he eow &ae;lce d&ae;g toweardes onet? 
 Hwi ne magon ge gesion &t;&ae;t he spyra&d; &ae;lce d&ae;g &ae;fter fuglum &amp; &ae;fter diorum &amp; &ae;fter monnum  &amp; ne forl&ae;t nan sw&ae;&d; &ae;r he gefeh&d; &t;&ae;t &t;&ae;t he &ae;fterspyre&d;. 
 Walawa &t;&ae;t &d;a unges&ae;ligan menn ne magon gebidon hwonne he him to cume  ac forsceota&d; hine foran  swa swa wilde deor willna&d; o&d;er to acwellenne. 
 Ac hit n&ae;re no manna ryht &t;&ae;t hiora &ae;nig o&d;erne fiode; ac &t;&ae;t w&ae;re ryht &t;&ae;t hiora &ae;lc gulde o&d;rum edlean &ae;lces weorces &ae;fter his gewyrhtum  &t;&ae;t is &t;&ae;t mon lufode &t;one godan  swa swa riht is &t;&ae;t mon do  &amp; mildsige &t;am yfelum  swa we &ae;r cw&ae;don. 
 lufie &t;one man  &amp; hatige his un&t;eawas; ceorfe him of swa he swi&d;ost m&ae;g. 
 &d;a he &t;a &t;is lio&d; asungen h&ae;fde  &t;a geswugode he ane hwile. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; ic: Nu ic ongite openlice &d;&ae;t sio so&d;e ges&ae;l&d; stent on godra monna geearnunga  &amp; sio uns&ae;l&d; stent on yfelra monna geearnunga. 
 Ac ic secge get &t;&ae;t me ne &t;ync&d; nauht lytel good &t;isses andweardan lifes ges&ae;l&d;a  ne eac nauht lytel yfel his unges&ae;l&d;a. 
 for&d;&ae;m ic n&ae;fre ne geseah ne geherde n&ae;nne wisne mon &t;e ma wolde bion wrecca &amp; earm &amp; el&d;iodig &amp; forsewen  &t;onne welig &amp; weor&d; &amp; rice &amp; forem&ae;re on his agnum earde. 
 For&d;&ae;m hi secga&d; &t;&ae;t hi m&ae;gen &t;e y&d; hiora wisdome fulgan &amp; hine gehealdan  gif hiora anwald bi&d; fullice ofer &t;&ae;t folc &t;e him under bi&d;; &amp; eac be sumum d&ae;le ofer &d;a &t;e him on neaweste bio&d; ymbutan  for&d;&ae;m &t;&ae;t hi m&ae;gen henan &d;a yflan &amp; fyr&d;ran &d;a goodan. 
 For&d;&ae;m se gooda bi&d; symle arwyr&d;e  &ae;g&t;er ge on &t;is andweardan life ge on &t;&ae;m toweardan; &amp; se yfela &t;e mon his yfel gestioran ne m&ae;g bi&d; symle wites wyr&t;e  ge on &t;isse worulde ge on &t;&ae;re toweardan. 
 Ac ic wundrie swi&d;e swi&d;lice forhwi hit swa went swa hit nu oft de&d;  &t;&ae;t is &t;&ae;tte mislicu witu &amp; m&ae;nigfeald earfo&d;u cuma&d; to &t;&ae;m godum swa hi to &d;&ae;m yflum sceoldon  &amp; &t;a good &t;e sceoldon beon edlean godum monnum godra weorca cuma&d; to yflum monnum. 
 For&d;&ae;m ic wolde witan nu &ae;t &t;e hu &d;e licode &t;&ae;t gewrixle. 
 Ic his wundrode micle &t;y l&ae;s  gif ic wisse &t;&ae;t hit weas gebyrede buton Godes willan &amp; buton his gewitnesse; ac se &ae;lmehtega God h&ae;f&d; geeced minne ege &amp; mine wafunga mid &d;isum &t;ingum. 
 For&d;&ae;m he hwilum sel&d; &t;a ges&ae;l&d;a &t;&ae;m goodum  &amp; &t;&ae;m yflum uns&ae;l&d;a  swa hit riht w&ae;re &t;&ae;t he symle dyde. 
 hwilum he eft ge&t;afa&d; &t;&ae;t &t;a goodan habba&d; uns&ae;l&d;a &amp; ungelimp on m&ae;negum &t;ingum  &amp; &t;a yflan habba&d; ges&ae;l&d;a  &amp; him limp&d; oft &ae;fter hiora agnum willan. 
 &t;y ic ne m&ae;g nan o&t;er ge&t;encan buton his weas swa gebyrige  buton &t;u me get &t;y gesceadlicor o&d;er gerecce. 
 &d;a andswarode he ymbe long &amp; cw&ae;&d;: Nis hit nan wundor &t;eah hwa wene &t;&ae;t swelces gehw&ae;t nu unmyndlinga geberige  &d;onne he ne con ongitan &amp; gereccan forhwy swylc God ge&t;afa&d;. 
 Ac &d;u ne scealt no twiogan &t;&ae;t swa good sceppend &amp; waldend eallra gesceafta rihtlice gesceop eall &t;&ae;t he gesceop  &amp; rihte dem&d; &amp; welt ealles  &t;eah &t;u nyte forhwy he swa &amp; swa do. 
 &d;a he &d;a &t;is spell areaht h&ae;fde  &t;a ongan he singan  &amp; cw&ae;&d;: Hwa unl&ae;redra ne wundra&d; &t;&ae;s roderes f&ae;reldes &amp; his swiftnesse  hu he &ae;lce d&ae;g uton ymbhwyrf&d; ealne &t;isne middangeard? 
 o&d;&d;e hwa ne wundra&d; &t;&ae;tte sume tunglu habba&d; scyrtran hwyrft &t;onne sume habban  swa swa tunglu habba&d; &t;e we hata&d; w&ae;nes &d;isla? 
 For&t;y hi habba&d; swa sceortne ymbhwyrft for&t;i hi sint swa neah &t;am nor&d;ende &t;&ae;re eaxe &t;e eall &t;es rodor on hwerf&d;. 
 O&d;&d;e hwa ne wafa&d; &t;&ae;s  buton &t;a ane &t;e hit witon  &t;&ae;t sume tunglu habba&d; lengran ymbhwyrft &t;onne sume habban  &amp; &t;a lengestne &t;e ymb &d;a eaxe middewearde hwearfa&d;  swa nu Boeties de&d;  &amp; Saturnus se steorra ne cym&d; &t;&ae;r &ae;r ymb &d;ritig wintra &t;&ae;s he &ae;r w&ae;s? 
 O&d;&d;e hwa ne wundra&d; &d;&ae;s &t;&ae;t sume steorran gewita&d; under &t;a s&ae;  swa swa sume men wena&t; &t;&ae;t sio sunne do &t;onne hio to setle g&ae;&d;? 
 Ac hio ne bi&d; &t;eah &t;y near &t;&ae;re s&ae; &d;e hio bi&d; on midne d&ae;g. 
 Hwa ne wafa&d; &t;&ae;s &t;onne se fulla mona wyr&d; ofertogen mid &t;iostrum  o&d;&d;e eft &t;&ae;t &t;a steorran scina&d; beforan &t;am monan  &amp; ne scina&d; beforan &t;&ae;re sunnan? 
 &t;ises hi wundria&d; &amp; manies &t;yllices  &amp; ne wundria&d; na &t;&ae;tte men &amp; ealle cwuca wuhta habba&d; singalne &amp; unnytne andan betwuh him. 
 O&d;&d;e hwy ne wundria&d; hi &t;&ae;s &t;&ae;t hit hwilum &t;unra&d;  hwilum na ne ongin&d;  o&d;&d;e eft gewinnes s&ae; &amp; winda &amp; y&t;a &amp; landes  o&d;&d;e hwy &t;&ae;t is weor&d;e &amp; eft for &t;&ae;re sunnan sciman to his agnum gecynde weor&d;e? 
 Ac &t;&ae;t ungest&ae;&d;&d;ige folc wundra&d; &t;&ae;s &t;e hit seldost gesieh&d;  &t;eah hit l&ae;sse wundor sie  &amp; wena&d; &t;&ae;t &t;&ae;t ne sie eald gesceaft  ac se weas geworden niwane. 
 Ac &t;a &d;e firwetgeorne weor&t;a&d; &amp; onginna&d; &t;onne leornian  gif him God abrit of &t;am mode &t;&ae;t dysig &t;&ae;t hit &ae;r mid oferwrigen was  &t;onne ne wundria&d; hi no fela &t;&ae;s &t;e hi nu wundria&d;. 
 &d;a se Wisdom &t;a &t;is leo&d; asungen h&ae;fde  &t;a geswugode he ane lytle hwile. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; ic: Swa hit is swa &t;u s&ae;gst; ac ic wolde get &t;&ae;t &t;u me hw&ae;thwugu openlicor gereahte be &d;&ae;re wisan &t;e min mod swi&d;ost gedrefed h&ae;f&d;; &t;&ae;t is &t;&ae;t ic &d;e &ae;r ymb acsode; for&d;&ae;m hit w&ae;s symle giet &t;in gewuna &t;&ae;t &t;u woldest &ae;lcum mode deglu &d;ing t&ae;can &amp; sel&d;cu&d;. 
 &d;a ongon he smearcian &amp; cw&ae;&d; to me: &d;u sp&ae;nst me on &d;a m&ae;stan spr&ae;ce &amp; on &t;a earfo&d;estan to gereccanne. 
 &t;a race sohton ealle u&d;wiotan  &amp; swi&d;e swi&d;lice ymb swuncon  &amp; unea&d;e &ae;nig com to ende &t;&ae;re spr&ae;ce; for&d;&ae;m hit is &t;eaw &t;&ae;re spr&ae;ce &amp; &t;&ae;re ascung&ae; &t;&ae;tte symle &t;onne &d;&ae;r an tweo of adon bi&d;  &t;onne bi&d; &t;&ae;r unrim astyred. 
 swa swa mon on ealdspellum s&ae;g&d; &t;&ae;t an n&ae;dre w&ae;re &t;e h&ae;fde nigon heafdu  &amp; symle gif mon anra hwelc of aslog  &t;onne weoxon &t;&ae;r siofon on &d;&ae;m anum heafde. 
 &t;a geberede hit &t;&ae;t &t;&ae;r com se forem&ae;ra Erculus to  se w&ae;s Iobes sunu; &t;a ne meahte he ge&t;encan hu he hi mid &ae;nige cr&ae;fte ofercuman sceolde  &ae;r he hi bew&ae;g mid wuda utan &amp; forb&ae;rnde &t;a mid fyre. 
 Swa is &d;isse spr&ae;ce &t;e &t;u me &ae;fter acsast; unea&d;e hire cym&d; &ae;nig mon of  gif he &ae;rest an cem&d;; ne cym&d; he n&ae;fre to openum ende  buton he h&ae;bbe swa scearp andgit swa&d;&ae;r fyr. 
 For&d;&ae;m se &d;e ymb &t;&ae;t acsian wile  he sceal &ae;rest witan hw&ae;t sie sio anfealde foresceawung Godes  &amp; hw&ae;t wyrd sie  &amp; hw&ae;t weas gebergie  &amp; hw&ae;t sie godcund andgit &amp; godcund foretiohhung  &amp; hw&ae;t monna freodom sie. 
 Nu &d;u miht ongitan hu hefig &amp; hu earfo&d;e &t;is is eall to gerecanne; ac ic sceal &t;eah hw&ae;thwugu his onginnan &t;e to t&ae;canne  for&d;&ae;m ic h&ae;bbe ongitan &t;&ae;t hit is swi&d;e micel l&ae;cedom &t;inre sorge  gif &t;u &t;ises auht ongitst  &t;eah hit me lange to l&ae;ranne sie. 
 For&d;&ae;m hit is neah &t;&ae;re tide &t;e ic getiohhod h&ae;fde on o&d;er weorc to fonne  &amp; get n&ae;bbe &t;is gedon; &amp; me &t;inc&d; eac &t;&ae;t &t;u sadige hw&ae;thwugununges  &amp; &t;e &d;yncen to &ae;lenge &t;as langan spell  swelce &t;e nu lyste lio&d;a. 
 Ic wat eac &t;&ae;t &t;e hiora lyst  ac &d;u scealt &t;eah ge&t;olian sume hwile; ic ne m&ae;g hit nu swa hra&d;e asingan  ne &ae;mettan n&ae;bbe  for&d;&ae;m hit is swi&d;e long spell. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; ic: Do sw&ae;&d;er &d;u wolde. 
 &t;a ongan he sprecan swi&d;e fiorran ymbutan  swelce he na &t;a spr&ae;ce ne m&ae;nde  &amp; tiohhode hit &d;eah &t;iderweardes &amp; cw&ae;&d;: Ealla gesceafta  gesewenlica &amp; ungesewenlica  stillu &amp; unstillu  onfo&d; &ae;t &t;&ae;m stillan &amp; &ae;t &t;&ae;m gest&ae;&d;&d;egan &amp; &ae;t &t;&ae;m anfealdan Gode endeberdnesse &amp; andwlitan &amp; gemetgunge. 
 &amp; for&t;&ae;m hit swa gesceapen w&ae;s  for&d;&ae;m he wat hwy he gesceop eall &t;&ae;t he gesceop. 
 Nis him nanwiht unnyt &t;&ae;s &t;e he gesceop. 
 Se God wuna&d; symle on &t;&ae;re hean ceastre his anfaldnesse &amp; bilewitnesse; &t;onan he d&ae;l&d; manega &amp; misleca gemetgunga eallum his gesceaftum  &amp; &t;onan he welt eallra. 
 Ac &t;&ae;t &d;&ae;tte we hata&d; Godes fore&t;onc &amp; his foresceawung  &t;&ae;t bi&d; &t;a hwile &t;e hit &d;&ae;r mid him bi&d; on his mode  &ae;r&d;&ae;m &t;e hit gefremed weor&d;e  &t;a hwile &d;e hit ge&t;oht bi&d;; ac si&d;&d;an hit fullfremed bi&d;  &t;onne hata&d; we hit wyrd. 
 Be &t;y m&ae;g &ae;lc mon witan &t;&ae;t hit sint &ae;g&t;er ge twegen naman ge twa &t;incg  fore&t;onc &amp; wyrd. 
 Se fore&t;onc is sio godcunde gesceadwisnes; sio is f&ae;st on &t;&ae;m hean sceppende &t;e eall forewat hu hit geweor&d;an sceall &ae;r &ae;r hit geweor&d;e. 
 Ac &t;&ae;t &t;&ae;t we wyrd hata&d;  &t;&ae;t bi&d; Godes weorc &t;&ae;t he &ae;lce d&ae;g wyrc&d;  &ae;g&t;er ge &t;&ae;s &d;e we gesio&d; ge &t;&ae;s &t;e us ungesewenlic bi&d;. 
 Ac se godcunda fore&t;onc hea&d;era&d; ealle gesceafta  &t;&ae;t hi ne moton toslupan of hiora endebyrdnesse. 
 Sio wyrd &t;onne d&ae;l&d; eallum gesceaftum anwlitan &amp; stowa &amp; tida &amp; gemetgunga; ac sio wyrd cym&d; of &d;&ae;m gewitte &amp; of &d;&ae;m fore&t;once &t;&ae;s &ae;lmehtigan Godes. 
 Se wyrc&d; &ae;fter his unasecgendlicum fore&t;once &t;onne swa hw&ae;t swa he wile. 
 Swa swa &ae;lc cr&ae;ftega &d;enc&d; &amp; mearca&d; his weorc on his mode &ae;r &ae;r he hit wyrce  &amp; wyrc&d; si&d;&d;an eall  &t;ios wandriende wyrd &t;e we wyrd hata&d; f&ae;r&d; &ae;fter his for&t;once &amp; &ae;fter his ge&t;eahte  swa swa he tiohha&d; &t;&ae;t hit sie. 
 &t;eah hit us manigfaldlic &d;ince  sum good  sum yfel  hit is &d;eah him anfeald good; for&d;&ae;m he hit eall to godum ende breng&d;  &amp; for goode de&d; eall &t;&ae;t &t;&ae;t he de&d;. 
 Si&d;&d;an we hit hata&d; wyrd si&d;&d;an hit geworht bi&d;; &ae;r hit w&ae;s Godes fore&t;anc &amp; his foretiohhung. 
 &d;a wyrd he &t;onne wyrc&d; o&d;&d;e &t;urh &d;a goodan englas o&d;&d;e &t;urh monna sawla  o&d;&d;e &t;urh o&d;erra gesceafta lif  o&d;&d;e &t;urh heofones tungl  o&d;&d;e &d;urh &t;ara scuccena mislice lotwrencas; hwilum &t;urh an &d;ara  hwilum &t;urh eall &d;a. 
 Ac &t;&ae;t is openlice cu&d; &t;&ae;t sio godcunde foretiohhung is anfeald &amp; unandwendlic  &amp; welt &ae;lces &t;inges endebyrdlice  &amp; eall &t;ing gehiwa&d;. 
 Sumu &t;ing &t;onne on &t;isse weorulde sint under&d;ied &t;&ae;re wyrde  sume hire nanwuht under&d;ied ne sint; ac sio wyrd &amp; eall &d;a &t;ing &t;e hire under&d;ied sint  sint under&d;ied &d;&ae;m godcundan fore&t;once. 
 Be &d;&ae;m ic &d;e m&ae;g sum bispell secgan  &t;&ae;t &t;u meaht &t;y sweotolor ongitan hwilce men bio&d; under&d;ied &t;&ae;re wyrde  hwylce ne bio&d;. 
 Eall &d;ios unstille gesceaft &amp; &t;ios hwearfiende hwearfa&d; on &d;&ae;m stillan Gode  &amp; on &d;&ae;m gest&ae;&d;&d;egan  &amp; on &d;&ae;m anfealdan; &amp; he welt eallra gesceafta swa swa he &ae;t fruman getiohhod h&ae;fde &amp; get h&ae;f&d;. 
 Swa swa on w&ae;nes eaxe hwearfia&d; &t;a hweol &amp; sio eax stint stille &amp; byr&d; &t;eah ealne &t;one w&ae;n  &amp; welt ealles &t;&ae;s f&ae;reltes; &t;&ae;t hweol hwerf&d; ymbutan &amp; sio nafu next &t;&ae;re eaxe sio f&ae;r&d; micle f&ae;stlicor &amp; orsorglicor &t;onne &d;a felgan don  swelce sio eax sie &t;&ae;t hehste god &t;e we nemna&d; God  &amp; &t;a selestan men faren nehste Gode  swa swa sio nafu f&ae;r&d; neahst &t;&ae;re eaxe  &amp; &t;a midmestan swa swa &d;a spacan. 
 for&d;&ae;m&t;e &ae;lces spacan bi&d; o&d;er ende f&ae;st on &d;&ae;re nafe  o&d;er on &t;&ae;re felge. 
 Swa bi&d; &t;&ae;m midlestan monnum; o&d;re hwile he smea&d; on his mode ymb &t;is eor&d;lice lif  o&d;re hwile ymb &d;&ae;t godcundlice  swilce he locie mid o&d;re eagan to heofonum  mid o&d;re to eor&t;an. 
 Swa swa &t;a spacan sticia&d; o&d;er ende on &t;&ae;re felge o&t;er on &t;&ae;re nafe  middeweard se spaca bi&d; &ae;g&d;rum emnneah  &d;eah o&d;er ende bio f&ae;st on &t;&ae;re nafe  o&d;er on &t;&ae;re felge. 
 swa bio&d; &t;a midmestan men onmiddan &t;am spacan  &amp; &t;a betran near &t;&ae;re nafe  &amp; &t;a m&ae;tran near &d;&ae;m felgum; bio&d; &t;eah f&ae;ste on &d;&ae;re nafe  &amp; se nafa on &d;&ae;re eaxe. 
 Hw&ae;t  &t;a felga &t;eah hongia&d; on &t;&ae;m spacan  &t;eah hi eallunga wealowigen on &t;&ae;re eor&d;an; swa do&d; &t;a m&ae;testan men on &t;&ae;m midmestum  &amp; &t;a midmestan on &t;&ae;m betstan  &amp; &t;a betstan on Gode. 
 &t;eah &t;a m&ae;testan ealle hiora lufe wenden to &d;isse weorulde  hi ne magon &t;&ae;ron wunigan  ne to nauhte ne weor&d;a&d;  gif hi be nanum d&ae;le ne beo&d; gef&ae;stnode to Gode. 
 &t;on ma &t;e &t;&ae;s hweoles felga magon bion on &d;&ae;m f&ae;relte  gif hi ne bio&d; f&ae;ste on &t;&ae;m spacum  &amp; &t;a spacan on &t;&ae;re eaxe. 
 &t;a felgea bio&d; fyrrest &d;&ae;re eaxe; for&d;&ae;m hi fara&d; ungeredelicost. 
 Sio nafu f&ae;r&d; neaxst &t;&ae;re eaxe; for&d;y hio f&ae;r&d; gesundlicost. 
 Swa do&d; &d;a selestan men; swa hi hiora lufe near Gode l&ae;ta&d;  &amp; swi&d;or &t;as eor&d;licon &t;ing forsio&d;  swa hi beo&d; orsorgran  &amp; l&ae;s recca&d; hu sio wyrd wandrige  o&d;&d;e hw&ae;t hio brenge. 
 Swa swa sio nafu bi&d; symle swa gesund  hn&ae;ppen &t;a felga on &t;&ae;t &d;e hi hn&ae;ppen  &amp; &t;eah bi&d; sio nafu hw&ae;thwugu tod&ae;led from &t;&ae;re eaxe. 
 Be &t;y &t;u meaht ongitan &t;&ae;t se w&ae;n bi&d; micle leng gesund &t;e l&ae;s bi&d; tod&ae;led from &t;&ae;re eaxe; swa bio&d; &t;a men eallra orsorgest&ae; &ae;g&d;er ge &t;isses andweardan lifes earfo&d;a  ge &t;&ae;s toweardan  &t;a &t;e f&ae;ste bio&d; on Gode. 
 ac swa hi swi&d;ur bio&d; asyndrede from Gode  swa hi swi&d;ur bio&d; gedrefde &amp; geswencte  &ae;g&t;er ge on mode ge on lichoman. 
 Swylc is &t;&ae;t &t;&ae;t we wyrd hata&d; be &t;&ae;m godcundan fore&t;once  swylce sio smeaung &amp; sio gesceadwisnes is to metanne wi&d; &t;one gearowitan  &amp; swylce &t;as l&ae;nan &t;ing bio&d; to metanne wi&d; &d;a ecan  &amp; swilce &t;&ae;t hweol bi&d; to metanne wi&d; &d;a eaxe; for&d;&ae;m sio eax welt ealles &t;&ae;s w&ae;nes. 
 Swa de&d; se godcunda fore&d;onc; he astere&d; &t;one rodor &amp; &t;a tunglu  &amp; &t;a eor&d;an gede&d; stille  &amp; gemetga&d; &t;a feower gesceafta; &t;&ae;t is w&ae;ter &amp; eor&d;e &amp; fyr &amp; lyft. 
 &d;a he ge&d;w&ae;ra&d; &amp; wlitega&d;  hwilum eft unwlitega&d;  &amp; on o&d;rum hiwe gebreng&d;  &amp; eft geedniwa&d;  &amp; tidre&d; &ae;lc tudor  &amp; hi eft gehyt &amp; gehelt &t;onne hit forealdod bi&d; &amp; forsearod  &amp; eft geew&d; &amp; geedniwa&d; &t;onne &t;onne he wile. 
 Sume u&d;wiotan &t;eah secga&d; &t;&ae;t sio wyrd wealde &ae;g&t;er ge ges&ae;l&d;a ge unges&ae;l&d;a &ae;lces monnes. 
 Ic &t;onne secge  swa swa ealle cristene men secga&d;  &t;&ae;t sio godcunde foretiohhung his walde  n&ae;s sio wyrd; &amp; ic wat &t;&ae;t hio dem&d; eall &t;ing swi&d;e rihte  &t;eah ungesceadwisum men swa ne &t;ince. 
 Hi wena&d; &t;&ae;t &t;ara &ae;lc sie god &t;e hiora willan fulg&ae;&d;; nis hit nan wundor  for&d;&ae;m hi beo&d; ablende mid &d;&ae;m &t;iostrum heora scylda. 
 Ac se godcunda fore&t;onc hit understent eall swi&d;e rihte  &t;eah us &t;ince for urum dysige &t;&ae;t hit on woh fare; for&d;&ae;m we ne cunnon &t;&ae;t riht understandan. 
 He dem&d; &t;eah eall swi&d;e rihte  &t;eah us hwilum swa ne &d;ince. 
 Ealle men spiria&d; &ae;fter &t;&ae;m hehstan goode  ge goode ge yfle; ac for&d;y ne magon &t;a yflan cuman to &d;&ae;m hean hrofe eallra gooda  for&d;&ae;m hi ne spyria&d; on riht &ae;fter. 
 Ic nat &t;eah &t;u cw&ae;&d;e nu hwonne to me: hwylc unriht m&ae;g beon mare &t;onne ge&t;afige &t;&ae;t hit geweor&d;e  swa hit hwilum gewyr&d;  &t;&ae;t &t;&ae;m goodum becym&d; anfeald yfel on &t;isse weorulde  &amp; &t;&ae;m yflum anfeald god  &amp; o&d;re hwile &ae;g&d;er gemenged  &ae;g&t;er ge &d;&ae;m goodum ge &t;&ae;m yflum? 
 Ac ic &t;e acsige hw&ae;&d;er &t;u wene &t;&ae;t &ae;nig mon sie swa andgitfull &t;&ae;t he m&ae;ge ongitan &ae;lcne mon on ryht hwylc he sie  &t;&ae;t he naw&d;er ne sie ne betra ne wyrsa &t;onne he his wene. 
 Ic wat &t;eah &t;&ae;t hi ne magan. 
 Ac wyr&d; swi&d;e oft on won se sido &t;e sume men secga&d; &t;&ae;t sie mede wyr&d;e  sume men secga&d; &t;&ae;t he sie wites wyr&d;e. 
 &t;eah hwa m&ae;ge ongitan hw&ae;t o&d;er do  he ne m&ae;g witan hw&ae;t he &t;enc&d;; &t;eah he m&ae;ge sume his willan ongitan  &t;onne ne m&ae;g he eallne. 
 Ic &t;e m&ae;g eac reccan sum bispell be &t;&ae;m &t;&ae;t &t;u hit meaht &t;e sweotolor ongitan  &d;eah hit ungesceadwise men ongitan ne m&ae;gen. 
 &t;&ae;t is forhwi se gooda l&ae;ce selle &t;am halum men seftne drenc &amp; swetne  &amp; o&d;rum halum biterne &amp; strangne; &amp; hwilum eft &t;am unhalum  sumum li&d;ne  sumum strangne  sumum swetne  sumum biterne. 
 Ic wat &t;&ae;t &ae;lc &t;ara &t;e &t;one cr&ae;ft ne can wile &t;&ae;s wundrian forhwy hi swa don. 
 Ac his ne wundria&d; &t;a l&ae;cas nauht  for&d;&ae;m hi witon &t;&ae;t &d;a o&d;re nyton; for&d;&ae;m hi cunnon &ae;lces hiora medtrymnesse ongiton &amp; oncnawan  &amp; eac &d;a cr&ae;ftas &t;e &t;&ae;rwi&d; sculon. 
 Hw&ae;t is sawla h&ae;lo bute rihtwisnes? 
 o&d;&d;e hw&ae;t is hiora untrymnes bute un&t;eawas? 
 Hwa is &t;onne betera l&ae;ce &t;&ae;re sawle &t;onne se &t;e hi gesceop  &t;&ae;t is God? 
 He ara&d; &t;&ae;m goodan  &amp; witna&d; &d;a yflan; he wat hw&ae;s &ae;lc wyr&d;e bi&d;. 
 Nis hit nan wundor  for&d;&ae;m he of &t;&ae;m hean hrofe hit eall gesih&d;  &amp; &t;onan misca&d; &amp; metga&d; &ae;lcum be his gewyrhtum. 
 &T;&ae;t we &t;onne hata&d; wyrd  &t;onne se gesceadwisa God  &t;e &ae;lces monnes &d;earfe wat  hw&ae;t wyrc&d; o&d;&d;e ge&t;afa&d; &t;&ae;s &t;e we ne wena&d;. 
 &amp; git ic &t;e m&ae;g sume bisne feaum wordum secgan be &t;&ae;m d&ae;le &t;e sio mennisce gesceadwisnes m&ae;g ongitan &t;a godcundnesse. 
 &t;&ae;t is &t;onne &t;&ae;t we ongita&d; hwilum mon on o&d;re wisan  on o&d;re hine God ongit. 
 Hwilum we tiohhia&d; &t;&ae;t he sie se betra  &amp; &t;onne wat God &t;&ae;t hit swa ne bi&d;. 
 &t;onne hw&ae;m hw&ae;t cym&d; o&d;&d;e goodes o&d;&d;e yfles mare &t;onne &d;e &t;inc&d; &t;&ae;t he wyr&d;e sie  ne bi&d; sio unrihtwisnes no on Gode  ac sio ungleawnes bi&d; on &d;e selfum  &t;&ae;t &t;u hit ne canst on riht gecnawan. 
 Oft gebyre&d; &t;eah &t;&ae;tte men ongita&d; man on &d;a ilcan wisan &t;e hine God ongit. 
 Oft hit gebyre&d; &t;&ae;tte manige men bio&d; swa ungetrume &ae;g&t;er ge on mode ge on lichoman &t;&ae;t hi ne magon nan good don  ne nan yfel nylla&d; unnedige  &amp; bio&d; eac swa unge&t;yldige &t;&ae;t hi ne magon nan earfo&d;u ge&t;yldelice aberan. 
 For&d;&ae;m hit gebyre&d; oft &t;&ae;t God nylle for his mildheortnesse nan unaberendlice broc him an settan  &t;y l&ae;s hi forl&ae;ten hiora unsce&d;fulnesse &amp; weor&d;en wyrsan  gif hi asterede bio&d; &amp; geswencte. 
 Sume men beo&d; &ae;lces cr&ae;ftes full cr&ae;ftige  &amp; full halige weras &amp; rihtwise. 
 &t;onne &t;inc&d; &t;&ae;t Gode unriht &t;&ae;t he swylce swence; ge fur&d;um &t;one dea&d; &t;e eallum monnum is gecynde to &t;olianne  he him gede&d; seftran &t;one o&d;rum monnum. 
 swa swa gio sum wis mon cw&ae;&d; &t;&ae;t se godcunda anwald gefrio&d;ode his deorlingas under his fi&d;ra sceate  &amp; hi scilde swa geornlice swa swa man de&d; &t;one &ae;ppel on his eagan. 
 Manige tilia&d; Gode to cwemanne to &t;on georne &t;&ae;t hi wilnia&d; hiora agnum willum manigfeald earfo&d;u to &t;rowianne  for&d;&ae;m hi willnia&d; maran are &amp; maran hlisan &amp; maran weor&d;scipe mid Gode to habbanne &t;onne &t;a habba&d; &t;e softor libba&d;. 
 Oft eac becym&d; se anwald &t;isse worulde to swi&d;e goodum monnum  for&d;&ae;m &t;&ae;t se anwald &t;ara yfelana weor&d;e toworpen. 
 Sumum monnum God sele&d; &ae;g&d;er ge good ge yfel gemenged  for&d;&ae;m hi &ae;g&t;res earnia&d;; sume he bereafa&d; hiora welan swi&d;e hra&d;e  &t;&ae;s &t;e hi &ae;rest ges&ae;lige weor&d;a&d;  &t;y l&ae;s hi for longum ges&ae;l&d;um hi to up ah&ae;bben  &amp; &t;onan on ofermettum weor&d;en; sume he l&ae;t &t;reagan mid heardum broce  &t;&ae;t hi leornigen &t;one cr&ae;ft ge&t;yldelice on &d;&ae;m langan geswince. 
 Sume him ondr&ae;da&d; earfo&d;u swi&d;or &t;onne hi &t;yrfen  &t;eah hi hi ea&d;e adreogan m&ae;gen; sume hi gebycga&d; weor&d;licne hlisan &t;isses andweardan lifes mid hiora agnum dea&d;e  for&d;&ae;m hi wena&d; &t;&ae;t hi n&ae;bben nan o&d;er fioh &t;&ae;s hlisan wyr&d;e buton hiora agnum fiore. 
 Sume men w&ae;ron gio unoferswi&d;edlice  swa &t;&ae;t hi nan ne meahte mid nanum wite oferswi&t;an; &t;a bisnodon hiora &ae;ftergengum &t;&ae;t hi n&ae;ren mid witum oferswi&d;de. 
 On &t;&ae;m w&ae;s sweotol &t;&ae;t hi for heora godum weorcum h&ae;fden &d;one cr&ae;ft &t;&ae;t hi mon ne meahte oferswi&d;an. 
 Ac &t;a yflan for hiora yflum weorcum w&ae;ron gewitnode &amp; oferswi&d;de  for&d;&ae;m &t;&ae;t &d;a witu gestirden o&d;rum &t;&ae;t hi swa gedon ne dorsten  &amp; eac &t;a gebetan &t;e hi &t;onne brocia&d;. 
 &t;&ae;t is swi&d;e sweotol tacn &t;&ae;m wisan &t;&ae;t he ne sceal lufian to ungemetlice &d;as woruldges&ae;l&d;a  for&d;&ae;m hie oft cuma&d; to &d;&ae;m wyrrestum monnum. 
 Ac hw&ae;t wille we cwe&d;an be &t;&ae;m andweardan welan &t;e oft cym&d; to &d;&ae;m goodum  hw&ae;t he elles sie buton tacn &t;&ae;s toweardan welan  &amp; &t;&ae;s edleanes angin &t;e him God tiohhod h&ae;f&d; for his goodan willan? 
 Ic wene eac &t;&ae;tte God selle m&ae;negum yfelum men ges&ae;l&d;a for&d;&ae;m&t;e he wat hiora gecynd &amp; hiora willan swa geradne &t;&ae;t hi for nanum erm&d;um ne byo&d; no &t;y betran ac &t;y wyrsan. 
 Ac se gooda l&ae;ce  &t;&ae;t is God  lacna&d; hiora mod mid &d;&ae;m welan; wile &t;&ae;t hi ongiten hwonon him se wela come &amp; olecce &t;&ae;m &t;e l&ae;s he him &t;one welan afyrre  o&d;&d;e hine &t;am welan  &amp; wende his &t;eawas to gode  &amp; forl&ae;te &d;a un&t;eawas &amp; &t;a yfel &t;e he &ae;r for his erm&d;um dyde. 
 Sume bio&d; &t;eah &t;y wyrson gif hi welan habba&d;  for&d;&ae;m hi ofermodiga&d; for &d;&ae;m welan &amp; his ungemetlice bruca&d;. 
 Manegum men bio&d; eac forgifene for&d;&ae;m &t;as weoruldges&ae;l&d;a &t;&ae;t he scile &t;&ae;m goodum leanian hiora good  &amp; &t;&ae;m yflum hiora yfel. 
 For&d;&ae;m symle bio&d; &t;a goodan &amp; &t;a yflan unge&t;were betwuh him  ge eac hwilum &t;a yflan bio&d; ungerade betwuh him selfum. 
 ge for&d;um an yfel man bi&d; simle unge&t;w&ae;re him selfum  for&d;&ae;m &t;e he wat &t;&ae;t he untela de&d;  &amp; wen&d; him &t;ara leana  &amp; nyle &t;eah &t;&ae;s geswican  ne hit fur&d;um him ne l&ae;t hreowan; &amp; &t;onne for &d;&ae;m singalum ege ne m&ae;g no weor&d;an ge&t;w&ae;re on him selfum. 
 Oft hit eac gebyre&d; &t;&ae;t se yfla forl&ae;t his yfel for sumes o&d;res yfles mannes andan  for&d;&ae;m he wolde mid &t;y t&ae;lan &t;one o&d;erne &t;&ae;t he onscunode his &t;eawas. 
 swinc&d; &t;onne ymb &t;&ae;t swa he swi&d;ost m&ae;g &t;&ae;t he tiola&d; ungelic to bionne &t;&ae;m o&d;rum for&d;&ae;m hit is &t;&ae;s godcundan anwealdes gewuna &t;&ae;t he wirc&d; of yfle good. 
 Ac hit nis nanum men alefed &t;&ae;t he m&ae;ge witan eall &t;&ae;t God getiohhod h&ae;f&d;  ne eac areccan &t;&ae;t &t;&ae;t he geworht h&ae;f&d;. 
 Ac on &t;&ae;m hi habba&d; genoh to ongitanne &t;&ae;t se scippend &amp; se waldend eallra gesceafta welt  &amp; rehte gesceop eall &t;&ae;t he gesceop  &amp; nan yfel ne worhte ne get ne wyrc&d;  ac &ae;lc yfel he adrif&d; of eallum his rice. 
 Ac gif &t;u &ae;fter &t;&ae;m hean anwalde spyrian wilt &t;&ae;s &ae;lmehtigan Godes  &t;onne ne ongitst &t;u nan yfel on nanum &t;inge  &t;eah &t;e nu &d;ince &t;&ae;t her micel on &t;ys middangearde sie. 
 for&d;&ae;m hit is riht &t;&ae;t &d;a goodan h&ae;bben good edlean hiora godes  &amp; &t;a yflan h&ae;bban wite hiora yfles; ne bi&d; &t;&ae;t nan yfel &t;&ae;tte riht bi&d;  ac bi&d; good. 
 Ac ic ongite &d;&ae;t ic &t;e h&ae;bbe a&d;retne nu mid &t;y langan spelle  for&d;&ae;m &t;e lyst nu leo&d;a; ac on foh hiora nu  for&d;&ae;m hit is se l&ae;cedom &amp; se drenc &t;e &t;u lange wilnodest  &t;&ae;t &d;u &t;y e&d; m&ae;ge &t;&ae;re lare onfon. 
 &d;a se Wisdom &t;a &t;is spell areaht h&ae;fde  &t;a ongon he eft singan &amp; &t;us cw&ae;&d;: Gif &t;u willnige mid hlutrum mode ongitan &t;one hean anweald  beheald &t;a tunglu &t;&ae;s hean heofnes. 
 Healda&d; &t;a tunglu &t;a ealdan sibbe &t;e hi on gesceapne w&ae;ron  swa &t;&ae;t sio fyrene sunne ne onhrin&d; no &t;&ae;s d&ae;les &t;&ae;s heofenes &t;e se mona on irn&d;  ne se mona no ne onhrin&d; &t;&ae;s d&ae;les &t;e sio sunne on irn&d;  &t;a hwile &d;e hio &t;&ae;ron bi&d;. 
 Ne se steorra &t;e we hata&d; Ursa ne cym&d; n&ae;fre on &t;am westd&ae;le  &t;eah ealle o&d;re steorran faren mid &t;am rodore &ae;fter &t;&ae;re sunnan on &t;a eor&t;an. 
 Nis hit nan wundor  for&t;am he is swi&d;e neah &t;am upende &t;&ae;re eaxe. 
 Ac se steorra &t;e we hata&d; &ae;fensteorra  &t;onne he bi&d; west gesewen  &t;onne tacnna&d; he &ae;fen. 
 F&ae;r&d; &t;onne &ae;fter &t;&ae;re sunnan on &d;&ae;re eor&d;an sceade o&d; he ofirn&d; &t;a sunnan hindan; cym&d; wi&d;foran &t;a sunnan up. 
 &t;onne hate we hine morgensteorra  for&t;am he cym&d; eastan up; boda&d; &t;&ae;re sunnan cyme. 
 Sio sunne &amp; se mona habba&d; tod&ae;led betwuht him &t;one d&ae;g &amp; &t;a niht swi&d;e emne  &amp; swi&d;e ge&t;w&ae;rlice ricsia&d; &t;urh godcundan foresceawunga  &amp; una&t;rotenlice &t;iowia&d; &t;am &ae;lmihtigan Gode o&d; domes d&ae;g. 
 For&t;i hi ne l&ae;t God on ane healfe &t;&ae;s heofones bion  &t;y l&ae;s hi fordon o&d;ra gesceafta. 
 Ac gesibsuma God gemetga&d; ealla gesceafta &amp; ge&t;w&ae;ra&d; &t;a &d;e betwuh him wunia&d;. 
 Hwilum flih&d; se w&ae;ta &t;&ae;t dryge; hwilum he gemenge&d; &t;&ae;t fyr wi&d; &t;am cile; hwilum &t;&ae;t leohte fyr &amp; &t;&ae;t beorhte up gewit  &amp; sio hefige eor&d;e sit &t;&ae;r ni&d;ere. 
 Be &t;&ae;s cyninges gebode breng&d; eor&d;e &ae;lcne westm &amp; &ae;lc tudor &ae;lce geare  &amp; se hata sumor dryg&d; &amp; gearwa&d; s&ae;d &amp; bleda  &amp; westmb&ae;ra h&ae;rfest bryng&d; ripa bleda. 
 H&ae;glas &amp; snawas &amp; se oftr&ae;da ren lecca&d; &t;&ae; eor&d;an on wintra; for&t;am underfeh&d; sio eor&d;e &t;&ae;t s&ae;d &amp; gede&d; &t;&ae;t hit grew&d; on lengten. 
 Ac se metod eallra gesceafta fet on eor&d;an ealle growende westmas &amp; ealle for&d;breng&d;; &amp; gehyt &t;onne he wyle  &amp; eowa&d; &t;onne he wile  &amp; nim&d; &t;onne he wile. 
 &t;a hwile &t;e &d;a gesceafta &t;iowia&d;  sit se hehsta sceoppend on his heahsetle; &t;anon he welt &t;am gewealdle&d;erum ealle gesceaftu. 
 Nis nan wundor  for&t;am&d;e he is cyning &amp; dryhten &amp; &ae;welm &amp; fruma &amp; &ae; &amp; wisdom &amp; rihtwis dema. 
 He sent ealla gesceafta on his &ae;rendo  &amp; he het ealle eft cuman. 
 &t;&ae;r se an gest&ae;&t;&t;ega cyning gif he ne sta&t;elode ealla gesceafta  &t;onne wurdon hi ealle toslopene &amp; tostencte  &amp; to nauhte wurdon ealle gesceafta. 
 &t;eah habba&d; gem&ae;nelice &t;a ane lufe &t;&ae;t hi &t;eowian swilcum hlaforde  &amp; f&ae;gnia&d; &t;&ae;s &t;&ae;t he hiora wealt. 
 Nis &t;&ae;t nan wundor  for&t;am hi ne mihton elles bion  gif hi ne &d;iowedon hiora fruman. 
 &d;a forlet se Wisdom &t;&ae;t leo&d;  &amp; cw&ae;&d; to me: Hw&ae;&d;er &d;u nu ongite hwider &t;ios spr&ae;ce wille? 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; ic: Sege me hwider sio wille. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; he: Ic wille secgan &t;&ae;t &ae;lc wyrd bio good  sam hio monnum good &t;ince  sam hio him yfel &t;ince. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; ic: Ic wene &t;&ae;t hit ea&d;e swa bion m&ae;ge  &t;eah us hwilum o&d;er &t;ynce. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; he: Nis &t;&ae;s nan tweo &d;&ae;t &ae;lc wyrd bi&d; good &t;ara &d;e riht &amp; nytwyr&d;e bi&d;. 
 for&d;&ae;m &ae;lc wyrd  sam hio bio wynsum sam hio sie unwynsum  for&d;y cym&t; to &d;&ae;m goodan &t;&ae;t hio o&d;er twega do  o&d;&d;e hine &t;reatige to &d;on &t;&ae;t he bet do &t;onne he &ae;r dyde  o&d;&d;e him leanige &t;&ae;t he &ae;r tela dyde. 
 &amp; eft &ae;lc wyrd &t;ara &t;e to &d;&ae;m yflum cym&d;  cym&d; for &t;&ae;m tw&ae;m &t;ingum  sam hio sie re&d;e  sam hio sy wynsum. 
 Gif to &d;&ae;m yflum cym&d; re&d;u wyrd  &t;onne cym&d; he to edleane his yfla  o&d;&d;e to &t;reunge &amp; to l&ae;re &t;&ae;t he eft swa ne do. 
 &t;a ongann ic wundrian  &amp; cw&ae;&d;: Is &t;&ae;t forinweardlice riht racu &t;&ae;t &t;u &d;&ae;r recst. 
 &t;a cw&ae;&d; he: Swa hit is swa &d;u s&ae;gst; ac ic wolde  gif &d;u wolde  &d;&ae;t wit unc wenden sume hwile to &t;ises folces spr&ae;ce  &t;yl&ae;s hi cwe&t;an &t;&ae;t wit sprecan ofer monnes gemet. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; ic: Sprec &t;&ae;t &d;u wille. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; he: Wenst &t;u &d;&ae;t &t;&ae;t ne sie good &t;&ae;t nit bi&d;? 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; ic: Ic wene &t;&ae;t hit sie. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; he: &ae;lc wyrd is nyt &t;ara &t;e au&d;er de&d;  o&d;&d;e l&ae;r&d;  o&d;&d;e wyrc&d;. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; ic: &t;&ae;t is so&d;. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; he: Sio wi&d;erwearde wyrd is &d;&ae;m good &t;e winna&d; wi&d; un&d;eawas &amp; wenda&d; hi to goode. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; ic: Ne m&ae;g ic &t;&ae;s o&d;sacan. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; he: Hw&ae;t wenst &t;u bi &t;&ae;re goodan wyrde &d;e oft cym&d; to goodum monnum on &d;isse weorulde  swylce hit sie foretacn ecra gooda? 
 hw&ae;&t;er &t;is folc m&ae;ge cwe&d;an &t;&ae;t hit sie yfel wyrd? 
 &d;a smearcode ic &amp; cw&ae;&d;: Ne cwi&d; &t;&ae;t nan mon  ac cwi&d; &t;&ae;t hio sie swi&d;e good  swa hio eac bi&d;. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; he: Hw&ae;t wenst &t;u be &t;&ae;re unwenlicran wyrde &t;e oft &t;reata&d; &t;a yflan to witnianne? 
 hw&ae;&d;er &t;is folc wene &t;&ae;t &t;&ae;t good wyrd sie? 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; ic: Ne wena&d; hi no &t;&ae;t &t;&ae;t god wyrd sie  ac wena&d; &t;&ae;t hio sie earmlico. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; he: Uton healdan unc &t;&ae;t wit ne wenen swa swa &t;is folc wen&d;; gif wit &t;&ae;s wena&d; &d;e &t;is folc wen&d;  &t;onne forl&ae;te wit &ae;lce gesceadwisnesse &amp; &ae;lce rihtwisnesse. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; ic: Hwy forl&ae;te wit hi a &t;a ma? 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; he: For&d;y &t;e folcisce men secga&d; &t;&ae;t &ae;lc re&d;u wyrd &amp; unwynsumu sie yfel; ac we ne sculon &t;&ae;s gelefan  for&d;&ae;m &t;e &ae;lc wyrd bi&d; good  swa we &ae;r spr&ae;con  sam hio sy re&d;e  sam hio sie wynsum. 
 &d;a wear&d; ic af&ae;red &amp; cw&ae;&d;: &t;&ae;t is so&d; &t;&ae;t &t;u s&ae;gst; ic nat &t;eah hwa hit dyrre secgan dysegum monnum  for&d;&ae;m his ne m&ae;g nan dysi man gelefan. 
 &d;a onsac se Wisdom sarlice  &amp; cw&ae;&d;: For&d;y ne scyle nan wis mon forhigan ne to swi&d;e ymb &t;&ae;t gnornian  to hw&ae;m his wise weor&d;e  o&d;&d;e hw&ae;&d;er him cume &t;e re&d;u wyrd &t;e li&d;u  &d;on ma &t;e se hwata esne scyle ymb &t;&ae;t gnornian  hu oft he fiohtan scyle. 
 Ne bi&d; his lof na &d;y l&ae;sse  ac is wen &t;&ae;t hit sie &t;y mare; swa bi&d; eac &t;&ae;s wisan med &t;e mare  &t;e him wra&d;re wyrd &amp; re&d;re to becym&d;. 
 &t;i ni sceolde nan wis man wilnian seftes lifes  gif he &ae;nigra cr&ae;fta rec&d; o&d;&d;e &ae;niges weor&d;scipes her for weorulde o&d;&d;e eces lifes &ae;fter &t;isse weorulde. 
 Ac &ae;lc wis man scyle awinnan &ae;g&d;er ge wi&d; &t;a re&d;an wyrde ge wi&d; &t;a wynsuman  &t;y l&ae;s he hine for &d;&ae;re wynsuman wyrde fortruwige  o&d;&d;e for &d;&ae;re re&d;an for&d;ence. 
 Ac him is &d;earf &t;&ae;t he aredie &t;one midmestan weg betweoh &t;&ae;re re&d;an wyrde &amp; &d;&ae;re li&d;an  &t;&ae;t he ne wilnige wynsumran wyrde &amp; maran orsorgnesse &d;onne hit gemetlic sie  ne eft to re&d;re  for&d;&ae;m he ne m&ae;g nau&t;res ungemet adriogan. 
 Ac hit is on hiora agnum anwealde hw&ae;&d;re &t;ara hi geciosen. 
 Gif hi &t;onne &t;one midmestan weg aredian willa&d;  &t;onne sculon hi selfe him selfum gemetgian &t;a wynsuman wyrde &amp; &t;a orsorgan. 
 &t;onne gemetga&d; him God &t;a re&d;an wyrde ge on &t;isse weorulde ge on &t;&ae;re toweardan  swa swa hi ea&d;e adreogan magan. 
 Wella  wisan men  wel; ga&d; ealle on &t;one weg &d;e eow l&ae;ra&d; &t;a forem&ae;ran bisna &t;ara godena gumena &amp; &t;ara weor&d;geornena wera &t;e &ae;r eow w&ae;ron. 
 Eala  ge eargan &amp; idelgeornan; hwy ge swa unnytte sien &amp; swa aswundne? 
 Hwy ge nyllen ascian &ae;fter &t;&ae;m wisum monnum &amp; &ae;fter &t;&ae;m weor&d;geornum  hwylce hi w&ae;ron &t;a &t;e &ae;r eow w&ae;ron? 
 &amp; hwy ge &t;onne nyllen  si&d;&d;an ge hiora &t;eawas geascod h&ae;bben  him onhirian  swa ge swi&d;ost m&ae;gen? 
 for&d;&ae;m hi wunnon &ae;fter weor&d;scipe on &t;isse worulde  &amp; tiolodon goodes hlisan mid goodum weorcum  &amp; worhton goode bisne &t;&ae;m &t;e &ae;fter him w&ae;ron. 
 For&d;&ae;m hi wunia&d; nu ofer &d;&ae;m tunglum on ecre eadignesse for hiora godum weorcum. 
 Her enda&d; sio fior&d;e boc Boeties  &amp; ongin&d; sio fifte. 
 &d;a se Wisdom &t;a &t;is spell areaht h&ae;fde  &t;a cw&ae;&d; ic: Swi&d;e riht is &t;in lar; ac ic wolde &t;e nu myndgian &t;&ae;re m&ae;nigfealdan lare &t;e &t;u me &ae;r gehete be &t;&ae;re Godes foretiohhunge. 
 Ac ic wolde &ae;rest witan &ae;t &t;e hw&ae;&d;er &t;&ae;t auht sie &t;&ae;t we oft gehera&d; &t;&ae;t men cwe&d;a&d; be sumum &t;ingum &t;&ae;t hit scyle weas gebyrian. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; he: Me w&ae;re leofre &t;&ae;t ic onette wi&d; &t;&ae;s &t;&ae;t ic &t;e moste gel&ae;stan &t;&ae;t ic &t;e &ae;r gehet  &amp; &t;e moste get&ae;can swa scortne weg swa ic scyrtestne findan meahte to &d;inre cy&d;&d;e. 
 Ac hit is swi&d;e feor of uncrum wege  of &t;&ae;m wege &t;e wit getiohhod habba&d; on to farenne; &t;&ae;t &t;&ae;t &t;u me &ae;r b&ae;de hit w&ae;re &t;eah nyttre to gecerranne &amp; to ongitanne. 
 Ac ic ondr&ae;de &t;&ae;t ic &t;e l&ae;de hidres &t;idres on &d;a pa&d;as of &t;inum wege  &t;&ae;t &t;u ne m&ae;ge eft &t;inne weg aredian. 
 Nis hit nan wundor &t;eah &t;u getiorie  gif ic &t;e l&ae;de bi &d;&ae;m wege. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; ic: Ne &t;earft &t;u no &t;&ae;t ondr&ae;dan; ac ic bio swi&d;e swi&d;e gef&ae;gen gif &t;u me l&ae;dst &t;ider ic &d;e bidde. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; he: Ic &t;e wille l&ae;ran bispellum  swa ic &t;e ealne weg dyde  &amp; &t;e &t;eah secgan wille &t;&ae;t hit nis nauht &t;&ae;t mon cwi&d;  &t;&ae;t &ae;nig &t;ing weas gebyrige. 
 For&d;&ae;m &ae;lc &t;ing cim&d; of sumum &t;ingum  for&d;&ae;m hit ne bi&d; weas gebyred; ac &d;&ae;r hit of nauhte ne come &t;onne w&ae;re hit weas gebyred. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; ic: Ac hwonan com se nama &ae;rest? 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; he: Aristoteles min diorling hit gerehte on &t;&ae;re bec &t;e Fisica hatte. 
 &t;a cw&ae;&d; ic: Hu rehte he hit? 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; he: Men cw&ae;don gio &t;onne him hw&ae;t unwenunga gebirede &t;&ae;t &t;&ae;t w&ae;re weas gebyred; swylce hwa nu delfe eor&d;an  &amp; finde &d;&ae;r &t;onne goldhord  ond secge &d;onne &t;&ae;t &t;&ae;t sie weas gebered. 
 Ic wat &t;eah gif se delfere &t;a eor&d;an no ne delfe  ne nan mon &ae;r &t;&ae;t gold &t;&ae;r ne hydde  &t;onne ne funde he hit no. 
 For&d;y hit n&ae;s na weas funden; ac sio godcunde foretiohhung l&ae;rde &t;one &t;e he wolde &t;&ae;t he gold hydde  &amp; eft &d;one &t;e he wolde &t;&ae;t hit funde. 
 hw&ae;t we ne ne don  &t;e sio godcunde foretiohhung o&d;&d;e sio wyrd us nede to &t;am &t;e we willan. 
 &T;a cw&ae;&d; he: We habba&d; micelne anwald; nis nan gesceadwis gesceaft &t;&ae;t n&ae;bbe friodom. 
 Se &t;e gesceadwisnesse h&ae;f&d;  se m&ae;g deman &amp; tosceadan hw&ae;s he wilnigan sceal &amp; hw&ae;t he onscunian sceal. 
 &amp; &ae;lc mon h&ae;f&d; &t;one freodom &t;&ae;t he wat hw&ae;t he wile hw&ae;t he nele; &amp; &t;eah nabba&d; ealla gesceadwisa gesceafta gelicne friodom. 
 Englas habba&d; rihte domas &amp; goodne willan  &amp; eall &t;&ae;t hi wilnia&d; hi begita&d; swi&d;e ea&d;e  for&d;&ae;m&t;e hi nanes wos ne wilnia&d;. 
 Nis nan &t;e h&ae;bbe friodom &amp; gesceadwisnesse buton englum &amp; monnum; &t;a men habba&d; simle freodom &t;y maran &t;e hi heora mod near godcundum &d;ingum l&ae;ta&d;  &amp; habba&d; &t;&ae;s &t;y l&ae;ssan friodom &t;e hi hiora modes willan near &t;isse weoruldare l&ae;ta&d;. 
 Nabba&d; hi n&ae;nne freodom &t;onne hi heora agnum willum hi selfe un&d;eawum under&d;ioda&d;; ac sona swa hi hiora mod onwenda&d; from gode  swa weor&d;a&d; hi ablende mid unwisdome. 
 Swa&t;eah is an &ae;lmihtig God on his &t;&ae;re hean ceastre; se gesih&d; &ae;lces monnes ge&t;oht  &amp; his word &amp; his d&ae;da toscead  &amp; gilt &ae;lcum &ae;fter his gewyrhtum. 
 &d;a se Wisdom &t;a &t;is spell as&ae;d h&ae;fde  &t;a ongon he singan &amp; &t;us cw&ae;&d;: &t;eah Omerus se goda sceop  &t;e mid Crecum selest was: se was Firgilies lareow; se Frigilius w&ae;s mid L&ae;denwarum rum selest. 
 &t;eah Omerus on his leo&d;um swi&d;e herede &t;&ae;re sunnan gecynd &amp; hiore cr&ae;ftas &amp; hiore biorhto  ne m&ae;g heo &t;eah ealle gesceafta gescinan  ne &t;a gesceafta &t;e heo gescinan m&ae;g ne m&ae;g hio ealle endemest gescinan  ne ealle innan geondscinan. 
 Ac nis &t;am &ae;lmihtigan Gode swa  &t;e is scyppend ealra gesceafta; he geseoh&d; &amp; &t;urhseoh&d; ealle his gesceafta &ae;ndemest. 
 &t;one mon m&ae;g hatan buton lease so&t;e sunne. 
 &d;a se Wisdom &t;a &t;is leo&d; asungen h&ae;fde  &d;a geswugode he ane lytle hwile. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; ic: Sum tweo me h&ae;f&d; swi&d;e gedrefed. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; he: Hw&ae;t is se? 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; ic: Hit is &t;&ae;t &t;&ae;t &d;u s&ae;gst &t;&ae;t God selle &ae;lcum men freodom swa good to donne swa yfel  sw&ae;&d;er he wille; &amp; &t;u s&ae;gst eac &t;&ae;t God wite &ae;lc &t;ing &ae;r hit geweor&d;e; &amp; &t;u s&ae;gst eac &t;&ae;t nan &t;ing ne geweor&d;e bute hit God wille o&d;&d;e ge&d;afie; &amp; &t;u s&ae;gst &t;&ae;t hit scyle eall faran swa he getiohhod h&ae;bbe. 
 Nu wundrie ic &t;&ae;s hwy he ge&t;afige &t;&ae;t &t;a yflan men h&ae;bben &t;one freodom &t;&ae;t hi m&ae;gen don swa god swa yfel  sw&ae;&d;er swa hi willan  &t;onne he &ae;r wat &t;&ae;t hi yfel don willa&d;. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; he: Ic &t;e m&ae;g swi&d;e ea&d;e geandwyrdan &t;&ae;s spelles. 
 Hu wolde &t;e nu lician gif hwilc swi&d;e rice cyning w&ae;re &amp; n&ae;fde n&ae;nne freone mon on eallum his rice  ac w&ae;ren ealle &t;iowe? 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; ic: Ne &t;uhte me hit no rihtlic  ne eac nauht gerisenlic  gif him sceolden &t;iowe men &t;enian. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; he: &t;&ae;t w&ae;re uncynlicre  gif God n&ae;fde on eallum his rice nane frige gesceaft under his anwalde. 
 For&d;&ae;m he gesceop twa gesceadwisa gesceafta freo  englas &amp; men; &t;&ae;m he geaf micle gife freodomes  &t;&ae;t hi mosten don swa god swa yfel  sw&ae;&d;er swa hi wolden. 
 He sealde swi&d;e f&ae;ste gife &amp; swi&d;e f&ae;ste &ae; mid &d;&ae;re gife &ae;lcum men o&d; his ende; &d;&ae;t is se freodom &d;&ae;t se mon mot don &t;&ae;t he wile  &amp; &t;&ae;t is sio &ae; &t;&ae;t he gilt &ae;lcum be his gewyrhtum &ae;g&d;er ge on &t;isse worulde ge on &t;&ae;re toweardan swa good swa yfel  sw&ae;&d;er he de&d;. 
 &amp; men magon begitan &t;urh &t;one freodom swa hw&ae;t swa hi willa&d;  buton dea&d; hi ne magon forcerran; &ae;c hi hine magon mid goodum weorcum gelettan  &t;&ae;t he &t;e lator cym&d;; ge fur&t;um o&d; oreldo hi hine hwilum geletta&d;. 
 Gif men to goodum weorce ne onhagie  h&ae;bbe goodne willan; &t;&ae;t is emngood. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; ic: Wel &d;u me h&ae;fst aretne on &t;am tweon  &amp; on &t;&ae;re gedrefednesse &t;e ic &ae;r on w&ae;s be &d;&ae;m freodome. 
 Ac ic eom nu giet on micle maran gedrefednesse geunrotsod  fulneah o&d; ormodnesse. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; he: Hw&ae;t is sio micle unrotnes? 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; ic: Hit is ym &d;a Godes foretiohhunge; for&d;&ae;m we gehera&d; hwilum secgan &t;&ae;t hit scyle eall swa geweor&d;an swa swa God &ae;t fruman getiohhad h&ae;fde  &t;&ae;t hit ne m&ae;ge nan mon onwendan. 
 Nu &d;inc&d; me &t;&ae;t he do woh  &t;onne he ara&d; &t;a goodan  &amp; eac &t;onne he witna&d; &t;a yflan  gif &t;&ae;t so&d; is &t;&ae;t hit him swa gesceapen w&ae;s &t;&ae;t hi ne mosten elles don. 
 Unnytlice we swinca&d; &t;onne we us gebidda&d;  &amp; &d;onne we f&ae;sta&d;  o&d;&d;e &ae;lmessan sella&d;  gif we his nabba&d; &d;y maran &t;anc &t;e &t;a &t;e on eallum &t;ingum wada&d; on hiora agenne willan  &amp; &ae;fter hiora lichoman luste irna&d;. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; he: &t;is is sio ealde siofung &t;e &t;u longe siofodes  &amp; manige eac &ae;r &d;e; &t;ara w&ae;s sum Marcus  o&d;re naman Tullius  &t;riddan naman he was gehaten Cicero; se w&ae;s Romana heretoga; se w&ae;s u&d;wita. 
 Se w&ae;s swi&d;e abisgod mid &d;&ae;re ilcan spr&ae;ce  ac he hi ne meahte brengan to nanum ende. 
 For&d;y he ne meahte  ne nan mon on &t;one timan  &t;a spr&ae;ce to nanum ende bringan  for&d;y hiora mod w&ae;s abisgod on &d;isse weorulde wilnunga. 
 Ac ic &t;e secge  gif &t;&ae;t so&d; is &t;&ae;t ge secga&d;  &t;&ae;t hit w&ae;s unnet gebod on godcundum bocum &t;&ae;t God bebead &t;&ae;t mon sceolde forl&ae;tan yfel &amp; don good; &amp; eft se cwide &t;e he cw&ae;&d;: swa mon ma swinc&d;  swa mon maran mede onfeh&d;. 
 &amp; ic wundrige hwy &t;u h&ae;bbe forgiten eall &t;&ae;t &t;&ae;t wit &ae;r spr&ae;con. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; ic: Hw&ae;t h&ae;bbe ic forgiten &t;&ae;s &t;e wit &ae;r spr&ae;con? 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; he: Wit s&ae;don &ae;r &t;&ae;t sio godcunde foretiohhung &ae;lc god worhte &amp; nan yfel  ne nan ne tiohhode to wyrcanne  ne n&ae;fre ne worhte. 
 Ge fur&d;um &t;&ae;t wit gereahton to goodum &t;&ae;t folciscum monnum yfel &t;uhte; &t;&ae;t w&ae;s &t;&ae;t mon wr&ae;ce &amp; witnode hwone for his yfle. 
 Hu ne s&ae;don wit eac &ae;r on &t;isse ilcan bec &t;&ae;t God h&ae;fde getiohhod freodom to sellanne monnum  &amp; swa dyde. 
 &amp; gif hi &t;one freodom tela gehealdon  &t;&ae;t he hi wolde swi&d;e weor&d;ian mid ece life; &amp; gif hi &d;one freodom forheolden  &t;&ae;t he hi &t;onne wolde witnian mid dea&d;e. 
 He tiohhode  gif hi hw&ae;t gesyngoden on &d;&ae;m freodome  &t;&ae;t hi hit eft on &d;&ae;m freodome mid hreowsunga gebeten; &amp; gif hiora hwylc swa heardheort w&ae;re &t;&ae;t he nane hreowsunge ne dyde  &t;&ae;t he &t;onne h&ae;fde rihtlic wite. 
 Ealla gesceafta he h&ae;fde getiohhod &t;eowu  buton englum &amp; monnum. 
 For&d;y&t;e &t;a o&d;ra gesceafta &t;eowe sint  hi healda&d; hiora &t;egnunga o&d; domes d&ae;g; ac &t;a men &amp; &t;a englas  &t;e freo sint  forl&ae;ta&d; hiora &t;egnunga. 
 Hw&ae;t magon men cwe&d;an &t;&ae;t sio godcunde foretiohhung getiohhod h&ae;fde &t;&ae;s &d;e hio ne &t;urhtuge? 
 o&d;&d;e hu magon hi hi aladian &t;&ae;t hi ne m&ae;gen good don  nu hit awriten is &t;&ae;t God gelde &ae;lcum men be his gewyrhtum? 
 Hwy sceall &t;onne &ae;nig mon bion idel  &d;&ae;t he ne wyrce? 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; ic: Genoh &t;u me h&ae;fst gefreolsod &t;&ae;re tweounge mines modes be &t;&ae;re ascunga &t;e ic &t;e ahsade. 
 Ac ic &t;e wolde giet acsian sumre spr&ae;ce &d;e me ymbe tweo&d;. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; he: Hw&ae;t is &t;&ae;t? 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; ic: Genog cu&d; me is &t;&ae;t God hit wat eall beforan  ge good ge yfel  &ae;r hit geweor&d;e; ac ic nat hw&ae;&d;er hit eall geweor&d;an sceal unanwendendlice &t;&ae;t he wat &amp; getiohhod h&ae;f&d;. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; he: Ne &d;earf hit no eall geweor&d;an unanwendendlice; ac sum hit sceal geweor&d;an unanwendendlice; &t;&ae;t bi&d; &t;&ae;tte ure ned&t;earf bi&d;  &amp; his willa bi&d;. 
 Ac hit is sum swa gerad &t;&ae;t his nis nan ned&t;earf  &amp; &t;eah ne dere&d; no &t;eah hit geweor&d;e; ne nan hearm ne bi&d;  &t;eah hit no ne geweor&d;e. 
 Ge&t;enc nu be &d;e selfum hw&ae;&d;er &t;u &ae;nig &t;ing swa f&ae;st getiohhod h&ae;bbe &t;&ae;t &t;e &t;ince &t;&ae;t hit n&ae;fre &t;inum willum onwend ne weor&d;e  ne &t;u butan bion ne m&ae;ge; o&d;&d;e hw&ae;&d;er &t;u eft on &ae;ngum ge&t;eahte swa twior&ae;de sie &t;&ae;t &t;e helpe hw&ae;&d;er hit geweor&d;e  &d;e hit no ne geweor&d;e. 
 Fela is &t;ara &t;inga &t;e God &ae;r wat &ae;r hit geweor&d;e  &amp; wat eac &t;&ae;t hit dere&d; his gesceaftum gif hit gewyr&d;. 
 Nat he hit no for&d;y&t;e he wille &t;&ae;t hit geweor&d;e  ac for&d;y &t;e he wile forwernan &t;&ae;t hit ne geweor&d;e  swa swa good scipstiora ongit micelne wind on hreore s&ae; &ae;r &ae;r hit geweor&d;e  &amp; h&ae;t fealdan &t;&ae;t segl &amp; eac hwilum lecgan &t;one m&ae;st  &amp; l&ae;tan &t;a b&ae;tinge. 
 gif he &ae;r &t;weores windes b&ae;tte  warena&d; he hine wi&d; &d;&ae;t weder. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; ic: Swi&d;e wel &t;u min h&ae;fst geholpen &ae;t &t;&ae;re spr&ae;ce  &amp; ic wundrige hwy swa m&ae;nige wise men swa swi&d;e swuncen mid &t;&ae;re spr&ae;ce  &amp; swa lytel gewis funden. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; he: Hw&ae;s wundrast &t;u &t;&ae;r swa swi&d;e  swa e&d;e swa hit is to ongitanne? 
 Hu ne wast &t;u &t;&ae;t manig &t;ing ne bi&d; no ongiten swa swa hit bi&d;  ac swa swa &t;&ae;s andgites m&ae;&d; bi&d; &t;e &t;&ae;r&ae;fter spyre&d;? 
 Swilc is se wisdom &t;&ae;t hine ne m&ae;g nan mon of &t;isse weorulde ongitan swilcne swylce he is; ac &ae;lc win&d; be his andgites m&ae;&d;e &t;&ae;t he hine wolde ongitan gif he meahte. 
 Ac se wisdom m&ae;g us eallunga ongitan swylce swylce we sint  &t;eah we hine ne m&ae;gen ongitan eallunga swylcne swylce he is; for&d;&ae;m se wisdom is God. 
 He gesih&d; eall ure weorc ge good ge yfel  &ae;r hi gewordene sien  o&d;&d;e fur&d;um ge&t;oht; ac he us ne ned no &t;y hra&d;or to &t;&ae;m &t;&ae;t we nede scylen good don  ne us ne wern&d; &t;&ae;t we yfel don  for&d;&ae;m&t;e he us sealde freodom. 
 Ic &t;e m&ae;g eac t&ae;can sume bisne &t;&ae;t &t;u &t;e y&d; ongitan meahte &d;a spr&ae;ce. 
 Hw&ae;t  &t;u wast &t;&ae;t gesih&d; &amp; gehernes &amp; gefrednes ongita&d; &t;one lichoman &t;&ae;s monnes  &amp; &t;eah ne ongita&d; hi hine no gelicne. 
 &t;a earan ongita&d; &t;&ae;t hi gehera&d;  &amp; ne ongita&d; hi &t;eah &t;one lichoman eallunga swylcne swylce he bi&d;; sio gefrednes hine m&ae;g gegrapian &amp; gefredan &t;&ae;t hit lichoma bi&d;  ac hio ne m&ae;g gefredan hw&ae;&d;er he bi&d; &t;e bl&ae;c &t;e hwit  &d;e f&ae;ger &d;e unf&ae;ger. 
 Ac sio gesih&d; &ae;t frumcerre  swa &t;a eagan on besio&d;  hi ongita&d; ealle &t;one andwlitan &d;&ae;s lichoman. 
 Ac ic wolde get reccan sume race  &t;&ae;t &d;u wisse hw&ae;s &t;u wundrode. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; ic: Hw&ae;t is &t;&ae;t? 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; he: Hit is &t;&ae;t se an man ongit &t;&ae;t &t;&ae;t he on o&d;rum ongit synderlice; he hine ongit &t;urh &t;a eagan synderlice  &t;urh &t;a earan synderlice  &t;urh his r&ae;delsan synderlice  &t;urh gesceadwisnesse synderlice  &t;urh gewis andgit. 
 Manige sint cwucera gesceafta unstirende  swa swa nu scylfiscas sint  &amp; habba&d; &t;eah sumne d&ae;l andgites  for&d;&ae;m hi ne meahton elles libban  gif hi nan grot andgites n&ae;fden. 
 Sume magon gesion  sume magon geheran  sume gefredan  sume gestincan. 
 Ac &t;a styriendan netenu sint monnum gelicran  for&d;&ae;m hy habba&d; eall &t;&ae;t &d;a unstyriendan habba&d;  &amp; eac mare to; &t;&ae;t is &t;&ae;t hi onhyria&d; monnum; lufia&d; &t;&ae;t hi lufia&d; &amp; hatia&d; &t;&ae;t hi hatia&d;  &amp; flio&d; &t;&ae;t hi hatia&d; &amp; seca&d; &t;&ae;t hi lufia&d;. 
 &d;a men &d;onne habba&d; eall &t;&ae;t we &ae;r ymbe spr&ae;con  &amp; eac toeacan &t;am micle gife gesceadwisnesse. 
 Englas &t;onne habba&d; gewiss andgit. 
 For&t;am sint &d;as sceafta &t;us gesceapene &t;&ae;t &d;a unstyriendan hi ne ahebben ofer &t;a styriendan  ne him wi&d; ne winnan  ne &t;a styriendan ofer &t;a men  ne &t;a men ofer &t;a englas  ne &t;a englas wi&d; God. 
 Ac &t;&ae;t is earmlic &t;&ae;t se m&ae;sta d&ae;l monna ne sec&d; no &t;&ae;t &t;&ae;t him forgifen is  &t;&ae;t is gesceadwisness; ne &t;&ae;t ne sec&d; &t;&ae;t him ofer is  &t;&ae;t is &t;&ae;t englas habba&d; &amp; wise men; &t;&ae;t is gewis andget. 
 Ac mest monna nu onhyre&d; nu neatum on &t;am &t;&ae;t hi willnia&d; woruldlusta swa swa netenu. 
 Ac gif we nu h&ae;fdon &ae;nigne d&ae;l untwiogendes andgites swa swa englas habba&d;  &t;onne mihte we ongiton &t;&ae;t &t;&ae;t andget bi&d; micle betere &t;onne ure gesceadwisnes se. 
 &t;eah we fela smean  we habba&d; litellne gearowitan buton tweon; ac &t;am englum nis nan tweo nanes &t;&ae;ra &t;inga &t;e hi witon. 
 for&t;i is hiora gearowito swa micle betra &t;onne ure gesceadwisnes se  swa ure gesceadwisnes is betere &t;onne nytena andgit sie  o&d;&d;e &t;&ae;s gewittes &ae;nig d&ae;l &t;e him forgifen is au&t;er o&d;&d;e hrorum neatum o&d;&d;e unhrorum. 
 Ac uton nu habban ure mod up swa swa we yfemest m&ae;gen wi&d; &t;&ae;s hean hrofes &t;&ae;s hehstan andgites  &t;&ae;t &d;u m&ae;ge hr&ae;dlicost cumon &amp; e&d;elicost to &t;inre agenre cy&d;&d;e &t;onan &t;e &d;u &ae;r come. 
 &t;&ae;r m&ae;g &t;in mod &amp; &t;in gesceadwisnes geseon openlice &t;&ae;t &t;&ae;t hit nu ymb tweo&d; &ae;lces &t;inges  &ae;g&t;er ge be &t;&ae;re godcundan foresceawunge &t;e we nu oft ymb spr&ae;con  ge be urum frydome  ge swa be eallum &t;ingum. 
 &d;a se Wisdom &t;a &t;is spell as&ae;d h&ae;fde  &t;a ongan he singan &amp; &t;us cw&ae;&d;: Hw&ae;t  &t;u miht ongitan &t;&ae;t manig wyht is mistlice ferende geond eor&t;an  &amp; sint swi&d;e ungelices hiwes  &amp; ungelice fara&d;. 
 Sume licga&d; mid eallon lichoman on eor&t;an  &amp; swa smuhende fara&d; &t;&ae;t him nau&t;er ne fet ne fi&d;eras ne fultuma&d;. 
 &amp; sume bi&d; twiofete  sume fiowerfete  sume fleogende  &amp; ealle &t;eah bio&d; ofdune healde wi&d; &t;&ae;re eor&d;an  &amp; &t;ider willnia&d;  o&d;&d;e &t;&ae;s &t;e hi lyst o&d;&d;e &t;&ae;s &t;e hi be&t;urfon. 
 Ac se mann ana g&ae;&t; uprihte; &t;&ae;t tacna&d; &t;&ae;t he sceal ma &t;encan up &t;onne ny&d;er  &t;i l&ae;s &t;&ae;t mod sie nio&d;oror &t;onne &d;e lichoma. 
 &d;a se Wisdom &d;a &d;is leo&d; asungen h&ae;fde  &d;a cw&ae;&d; he: For&d;y we scoldon ealle m&ae;gene spyrian &ae;fter Gode  &t;&ae;t we wissen hw&ae;t he w&ae;re. 
 &d;eah hit ure m&ae;&d; ne sie &t;&ae;t we witen hwylc he sie  we sculon &t;eah be &t;&ae;s andgites m&ae;&d;e &t;e he us gif&d; fandian; swa swa we &ae;r cw&ae;don &t;&ae;t mon scolde &ae;lc &t;ing ongitan be his andgites m&ae;&t;e  for&d;&ae;m we ne magon &ae;lc &t;ing ongitan swylc swylce hit bi&d;. 
 &ae;lc gesceaft &d;eah &ae;g&d;er ge gesceadwis ge ungesceadwis &t;&ae;t sweotola&d; &t;&ae;t God ece is  for&d;&ae;m n&ae;fre swa manega gesceafta &amp; swa micla &amp; swa f&ae;gra hi ne under&d;iodden l&ae;ssan gesceafte &amp; l&ae;ssan anwalde &t;onne hi ealle sindon  ne fur&d;um emnmiclum. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; ic: Hw&ae;t is ecnes? 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; he: &t;u me ahsast micles &amp; earfo&d;es to ongitanne; gif &t;u hit witan wilt  &d;u scealt habban &ae;r &t;ines modes eagan cl&ae;ne &amp; hlutor. 
 Ne m&ae;g ic &d;e nauht helan &d;&ae;s &d;e ic wat. 
 Wast &t;u &t;&ae;t &t;reo &d;ing sindon on &t;is middangearde? 
 An is hwilendlic  &d;&ae;t h&ae;f&d; &ae;g&d;er ge fruman ge ende; &amp; ic nat &d;eah nanwuht &d;&ae;s &d;e hwilendlic is  nau&d;er ne his fruman ne his ende. 
 O&d;er &d;ing is ece  &t;&ae;t h&ae;f&d; fruman &amp; n&ae;f&d; n&ae;nne ende; &amp; ic wat hwonne hit ongin&d;  &amp; wat &t;&ae;t hit n&ae;fre ne geenda&d;; &t;&ae;t sint englas &amp; monna saula. 
 &t;ridde &d;ing is ece buton ende &amp; buton anginne; &t;&ae;t is God. 
 Betweoh &t;&ae;m &t;rim is swi&d;e micel toscead. 
 Gif wit &t;&ae;t eall sculon tosmeagan  &t;onne cume wit late to ende &t;isse bec  o&d;&d;e n&ae;fre. 
 Ac an &t;ing &d;u scealt nede &t;&ae;ran witan: forhwy God is gehaten sio hehste ecnes. 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; ic: Hwy? 
 &d;a cw&ae;&d; he: For&d;on &t;e we witon swi&d;e lytel &d;&ae;s &t;e &ae;r us w&ae;s buton be gemynde &amp; be ge&ae;scum  &amp; get l&ae;sse &t;&ae;s &d;e &ae;fter us bi&d;. 
 &t;&ae;t an us is gewislice andweard &t;&ae;t &t;e &t;onne bi&d;; ac him is eall andweard  ge &t;&ae;tte &ae;r w&ae;s  ge &t;&ae;tte nu is  ge &t;&ae;tte &ae;fter us bi&d;; eall &t;&ae;t is him andweard. 
 Ne wex&d; his wela na  ne eac n&ae;fre ne wana&d;. 
 Ne ofman he n&ae;fre nane wuht  for&d;&ae;m he n&ae;fre nauht ne forgeat. 
 Ne sec&d; he nanwuht  ne ne smea&d;  for&d;&ae;m&t;e he hit wat eall. 
 Ne sec&d; he nanwuht  for&d;y he nanwuht ne forleas. 
 Ne eht he nanre wuhte  for&d;y hine nanwuht ne m&ae;g flion; ne ondr&ae;t he him nane wuht  for&d;&ae;m he n&ae;f&d; n&ae;nne ricran ne fur&d;um n&ae;nne gelican. 
 Simle he bi&d; gifende  &amp; ne wana&d; his n&ae;fre nauht. 
 Symle he bi&d; &ae;lmihtig  for&d;&ae;m he symle wile good &amp; n&ae;fre nan yfel. 
 Nis him nanes &t;inges ned&t;earf. 
 Symle he bi&d; lociende  ne sl&ae;p&d; he n&ae;fre. 
 Symle he bi&d; gelice man&t;w&ae;re. 
 Symle he bi&d; ece  for&t;&ae;m n&ae;fre sio tid n&ae;s &t;&ae;t he n&ae;re  ne n&ae;fre ne wyr&d;. 
 Simle he bi&d; freoh  ne bi&d; he to nanum weorce geneded. 
 For his godcundlicum anwalde he is &ae;ghw&ae;r andweard. 
 His micelnesse ne m&ae;g nan man ametan; nis &t;&ae;t &d;eah no licumlice to wenanne  ac gastlice  swa swa nu wisdom is &amp; rihtwisnes  for&d;&ae;m he &t;&ae;t is self. 
 Ac hw&ae;t ofermodie ge &t;onne  o&d;&d;e hwy ahebbe ge eow wi&d; swa heane anwald? 
 for&d;&ae;m ge nauht wi&d; hine don ne magon; for&d;&ae;m se eca &amp; se &ae;lmehtga symle sit on &t;&ae;m heahsetle his anwaldes; &t;onan he m&ae;g eall gesion  &amp; gilt &ae;lcum be &t;am swi&d;e rihte &ae;fter his gewyrhtum. 
 For&d;&ae;m hit nis no unnet &t;&ae;t we hopien to Gode  for&d;&ae;m he ne went no swa swa we do&d;. 
 Ac bidda&d; hine eadmodlice  for&d;&ae;m he is swi&d;e rummod &amp; swi&d;e mildheort. 
 Hebba&d; eower mod to him mid eowrum hondum  &amp; bidda&d; &t;&ae;s &t;e riht sie &amp; eower &t;earf sie  for&d;&ae;m he eow nele wyrnan. 
 Hatia&d; yfel &amp; fleo&d; swa ge swi&d;ost m&ae;gen; lufia&d; cr&ae;ftas  &amp; folgia&d; &t;&ae;m. 
 Ge habba&d; micle ned&d;earfe &t;&ae;t ge symle wel don  for&d;&ae;m ge symle beforan &t;am ecan &amp; &t;&ae;m &ae;lmihtgan Gode do&d; eall &t;&ae;t &t;&ae;t ge do&d;; eall he hit gesih&d;  &amp; eall he hit forgilt.
